Apastama-Sulbasutra
with the commentaries of Kapardi, Karavinda and Sundararaja


Input by members of the Sansknet project


This GRETIL version has been converted from a custom Devanagari encoding.
Therefore, word boundaries are usually not marked by blanks.
These and other irregularities cannot be standardized at present.


THE TEXT IS NOT PROOF-READ!

The SUTRA TEXT (only) of this GRETIL version has been checked
against the edition by Albert BÅrk, ZDMG 55 (1901), pp. 578-591.
Despite numerous corrections, the text of the commentaries
is in urgent need of proof-reading!

Extracted sutra text available as a separate file.


REFERENCE SYSTEM according to BÅrk's edition.
Where required by the commentaries, the sutras were split,
e.g.: ˘p¡us_1.2a, ˘p¡us_1.2b, ˘p¡us_1.2c etc.

shrIH

ApastambashulbasUtraM kapardibhAShyasahitam


uktA yaj~nAH /
teShAM agnyAyatanAni niyatapramANAni niyatadeshAni /

teShAmAyAmavistArAnvaktukAma Aha--vihAra yogAniti--


___________________________________________________________


vihArayogAn vyAkhyAsyAmaH || ˘p¡us_1.1 ||

___________________________________________________________



vihiyante 'sminnagnaya iti vihArAH prAgvaMshAdayo gArha patyAdayash ca /

yujyate 'neneti yogaH rajjuvisheShaH /
vihArANAM yogo vihArayogaH /
viharaNameva vA vihAraH /

teShAM yogo vihArayogaH /
tasya kR^itsnaM pratipAdanamityarthaH /
yogAniti bahuvacanaM bahubhiH prakArairdarshayitum /
darshanaM ca prAdhAnya pratipacyartham /
yathA rathAdayo niyatAN^gapramANA ekasiminn aN^ge 'pi mAtrayA vihIyamAne samyakU na gacchanti evamagnyAyata nAdInyapi mAtrayA vihIyamAnAni sAdhanabhAvaM na gacchanti tasmAdyatnena sampAdanIyAni. sarvatra vij~nAyata iti shrutInAmupanyAsAtsarvathA AyAmAdaya iktaireva margaiHsamyaksampAdanIyAH /
AyatanAnAM bhreShe ca prAyashvittena bhavitavyam /

amumevArthaM pradarshayituM shulbAntare "athAtaH' shabdau prayuktau--"athAto vihArayogAn' iti /

AditastAvaddishAM grahaNaM vaktavyamanenAyAryeNa noktam /
tacchulbAntarato grAhyam /
""kR^ittikAH khalvimAH prAcIM dishaM na paricahati /
tAsAM darshanena mApayedityekam /
shroNAdarsha nena mApayedityekam /
citnAsvAtyorantarAlenetyaparam /
"iti bhagapatA bodhAyanena prAgvaMshamAnamadhikR^ityoktam /
kR^ittikAdayo yatra nilIyante sA prAcI digiti citrAsvAtyor madhye udakamapasthApya pradibimbaM dR^iShTva grAhyam /
atha vA yatra devayajanaM, mR^ijjalena taM deshaM samIkR^itya madhye shaN^kuM nihatya shaN^kupramANayA ravjjA maNDalaM parilikhya shaN^kucchA yAgraM pUrvAhne yatra maNDalalekhAM spR^ishati tatra shaN^kuM nihatya nirgamavelAyAM cAparahNe /
tau pUrvAparau /
sUkShmamicchan shvobhUte-pUrvAhte shaN^kucchAyAgrarekhAyAmeva lakShaNaM kR^itvA shaN^kulakShaNayorantarAlaM pratIcyAM dishi yaHshaN^kuH taM pratsapasArayet upakramadeshaM prati /



ApastambashulbasUtravyAkhyA karavindIyA


omityekAkShArAkhyeyaM vande vA«nasAtigam /
pashyanti kavayo yaddhi tadviShNoH paramaM padam /
lakShmIsahAyamatasIkusumacchavi shAshvatam /
jyotirmeM hR^idaye bhUyAtAsadA rAjIvalocanam //

ApastambAya munaye namo vedArthabhUmayo /
yatsUtrasaktAstiShThante yaj~nashrutikumArikAH /
tatsUtrashulbavyAkhyeyamakSharArthAvabodhinI /
karavindAdhipenAdya kriyate bhAShyakR^inmate //


yaj~navyAkhyApratij~nAM kurvatA bhagavatA'pastambena vyAkhyeyatayA haviryaj~nAH somayaj~nAH pAkayaj~nAsh ca pratij~nAtA vyAkhyAtAsh ca /
tatra tAvadaiShTikasaumikapAshubandhikadArvIhaumikAH samaviShama dhanirmaNDalacaturashratrayashranAnAshrayo gArhapatyAyatanaprabhR^iticityeShTakAparyantA niyataparimaNadeshavisheShAstatratatroktAH, te 'pi mAtavyA iti tadvimAnaM prati sAdhanabhUtaravjjAdInAM sAdhanabhUtasyaitAvatI rajjuretAvataH kShetrasya karaNIti svarUpamAtreNa j~nAtumashakyatvAttatpratipAdanamapashyaM kartavyamiti yaj~navyAkhyAnAnantaraM vihArayogavyAkhyA kriyate--

vihAro viharaNam /
yogastatsAdhanam /
vihArANAM yogAH

vihArayogAstAnvyAkhyAsyAmaH pratipAdayiShyAmaH /
vipUrvo haratiH

krIDAprajvalanabandhanasaMcaraNavimAnAdyanekArthakaH /
tatkriyAvisheShasambandhAdeva deshAdiShu tatratatrArthe vihAravyapadeshaH /
atra tuvimAnavAcI /
yujish ca dvividhaH--samAdhivAcI

saMbandhavAcI ca /
atra tu samAdhivAcI /
vedyAdeHsamyagavasthAnaM samAdhiH, "sa samAviH' ityatra vakShyate /
yujyante ebhiriti yogAH, viharaNopAyabhUtA ravjjAdayaH /

"pR^iShThyAntayoH' ityAdinA vimAtavyasya vedyAdikShetrasya shroNyaMsAnAM vividhasaMpAdanAvacchedo viharaNam /
tatsAdhanabhUtA ravjjAdayo vihArayogAH, tAnvacAkhyAsyAmaH /
vyArUyAnaM nAma sati sandehe balavatA hetunopapAdya vivaraNaM, yathA-

"sama caturashrA anupapadatvAcchabdasya mAnArtheShu yathAkAmishabdArthasya vishayitvAt, ityevamAdikam /
nanu kuto vihArasya bhAvavA citvaM, kuto vA tasya vimAnaparyAyatvaM, kuto viharaNasya vedyAdisaMbandhaH, kuto vA tatra ravjjAdInAM karaNatvaM, kuto vA

yujeHsamAdhivacanatA, kathaM vA ravjjAdiShu yogavAyavahAraH? ucyate--"uktaM viharaNaM "vyAkhyAtaM viharaNam' iti bhAvapratyayanirdeshAt bhAvavacano vihArashabdaH

"tadekaravjjA viharaNaM' "ravjjA vA vimAya' iti ravjjakArye vimAnaviharaNayoratra

darshanAdubhayoH paryAya tvAm /
"etAvanti j~neyAni vediviharaNAni bhavanti' ityanena viharaNasya vedyAdisambandhaH /
"AgantucaturthamAyAmashvAkShNayArajjuH pramANamAtrI rajjuM' iti tatra tatra karaNIShu rajju vyapadeshitvavashAt pArshvamAnI tirya«bhAnIdi karaNyaShTAdashakaraNIti tatratatra rutrIliN^ganirdeshAt rajjveti tR^itIyAshrutesh ca

rajjUnAM viharaNe sAdhanatvaM ata eva hetoretatkarma shulbamityAcakShate /
AcAryA etaM grantharAshiM "sa samAdhiH' "athAparo yogaH' iti vakShyanti /
tena j~nAyate yujeHsamAdhivacanatA /
yujerarthasya samAdherviharaNasAdhyatvAt /
viharaNasAdhanAnyapi yogasAdhanAni bhavantIti ravjjAdayo yogA ityucyante /
vi hArayogaparatAM j~nApayituM viharaNasAdhaneShu yogavyavahAraH /
yogagrahaNaM kimarthaM ? sAdhanatvapratItyarthamityuktam /

evaM tarhi na vaktavyaM darshapUrNamAsau vyAkhyAsyAma ityAdiShu pratij~nAnantaraM sAdhanAnyeva vyAkhyeyatayAvagamyante /
evaM tarhi yogagrahaNaM mAnasAdhaneShu prAdhAnyakhyApanArthaM /
kiM tat prAdhAnyam ? yadyapi padaveNvAdIni mAnasAdhanAni santi, tadhApi tairvimAne bahu prayatnasAdhyA samyagvedyAdikShetrasamAdhisiddhiH, pajjusIrAdibhir vimAne tasyAH siddhirIShatkarItyetadatra prAdhAnyaM /
nanu ravjjAdInAM viharaNasAdhanatvaM lokato 'pi setsyati, kimarthamidamucyate vihArayogAnvyAkhyAsyAma iti? ucyate--satyaM setsyati /
tathApi

kAlavaddeshasyApyaN^gatvAduktapramANasya deshasya tilamAtrapra mANAdapi nyUnAdhikabhAve

satyaN^gavaiguNyaM syAditi manyamAna AcAryo ravjjAdInAmasandigdhamIShatkaramupAyabhAvaM svayameva pratipAdayitumidaM brUte /
ato nyUnAdhikabhAve pariharaNIye sati pramAdAdasAmatharyAdvA yadi bhreSha upajAyate tatrAvashyaM prAyAshvittaM kartavyamityetadarthamidamucyate "vihArayogAnvyAkhyAsyAmaH' iti /

athavA vihriyanta iti vihArAH /
yogAsh ca tatsaMpAdanopAyabhUtAsta eva rajjvAdayaH /
atra kecinniyatadiksaMyogAdInAM vedyAdInAmaj~nAtadigvisheShaiH puruShairviharaNaM kartum ashakyamiti digvisheShaj~nApanArthamAdAveva dishaM lakShaNIkurvanti /

yathA'ha bhagavAn kAtyAyanaH-- "same shaN^kuM nikhAya shaN^kusaMmitayA ravjjA maNDalaM parilikhya yatra lekhayoHshaN^kagravacchAyA nipatati sA prAcI /
tatra shaN^kuM nikhAya tadanantaraM ravjjAbhyasya pAshau kR^itvA shak«voH pAshau pratimucya lakShaNena dakShiNApAyamya madhyamashaN^kurevamuttarataHsodIcI'' iti /

asyArthaH--atha yatra shucau deshe devayajanaM kIraShyan bhavati taM deshaM jalena samIkR^itya madhye shaN^kuM nihatya shaN^kusaMmitAmekataH pAshAM rajjuM kR^itvA shak«au pratimucya tayA maNDalaM parilirUya maNDalarekhAyAM pUrvAhne yatra shak«vagracchAyA nipatati tatra binduM kuryAt tau pUrvaparau bindU sA ca pracI dik /

bindvordvayoHshaN^kuM nikhAya tadantaradviguNAM rajjumubhayataHpAshAM kR^itvA madhye lakShaNaM kR^itvA shak«voH pAshau pratimucya lakShaNena dakShiNApAyamya lakShaNe shaN^kuM kuryAd evam uttarato 'pi lakShaNenApAyamya shaN^kuM kuryAt /
tau shaN^kU dakShiNottarau sA udIcI digiti /
tathA jyotirj~nAne /



iShTamaNDalamadhyasthashaN^kucchAyAgravTattayoH /

yogAbhyAM kR^itamatsyena j~neye yAmyottare dishau' iti /
evamanyairapi bahuprakAraM dishAM grahaNaM tatra tatroktamiti

prasiddhatvAdevAcAryeNeha noktaM /
pramIyate 'neneti vyutpacyA pArshvamAnyAdInAM pramANatve siddhe pramANAmiti paribhAShyate //


ApastambashulbasUtravyAkhyA

sundararAjIyA



Apastambena yo 'yaM vyaraci bhagavatA shulbasaMj~no gabhIraH prashno 'rthaM tasya bhAShyaprabhR^itiShu kathitaM vIkShya kR^itsnam /

saMkShipyobdodhanArthaM kushikakulanidhermAdhavAryasya yaShTuH putraH shulbapradIpaM vivaraNamadhunA sundaro nirmimIte //


vihAro viharaNaM, caturashrAdirUpeNa bhmeH karaNam /
tasya yogAH upAyAH /



kapardibhAShyam


___________________________________________________________


yAvadAyAmaM pramANam || ˘p¡us_1.2a ||

___________________________________________________________



yAvadAyAmamityavyayIbhAvaH /
yAvadavadhAraNa iti /
kimatrAvadhAryate? AyAmaH /

AyAma eva pramANamiti na, tirya«bhAnyakShNayA rajjU /
tAbhyAmapi piharaNasya shakyatvAt /

pramANasaMj~nAyAH prayojanaM "pramANaM tR^itIyena vardhayedityAyAma saMpraj~nAnArtham /



karavindIyA vyAkhya

yAvamANama.

yAvacchabdaH parimANavAcI, AyAmashabdo vistArapratiyogivacanaH /

"yAvadavadhAraNe iti samAsaH /
yAvAnAyAmastAvat pramANaM bhavati, kimatrAvadhAryate?

AyAmaparimANameva pramANamiti /
tadatrA'yAmasya dviguNatvAttadAshrayabhUtarajjvAdipramANam iti /
asya pramANaM tiryagAdiShu prayojanam,

kapardibhAShyam



___________________________________________________________


tadardhamabhyasyAparasmiMstR^itIye ShaDbhAgone lakShaNaM karoti || ˘p¡us_1.2b ||

___________________________________________________________



taditi pramANaM rAmR^ishyate /
tadardhaM abhyasya prakShipya pramANasyopari

aparasmiMstR^itIye ShaDbhAgone lakShaNaM karoti /
abhyAsasahitaM pramANaM ubhayataH pAshau kR^itvAparasmin bhAge tR^itIye lakShaNaM tiraJNjanaM karoti /
AyAmasya ShaDbhAgone lakShaNaM kuryAt //


___________________________________________________________


pR^iShThyAntayorantau niyamya lakShaNena dakShiNApAyamya nimitaM karoti || ˘p¡us_1.2c ||

___________________________________________________________



pR^iShThe bhavA pR^iShThyA /
tasyA antayoHshaN^kU nihatya tayoH pAshau pratimucya lakShaNena dakShiNApAyamya nimittaM karoti, lakShaNena prasArya yathA ShaDbhAgonA tirya«bhAnI shiShTAkShNayA rajjuH evamapasArayati /
nimittaM nihanyAt //


karavindIyA vyAkhyA

tadardha karoti.

idAnIM tAvadaiShTikasaumikapAshubandhikAnAM prAyeNa dIrghacaturashratvAttadanurUpaMviharaNamucyate--

pramANamityeva tacchabdenAyAmabhUtaM pramANaM parAmR^ishyate /
tasyArdhaM tadardhaM, abhyasanamuparikShepaH, aparasmina pashcAddhAvi nyAgantau, tR^itIye pramANArdhAbhyAM saha tR^itIye, ShaDbhAgone--ShaShTho bhAgaHShaDbhAgaH tena bhAgena hIne tasminneva tR^itIye, lakShaNaM lakShyate yena tallakShaNaM vimAtavyakShetrasya koTiparij~nAnopAyabhUtaM cihnaM karoti

kuryAt, pR^iShThyAntayoH--vimAtavyakShetrasya madhyaM pR^iShThaM, kuta etadavagamyate?

tadavayaveShu shroNyaMsapArshvavyapadeshAdyathA shroNyaMsadeshapArshvAnAM madhyaM pR^iShThaM epamidamapIti! tatra bhavA rekhA pR^iShThyA /
tadantayoHshaN^kuM nikhAya rajjvantau pAshau kR^itvA tayorniyamya pratimucya lakShaNena cihnena dakShiNApAyamya--dakShiNato 'pakR^iShya rajjuM tatra nimittaM kShetrakoTij~nAnahetuM shaN^kuM kuryAt /



kapardibhAShyam

___________________________________________________________


evamuttarato viparyasyetarataH sa samAdhiH  || ˘p¡us_1.2d ||

___________________________________________________________



evamudagapasArya pUrvavatkuryAt /
viparyasyetarataH pUrvesmAcchaN^kAH pAshamunmucyAparasmin shak«au pratimuJNcet /
aparasmAc chaN^kAH pAshamunmucya pUrvasminpratimuJNcet /
sa viparyAsaH /
taM kR^itvetarataH aMsau tenaiva prathamakR^itena ShaDbhAgonena lakShaNena dakShiNamaMsaM udagapasAryottaramaMsamiti sa samAdhiH /
uktena mArgavisheSheNApAditAH pArshvamAnyAdaya iti samAdhiH /



karavindIyA vyAkhyA

evamuttarato 'pi vikR^iShya rajjuM nimittaM kuryAt, viparyAso rajjvantayoH pUrvaM pAshaM pashcime shak«au pashcimaM ca pUrvasmin kR^itvA itarataH kR^itanimittAt pradeshAdanyatra tatra ca dakShiNata uttaratash ca vikR^iShya nimitte kuryAt /
etaduktaM bhavati--ayAmArthaM pramANe prakShipya prakShiptaM ShoDhA vibhajya tasmin antAdArabhya paJNcasu bhogeShvatIteShu lakShaNasyAntau pAshau kR^itvA pR^iShThyAntayoHshaN^kuM nikAya tayoH pratimucya lakShaNena dakShiNApAyamya shaN^kuM kuryAt, uttarato 'pyevameva vikR^iShya shaN^kuM kuryAt, rajjvantau viparyasyetarasminnapi pradeshe shaN^kudvayaM kuryaditi, nanu aparagrahaNaM pUrvatR^itIye lakShaNavyAvR^icyarthaM kiM na syAt, tatrApi tasyAvirodhAdeva na syAt /
tarhi madhayamatR^itIyaM vyAkartya pUrvAparayoH pradarshanArthaM bhaviShyatIti cennaitatyadyevamiShTamabhaviShyattarhi spaShTataraMmadhyame tR^itIya ityevAvakShyat, na cAsau tattathoktavAn /
atha manyase? tadarthamabhayasyAparasminn ityukte 'bhyAsAdanyat, pramANamaparaM pratIyate, sAmarthyAttatra tR^itIye lakShaNaM bhavatviti, naitadapi yuktaM--yadayamAgantvAyAmAbhyAsaH iti

AgantvavayavasyAkShNayArajjusheShatAM vakShyati /
pahAvedimAne ca ShaTAtriMshikAyAmaShTAdashopa shamasyetyAdau paJNcadashikenaivApAyamya shroNyaMsAnAM viharaNaM vakShyAti, tenAtrAbhyAsAganturevAparaH, tatra ShaDbhAgone niraJNjanamiti vij~nAyate /

nanu yadyAgantuparo 'parashabdaH tarhi ShaDbhAgone lakShaNamityetAvadevAlaM, kimarthaH

tR^itIyashabdaH, naivAsya prayojanaM pashyAmaH, ucyate--astyevAsya prayojanaM, kuM tat, atrocyamA naviharaNasya sarvAbhyAsaviShayatvakhyApanArthaM, tatkathaM, atra tAvadAcAryeNa sarvaj~nena sarvAnugrahakAriNA prayuktasyAkSharAvayavasyApi nAnarthakatA yuktA, kiM punaH padasya /
ato mukhyayA vR^icyA yathA shabdor'thavAn bhavati tathA vyAkhyeyaH /

ata evAyaM shabda evaM vyAkhyAyate--AgantusamAnAdhikaraNIbhUtatR^itIyashabdasyAvayavabhUtatrishabdavAcyena tritvena sAbhyAsasya pramANasyAgantuparimitA yAvanto bhAgAHsaMbhavanti tAvatAM bhAgAnAM sakh«yA lakShyate, tathA--ShaDbAgashabdAvayavabhUtaShaTachabdavAcyena ca ShaTtvena tadanurUpatvAya tritvalakShitasakh«yAdviguNIbhUtAbhAgasaMkh«yA lakShyate /
etenAyamarthaHsaMpadyate-- 
sarveShvabhyAseShu sAbhyAsasya pramANasyAgantuparimitA yAvanto bhAgAHsampadyante tAvaddviguNabhAgamAgantuM kR^itvA tasmin bhAgenaikena hIne lakShaNakaraNamiti /

tadyathA--ardhAbhyAse tAvadardhameko bhAgaH, pramANantu tattulyau bhAgau, adaHsAbhyAsasya pramANasyAgantutulyAstrayo bhAgAH, Agantau taddviguNacchede tasya ShaDbhAgAH, tatra bhAgenaikena hIne lakShaNam, tathA AyAmAbhyAse AyAma eko bhAgaH, ca tatsadR^isha eko bhAgaH /
tena sAbhyAsasya pramANAsya dvau bhAgau taddviguNacchede abhyAse catvAro bhAgAH /
tatra caturbhAgone lakShaNam /
tathA--tR^itIyAbhyAse abhyAsa eko bhAgaH, pramANaM tattulyAstrayo bhAgAH, dviguNacchede 'bhyAse 'ShTau bAgAH, tatrAShTabhAgone lakShaNam, evameva turIyAdyabhyAse 'ShTau pramANasyAbhyAsavashenaiva bhAgakalpanam, Agantau taddviguNasakh«yayA bhAgaka lpanam, bhAgone lakShaNaM ca draShTavyam /
nanu yatrAbhyAse 'bhyAsatulyatA pramANasya na sambhavati kathaM tatra pramANe cAgantau ca bAgakalpanaM lakShaNaM ca, yathAdhikAbhyAse chedanaM nyUnAbhyase ca ?

ucyate--tatrApyayameva prakAraH, kintu sAbhyAsaM pramANamaMshena ca sadR^ishacchedaM kR^itvA Agantum api chedasakh«yAdviguNasakh«yayA chedaM kR^itvA tatra yAvadbhir aMshairhInaireko bhAgo hIno bhavati tAvadbhiraMshairnyUne 'bhyAse nihaJNjanaM kuryAt, adhikAbhyAse tAvaddviguNAbhyAse 'bhyAsa eko bhAgaH, pramANaM bhAgArthaM, tatrArdhena ca sadR^ishacchede sAbhyAse pramANe trayor'dhacchedAH, tatsakh«yAdviguNacchede tatra ShaDardhacchedAH, teShu dvAbhyAmUnAbhyAmeko bhAgo hIyata iti taDhUne lakShaNaM syAt /

triguNAbhyAse 'bhyAsa eko bhAgaH, pramANaM tu tR^itIyAMshakaH, tatsadR^ishA abhyAse trayastR^itIyAM shakAH, tena sAbhyAsasya pramANasya catvArastR^itIyAMshAH, taddviguNacchede AgantAvaShTau tR^itIyAshAH, tatra tribhiraMshairUne lakShaNam /
evaM caturguNAbhyAseShu bhAgAnunnIya tadanuMrUpamA gantau lakShaNaM kuryAt /
tathA tripAdAbhyAse 'bhyAsa eko bhAgaH, pramANaM tatsadR^isha eko bhAgastR^itIyAMshashva, aMshena ca sadR^ishacchede sAbhyAsapramANe sapta tR^itIyAMshAH, taistribhirUne tatra lakShaNam /
evam evAnyeShvapi sAMshacchedeShu bhAgakalpanaM lakShaNaM ca draShTavyam /
etadapi na vismartavyaM sarveShvabhyAseShvAgantubhAgaikyaM tadvashenana pramANe bhAgaukyaM bhAgAnekatvaM kevalAM shatvaM ceti, evamasya viharaNasya sarvAbhyAsaviShayatvamavagantavyam /
yadyevam upapadyate, kuto j~nAyate nyAyo 'N^gaIkR^ita iti, ucyate--AgantucaturthamAyAmashvAkShNayArajjuriti AyAmAbhyAso 'bhyAsacaturthasyAkShNayArajjuvisheShatvapratipAdanAdardhAbhyAsAyAmAbhyAM siddhasya paJNcadashikAShTikayoHsaptadashikAkShNayArajjurityAderviShamAbhyAsopanyAsAcca j~nAyate nyAyo 'yamaN^gIkR^ita ityalamatirthaM, tirya«bhAnyakShNayArajjuvivekArthaM ca, dakShiNottaragrahaNaM kimarthaM, pradarshanArthaM tirashvyAH, itarathA sadaHprabhR^itiShu virodhAt /

asya viharamasyAnte 'nyasya pratipAdanAyAhasa samAdhiH /

dvipadamidam /
tacchabdena viharaNamucyate, samAdhyAbhiprAyaH puMlliN^ganirdeshaH, saMshabdaH samyagarthe samashabdArthe vA, A« samantatobhAve, dadhAtiH karotyarthe samashabdArthe vA, A« samantatobhAve, dadhAtiH karotyarthe, samyaganyUnAnatiriktaM kShetraM samantAdApAdayatIti samAdhiH, yadvA--samAnAnAmAdhiH samAdhiH /
pArshvamAnyau tirya«bhAnyau akShNayArajjush ca parasparamanyonyasamAHsaMpAdayatIti, caturdikShu samaM kShetramApAdayatIti samAdhiH, ayamarthaH-- 
vimIyamAnakShetrasyAnyunAnatirekitvenAvasthAnaM samAdhAnam, tacca samyagupAyasya viharaNasya phalam, taddhetutvAdviharaNasya, hetuphalayorabhedopacAreNa tadeva viharaNaM samAdhirityucyate, yoga iti ceti, kimarthamidamucyate? shrotÃNAM pratipattiprarocanArthaM, yadedadR^iktaM viharaNaM sa samAdhiH, samIcaH shroNyaMsAn saMpAdayati tasmAdidaM niHsaMdigdamanena vihartavyamiti //


kapardibhAShyam


___________________________________________________________


tannimitto nirhrAso vivR^iddhirvA  || ˘p¡us_1.2e ||

___________________________________________________________



nimittaM karaNaM prakR^itiH iti paryAyAH /
tadeva niraJNjanArthaM yasya sa tannimittaH /
nirhrAsaH tirya«bhAnyAH /
vR^idvirvA tirya«bhAnyA eva /
kimuktaM bhavati? uktena mArgeNa prAgAyatAH tiryagAyatAHsamAshcaturashrAH kR^itA ityarthaH /



karavindIyA vyAkhyA

(tannimitvA)

taditi samAdhirheturviharaNamucyate--nimittaM kAraNaM heturiti paryAyAH, nirhrAso 'pacayaH, vivR^iddhirupacayaH, tau tannimittau syAtAM, lAghavArthamidamucyate, mahati caturashre vihR^ite tadekadeshabhUtaM caturashraM saMpAdIyatumicchan mahatashcaturashrasya shroNyaMsAdisaMsthita shaN^kvanirUpamabimata pradesheShu shaN^kUnnihatya shaN^kuShu rajjuM prabaddhaca yAvadabhimataM prasArya tAbhiralpaM caturashraM sampAdayet, vivR^iddhau caturashrapArshvamAnyAdibhiryAvadabhimatA dIrgharajjUH prabaddhya tAstatkUTasaMsthitashaN^kvanurUpAH prasAryAbhimatapradesheShu shaN^kuM nihatya tadantaraM gR^ihNIyAt, pR^iShThyAyAM karaNIShu cAbhimatapradesheShu shaN^kuM nihatya tadanurUpANi nimittAntarANi kR^itvA rajjuH prasArya kShetrasyApacayamupacayaM vA kuryAdityarthaH /
nirhrAsodAharaNaM mahAvedyuttaravedidhiShNyAdayaH /
vivR^idbhuyadAharaNaM mahAvedyAdayaH /



sundararAjIyA

(tannimitvA.)

abhIShTakShetrAyAmasaMmitA rajjuH pramANam /
sA sarvamAneShUbhayataHpAshA prAcI /
sA pUrvAparayoHshaN^kvorniyatA bhavati /
saiva pR^iShThabhavatvAt pR^iShThyetyapi vyapadishyate /
tadyAvadAyAmaM tAvadAyAme shulbAntare tasyArdhamabhyasyopari prakShiNya antayoH pAshau kuryAt /
tatra trINi pramANArdhani bhavanti /
teShAmaparabhAgabhAvitR^itIyamardhdhaM ShoDhA mbhujya pAshAdArabhya paJNcasu bhAgeShviti teShu lakShaNaM kuryAt /
asya shulbasyAntau pR^iShThyAntayorniyamya kR^itena lakShaNena dakShiNA prasArya nimittaM karoti shaN^kuM nihanti /
evamuttarataH pAshau viparyasya pUrvAnte 'pyevaM shaN^kum /
sa samAdhiH sa eko vihArayogaH /
asyodAharaNam--

"ShaTtriMshikAyAmaShTAdashe' tyAdi /
evaM kR^ite yadi tirya«bhAnyA nirhrAso vivR^iddhirveShyate so 'pi tannimittaH /
ye dakShiNottarA nimittabhUtAHshaN^kavaH tAneva cihnIkR^itya kartavyAH /

nirhrAsasyodAharaNam--"paJNcadashikenaikApAyamyArdhena tataH' ityAdi /
pracI tu sarvatra lokala eva grAhyA /
tatra bodhAyanaH "kR^ittikAH khalvimAH prAcIM na jahati kadAcana /
tAsAM sandarshanena mApayedityekam /
shroNAsandarshanenamApayedityekam /
citrAsvAtyorantarAlena mApayedityaparaM' iti /
etani lakShaNAni deshaviseShetu vyavatiShThante, sarvadeshasAdhAraNaM lakShaNamAha kAtyAyanaH "same kShetre shaN^kuM nikhAya shaN^kusaMmitayA rajjvA maNDalaM parilikhya yatra lekhayoHshaN^kvagracchAyA nipatati sA prAcI' iti /
lekhayoriti /
maNDalarekhayAH pUrvApara bhAgayorityarthaH //



kapardibhAShyam


___________________________________________________________


AyAmaM vAbhyasyAgantucaturtham AyAmashcAkShNayA rajjus tirya«bhAnIsheShaH | vyAkhyAtaM viharaNam  || ˘p¡us_1.3a ||

___________________________________________________________



pramANaM vAbhyasya AyAmamAtrIM rajjumAyAme prakShipya AgantoshcaturthamabhyastacaturthaM bhAgaM AyAme saMyojya lakShaNaM kR^itvA sapAda AyAmo 'kShNayA rajjuH /
sheShaH--pAdonAyAmaH /
sA tirya«bhAnI /
vyAkhyAtaM viharANaM /
vistaraNavidhiruktaH iyAMstu visheShaH aMsau pUrvaM mApayitavyau /
viparyasya shroNI samamanyat /
vAcoyuktibhedena vidAnasyaitat prayojanam--AyAmatR^itIyamabhyasya pUrvasmiMshcaturthe 'ShTabhAgone lakShaNamityevamAdInAmupasaN^gahArtham /
tatra shlokaH--

agantvardhena cihnaM yadbhAgAnatra karoti ca /

dhruvaM sa yAvadAgantu kR^itvaikone niraJNcanm //


vikalpavidhinokte siddhe "vyAkhyAta viharaNam' iti kimarthamuktam? shulbAntaroktAnAM saptamamamDalAdInAM gauravapratipAdanArdhamuktameva viharaNaM laghIya iti pratipAdayitum /

karavindIyA vyAkhyA

asyaiva viharamasyApAtadarshanAyAbyAsAntaramAha--(AyAmaM - sheShaH)

AyAmapramANaM kR^itsnamabhAyasya kimataH kartavyaM, pUrvokta prakAreNa lakShaNAdi kuryAdityabhiprAyaH /
ayamarthaH--AyAmamabhyasyAparasmin dvitIye caturthabhAgone lakShaNaM kuryAditi /
evaM kR^ite satyAgantucaturthamAgantau caturthaM pratIkamAyAmashvAkShNayArajjuHsyAt /
akShNayeti nipAto vibhaktipratirUpakaH koNavAcI. koNagatA rajjurakShNayArajjuH, karmarajjurityarthaH /
sheShaH akShNayArajjubhUtapratIkAdanyAni trINi prIkAni /
tiryak mIyate anayeti tirya«bhAnI, tiryagavashtitA rajjuH /
rajjvabhiprAyaH strIliN^ganirdeshaH /
vA shabdo 'bhyAsAntarasamuccayArthaH /
AyAmaM vA dbiguNaM vA triguNAM vA tR^itIyaM vA turIyaM vetyevamAdyabhyAsavisheShArthaM vAghaNam /
ayamrthaH--yAvatIrajjuH pramANaM tasmAt nyUnA tadadhikA vAtatsamA vAbhyasyate tatra tatra pUrvoktaprakAreNa tAvatastavato vargAn kR^itvA bhAgenaikena hIne lakShaNaM kR^itvA pR^iShThyAntayorantauniyamyetyAdinA prakAreNa viharediti /
eShAmudAharaNAnyuttarasUtre darshayiShyante /
nanuca lakShaNanimittararthaM rajjavAmapAyAtAyAM lakShaNapUrvabhavinaH pramANAdanantarasya ekasya bhAgasyAkShNayArajjutA, bhAgAntarANAM tirya«bhAkShmayArajjustirya«bhAnI sheSha iti /

ucyate--prathamabhUter'dhAbhyAse ShaDbhAgone lakShamamityetAvanmAtramityabhi matam, tAvatArdha UnabhAgaH kimarthaH, kimabhyAso mUlato hIyate utAntataH, anye ca bhAgAH kimarthaM, te ca kuta iti na j~nAyate, tatra niyamahetorabhAvAt /
apravR^ittiraniyamo va syAdihAgantucaturthamAyAmashvAkShNayArajjuH tirya«bhAnI sheSha iti ataHsa eko bhAgo 'bhyAsamUlataH, itare bhAgasyAkShNayArajjutve bhAgAntarANAM tirya«bhAnitve ca pR^ithagbhUtAbhyAsa eva vaktavye kasmAttadviparItaM kR^itaM, ucyate--ardhAbhyAsArdhAyAmAbhyAsayonyAyamabhyAsaviShaye sUtrAvayavairdraDhayituM viparItaM kR^itam /
kiM cAtrAbhyAsasya ShoDhA vibhAge caturdhA vibhAge ca ekasya bhAgasyAkShNayArajjutA bhAgAntarANAM sarveShAM tirya«bhAni tA ca pratipadyate /
vyAkhyAtaM viharaNamityatra vyAkhyAtameva viharaNaM nAnyadviharaNamityayamarthaH, Agantau nyUgAnAmanekaviShayatve 'pi parvoktameva, viharaNaM nAnyadviharaNamiti /

tatra shlokAH--

bhAgAHsAbhyAsamAnasya yAvanto 'bhyAsasaMmitAH /
dvistAvantaHsyurAganatau tadekone 'tra lakShaNam // .1 //

te cet sabhyAsamAnasya sAMshAHsyuHsAMshasaMkhyayA /
chindyyAddviguNayA'gantuM bhAgone 'traiva lakShamam // .2 //

Une 'dhike vA tvAgantau kathaM sAbhyAsamAnake /
bhAgAnAM parikliptiHsyAt kathaM vA syAnniraJNjanam // .3 //

samatA nyUnatAdhikyo 'pyA gantau syAtsadaikatA /
tadvashena pramANe syurbhAgaikyAne kalAshatA // .4 //

AgantAvadhike mAnaM kevalaMsho bhavetsadA /
nyune bhAgaikyanAnAtve syAtAM sAMshe ca kevale // .5 //

tripAdone tu sAMshatvamardhone syAnniraJNjanam /
same bhAgaikyameva syAdityevaM bhAgakalpanA // .6 //

sAMsheM'shasadR^ishacchedaM kR^itvA sAbhyAsamAnakam /
tacchedasaN^khyAdviguNacchedamAgantumapyatha // .7 //

yAvAdbhiraMshairUne 'tra bhAgenaikena hIyate /
tAvadbhiraMshairUne syAdAgantau lakShaNakriyA // .8 //

yAvatAM pUraNe 'bhyAso yena bhAgena hIyate /
lakShaNArtaM sa bhAgastaddvistAvadbhAgapUraNam // .9 //

tR^itIyagrahaNaM kurvan ShaDbhAgasahitaM muniH /
sAbhyAsamAnagAn bhAgAn dvikAbhyAse 'tra manyate // .10 //

sAbhyAsasya pramANAsya tredhAkaraNapUrvakam /
abhyAsasya tR^itIyatvamuktvA ShaDbhAginaM matam // .11 //

aN^gIkR^itya tu tatraikabhAgone lakShaNaM vyadhAt /
yadayaM tena sAbhyAsamAnabAgasdhasaN^khyayA // .12 //


bhindyAddvigumayA'gantuM bhAgone syAnniraJNjanam /
anantaraM trisaN^khyAyAM ShaTsaN^khyAM vadatAmunA // .13 //

sAbhyAsamAnabhAgIyA saN^khyA'gantau dviriShyate /
tR^itIyaShaDbhAgokte dve yataHsAbhyAsagocare // .14 //

sAbhyAsamAnAdabhyAsaM dviguNacchedamAhatuH /
yadvaikasaN^khyAsaMyuktamUnabhAgasthasaMN^khyayA // .15 //

dviguNIgR^itayA yA syAdAgantau bhAgakalpanA /
yadvAbhyAsArdhasadR^ishabhAgaM sAbhyAsamAnakam // .16 //

kR^itvA tatsaMkhyayA'gantuM chicvaikone 'tra lakShaNam /
tR^itIyashabdasAmarthyAdayaM nyAya utIryate // .17 //

paJNcadashikAShTikayorityAderuktireva ca /
paJNcadashikAShTikayoriti yatsAmyamAnakam // .18 //

yaddvAdashikapaJNcatriMshakayoriti vA param /
triguNAgantutatpUrvatryaMshAbhyA mathavAnvitaM // .19 //

parayuktaM paJNcamAbhyAM yadvA paJNcaguNAnvitam /
ete viharaNArthAyAyAmAbhyAsasya gocare // 20 //

yataste na bhavetAM te abhyAsanyAyahetuke /
ardhAbhyAse tathA'yAmAbhAyAsAya tu parasparam // 21 //

sApekShAN^gavidhistadvannyAyasyAsya nibandhanam /
nAnAbhUte 'pi vA'gantau tadbhAge ca tathAvidhe // 22 //

niraJNcanaM vidhiH kasmAdbhAgenaikena varjite /
ardhabhyAse tu bhAgone lakShaNaM yat tR^itIyake // 23 //

taddUrIkR^itya cAyAmAbhyAse tatphalabhAginaH /
trirya«bhAnyakShNayArajjuvivekasyaikabhAgakam // 24 //

Ashritya nirNayaM brUte tenaikone 'tra lakShaNam /
alamativistareNa //



sundararAjIyA

(AyAmaMvA viharaNam)

atha yogAntaramAha-- 
pramANamAtre shulbe (pramANamevAbhyashca tAM rajjuM caturdhA saMbhujya tR^itIyacaturthayormadhye lakShaNaM kR^itvA pUrvAparayoH pAshau pratimucya caturthamAyAmashva) viharaNakAle 'kShNayArajjuH kAryA /
sheShaH pAdona AyAmastirya«bhAnIsthAnIyaH /
etaduktaM bhavati--AyAmaM dviguNaM kR^itvAnyatarasminnarghe caturthabhAgena lakShaNamiti /
yathA gArhapatyaciterAyatane caturaratnau caturaratnimabhyashca triShvaratniShu lakShaNamiti kR^itvA viharet /

vyAkhyAtamiti /
pR^iShThyAntayorantAvityAdinA //
atremAvabh.I ShTAbhyAsayA rajjvA viharaNArthau shlokau--

iShTAyAM pR^iShThyAyAmiShTAmAganturajjumabhyasyet /
abhyAsArdhasamAnA yAvantoM'shAHsahAdhikAyAme // 1 //


abhyAsaM tAvaddhA saMbhujyaikonite 'tra cihnaM syAt /
ekoM'shaHsAyAmaH karNastaryaN^ktu sheShaHsyAt // 2 //


kapardibhAShyam



___________________________________________________________


dIrghasyAkShNayArajjuH pArshvamAnI tirya«mAnI ca yat pR^ithagbhute kurutas tad ubhayaM karoti  || ˘p¡us_1.4a ||

___________________________________________________________



dIrghacaturashrasyetyarthaH /
samamaNDalasya pArshvamAnyAdInAm abhAvAd viShamacaturashrAccAyAmAH parigR^ihyante /
pArshvamAnI tirya«bhAnI kuruta iti nirdeshAdakShNayArajjurityekavacananirdeshAcca yasya caturashrasya pArshvamAnyekA tirya«bhAnyekaivAkShNayArajjuHsaN^gR^ihyate pArshvamAnyA kR^ite caturashre yAvat kShetraM bhavati tirya«bhAnyA ca, tadubhayamakShNayArajjuH karoti--pArshvamAnIkShetraM tirya«mAnIkShetraM ca karotItyarthaH /
vakShyati ca "trikacatuShkayoH' ityAdinA /
trikasya vargo nava (3n3u9);

catuShkasya vargaH ShoDasha (4n4u16) /
ShoDashasu navake kShipte (16a9u25)paJNcaviMshatiH /
paJNcakA vargAH paJNcaviMshatiH (5u5n5)evaM savatra draShTavyam /
pR^ithaggrahaNaM saMsargo mA bhUdityevamartham /
bhUtagrahaNaM kimarthaM? pR^ithakkuruta ityucyamAne saMsargavisheSho 'pi syAt /
bhUtagrahaNe satyetaddoSho na bhavati /



___________________________________________________________


tAbhir j~neyAbhir uktaM viharaNam  || ˘p¡us_1.4b ||

___________________________________________________________



tAbhiruktAbhistasR^ibhiruktaM viharaNam /
j~neyAbhiH j~nAtuM shakyAbhiH--manasA parikalpitAbhiH /
uktena mArgeNa viharedityathaH /
praugAdiShu karaNaparij~nAnArthametatsUtramihApyupakariShyatItyatroktam /

karavindIyA vyAkhyA

etadviharaNaM kShetrasamAdhAnAt samAdhirityuktam /
asyasamAdhihetutvaM darshayannAha--

(dIrghasya viharaNam)

dIrghasya--dIrghacaturashrasya, samasyeti ca sAmarthyAllabhyate, tadatrraivaM vyAkhyAsyate--akShNayArajjustirya«mAnI coktA, pArshvaM yayA mIyate sA pArshvamAnI, yat pR^ithagbhUte--nAnAbhUte, kurutaH--saMpAdayataH tadubhayamubhayakShetraparimitaM ekaM kShetraM karoti--saMpAdayatItyarthaH, dIrghasya caturashrasya pArshvamAnI svayameva pAshvamAnI svayameva pArshvamAnI tirya«nAnIca bhUtvA yatkShetraM karoti akShNayA rajjuHsvayameva pArshvamAnI tirya« mAnI ca bhUtvA tadubhayakShetraparimitaM kShetraM karoti /
tAbhir j~neyAbhiruktaM viharaNaM--yA evaMbhatAH pAshvamAnItirya«mAnyakShNayArajjavaH

tAbhirj~neyAbhirj~nAtuM shakyAbhiH, uktaprakArapArshvamAnItirya«mAnyakShNayArajjUnAmanyatarayoH parimANaj~nAnenAnyatarA j~nAtuM shakyeti tA j~neyAH /
tatkathaM, yathA iyatkaraNI pArshvamAnI iyatkaraNi tirya«mAnIti j~nAte 'kShNayArajjustadubhayaphalakShetrakaraNIti j~nAyate /
evamiyatkaraNI pArshvamAnI iyatkaraNyakShNayArajjuriti j~nAte 'kShNayArajjuphalabhUtakShetrAt pArshvamAnIphalabhUtakShetre shodhite shiShTakShetrasya karaNI tirya«mAnIti j~nAyate, tatheyatkaraNI tirya«mAnI iyatkaraNyakShNayArajjuriti

j~nAte 'kShNayArajjuphalabhUtakShetrAttirya«mAnIphalabhUtakShetre shodhite shiShTakShetrasya karaNI pArshvamAnIti j~nAtuM shakyate /
evametA j~neyAH, tAbhirj~neyAbhiruktaM viharaNaM--yaduktaM viharaNaM tattAbhirj~neyAbhirnAj~neyAbhirityarthaH, evamuktasya viharaNasyasamAdhihetutvamavagantavyamityabhiprAyaH /
athavA j~neyAbhiH manasi kalpitumucitAbhiH pUrvoktaM viharaNaM kartavyam /
ayamarthaH--pArshvamAnItirya«mAnyakShNayArajjUnAM pramANaM j~nAtvA tirya«mAnyakShNayArajjUbhayapramANAmekAM rajjuM mItvA tirya«mAnyante lakShaNaM kR^itvA tayA pUrvoktaM viharaNaM kartavyamiti /
pUrvoktAnAmArdhAbhyAsAdInAM kAni cidudAharaNAnyatrocyante /
ardhAbhyAse tathA--dvAdashaN^gulapramANe ShaDaN^gulamabhyaste tadaShTAdashAN^gulam /
tatrAgantunA ShaDaN^gulena pramANe paricchinne sAbhyAsasya pramANasya ShaDaN^gulAstrayo bhAgAH /
tatra bhAgasa yAstisraH, tAbhistisR^ibhiH

dviguNAbhiHShaDbhirAgantau ShaDaN^gule cchinne tasyaiko bhAga ekaikamaN^gulaM /
tatra ShaDbhAgone lakShaNe kR^ite bhAgenaikena sahita AyAmaH trayodashAN^gulaM akShNayArajjuH sheShAH paJNcabhAgAH /
paJNcAN^gulI tirya«mAnI, tatra dvAdashAN^gulaM pramANam, caturashrANi catushcatvAriMshacchatamaN^gulikShetrANi karoti /
tathA trayodashAN^gulAkShNayArajjuH, tadubhayamekonasaptatyAdhikashatamaN^gulikShetrANi karoti /
AyAmAbhyAse yathA--AyAmo dvAdashAN^gulaH /
Agantush ca tAvAneva /
sAbhyAsashca pramANasyAgantuparimito dvau bhAgau /
taddviguNasaN^khyayA'gantau chinne tryaN^gulAshcatvAra Agantau bhAgAH /
tatrAgantucaturthamAyAmashvAkShNayArajjuH paJNcadashAN^gulA, sheShatirya«mAnI navAN^gulA, tatra navAN^gulaikAshItimaN^gulikShetrANi karoti, AyAmaH pUrvavadeva, paJNcadashAN^gulA akShNayArajjuH tadubhayaM paJNcaviMshatyadhikashatamaN^gulikShetrANi karoti /
AyAmadviguNAbhyAse yathA--AyAmo dvAdashAN^gulaH, dviguNashcaturviMshatyaN^gulaH, tatrAbhyAsena pramANe paricchidyamAne abhyAsa eko bhAgaH, pramANaM tadardhaM, ardhenaikasmin paricchidyamAne trINyardhAni taddviguNacchedAH, tatraikaikamardhaM caturaN^gulaM dve ardhe aShTAN^gule eko bhAgaH, tadane lakShaNaM, tena yuktaM pramANaM, viMshatyaN^gulamakShNayArajjuH, tadna Agantau caturaN^gulaM pArshvacatuShTayaM ShoDashAN^gulaM, sA tirya«mAnI tatra ShoDashAN^gulA ShaTpaJNcAshacchatadvayamaN^gulikShetrANi karoti, AyAmo dvAdashAN^gulaH, catushvatvAriMshacchataM tadubhayaM catvAriMshacchatAni viMshatyaN^gulAkShNayArajjuH karoti, yadvAbhyAsa eko bhAgaH pramANaM tadardhamekasmin bhAge dviguNe dve saMkhye, arghe dviguNite dve ardhe /
tatraikA saMkhyA trisaMkhyayA'gantau caturviMshatyaN^gule chinne tasyaikaiko bhAgaH aShTAN^gulaH, tenaikena sahitaM pramANaM, viMshatyaN^gulA'kShNayayArajjurityAti pUrvoktameva /
tR^itIyAbhyAse yathA--pramANaM caturviMshatyaN^gulaM, tasyatR^itIyamaShTAN^gulaM, tasmiMshcaturviMshatyaN^gulaM, tasmiMshcaturviMshatyaN^gule prakShipte sAbhyAsaM pramANaM dvAtriMshadaN^gulaM, tatra sAbhyAsasya pramANasyAganatusahitAshvatvAro bhAgAH, taddviguNacchede AganturaShTabhAgAH, tatraiko bhAga ekAN^gulaM, tatra bhAgenaikena sahitaM pramANaM paJNcaviMshatyaN^gulaM, akShNayArajjuH saptAN^kulAni tirya«bhAnI saikonapaJNcAshatkaroti /
caturviMshatyaN^gulaM pramANaShaTsaptatiM paJNcaviMshatiH ShaT shatAni ca karoti evamevAbhyAsAntareShvapi draShTavyam /
trikacatuShkayorityAdinA kAnicidudAharaNAnyuttaratra svayameva vakShyati /
alamati prasaN^gena /



sundararAjIyA

(dIrghasyAkShNa viharaNam)

atha sanidAnamanekaprakAraM viharaNamAha------

dIrghasya caturashrasya pArshvamAnyA samacaturashre kR^ite yat kShetraM saMpadyate,yacca tirya«bhAnyA tadubhayaM akShNayArajjvA samacaturashre kR^ite saMpadyate kShetraM /

trikacatuShkayorityAdyudA haraNam /

evaJNcAsAM dvayorj~nAtayostR^itIyA j~nAtuM shakyate /
yathA pArshvamAnItirya«bhAnyorj~nAtayoH te pR^ithagvargayitvA saMyojya tadvargamlamakShNayArajjuH /
tathA pArshvamAnyakShNayArajjvorj~nAtayoH akShNayArajjuvargAtpArshvamAnIvarN^ga vishodhya (vi) shiShTasya mUlaM tirya«bhAnI /
evaM tirya«bhAnIvargaM vishedhya pArshvamAnI /
evaM bhUtAbhirj~neyAbhiH pUrvoktaM viharaNam /
trikacatuShkayorityAdInyevodAharaNAni /
pUrvayogAvapyasyaiva prapaJNcau //

samasya dvikaraNI /
samasya caturashrasya akShNayArajjuH samacaturashrasya kShetraM yAvadbhavati tasya dviguNaM karoti /

akShNayArajjorabhAvAnmaNDalasyAprasaN^gaH /

akShNayArajjurityekavacananirdeshAt /

taccaturthena /
taditi prakShiptatR^itIyaM parAmR^ishyate /

AtmacatustriMshonena--etat caturthasya visheShaNam, taccaturthaM catustriMshaddhA vibhajyaikaM bhAgamutsR^ijya shiShTenetyarthaH /

(1a1§3a1§34-1§3n4n34u1.4142156)

dvAdashe catvAri caturShu ekaM catustriN^kShaddhA vibhajya ekaM bhAgamutsR^ijya, evaM tilonasaptadashAN^gulaM bhavati /
dvAdashAN^gulasya tilavargaH ; ekaM niyutaM ShaDayutAni ShaT sahasrANi catvAri shatAni ShaShTiH catvArIti (166464) tilapramANAni saptadashAN^gulamAnasya tilonasya tilavargaH-- trINi niyutAni trINi niyutAni trINyayutAni dve sahasre nava shatAni vaMshatirnava ca (332929) atraikatrikayoHsheSho na bhavatIti veNoHsavisheShe gR^ihyamANe dashatilakShetrANyatiriktAni /

madhye lakShaNam ardhamadhyamayosh ca pR^iShThyAyAM rajjum Ayamya pAshayorlakShaNeShviti shaN^kUn nihaty upAntyayoH pAshau pratimucya madhyamena lakShaNena dakShiNApAyamya shaN^kuM nimittaM karoti | madhyame pAshau pratimucya, uparyupari nimittaM madhyamena lakShaNena dakShiNamaMsam Ayacchet | unmucya pUrvasmAd aparasmin pratimucya madhyamenaiva lakShaNena dakShiNAM shroNim Ayacchet | evamuttarau shroNyaMsau  || ˘p¡us_1.7c ||

prathamaHkhaNDaH


******************************************************************************


madhye lakShaNamardhamadhyamayoshva--pAshalakShamayormadhya ityarthaH /
pAshayorlakShaNeShviti shaN^kuM nihatya, upAntyayordvitIyacaturthayoH pAshau pratimucya madhyamena lakShaNena dakShiNApasArya, nimittaM sAdhyanimittaM kAkapadaM kR^itvA, madhyame pAshau pratimucya, uparyupari kAkapadaM tenaiva lakShaNena dakShiNApasArya, shuN^kaM nihatya, tasminnekataraM pAshaM pratimucya, pUrvasmin shaN^kAvitaraM pAshantenaiva lakShaNena dakShimamaMsamAyacchet /
tatra shaN^kuM nihanyAt /
sa dakShiNAsaH /
evamuttarataH pUrvasmAtpAshamunmucyAparasmin pratimucya, tenaiva lakShaNena dakShiNA shroNI /
evamuttarataH pakShaH /
tatra iyAnvisheShaH--shroNI pUrvaM pashcAdaMsaH /

karavindIyA vyAkhyA

nanu caturashrasyeti kathaM labhyate? tatkaraNIbhUtapArshvamAnyAdidarshanAt /
samasyeti kathaM? kurata iti dvivacananirdeshAt, akShNayArajjurityekavacananirdeshAcca /
kuruta iti dvivacananirdeshe kR^ite sati ekaprakArA pArshvamAnI tirya«bhAnI coti gamyate /
tathAkShNayArajjurityekavacananirdeshAt sAcApyekaprakAroti j~nAyate /
viShamo 'pi dIrghacaturashro vidyata eva /
yakyAkShNayArajjU anyoyaM same bhavataH sa nivartyate /
samasyeti labhyate /
pR^ithaggrahaNasya saMsargavisheShaNatvanivR^icyartham /
dIrghacaturashrasyAkShNayArajjuriyatkarotItyuktaM, samasya sA kiyatkarotItyata Aha--

(caturashca karoti)

samasya caturashrasyAkShNayArajjuddviMstAvatIMdviguNAM /
yasyA bhUmeriyamakShNayArajjuH tAvaddvigUNAM bhUmiM karoti /
dviguNAyA bhUmeH karaNIbhavatItyarthaH /
dvistAvatIti mayUravyaMsakAdilakShaNaHsamAsaH /
nanvakShNayArajjurityekavacananirdeshAt samacaturashrA "anupapadatvA cchabdasyeti' nyAyAcca dvitIyApi tAdR^ishyeveti vij~nAyate /
tena samasyeyaM na viShamasyeti gamyate /
ataH kimartaM samashabdaH? /
ucyate--evaM tarhi mishraNArthaH samashabdaH /
dvistAvIM bhUmiM yugapadeva ekIkR^itya karatIti /
uttarArtho vA sama shabdaH /
nanu pUrvasUtra eva dIrghashabdamapahAya caturashrasyetyastu tenAsyApi siddhirbhavatyeva, satyaM--tathAsatyuktanyAyena samasyaiva tatsyAbha dIrghasya, tasmAt pR^ithagevameva vaktavyam /
prakR^itopajIvanena saMj~nAM vidhAtumAha--

(saviseShaH.)

samasya caturashrasyAkShNayArajjuH sA dvikaraNIsaMj~nA bhavati /
anvarthaiShA saMj~nA, dvayoHkaraNI dvikaraNIti /
nanu pUrvasUtreNaiva dvikaraNItve siddhe ayuktA saMj~nA, satyaM, dvikaraNItvaM siddhantathApi dIrghatrikoNAdInAmapi dvikaraNyaHsanti, tatra dvikaraNItyukte asyA eva grahaNaM yathA syAdityevamarthaM saMj~nA /
nanu sA dvikaraNItyeva vaktavyaM, samagrahaNaM kimarthaM? vakShyamANApi saMj~nA samadvikaraNIviShayA yathA syAditi /
samagrahaNasya pUrvasUtraviShayatve atra sAmarthyAttatsiddhiH /
dvikaraNyA eva prakArAntaramAha--

samacaturashrasya pramANamAyAmaM tattR^itIyena vardhayedvR^iddhiM gamayet, tacca tR^itIyaM svacaturtheMna tR^itIyasya caturthabhAgenetyarthaH /
Atmacatustrishonena Atmashabdena caturtho bhAgaH parAmR^ishyate /
vardhayedityeva, sa visheShaH--tasya visheSha iti saMj~nA /
tR^itIyAdinA yena vR^iddhaM pramANaM tasya visheShasaMj~nA /
yathA--dvAdashAN^gulaM pramANaM caturaN^gulena vardhayet, taccaturaN^gulamekAN^gulena tilonena vardhayet /
caturviMshattilAH pR^ithusaMshliShTA aN^guliriti pramANavido manyante /
vakShyati, "ardhe tadvisheShamabhyasya bAhyavisheShAbhyAM parigR^ihNIyAt' ityAdi /
kathaM, madhyame savisheShaM pratimucya caturthena caturthasavisheSheNetyevamAdi /
atra saha visheSheNa vartata iti sa visheShaH /
visheShasahitaM pramANameva savisheSha ityavagantavyam /
kimarthaM mahatI saMj~nA, anvarthaiShA yathA syAditi, tatkathaM vipUrvaHshiShiratishayavAcI, " shiShirasarvopAdAne, vipUrvo 'tishaye ' ityupadeshAt /
akShNayArajjubhUtadvikaraNyAH pramANAtiriktAdaMshAt kiJNcidvisiShyate atiricyata iti visheShaH /
yadvA tataH kiJNcit kShetraM visheShayati atirecayati mAnakAla iti vA visheShaH /
tathAhi--catustriMshattilA aN^gulirityuktam /
dvAdashAN^gulasya tilavargaH--ekaM niyutaM ShaDayutAni ShaT sahasrANi catuvAri shatAni /
tilonasaptadashAN^gulasya tilavargaH--trINi niyutAni trINyayutAni dve sahasre nava shatAni viMshatirnava ca tilapramANAni caturashrakShetrANi /
atraikaM tilaM caturashrakShetradviguNAdatiricyate /
tatastasya visheSha iti saMj~nA /
veNunA savisheSheNa mIyamAne 'gnau pramIyamAne tvAtmani yat kShetramatiricyeta tena nIvArashUkamAtramapi sarvathAtiriktaM na bhavati tannathUne tato 'lpataramiti dvikaraNIkArye savisheShavyavahAraH /
idAnIM prAsaN^gikamekaM viharaNaM vyAkhyAya viharaNAntaramAha--

(athAparaMashroNyaMsau)

athAparaM viharaNaM--vyAkhyAsyAma iti sheShaH, pramANamAtrIM ayAmamAtrIM rajjuM ubhayataHpAshAM AdyantayoH pAshayuktAM, madhye lakShaNaM niraJNjanArthaM, ardhamadhyayoH pUrvArdhamadhye aparArdhamadhye ca lakShaNadvayaM niraJNjanaM kR^itvA pR^iShThyAyAM mAtavyabhUtalamadhyalekhAyAM rajjumAyamya--prasArya pAshayorlakShaNoShviti paJNca shaN^kvoH pAshau pratimucya madhyena niraJNjanabhUtena dakShiNApAyamya, nimittaM--cihnaM karoti /
nimittaM diksaMdarshanArtham /
madhyame shaN^kau pAshau pratimucya, uparyuparinimittaM tasyopariShTAdAsannataraM dakShiNApAyamya, rajjuM tadante shaN^kuM nikAya, madhyamAcchaN^koH pAshAvunmucya, dakShiNashaN^kAvekaM pAshaM pratimucya, pUrvasmin shaN^kAnitaraM pAshaM pratimucya, niraJNjanena dakShiNamaMsaM pratyAyacchet /
rajjuM yathA dakShiNAMsaHsaMpadyate tathAcha''yacchet /
evameva dakShiNAM shroNimAyacchedityevamAdIni unmucya, pUrvasmAdityAdInyuttarANi sUtrANi /
paJNcashaN^kurayaM yogaHsamacaturashraviShayaH //


sundararAjIyA

(caturashca karoti)

caturashrasyetyavisheShAt samasyetyatrApi saMbadhyate /
athavA uttarasUtragataM samasyeti padamatrApi saMbadhyate /

samasya dvikaraNI /



anantaroktA samasya caturashrasyAkShNayArajjuH dvikaraNIsaMj~nisA /
tAvatordvayoH kShetrayoH karaNAt /
tasya j~nAnopAyamAha--

(pramANaMashonena.)

yathA--dvAdashAN^gulasya pramANasya tR^itIyaM caturaN^gulaM, tasya caturthamaN^guliH aN^guleshvatustriMsho bhAgastilamAtram /
evaM dvAdashAN^gulasyAkShNayArajjustilonasapradashAN^gulA /
tathA aShTAcatvAriMshadaN^gulasyAkShNayArajjuH catustilonA aShTaShaShTyaN^guletyAdi /

(savisheShaH.)

yo 'kShNayAravjjA pramANAdatirikto 'MshaH sa visheShasaMj~naH /
"ardhe tadvisheShamabhyasya' ityAdyudAharaNam //

ardhayormadhye ardhamadhye /
upAntyayoH-dvitIyacaturthayoHshaN^kvoH /

nimittaM--cihnam /
spaShTamanyat /

viharaNAvisheShaH ityarthaH //



___________________________________________________________


pR^iShThyAntayor madhye ca shaN^kUn nihatyArdhe 'rdhe tadvisheSham abhyasya lakShaNaM kR^itvArdhamagamayet | antyayoH pAshau kR^itvA madhyame savisheShaM pratimucya pUrvasminn itaraM lakShaNena dakShiNamaN^kam Ayacchet | unmucya pUrvasmAd aparasmin pratimucya lakShaNenaiva dakShiNAM shroNim Ayacchet | evam uttarau shroNyaMsau  || ˘p¡us_2.1b ||

___________________________________________________________



caturashrapramANAntayoHshaN^kuM nihatya tayormadhye ca shaN^kuM nihatya ardhe--pramANArdhe, tadvisheShaM--tasyArdhasya visheShaM, pramANaM tR^itIyena vardhayediti nyAyena lakShaNaM kR^itvA punarAgamayet prakShipet /
antyayoH pAshau kR^itvA madhyame shaN^kau savisheShaM pAshaM pratimucya pUrvasmin shaN^kau itaraM pAshaM pratimucya lakShaNena dakShiNenApasArya shaN^kuM nihanyAt /
sa dakShiNAMsaH /
pUrvasmAcchaN^koH pAshamaparasmin shaN^kau pratimucya tenaiva lakShaNena dakShiNaM shroNimAyacchet /
tenaivodagapasArya uttarAM shroNiM viparyasyottaramaMsam //


yogadvayamidaM samacaturashrasya samyak //


karavindIyA vyAkhyA

(athAparo shroNyaMsau)

pramANamAtrIM rajjumityeva, viharaNopAyo yoga ityuktaM, pR^iShThyAntayoH madhye ca shaN^kuM nihatya /
vyAkhyAtametat /
ardhepramANAmAtracA rajjvA ardhe tadvisheShamabhyasya saMyojya lakShaNaM kR^itvA sUtrasavisheShArdhAnte ardhaM Agamayet shiShTaM yathA pramANaM bhavati tathA'gamayet, ayamarthaH--ardhadvikaraNImAtrIM kevalArdhamAtrIM ca ekAM rajjuM mItvArdhadvikaraNI mAtre lakShaNaM kR^itvA rajjvantau pAshau kR^itvA madhyame shaN^kau savisheShamardhaM pratimucya pUrvasmin shaN^kau kevalamardhaM pratimucya lakShaNena dakShiNamaMsamAyacchet--kuryAt /
unmucya pUrvasmAditi spaShTArthaH /
ayamapi yogaHsamacaturashraviShaya eva /
ardhe tadvisheShamiti pramAmasavisheShayoH prastutatvAt prasaN^genocyate /

sundararAjIyA

(athAparo shroNyaMsau)

ardhe--pramANArdhamAtre shulbe /
tadvisheShaMardhasyaiva visheShaM abhyasya tadvisheShAnte lakShaNaM kR^itvA anyadardhaM nirviroShamAgamayet /
yathA--gArhapatyaciteH ShaNNavatyaN^gulAyA antayayormadhye ca shaN^kUnnihatya arve 'ShTAcatvAriMshadaN^gule tadviroShaM catustilonaM viMshatyaN^gulamabhyasya lakShaNaM kR^itvAnyadardhaM aShTAcatvAriMshadaN^gulaM saMyojayet /
evaM catustilonaShoDashakottarashatAN^gulaM shulbam /
antayorityAdi spaShTam /

tR^itIyakaraNyetena vyAkhyAtA | vibhAgastu navadhA  || ˘p¡us_2.3 ||

___________________________________________________________



etenaiva mArgeNa tR^itIyakaraNI vyAkhyAtA /
anayaiva trikaraNyA tR^itIyakaraNyapyavagantuM shakyetyarthaH /
kathamityAha--trikaraNIkShetraM navadhA vibhajya ekaM bhAgaM gR^ihNIyAt /
pramANatR^itIyaM bhavati /
trikaraNyAH tR^itIyaM karoti /
tatra shlokaH--



akShNArajjustrikR^itproktA pramANasavisheShayoH /

asyA eva tR^itIyaM tu tR^itIyakaraNIM viduH //


karavindIyA vyAkhyA

(pramANaMatrikaraNI)

pramANadvikaraNyakShNayArajjava uktaH /
yasya caturashrasya praNANaM tirya«bhAnI dvikaraNI pArshvamAnI tasya caturashrasyAkShNayArajjuH pramANapArshvamAnI tirya«bhAnI kShetrasya trikaraNIbhavati //


tR^itIyakaraNyetena vyAkhyAtA /



trikaraNIvyAkhyAne tR^itIyakaraNyapi vyAkhyAtA /
kathaM ? tR^itIyaM tiryAgdvikaNyAyAmaH, tasyAkShNayArajjustR^itIyakaraNI /



tR^itIyakaraNyavagamAyAha

(vibhAgastu navadhA)

tR^itIyakaraNyavagame iyAMstu visheShaH /
kShetrasya navadhA vibhAgaH kAryaH, kasya kShetrasya ? pramANakShetrasya trikaraNIkShetrasya vA /
ayamarthaH--yasya kShetrasya tR^itIyakaraNI sAdhyate tat kShetraM navadhA vibhajya tatrakaisya bhAgasya pArshvamAnIM tirya«bhAnIM kR^itvA tasyaiva bhAgasyAkShNayArajjuM pArshvamAnIM kR^itvA tAbhyAM caturashre kR^ite caturashre navadhA vibhakte tatraikasya bhAgasya karaNIpramANacaturashcakShetrasya tR^itIyakaraNI bhavati /
sa ca vibhAgaH pramANakShetratR^itIyamiti pradarshanam /
etena catuShkaraNIcaturthakaraNIprabhR^itInAmapi /
tathAhi--pramANaM tiryak catuShkaraNyAyAmastasyAkShNayArajjuH paJNcakaraNI /
tathA pramANaM tiryakpaJNjakaraNyAyAmastasyAkShmayArajjuH ShaTkaraNItyAti draShTavyam /
tathAhidvikaraNI tirya«bhAnI trikaraNyAyAmaH tasyAkShNayArajjuH paJNcakaraNI /
tirya«bhAnI dashakaraNyAyAmastasyAkShNayArajjuH paJNcadashakaraNItyAdyapi draShTavyam /
tathA turIyaM tiryak trikaraNyAyAmastasyAkShNayArajjusturIyakaraNI /
tathA paJNjamaM tiryakcatuShkaraNyAyAmastasyAkShNayArajjuH paJNcamakaraNItyAdi draShTavyam /
trikaraNItR^itIyakaraNyoHsautrAmaNyAdAvupayAgeH /
nanu dIrghasyAkShNayArajjurityanena trikaraNItR^itIyakaraNIprabhR^itayaH siddhAH /
tatkimarthaM trikaraNyAdikaraNIvidhirArabhyate /
ucyate--dviprakArAH karaNyaH, shuddhamUlA ashuddhamUlAsh ca /
shuddhaM mUlaM yAsAM tAHshuddhamUlAH /
dvAbhyAM catvAri, tribhirnavetyAdivakShyamANAshvatuShkaraNInavakaraNIprabhR^itayaH tAsAM tu sarvadA dvikaraNI trikaraNI paJNcakaraNItyeva vyapadesha iti pradarshayitumidamucyate, dvayoH karaNI dvikaraNI, trayANAM karaNI trikaraNI, caturNAM karaNI catuShkaraNI, paJNcAnAM karaNI paJNcakaraNIti /
kiJNca dIrghasyAkShNayArajjurityanena sAmAnyena nAJNjasA trikaraNIprabhR^itInAmavagatirbhavati /
uktaprakAreNa saMpannAnAM karaNInAM tena saMvAdamAtraM bhavati /
tadyujyata eva dvikaraNyAdikaraNIvisheShavidhyArambhaH /



sundararAjIyA

atha trikaraNImAha

(pramANaMatrikaraNI)



yathA dvAdashAN^gulA tirya«bhAnI taddvikaraNI tironasatpadashAN^gulA pArshvamAnI /
evaM dIrghacaturashre kR^ite tasyAkShNayArajjurviMshatyaN^gulayaHsatpaviMshatitilAsh ca /
sA trikaraNI pramANaparimitaM kShetraM triguNaM karoti //


(tR^itIyakaraNyetena navadhA)

tR^itIyakaraNyA caturashre kR^ite navadhA vibhAgaH kAryaH /
tasyaiko bhAgaH pramANakShetrasya tR^itIyaM bhavati /
trikaraNyAstR^itIyaM tasya karaNI //


kapardibhAShyam


___________________________________________________________


tulyayosh caturashrayor uktaH samAsaH | nAnApramANayosh caturashrayoH samAsaH  || ˘p¡us_2.4a ||

___________________________________________________________



samAsa ekIkaraNam /
caturashrasyAkShNayArajjuriti sUtreNaspaShTaH /
nAnApramANayoshcaturashrayoHsamAsa ucyata iti sheShaH /
dIrghasya samasya caturashrasya samAsa ekIkaraNam /



___________________________________________________________


hrasIyasaH karaNyA varShIyaso vR^iddhram ullikhet | vR^iddhrasyAkShNayArajjur ubhe samasyati | tad uktam  || ˘p¡us_2.4b ||

___________________________________________________________



hrasIyasaH alpIyasaH kShetrasya karaNyA pramANena varShIyasaH varShIyasetyarthaH /

vR^iddhraM dIrghamullikhet /
yathAlpIyasaH karaNI tirya«bhAnI varShIyasaH karaNI pArshvamAnI, tathA dIrghacaturashramullikhet /
vR^iddhrasyAkShNayArajjurubhe samasyati /
uktaM--dIrghacaturashrasyAkShNayArajjuriti /



karavindIyA vyAkhyA

(tulyayoHasamAsaH)

tulyayoriti /
samAso nAma samasanaM mishraNaM ekIkaraNaM karaNItulyapramANayoHsamAsaH /
karaNyuktA caturashrasyAkShNayArajjurddvistAvatIM bhUmiM karoti samasyeti /
uktamanubhAShaNaM vakShyamANArthaM, idamatra parishiShyate, tAdidaM vakShyAmIti /

(nAnA taduktaM)

nAnApramANayorbhinnapramANayoHsamAsaH karaNyucyate, hrasIyasaH alpIyasashcaturashcasya karaNyA--karaNIpramANena, barShIyasaHmahatashcaturashrasya, vR^iddhraM--cihnamekadeshamullikhet vR^iddhrasyAkShNayArajjurubhe nAnApramANe caturashre samasyati ekIkaroti /
etaduktaM bhavati--nAnArapramANe caturashre samasya alpIyasashcaturashrasya karaNIpramANena mahadashcaturashrasya ekasyAM tirya«bhAnyAM paricchindyAt /
tata ArabhyordhvAM lekhAM yathA parasyAM tirya«bhAnyAM tAvati pradeshe nipatati tathA likhet /
lekhAvibhaktasyAlpIyasaH karaNIpramANaM tirya«bhAnI /
kasya? mahataH karaNIpramANapArshvamAnIkasya dIrghacaturashrasyAkShNayArajjurume nAnApramANe caturashre samasyati /
caturashra iti vartamAne punashcaturashragrahaNaM maNDalayorapi caturashraM kR^itvaiva samAsaHsukara iti j~nApayituM /
taduktaM--dIrghasyetyAdinA /
asyopayogo vidyAbhyAsAdiShu /



sundararAjIyA

(tulyayoHasamAsaH)

dvikaraNyA yathA dvipuruShe 'gnau puruShadvikaraNyA dvayoH puruShayoHsamAsa ityAdi /
trikaraNyA trayANAM puruShANAM samAsasyApyetadupalakShaNaM bhavati /

dIrghacaturashrayostu samAse ayaM visheShaH /
tirya«bhAnyA dvikaraNI tirya«bhAnI, pArshvamAnyAsh ca dvikaraNI pArshvamAnIti /
yathA dvistAvAyAmAshvamedhavedyAM ShaTtriMshikAyAH pR^iShThyAyA dvikaraNI pR^iShThyA /
tirya«bhAnyostriMshikArAntareNa vakShyate /
prakramasya dvikaraNI prakamasthAnIyA bhavatIti /
evaM dIrghacaturashrANAM samAse tirya«mAnyAstrikaraNI tirya«mAnIti /
pArshvamAnyAsh ca pArshvamAnI /
yathA--tristAve 'gnau pakShayoH puruShamAtrayAH tirya«mAnyAstrikaraNI aShTAdhikashatadvayAN^gulA paJNcatilonA tirya«mAnI bhavati /
pArshvamAnyAsh ca ShaDaratneH trikaraNI paJNcAshahdvishatAN^gulA viMshatitilonA pArshvamAnI bhavati /
pucchasya pArshvamAnyA ekAdashaprAdeshAyAH trikaraNI aShTAviMshatidvishatAN^gulA pArshvamAnI /
evamanyatra /



(nAnA samAsaH)

ucyata iti sheShaH //


(hasIyasaHataduktaM)

hrasIyasaH karaNIM tirya«mAnIM kR^itvA varShIyasaHsaMbandhinaM vR^irdhaM dIrghacaturashramullikhet, varShIyasaH karaNyeva pArshvamAnI /
evaM kR^itasya dIrghacaturashrasyAkShNayArajjuHsamastuyoH karaNI bhavati /
taduktaM "dIrghasyAkShNayArajjuH' ityAdinA /
yathA paJNcavidhe 'gnau kliyamANe dvipuruSheNa caturashre kR^ite catuShpuruSho bhavati /
tatra puruShamAtrashcaturashraH prakSheptavyaH /
tatra dvipuruShakaraNike caturashre tadAyAmaM puruShavyAsaM dIrghacaturashramullikhet /
tasyAkShNayArajjuraShTaShaShTishatAN^gulA saikAdashatilA, sA paJNcavidhAgneH karaNI bhavati /



kapardibhAShyam



___________________________________________________________


caturashrAc caturashraM nirjihIrShan yAvan nirjihIrShet tasya karaNyA varShIyaso vR^iddhramullikhet  || ˘p¡us_2.5a ||

___________________________________________________________


pUrvasmAccaturashrAccaturashraM nirjihIrShan caturashrapramANena vR^idhramullikhet /

saMyojayet /


___________________________________________________________


sA yatra nipatet tad apacchindyAt  || ˘p¡us_2.5c ||

___________________________________________________________



sA pArshvamAnI itarasmin pArshva yatra nipatati spR^ishati tatrApacchindyAt /

chinnayA nirastam  || ˘p¡us_2.5d ||

___________________________________________________________



chinnayA nirastIkR^ite tannirastaM bhavati /



karavindIyA vyAkhyA

(caturashrAtachinnayA nirastam)

caturashrAditi /
idamapi karaNIvidhAnameva /
mahatashcaturashrAdalpaM caturashraM nirjihIrShan vihartumicchan yAvat pramANaM caturashramapanetumicchati tasyAlpasya saraNyA mAhatashcaturashrasyaikadeshaM yathA chinnaM bhavati tathollikhet /
evaM kR^ite chinnaM nirasi tavyakShetrapramANatirya«bhAnIkaM mahatkShetrapArshvamAnIkaM pramANapArshva mAnIkaM dIrghacaturashraM bhavati /
asya kShetrasya pArshvamAnImakShNayetarat pArshvamupasaMharet--gamayet, sA pArshvamAnImakShNayetaratA yatretarasyAH pArshvamAnyAH pradeshe nipatati tadapachindyAt--pArshvamAnImapAcchityAdhikaM tyajet, chinnayA nirastaM--chinnaM pArshvamAnInirasitavyakShetrasya karaNI bhavati /
tayA pArshvamAnyA caturashre kR^ite nirasitavyakShetraM nirastaM bhavatItyarthaH /



sundararAjIyA vyAkhyA

caturashrAtachinnayA nirastam

nirhAro--nirasanam /
yathA nividhe 'gnau kriyamANe dvipuruSheNa caturashre kR^ite catuShpuruSho bhavati /
tatraikapuruShatyAgArthaM puruShamAtratirya«bhAnyA vR^idhramullikhya tasyottarAM pArshvamAnIM dakShiNAM prAcImitaratpArshvaM gamayet /
sA ca tatra dvipuruShapramANAyAM catvAriMshacchatadvayAN^gulapramANAyAM paJNcatilAshvApacchindyAt /
parishi ShTayA karaNyA caturashre kR^ite puruSho nirasto bhavati /



kapardibhAShyam

yathA svayameva darshayati--

___________________________________________________________


upasaMhR^itAkShaNayArajjuH sA catuShkaraNI chinnA cetarA ca yat pR^ithagbhUte kurutas tad ubhayaM karoti  || ˘p¡us_2.6a ||

___________________________________________________________


upasaMhR^itA pUrvaM pArshvamAnI /
idAnImakShNayArajjush ca rashrasyasA catuShkaraNI dvipuruShAt chinnA pArshvamAnI itarAtiryahbhAnI yatpR^ithagbhUte kurutaH tadubhayaM karoti //


kathamityAha--

tirya«mAnI puruShaM sheShas trIn  || ˘p¡us_2.6c ||

sheShastvakShNayArajjudvau /
tadubhayaM tasyAkShNayArajuriti trInkaroti //

tad uktam  || ˘p¡us_2.6d ||

___________________________________________________________


taccApyuktam //


karavindIyA vyAkhyA

imaM prakAramudAharaNamukhena spaShTikariShyannAha--

urasaMhatA taduktam upeti /
sarvato dvipuruShapramANaM catuShpuruShaM caturashraM viShayIkR^i tyodAharati /
ekasya caturashrasyAvayavabhUte dIrghacaturashre yA pArshvamAnyakShNayopasaMhR^itA sA catuShkaraNI catuShkaraNI catuShpuruShakaraNIti pratij~nAtA /
asya tirya«bhAnI ca puruShamAtrakaraNIti /
asya dIrghacaturashrasya chinnA pArshvamAnI kiyatkaraNIti na j~nAtA, saivAtrAvagantavyA /
atra puruShapramANaM tirya«bhAnyA pR^ithagbhUtayA yatkriyate chinnayA pArshvamAnyA pR^ithagbhUtayA yatkriyate akShNayArajjuH tadubhayakShetrakaraNIti nyAyato 'vagatA /
tatrAkShNayArajjuphalabhUtAccatuShpuruShAccaturashrAdekapramANaM tirya«bhAnIphale tvekasminnapanIte trayaH puruShAH parisheShyAt sA tripuruShakaraNItyavagantavyA /
ata idamuktaM tirya«bhAnI puruShaM karoti sheShaH chinnA pArshvamAnI /
trIn puruShAn iti pulliN^ganirdeshaH puruShabhiprAyaH /
puruShanirdeshashvAgnau puruSheNa vimAnaM puruShAbhyAsApacayau samAsanirhArayoH udAharaNamiti /
ayamarthaH--sarvato dvipramANAccatuShpuruShAccaturashrAdekaM puruShamapanIya tripuruShaM samacaturashraM kartumicchan taccaturashraM puruShapramANayA rajjvA madhye paricchidya dvidhA kR^itvA tadarghasyaikAM pArshvamAnImaparAM pArshvamAnIM pratyakShNayopagamayitvA tayoryatra saMpAtaH tatrAvasthitAM pArshvamAnIM chicvAvashiShTaM nirasya shiShTayA pArshvamAnyA samacaturashre kR^ite taccaturashraM tripuruShacaturashraM bhavati /
tathA sarvatashvatuShpuruShAccaturashrAccaturaH puruShAnapanIya dvAdashapuruShaM samacaturashraM kartumicchaddvipuruShapramANayA tirya«bhAnyA samacaturashraM vibhajyArdhasyaikAM pArshvamAnImanyAM prati gamayitvA tayoHsannipAte 'vasthitAM pArshvamAnImavacchidya chedaM nirasya shiShTayA pArshvamAnyA caturashre kR^ite tat kShetraM dvAdashapuruShasamacaturashraM bhavati /
chinnashiShTA pArshvamAnI tatkaraNI bhavatItyarthaH /
evaM pramANakShetre tR^itIyadvikaraNImapanIya tR^itIyakaraNI bhavati /
evameva sarvatra catuShkaraNIcaturthakaraNIprabhR^itayaH karaNyo 'vagantavyAH /
taduktaM "dIrghasyAkShmayArajjurityanena /
asyopayogo droNAdiShu, sundararAjIyA vyAkhyA

tadevodAharati----

upasaMhR^itA taduktam

yA akShNayopasaMhR^itA-ekIbhUtA rajjuHsA catuShkaraNI dvipuruShApacchinnA pArshvamAnI apacchinnA paJNcatilonAShTashatadvayAN^gulA /
itarA--puruShamAtrI tirya«bhAnI ca yatpR^ithagbhUte kurutastadubhayaM karati karNarajjutvAt /
tatra tirya«bhAnI spaShTameva hi puruShamAtraM karoti /
pArisheShyAtpArshvamAnI trIn puruShAn karotIti j~nAtuM shakyate /
taduktaM "dIrghasyAkShNayArajjuH' ityAdinA /



kapardibhAShyam

___________________________________________________________


dIrghacaturashraM samacaturashraM cikIrShan tirya«mAnyApacchidya sheShaM vibhajyobhayata upadadhyAt  || ˘p¡us_2.7a ||

___________________________________________________________



dIrghacaturashraM samacaturashraM kartumicchan tirya«bhanyA tirya«bhAnIpramANenApacchidya sheShaM vibhajya--dvidhA kR^itvA tadubhayataH agrataH pArshvatashropadadhyAt--nikShipet /



___________________________________________________________


khaNDam AgantunA saMpurayet  || ˘p¡us_2.7b ||

___________________________________________________________



khaNDamAgantunAtiriktena pUrayet /
pUrayitvA tadatiriktaM tyacet /

___________________________________________________________


tasya nirhAra uktaH  || ˘p¡us_2.7c ||

___________________________________________________________



tasya tyAgavidhiruktaH /

iti dvitIyaH khaNDaH

------------



karavindIyA vyAkhyA

dIrghacaturashraManirhrAsa uktaH

dIrghoti--sarvatastulyapramANaM samacaturashraM ekata AyAmato 'dhikaM dIrghacaturashraM samacaturashraM kurvan tirya«bhAnyA tirya«bhAnIpramANayA rajjvA parimite pradeshe madhye dakShiNottaramapa cchidya sheShaM purvabhAgaM madhye diryak dvidhA vibhajya tayoH pashcimaM bhAgaM tathaivAvasthApya pUrvabhAgaM prathamasyottarataH prAcInamupadadhyAt /
uttarapUrvabhAgaM shUnyabhUtaM khaNDamAgantunA saMpUrya samacaturashraM saMpAdya adhikamAgantubhUtaM khaNDaM tato nirharet--nirgamayet /
tasya nirhAra uktaH "caturashrAccaturashraM nirjhihIrShan' iti /
tasyopayogo rathacaktrAdiShu /



iti dvitIyaH khaNDaH

------------



sundararAjIyA vyAkhyA

dIrghacaturashraManirhAra uktaH

tirya«bhAnIpramANena pArshvamAnImapacchidya samacaturashraM kR^itvA sheShaM vibhajya purastAduttaratashvopadadhayAt, yathottarapUrvakoNe samacaturashraM AgantuH khaNDo bhaviShyati /
tasya nirhAra uktaH "caturashrAccaturashram' iti //


iti dvitIyaH khaNDaH

--------



kapardibhAShyam

___________________________________________________________


samacaturashraM dIrghacaturashraM cukIrShanA yAvaccikIrShet tAvatIM pArshvamAnIM kR^itvA yadadhikaM syAd yathAyogam upadadhyAt  || ˘p¡us_3.1 ||

___________________________________________________________



samacaturashraM dIrghacaturashraM kartumicchan yAvatA dIrghabhUtena prayojanaM tAvatpArshvamAlikhya yadadhikakShetraM tadyathAyogaM yathA tatkShetraM cujyate tathA kShipet /
caturashraM vibhajya ubhayataHprauge viniyogaH, avakIrNipashau ca /



karavindIyA vyAkhyA

samacaturashraM dvidhA kR^itvA tasyaikasmin bhAge bhAgAntarasyoparyupari nihite dIrghacaturashraM bhavatIti manvAnastasya prakAramAha--

samacatuhashraMaupadadhyAt sameti /
tirya«bhAnyA apacchidya sheShaM vibhajedityeva /
samacaturashraM dIrghacaturashraM kardumicchan samacaturashraM tribhAgAdvibhAgArdhAdInAmanyatamenaikAMshena parimitatiryakpramANaM dIrghacaturashraN^kartumicchati tAvatyA tirya«bhAnyA samacaturashramekato 'pacchidya sheShasya samacaturashrakaraNIsamAM pArshvamAnIM tAvatImuktayA tirya«bhAnyA samacaturashraM kR^itvA tatra sheShaM vibhajya yadadhikaM syAttadyathAyogamupadadhyAt /
adhikasya yathA vibhAge kR^ite vibhAgA ekaikasho vA sarvAH saMhasya vA bhAgAntarasyopari nidhIyamAnAstadvistAraM vyApyAnyonyasaMghaTitAstaddIrghaM saMpAdayanti tathA vibhajya sarvaM sheShaM bhAgAntarasyopari nidadhyAditi /
ayamarthaH--samacaturashraM dIrghacaturashraM cikIrShan ktriyamANasya cikIrShitavistArapramANayA tirya«bhAnyA samacaturashramekato 'vacchidya shiShTasya ca pArshvamAnIM tAvatIM kR^itvA tadadhimekayAnekayA vA vibhajya tesarve bhAgA dIrghacaturashraM yathA saMpAdayanti tathA sarvasheShaM bhAgAntarasyoparyupari nidadhyAditi /
atrAdhikR^ite sheShashabde karmavAcinyapi sannidheHsAmarthyAcca tasya ShaShThyartho 'pipratIyate /
tAvatImityAdishabdasya sheShasaMbandhitve sAmaJNjasyAdyAvaccikIrShedityapi dIrghavistAraviShayaHsyAt /
eka eva nyA yo dIrghasyApi dIrghavIdhAvavagantavyaH /



tatra shlokAH--

caturashraM samaM dvaidhaM kR^itvA bhAgAntaropari /

kShipte bhAgAntare dIrghacaturashraM tu taddhavet //


kariShyamANadIrghasya vistArasamapArshvakam /

vibhajya sheShamadhikaM yathAyogaM hi tatkriyA //


tAvatI pArshvamAnyAsh ca sheShasyAJNjasyabhAgataH /

kariShyamANadIrghasya tiryagyAvaccikIrShitam //


sundararAjIyA

(samacaturashraMaupadadhyAt)

ayamatra prakAraH-- yAvadicchaM pArshvamAnyA prAcyau vardhayitvA uttarapUrvAM karNarajjumAyacchet, sA dIrghacaturashramadhyasthAyAM samacaturashratirya«bhAnyAM yatra nipatati tata uttaraM hitvA dakShiNAMshaM tirya«bhAnIM kuryAt, taddIrghacaturashraM bhavati /
dIrghasya dIrghakahaNe 'pyayameva prakAraH //


kapardibhAShyam
___________________________________________________________



___________________________________________________________


caturashraM maNDalaM cikIrShan madhyAt koTyAM nipAtayet  || ˘p¡us_3.2a ||

___________________________________________________________



yaccaturashraM maNDalaM kartumicchet /
rathacaktracidAdau viniyogaH /
madhyAtkoT- cAM nipAtayet--madhyame shaN^kau pAshaM pratimucya koTyAmAyacchet karNenA'yacchet /
apasArya tatra lakShaNaM kR^itvA--



___________________________________________________________


pArshvataH parikR^iShyAtishayatR^itIyena saha maNDalaM parilikhet  || ˘p¡us_3.2b ||

___________________________________________________________


tenaiva lakShaNena pArshvataH AkarShet /
parikR^iShTaM yAvacca turashramatItya shete so 'tishayaH /
tasyAtishayasya tR^itIyena saha caturashrArghena maNDalaM parilikhet--sarvato likhet /



___________________________________________________________


sA nityA maNDalam  || ˘p¡us_3.2c ||

___________________________________________________________


sAnityA maNDalaM karoti /
anityA sathUlA //


___________________________________________________________


yAvad dhIyate tAvad Agantu  || ˘p¡us_3.2d ||

___________________________________________________________



straktiShu yAvaddhIyate tAvatpArshve na gacchati /
etacca vacanamAsannataratvakhyApanArtham /



karavindIyA vyAkhyA

(caturashraM maNDalaMatAvadAgantu)

samacaturashraM maNDalaM cikIrShana kartumicchan tasya caturashrasyAkShNayArajvarghapramANAt kiJNcidadhikAmekataHpAshAM rajjuM mItvA tatpAshaM caturashrasya madhyame shak«au pratimucya tAmakShNayAkoTyAM nipAtya tatra lakShaNaM kR^itvA pArshvapradeshAdatiriktalakShaNayorantarAlaM tredhA vibhajya antato dvau bhAgAvutsR^ijya bhAgenaikena sahitAyAM caturashrArddhapramANayA rajjvA yathA bhUmimaNDalaM bhavati tathA paritaHsarvato likhet /
evaM kR^ite sA nityA maNDalaM--caturashrakShetratilyakShetraM bhavati /
sA nityA--sA bhUmirnityA, yAvat caturashre bhUmiH maNDale 'pi sA bhavatI tyarthaH /
tatra hetumAha--yAvaddhIyate tAvadAgantu--yAvatpramANaM kShetraM hIyate hIyamAnatayA (iti) TR^ishyeta caturashabhaktiShu tAvanmaNDalasya pArshveShvAgantu TR^ishyate, tasmAnnityeti /
nanu viShkambhArdhena pariNAhArdhamabhyasya phalAvagatirityanena nyAyena bhUmeH nAtyantatulyatA, tatkathaM nityeti? ucyate--yadyapyanityA, tathApyanyeShAmupAyAntarANAmatisthUlatvAdasya copAyasyAsannatvAt samyagupAyasya vahuprayatnasAdhyatvena ashakyatvAccaivaM vadata AcAryasyAyamevopAyaHsAdhurityabhiprAyaH /
yAvadiha hIyate tAvadAgantu iti

tayoralpavaiShamyAttAvadeveti /
pravR^ittirocanArthamanityApi nityetyuktetyadoShaH /
athavA yA rajjurmaNDalaM karoti sA rajjuriti rajjvabhiprAyo 'pi tacchabdaH /



sundararAjIyA vyAkhyA

(caturashraM maNDalaMatavadAgantu)

caturashramadhye shaN^kuM nihatya tasmin rajjuM pratimucya koTyAmakShNayAM nipAtya cihnaM kR^itvA pArshve kR^itvA pArshva ca parikR^iShya tasmin cihnaM kR^itvA cuhnayorantarAlaM tredhA kR^itvA ekabhAgasahitena caturashrArghena maNDalaM parilikhetsA rajjuranityA maNDalaM karoti yAvaddhIyate koTiShu tAvatpramANaM pArshvaShvAgacchati //


kapardibhAShyam

___________________________________________________________


maNDalaM caturashraM cikIrShan viShkambhaM paJNcadasha bhAgAn kR^itvA dvAv uddharet | trayodashAvashiShyante | sA nityA caturashram  || ˘p¡us_3.3 ||

___________________________________________________________



maNDalaM caturashraM kartumicchan maNDalasya viShkabhyaM vyAsaM paJNcadashadhA vibhajya dvau bhAgau tyajet /
trayodashabhAgAHshiShyante /
taistrayodashabhirmitA rajjuH tAvatkShetraM caturashraM karoti /
sA cAnityA sthUlatarA /
trayodashAvashiShyanta iti vacanaM shulbAntaroktAdapi mAnasaM varamiti khyApanArtham /
tIvrasutasome viniyogaH /
tatra prAcyekAdashini mAtavyA /
tatrAN^gulena prAdeshamAtraM vedikhaNDamupAdAtavyam /
yadi dvAdashAN^gulA uparavAH ardhaprAdeshAN^kordakShiNataHShaDaN^gule shaN^kuM nihatya tAvadvayAsa catustriMshatprakramAyAmA prAcI vedirmantavyA /
dashAnAM kShetram /
sUtrakAropadeshena paJNcashatAni catvAriMshadadhikAni aN^gulakShetrANi /
tadardhAN^gulaM gR^ihyate /
tena vedicchedor'dhamAneShu /
pUrvArdhAnAM vedisaMskAro na kriyate /
atiriktakShetraM nirastaM bhavati /
vedeshrvAvaTeShu vicchittirbhavati--



karavindIyA vyAkhyA

(maNDalaM caturashraM cikIrShanacaturashram)

maNDalasya vistArapramANaM viShkambhaH /
tatpaJNcadashadhA vibhajya dvau bhAgAvapanayet /
shiShTAstrayodasha bhAgAshcaturashrasya karaNI bhavati /
atrApi sA nityetyAdi samAnaM /
tAveva codyaparihArau /



sundararAjIyA vyAkhyA

(maNDalaM caturashraM cikIrShanacaturashram)

trayodasha bhAgAH karaNI caturashrasya anityA caturashraM karoti /
anayoranityatvaM vij~nAyate gaNitavirodhAtparasparavirodhAcca /
tathAhi--saptavidhasya sAratniprAdeshasya rathacakracitAvagneH kShetraM lakShamaShTau ca sahasrANyaN^gulayaH, tasya caturashrIkR^itasya karaNI trINi shatAnyaShTAviMshatishrvAN^gulayor'dhadvAviMshAshrva tilAH /
tasminnuktena margeNa maNDale kR^ite trINi shatAni catuHsaptatishrvAN^gulayo viShkambho bhavati /
tasya pariNAhaHsahasraM paJNcasaptatishatAN^gulayaH /
yathA'huH--



caturadhikaM shatamaShTaguNaM dvAShaShTistathA sahasrANAm /

ayutadvayaviShkambhakyAsanno vR^ittapariNAhaH //


iti /
asya maNDalasya phalaM lakShaM navasahasramaShTau shatAni ShaShTishvAN^gulayo TR^ishyante uktaM ca --



samapariNAhasyArdhaM viShkambhArdhahatameva vR^ittaphalam /

iti /
evamagnikShetre rathacakracidAdau maNDale kR^ite ShaShTyadhikAni aShTashatAni sahasraM cAN^gulayo 'tiricyante /
tathA ca parasparavirodhaH /
ardhadvAviMshatitilasahitAShTAviMshatishatatrayAN^gulakaraNIkasyAgnermaNDalIkR^itasya viShkambhaH catuHsaptatishatatrayAN^gula uktaH /
tasyaiva maNDalasyoktena mArgeNa caturashrIkaraNe trINi bhavatIti pUrvoktAyAH karaNyAHsAShTAdashatilAshcatasro 'N^gulayo hIyante /
tasmAtsUkShmamicchatA caturashrasya maNDalakaraNe sUtroktAdatishayatR^itIyabhAgasahitAdviShkambhArdhAdaShTAdashashatAMshastyAjyaH /
evaM kR^ite rathacakracitau biShkambhaH ShaTratilonaikasaptatishatatrayAN^gulo bhavati /
pariNAhash ca paJNcaShaShTishatasahasrAN^gulayaH /
tasya maNDalasya samapariNAhasyetyAdinA pUrvoktena AnItaM phalaM lakShamaShTau sahasrANi bhavanti /
maNDalasyApi caturashrakaraNe sUtrokte viShkambhe svasmAt triguNAt trayastriMshacchatAMshaM yuJNjyAt /
tatra shlokAH--



caturashramaNDalakR^itau tyaktavyo 'ShTAdashashatAshaH /
sUtroktAdvyAsArdhAdvyAsArdhaM maNDalasyaitat //1 //

caturashravyAse vA triMshashatAMshaM samAbhyasya /
punaraShTamaM ca yuJNjyAdviShkambho maNDalasyaiShaH //2 //

maNDalacaturashrakR^itau viShkambhe sUtracodite yuJNjyAt /
triguNAtsvakAtrrayastriMshatsAtishayAnmaNDalasyaitat //3 //

maNDalaviShkambhAddvAtriMshashatAMshakaM parityajya /
shiShTAnnavamaM jahyAccaturashrasyaiSha viShkambhaH //4 //

evaM kR^ite hi vahnAvekashatavidhe 'pi vR^ittaviShkambhe /
sa tiladvitayavisheSho na ca bhavati parasparadhirodhaH //5 //

yAvatpramANA rajjus tAvatastAvato vargAn karoti  || ˘p¡us_3.8a ||

___________________________________________________________


yAvatpramANA--yAvadAyAmA rajjuH tAvato vargAnkaroti--paN^ktIH karoti--yAvatsaMkhyAyuktaM pramANaM tAvatsaMkhyAyuktAH paN^ktIH karoti /
paJNcamAnAM paJNcasakhyAyu ktAnvargAnkaroti /
evaM sarvatra yojanIyam /



tathopalabdhiH /

bhUmAvAlikhya prekShite tathaivopalabhyate /
dyAbhyAM kR^ite ubhayato likhaite catvAri shR^iN^gANi bhavanti, paJNcabhiH kR^ite paJNcadhA, ubhayato likhite paJNcaviMshatishR^iN^gANi bhavanti /
evaM sarvatra draShTavyam /



karavindIyA vyAkhyA

(yAvatpramANA yathopalabdhiH)

yAvanti pramANAni yasyA rajjvAH sA rajjustAvatastAvataH pramANasaMkhyAyuktAn tAvataH--tatsaMkhyAguNitAnvargAn samacaturashrAn karoti /
"vargasamacaturashraH' iti gaNitashAsreShu vyavahAraH /
tathA catuShpramANA rajjushcaturbhirguNitAshcaturo vargAn ShoDasha karoti /
paJNcapramANA paJNcabhirguNitAn paJNca vargAn paJNcaviMshatiM, ShaTpramANA ekonapaJNcAshataM, aShTapramANA catuHShaShTiM, navapramANA ekAshItiM, dashapramANA shataM, ekAdashapramANA ekaviMshottarashataM, dvAdashapramANA catushvatvAriMshacchatami tyAdi draShTavyam /
pramANamAha--upalabdhistathA--tathopalabhyate /
ukteShvartheShu pratyakShaM pramANamityarthaH /
tathA dvipramANaM caturashraM dvidhApacchidya catvAryupalabhyante /
tripamANaM tridhApacchidya nava, catuShpramANaM caturdhApacchidya ShoDasha, evaM paJNcapramANAdi Shvapi /
tathA dIrghasyAkShNayArajjurityAdiShu tathAtathopalabhyante /
dvAbhyAmekamabhyasya phale dve upalabhyete /
tribhirdve abhyasya ShaTa /
caturbhirdve abhyasyAShTau /
tathAhi--dvipramANapArshvamAnIkamekapramANatirya«bhAnIyakaM dvidhApacchidya dve upalabhyete /
dvipramANapArshvamAnIkaM tripramANatirya«bhAnIkaM pramAgdvidhodaka tridhApacchidya ShaDupalabhyante /
evamanyeShvapi pArshvamAnIpramANasaN^khyayodagavacchedaH tirya«bhAnIpramANasaN^khyayA prAgavaccheda iti kR^itvA phalAvagamaH /



sundararAjIyA vyAkhyA

yAvatA thedenAdhikena parilikiti tatpArshvayoragratashvopadadhAti /

ardhasya dvipramANAyAH pAdapUraNatvAt  || ˘p¡us_3.10b ||

___________________________________________________________


tR^itIyena navamI kalA  || ˘p¡us_3.10c ||

___________________________________________________________



ardhasya dvipramANA puruShamAtrI /
pAdAnAM pUraNaM yataH /
taduktaM--"dvAbhyAM catvAri' iti /
tR^itIyena navamI kalA, pramANatR^itIyena navamI kalA -- navamoM'sha ityarthaH /
tadapyuktaM-- tribhirnaveti.

ityApastambhasUtravivaraNe kapardibhAShye

shulbAkhyaprashne prathamaH paTalaH

tR^itIyaH khaNDaH

------



karavindIyA vyAkhyA.

idAnIM sacchedapramANamucyate--adhyardheti /



(adhyardhapuruShA navamI kalA)

adhyardhapuruShapramANenAdhyardhapuruShamabhyasya phalaM dvau sapAdau--pAdasahitau dvaupu ruShau karoti /
ardhatR^itIyapuruShA ShaT sapAdAn, ardhaM tR^itIyaM yeShAM te ardhatR^iyIyAH, te ca pramANaM yasyAH sAr'dhatR^itIyapuruShA /
sA yenAbhyastAH phalaM sapAdAn ShadpuruShAn karoti /
upalabdhirapi tathA adhyardhapuruShacaturashrasyArdhena caikena cApacchedaH prAkcodakca eka me kena dvAvardhau pAdashva, evamanyadapi ubhyataH sacchede sapAdarajjumadhyardhaM ShoDashAMshaM karoti /
caturashrakShetravipR^iddhau vR^iddhakShetraparij~nAnaprakAramAha--antaHsamIpaM prakaraNaM tadatItya vartata ityatyantaH atyantaH pradeshaH vidhiryasya so 'tyantapradeshaH--sArvatrika ityarthaH /
samacaturashra viShayo 'yam /
yAvatA--yAvatpramANena, yAvatAdhikena--yAvatpra mANonAdhikena /
eko yAvacchabdaH pramANamAtraviShayaH, anyo yAvacchabda AganduviShayaH /
yAvatA pramANena yAvanmAtrAdhikenetyarthaH /
parilikhati yaccaturashrakaraNArthaM parilikhati tatra tat adhikamAgantumUlacaturashrakShetraM pArshvayoH prAcI codIcI ca kShetramupadadhAti--saMyojayati /
yacca tenadhikamAtreNa caturashraM kriyate tatkShetraM koTyAM saMyojayati /
etaduktaM bhavati--sarvatra samacaturashrakShetravivR^iddhau vivR^iddhasya caturashrasya ca dakShiNapa shvima bhAge mUlapramANakR^itacaturashraM parikalpya tasyatasya pUrvottarapArshvayostatpAr shvamitapArshvamAnIkaM pramANAdhikamAtratirya«bhAnIkaM kShetraM parikalpya yacca tenA dhikamAtreNa ekenaikaM dvAbhyAM catvAri tribhirnavetyAdiphalakaraNaM caturashraM kriyate tatkShetraM prAgudakkoTyA parikalpayediti /
evaM sarvatra samacaturashrasya kShetravR^iddhau kShetrasya parigaNanaM kuryAdityarthaH /

ardhapramANena--pramANArdhenApAdapramANaM--pAdo 'tra caturthobhAgaH, tatpramANaM vidhIyate saMpAdyate pramANArdhamitaM kShetraM prameyasya catu rthabhAgo bavati /
kutaH? ardhasya dvipramANAyAH pAdapUraNatvAt ardhasya dvipramANakatayA bhUmeshcaturbhAgaH pUryate /

tR^itIyena navamI kalA--pramANatR^itIyena kShetrasya navamoM'shaH pUryate /
upalabdhi s tathA /
ekapramANAyA bhUmerardhena prAkyodakcApacchede kR^iter'dhapramANakR^itA bhUmirekapramANAyAH pAdo dR^ishyate, tasyA evaM prAkcodakcApacchede pramANatR^itIyamitA bhUmirekapramANAyA navamAsho dR^ishyate /
tathA caturthena ShoDasha kalA, paJNcamena paJNcaviMshatikalA, ShaShThena ShaTratriMshoM'shaH pUryate /
evamanyAnyapi chedaphalAni draShTavyAni //


iti shrIkaravindasvAmikR^itAyAM shulbapradIpikAyAM prathamaH paTalaH.

------



sundararAjIyA vyAkhyA

atha sacchedAnAM phalamAha----

(adhyardhapuruShA ShaT sapAdAn)

evaM ardhacaturthapuruShAd dAdasha sapAdAn, ardhapaJNcamapuruShA viMshatiM sapAdAnityAdi /
sapAdapuruShA adhyardhaM ShoDashabhAgaM cetyAdi draShTavyam /

sArvatriko 'yaM vidhiH--kR^itsnaM caturashraM vardhayitumicchan yAvatA pramANena vardhayitumicchati tatpurastAduttaratashvopadadhAti /
adhikapramANena yaccaturashraM kriyate taduttarapUrvasyAM koTyAm /
idAnIM tacchedAnAM phalamAha--

(athAtyantapradeshaH)

dvipramANAyA rajjvAH ardhasya pramANamAtrasya pAdapUraNa tvAt /
dvipramA NAyA rajjvAH phalaM catvAri /
tasya pAda ekam, tasya pUraNatvAdityarthaH //


(tR^itIye navamI kalA)

kalAbhAgastripramANAyAstattR^itIyasya navamapUNatvAditi gamyamAnatvAnnoktam /
caturthena ShoDasha, paJNcamena paJNcaviMshatirityAdi draShTavyam //


iti sundararAjIye ApastambashulbasUtravyAkhyAne

shulbapradIpe prathamaH paTalaH.

pUrvamavisheSheNa mAnamuktam, asyeyAnAyAmaH iyAnvistara evaM ca vihartavyamiti /
visheShavidhAnArthamAha--

gArhapatyAhavanIyayorantarAlaM yathA syAnnAhavanIyadakShiNAgnayoH dakShiNAgnigArhapatyayorvA mA bhUdityevamarthaM gArhapatyAhavanIyagrahaNam /
