aShTAsu prakrameShu brAhmaNo 'gnim AdadhIta | ekAdashasu rAjanyaH | dvAdashasu vaishyaH  || ˘p¡us_4.1b ||

___________________________________________________________



___________________________________________________________


caturviMshatyAm aparimite yAvatA vA cakShuShA manyate tasmAn nAtidUram Adheya iti sarveShAm avisheSheNa shrUyate  || ˘p¡us_4.2 ||

___________________________________________________________



prakrameNa pramANaM vakShyati /
aShTau prakramAnatItya gArhapatyAdAhavanIyaM pratiShThApayati /
evamekAdashasu rAjanyasya /
vaishyasyadvAdashasu /
caturviMshatyA vA parimite vA yAvAtA vA cakShuShA manyate /
tasmAnnAdidUramAdheyaH iti sarveShAmavisheSheNa shrUyate /
yAvatA veti sarveShAM vidhirvikalvena /
iyatAntarAlena vihArasaMpattirbhavatIti mananam /
atidUrapratiShedho vyavAyaparihArArthaH /
yadyatidUramAdhIyate tadA shvAdayo vyaveyuH /



karavindiyA vyAkhyA

uktAHsAmAnyato vihArAH /
idAnIM darshapUrNamAsAdiShu visheShavivakShayA prathamabhUtAgnayAdheyavihArayAgavidhirucyate /
agnaya adhIyante 'smin karmaNIti tadagnayAdheyaM /
tabhdava AgnayA dheyikaH /
vihriyante 'smin agnaya iti vihAraH, devayajanedashaH, tamadhikR^itya /
gArhapatyAhavanIyayorantarAle--gArhapatyAhavanIya shabdAbhyAM tattadAyatane lakShaNA antarAla shrutisAmarshyAt, antarAle antarAlaM prastutya vij~nAyate shrUyate /
sarvatra vij~nAyata ityasyAyamevArthaH gArhapatyAhavanIyagrahaNAt, tayorevAntarAle /
shrutirevaM paThyate--

aShTAsu prakrameShu brAhnaNo 'gnInAdadhItaikAdashasu rAjanyo dvAdashasu vaishyaH caturviMshatyAmaparimite yAvatA vA cashruShA manyate tasmAnnAtidUramAdheya iti //
sarveShAmavisheSheN.a shrUyate /
prakramaM vakShyati dvipadastripado veti /
aShTaprakramAdayo 'ntarAlavisheShaNaM /
aShTAsu prakrameShvantarAle ityAdi /
aparimitasaMkhyAyAM taccaturviMshateH parataH tadAnantaryAt, aparimitaM pramANAt bhUyaH, iti kAtyAyanaH /
yAvatA vA cakShuShA manyate tAvatA pramANena cakShuShA gR^ihItena manyate yathA iyAMshcaturviMshati prakrama iti cakShuShA mAnaM /
yadyapi caturvishateH parata eva paThyate tathApi dvAdashasu vikrameShvityArabhya yaM dvAdashasu vikrAmeShu ityAditaittirIyakashrutyanurodhAdaShTaprakramAdInamapi sarveShAM grAhyaM, tena iyAnaShTaprakrama iyAnekadasha iyAndvAdashaprakrama iti saMbhavati /
tasmAccaturviMshateradUramatidUrenAdheyaM /
anenAparimitavacanaprAptAtidUratA niShidhyate /
caturviMshatividhAnAdevetaH prAgatidUrA yogAH /
catuviMshatyAdi vidhicatuShTayaM sarveShAM brAhmaNAdInAmavisheSheNa bhavati /
dvAdashasu vikrameShvityapi sarveShAmavisheSheNa labhyate //


sundahahAjIyA vyAkhyA

(AgnayAdheyike vaishyaH)

gArhapatyasya purastAdeteShu prakrameShvatIteShviti vij~nAyate atha sAvarNikI shrutiH /

(caturviMshatyA shrUyate.)

aparimitaM "pramANAbhdUya' iti kalpAntaram /
cakShuShA manyata iti daNDAdimAnaniShedhaH /
iyAnaShTau prakramAH, iyAnekAdasha iyAn dvAdasheti cakShukShA yAvantaM deshaM manyate tasmAnnAtidaraM tasyAvadheHsamIpa AdheyaH /
etatsarvaM prayogakAla evoktamanUdyate /



kapardibhAShyam

___________________________________________________________


dakShiNataH purastAd vitR^itIyadeshe gArhapatyasya nedIyasi dakShiNAgner vij~nAyate  || ˘p¡us_4.3 ||

___________________________________________________________



dakShiNataH purastAt dakShiNAprAkkoNe deshe vitR^itIyadeshe--IShadUnatR^itIyadeshe--kasya vitR^itIyadeshaH--gArhapatyAhavanIyayorantarAlasya nedIyasi AsannatR^itIyadeshe pArshvAdityarthaH /
tatra dakShiNAgnerAyatanamiti shrUyate /



karavindIyA vyAkhyA.

(dakShimataHavij~nAyate)

dakShiNataH purastAt dakShiNAprAkkoNadeshe tasya gArhapatyasya nedIyasi sannikR^iShTe tasyaiva vitR^itIyadeshe vishabdo hInavacanaH kiJNciddhInatR^itIyadeshAntarAle dakShiNAgrerAyatanaM shrUyate //


sundararAjIyA vyAkhyA.

dakShiNAgrayAyatanavidhAnAthamAha /

(dakShiNataHavij~nAyate)

vitR^itIyadeshe vikalatR^itIyadeshe IShadUnatR^itIyadesha ityarthaH /
gArhapatyasya dakShiNataH purastAttasyaiva nedIyasi vitR^itIyadeshe dakShiNAgrerAyatanamiti //


kapardibhAShyam.

tatkathaM gR^ihyata ityAya /



___________________________________________________________


gArhapatyAhavanIyayor antarAlaM paJNcadhA ShaDdhA vA saMvibhajya ShaShThaM saptamaM vA bhAgam Agantum upasamasya samaM traidhaM vibhajyAparasmiMs tR^itIye lakShaNaM kR^itvA gArhapatyAhavanIyayor antau niyamya lakShaNena dakShiNApAyamya nimittaM karoti tad dakShiNAgner Ayatanam | shrutisAmarthyAt  || ˘p¡us_4.4 ||

___________________________________________________________



gArhapatyAhavanIyayorantarAlaM paJNcadhA vibhajya ShaDdhA vA vibhajyetyanvayaH /
yadi paJNcadhA tadA ShaShTho bhAga AgantuH /
ShaShThaM saptamaM vA bhAgaM Agantumupasamasya samaM traidhaM vibhajya /
yadi ShoDhA tadA saptamo bhAgaH AgantiH /
tamupasamasya saMyojya, samaM traidhaM vibhajya; AgantunA saha viShamaM mAbhUditi samagrahaNam /
aparasmiMstR^itIye lakShaNaM kR^itvA gArhapatyAvahanIyayorantau niyamya pAshau pratimucya lakShaNena dakShiNApAyamya shaN^kaM nihanyAt /
dakShiNAgnisthAnaM shrutisAmarthyAt /
sAmarthyamabhidhAnashaktiH asyAHshruterayamevArthaM iti /
tena gArhapatyAhavanIya yorantarAlaM, triprathamavistArAyAmAni trINi caturashrANi kR^itvAparasmin caturashre uttarasyAM shroNyAM gArhapatyaM dakShiNeM'sedakShiNAgnayAyatanaM pUrvasmin caturashre, uttareMsa AhavanIyamityevamAdayo nirastA bhavanti /
sarvatrAgnayAyatanAni caturashrANi maNDalAni vA /
iha tu maNDalaM gArhapatyamardhamaNDalAkAramanvAhAryapacanaM /
caturashramAhavanIyamiti smaranti maNDalacaturashrayorukto vidhiH /
idAnIM dakShiNAgneH dhanurAkAra ucyate--pishIladvikaraNyA caturashraM kR^itvA pUrvoktena vidhAnena maNDalaM kuryAt /
tasya maNDalasya viShkambhacaturbhAgaM dakShiNAgneH pUrvanihatAcchaN^korudagapasArya shaN^kaM nihatya tasminpAshaM pratimucya viShkambhArdhena maNDalaM parilikhyottaramardhaM tyajet /
tatra shlokau bhavataH----

dakShiNAgnerhatAcchaN^korudakchaN^kurdashAN^gule /

ekAdashatilairUne kAryasya dhanuShA samaH //


tasminpAshaM pratimucya viMshatyAyatayA likhet /

UnayA tu dvAviMshatitilairardhaM tyajedudak //


iti /

karavindIyA vyAkhyA

gArhapatyAhavanIyayoH--shrutisAmarthAt.

etasya viharaNamAha--

gArhapatyAhavanIyayorantarAlamaShTaprakramAdikaM daJNcadhA ShoDhA vA saMbhujya guNayitvA ShaShThaM saptamaM vA bhAgamAgantumupasamas paJNcadhA guNane ShaShThaM ShoDhA guNane bhAgamumasamasya saMyojyAgantun tR^itIye gArhapatyasannihite tR^itIye lakShaNaM niraJNjanaM kR^itvA gArhapatyAhavanIyayorantau niyamya rajjvantau pAshau gArhapatyasya pUrvashaN^kau pashcimaM pAshamAhavanIyasya pashcimashaN^kau pUrvaM pAshe pratimucya lakShaNena dakShiNApAyamya nimittaM cihnaM tatra kuryAt /
tannimittaM dhanurAkR^iterdakShiNAgnermadhyamaM, visheShAshravaNAt /
gArhapatyAhavanIyayormadhyamashaN^kvorantau niyamyeti kecit /
shrutisAmarthyAt /
"dakShiNataH purastAt' ityAdi shrutibalAdityarthaH /
atra paJNcadhApakShe gArhapatyAhavanIyayorantarAlasya dakShiNAgnayAyatanamadhyopakrAntAddakShiNottaralambAt pashcimo bhAga ekatriMshadaN^gulayaH tribhAgonasaptatilAsh ca /
pUrvabhAgo 'ShTAviMshatiraN^gulayaH tribhAgAdhikasaptaviMshatitilAsh ca /
lambakaH ShaTtriMshadaN^gulayaH pAdonaShoDashatilAsh ca /
ShaDdhApakShe dvAtriMshadaN^gulayaH sArdhasaptaviMshatitilAsh ca pUrvabhAgaH /
lambakastriMshadaN^gulayaH saptatilAsh ca /
pAdAShTakamite 'ntarAlavat prakramite ekAdashAdiShu ca bhAgayorlambakasya pramANamunneyaM, unnayanaprakAraM cAtraiva vakShyAmaH /
atrApyAyatanAni pishIlamAtrANi, athavA asyaiSha dhiShNyo lIyata iti prAjahitasyApi dhiShNyatvadarshanAdAyatanAnAM caturashramaNDalatvayoraniyamena prAptayorapi maNDajalameva gArhapatyAyatanaM agnanayo vai trayI vidyetyatrAnuvAkaparyAye tasya pR^ithivIstuteH tadAkAratvAccatasyAH ardhamaNDalAkAraM dhanurAkAraM dakShiNAgnayAyatanaM, tatraivAntarIkShastuteH tadAkAratvAcca nabhasashcaturashramAhavanIyam, tatraiva dyulokastuteH caturashramaindrasthAnamiti shAstrAntare darshanAcca sabhyAvasathyayorapi caturashrameva, tayostaddvikAratvAt /
atra yogaH gArhapatyAyatane pishIlamAtraM caturashraM vihR^itya maNDalaM kuryAddakShiNAgnerapi vacanAt, vishIladvikaraNyA caturashraM vihR^itya maNDalakTitya maNDalaviShkambhacaturbhAgena dakShiNAgnanayAyatanaM tannimittAduttarataHshaN^kuM nihatya tatra shaN^kau tadviShkambhamadhyaM niyamyAntau samau kR^itvA maNDalaM vilikhya maNDaladhye prAcIM lekhAM vilikhya udagardhaM tyajet /
dakShiNArdha AyatanaM gArhapatyasya purastAdaShTaprakramAdInatItya pishIlamAtraM caturashramAhavanIyaM kuryAt tatpurastAt saJNcaramavashiShya AhavanIyavat sabhyaM tatpurastAdAvasathyamapi /
tadvat pishIlapramANaM ca /
dviprAdeshaM pishIlam /
muShTikR^ito 'ratniH pishIlamityeke /
bAhvorantarAlaM pishIlamityeka iti kecit /
prakramyata iti pakrama iti padasyApi prakramatAmicchanti /
tathApi labhyate, ayamatra vimAnakramaH--gArhapatyAhavanIyadhiShNiyau vimAya gArhapatyAhavanIyayorantarAlamityAdi dakShiNApAyamya niyamya nimittaM kR^itvA tenaiva lakShaNenottaratash ca nimittaM viparyasya dakShiNata uttaratash ca nimittaM kR^itvA pishIladvikaraNIcaturashramaNDalIvaShkambhacaturthAMshena dakShiNayornimittayorudakkR^itanimittadvayAnukUlyena shaN^kuM nikhanet /
anayoH pashcimashaN^kau pishIladvikaraNI caturashramaNDalaviShkambhArdhena maNDalamAlikhya purvashaN^kvAnukUlyena prAcIM j~nAtvA maNDalasyottarArdhaM tyajet /
dakShiNArdho dakShiNAgnidhiShNiyo bhavati /

sundararAjIyA vyAkhyA.

(gArhapatyAhavanIyayoHashrutisAmarthAt.)

tatkathaM grAhyamityata Aha----

samaM sarvaM, gArhapatyAhavanIyayoH gArhapatyasya paurastye shaN^kau AhavanIyasya pAshvAtye shaN^kau ca dakShiNato dakShiNAgnayAyatanam /
tadAyatanamadhyamityanye /
tasmin, pakShe gArhapatyAhavanIyayorApi madhyayoreva grahaNam /
sarvANyevAgrayAyatanAni pishIlamAtrANi caturashrANi parimaNDalAni vA dhiShNiyatvAnmaNDalaM gArhapatyasya /
ardhamaNDalaM dakShiNAgneshcaturashramAhavanIyasyetyaitihAsikAHsarvANi cAyatanAni kShetratastulyAnItyAhuH /
tatrokto maNDalavidhiH AhavanIyasyAkShNayArajjvA caturashraM vihR^itya vidhAnena maNDalaM kR^itvA uttarArvaM jahyAttaddakShiNAgnayAyatanam //


kapardikShAShyam


___________________________________________________________


yajamAnamAtrI prAcy aparimitA vA yathAsannAni havIMShi saMbhaved evaM tirashcI prAJNcau vedyaMsAv unnayati | pratIcI shroNI purastAd aMhIyasI pashcAt prathIyasI madhye saMnatataraivam iva hi yoSheti dArshikyA veder vij~nAyate  || ˘p¡us_4.5 ||

___________________________________________________________



yajamAnamAtrItyAdi dArshikyAvedeHshrutiH /
asyAHshruterarthaM vimAnavidhinaiva vyAcaShTe /



karavindiyA vyAkhyA

AyatanaviharaNAnantaraM prakR^itibhUtayordarshapUrNamAsayorviharaNamucyate /

(yajamAnamAtrI--vedervij~nAyate.)

yajamAnamAtrIti // .//
yajamAmAtrI ShaNNavatyaN^gulA prAktvenApari mitA /
tadadhikA prAcI prA«mukhA, saMbhavo vyAptiH, yathA havIMShi parasparasaMbandhena AsannAni bhavanti tathA tirashvI tirya«bhAnI syAt, AyAmasya tribhAgonA pashcattirashvI /
"AyAmAsyArdhena purastAttirashvI' iti bodhAyanaH /
pashubandhe ca tathA dR^ishyate, aratnibhirvA caturbhiH pashcAt ShaDbhiH prAcI tribhiH purastAditi, vikR^itiShu vahuhaviHShu bhahuvistArA, alpahaviH Shu prakR^itivat /
prAJNcau vedyaMsAvunnayati prAktvena pUrvAntamatItAvaMsau kuryAt pratIcI shroNI tathA pR^ithaktvena shroNyAkuryAt aMhIyasI--tanvI prathIyasI-- vistIrNA sannatatarA atishayena tanuH, evamiva hi yoSheti /
evamivahIti shabdo nipAtasamudAyaH prasiddhavacanaH /
yathA--evamiva hi pashuH, evamiva hyannamadyata iti /
etadeva hi yoShA sAdR^ishyamasyAH /
yanmadhye kR^ishatvaM pR^ithvaMsatvaM pR^ithutarashroNItvaM ca /
etat "catuHshikhaNDA yuvatiHsupeshA' iti mantravarNAcca labhyeta, dArshikyA vedeH darshapurNamAsayoHsAdhAraNA ' pi vediH darshe pUrvedyurddashyatayA dArshikItyucyate /
yadvA--darshapUrNamAsayorekasheShaM kR^itvA nirdeshaH,

sundararAjIyA vyAkhyA

(yajamAnamAtrI vij~nAyate.)

yajamAnamAtrI caturaratniH paJNcAratnirvA yathA'sannAni havIShi saMbhavet saMgR^ihNIyAt /
evaM tirashvI ardhalakShaNaM tiryagityarthaH /
unnayati dIrghaM nayati /
pratIcI pratIcyA yoShAsAdR^ishyaM ca "catuHshikhaNDA' iti mantravarNAt darshikyAH-- darshapUrNamAsikyAH /



kapardikShAShyam


___________________________________________________________


apareNAhavanIyaM yajamAnamAtrI dIrghaM caturashraM vihR^itya tAvatIM rajjum Ayamya madhye lakShaNaM kR^itvA dakShiNayoH shroNyaMsayor antarA niyamya lakShaNena dakShiNApAyamya nimittaM karoti | nimitte rajjuM niyamyAntau samasya | dakShiNAyAH shroNer dakShiNam aMsam Alikhet | evam uttarataH | tirya«mAnIM dviguNAM tathA kR^itvA pashcAt purastAc copalikhet | vimitAyAM purastAt pArshvamAnyAv upasaMharet | shrutisAmarthyAt  || ˘p¡us_4.6 ||

___________________________________________________________


iti caturthakhaNDaH.

--------

apareNAhavanIyaM ekarajjvAdibhidIrN^ghaM caturashraM vihR^itya saMpAdya yajamAnamAtrI pArshvamAnI yathA sannAni havIMShi saMbhavet parasparAsaMghaTitAni tiShThanti tathA tirya«bhAnI /
tasyAstribhAgona vA tirashvIti bodhAyanIye shulbAntare pratipAditam /
tAvatIM rajjumabhyasya ubhayataH pAshau kR^itvA dakShiNayoHshroNyaMsayorantau niyamya pAshau pratimucya lakShaNena jakShiNApAyamya nimittaM shaN^kuM nihatya tAsmin shaN^kau rajjuM saMyojya pAshAvunmucya tena hastena gR^ihItvA dakShiNAM shroNimArabhya yAvaddakShiNAMsamAlikhet /
evamuttarapArshvamAlikhet /
etatsannatatvaM vedeH /
tirya«bhAnyApyevaM kuryAt /
tirya«bhAnIpramANAM rajjumabhsya madhye lakShaNaM kR^itvA shroNyorante pAshau pratimucya pArshvAdapasArya tatra shaN^kuM nihatya tatra rajju prabadhyAntau samasya dakShiNAM shroNimArabhya yAvaduttarA kShoNI tAvadAlikhet /
evaM purastAdapi karoti /
evamunnayanaM shroNyaMsau /
evaMprakArA hi yoShA /
hishabdo rUpaprasiddhau /
prAkchirAHstrI evamevetyarthaH /
vimitAyA mevaM caturashramApAditAyAM purastAtpArshvamAnyAvupasaMharet, saN^kocayet /
shrutisAmarthyAt--"purastAdaMhIyasI' iti yaiShA shrutiH tasyAHsAmarthyAt /
itarathA yoShAsAdR^ishyamapi na syAt //


iti caturthaHkhaNDaH

--------



karavindIyA vyAkhyA



etAdviharaNena vyAcaShTe.

(apareNAhavanIyam evamuttarataH.)

apareNeti /
apareNAhavanIyaM AhavanIyasya pashcAtsamIpe /
gArhapatyAhavanIyayoryadyapi mahadantarAlaM tathApyAhavanIyasamIpa eva vediH /
kecidvistAradviguNAyAmaM dIrghamicchanti /
uktapramANaM dIrghacaturashramAhavanIyamapareNa vihR^itya shroNyaMseShu shaN^kunnihatya yAvadAyAmaH tAvatIM rajjumabhyasya AyAmadviguNAM rajjuM kR^itvA madhye lakShaNaM niraJNjanaM kR^itvA dakShimayoHshroNyaMsayorantau niyamya niraJNjanena dakShiNApAyamya shaN^kuM nihatya tasmin rajjuM pratimucya pAshAvekIkR^itya shroNyA Arabhya yAvadaMsaM vR^ittamArgeNAlikhet /
uttarapArshva uttarato 'pAyamya evameva kuryAt //


(tirya«bhAnIM dviguNAM--likhet)

tirya«bhAnImiti /
pUrvAM tirya«bhAnIM pUrvavaddviguNAM kR^itvA purato 'pAyamya dakShiNasmadaMsAt prakramya uttaramaMsamAlikhet, pashcimayA tirya«bhAnyA pashcAdapyevameva kuryAt, vediprAcImitAM rajjuM gArhapatyAhavanIyayorantarAlamityuktaprakAreNa vedyA dakShiNottaramAyamya pUrvavaddvitR^itIyadeshe lakShaNaM kuryAt udagbahirvederuttarataH uttarArthaM lakShaNaM ca kR^itvA vedyAH pashcAdapyavemeva vitR^itIye lakShaNaM kuryAt. gArhapatyAhavanIyayormadhyaM--madhyadeshaH tatra lakShaNaM kuryAt //


(vimitAyAMashrutisAmarthyAt.)

vimitAyAmiti /
vimitAyAM caturashrIkR^itamAtrAyAM lekhAkaraNAt prAgeva pArshvamAnyau purastAtpurata upasaMhAret--saMkocayet /

iti caturthaH khaNDaH.

----------



sundararAjIyA vyAkhyA.

(apareNa shrutisAmarthyAt)

tasyA viharaNamAha--

nimitte rajjuM rajjumadhyaM niyamya pratimucya dakShiNAyai dakShiNasyAH shroNerArabhya dakShiNamaMsaM pratyAlikhet /
tirya«bhAnyorapi madhye lakShaNaM kR^itvA shroNyoraMsayoshvAntau niyamya pashcAtpurastAccApAyamyetyAdi draShTavyam /
etadeva shroNyaMsayorunnayanam /
vimitAyAM caturashrIkR^itAyAM saMnamanAtpUrvameva kiJNcidupasaMharet, "purastAdaMhIyasI' iti shrutisAmarthyAt /
atra bodhAyanaH--

"yajamAnamAtrI prAcI, tasyA evArdhaM purastAttirashvI, tribhAgonA pashcAt tirashvI triMshatpadAni' iti //


kapardibhAShyaM

___________________________________________________________


triMshat padAni prakramA vA pashcAttirashvI bhavati | ShaTtriMshat prAcI caturviMshatiH purastAt tirashcIti saumikyA veder vij~nAyate  || ˘p¡us_5.1 ||

___________________________________________________________


___________________________________________________________


ShaTtriMshikAyAm aShTAdashopasamasya aparasmAd antAd dvAdashasu lakShaNaM paJNcadashasu lakShaNaM pR^iShThyAntayor antau niyamya paJNcadashakena dakShiNApAyamya shaN^kuM nihantyevam uttarataHshroNI | viparyasyAMsau paJNcadashikenaivApAyamya dvAdashike shaN^kuM nihanti | evam uttaratastAv aMsau  || ˘p¡us_5.2a ||

___________________________________________________________



padAnItyasmadIyA shrutiH /
triMshatpadAni prakramA vA pashcAttirashvIti /
tirya«bhAnI bhavati /
ShaTtriMshatpR^iShThyA prAcI caturviMshatiH purastAt tirya«bhAnI bhavatIti saumikyA vedeH some shrutiH /
ShaTtriMshikAyAM rajjvAM aShTAdashopasamasya prakShipyAntayoH pAshau kR^itvAparasmAdantAddvAdashasu lakShaNaM paJNcadashasu lakShaNaM niraJNjanaM kR^itvA pR^iShThyAntayoH prAgvaMshasya madhyamAllAlATikAttInprAcaH prakramAn prakramya shaN^kuM nihatya tasmAcca purastAt ShaTtriMshatprakrame shaN^kU nihatya tayoH pAshau pratimucya paJNcadashakena dakShiNApAyamya shaN^kaM nihanyAt /
sA dakShiNA shroNI /
evamuttarato 'pasArya shaN^kuM nihanyAt /
sottarA shroNI /
viparyastayAMsau /
paJNcadashikenaivopAyamya dvAdashake shaN^kU nihantyaivamuttaratastAvaMsau /
shaN^koH pAshAvunmucya pUrvapAshamaparasminpratimuJNcet /
aparaM pUrvasminpratimuJNcet /
sa viparyAsaH /
viparyastayA--evaM kR^itayA rajjvAM'sau mAtavyau /
tenaiva niraJNjanena dakShiNApasArya dvAdashake shaN^kuM nihanyAt /
tenaivodagapasArya dvAdashake shaN^kuH /
tAvaMsau /
mahAvedyA mAnaM kimirthamidamucyate /
yAvatA siddhametat? anekarajjuviharaNavivakShayoktamiti kecitpariharanti /
AyAmaM vetyasmin pakShe dvAdashake lakShaNam /
paJNcadashake lakShaNe ca saptaviMshatau niraJNjanamiti lakShaNabAhulyapratipAdanArthamityapare /
samacaturashrANAM dIrghacaturashrANAM ca viharaNamuktam /
iha tu dIrghaviShamacaturashrasyetyanye /



___________________________________________________________


tadekarajjvA viharaNam  || ˘p¡us_5.2b ||

___________________________________________________________



___________________________________________________________


trikacatuShkayoH paJNcikAkShNayArajjuH | tAbhis trirabhyastAbhir aMsau | caturabhyastAbhiHshroNI  || ˘p¡us_5.3 ||

___________________________________________________________



yasya caturashrasya trikA tirya«bhAnI catuShkA pArshvamAnI tasyA akShNayA rajjuH paJNcikA /
tAbhiraMsau mAtavyau /
trikaM trirabhyAsayuktaM dvAdasha bhavanti /
catuShkaM (ShoDasha paJNcikA) vishatiHSha /
yupAvaTIyAcchaN^koH pashcAt ShoDashasu shaN^kuM nihatya tasmin paJNcikAM sAbhyAsaM pratimucya yUpAvaTIye sAbhyAsaM trikaM pratimucyAMsAvAyacchet /
caturabhyastAbhiHshroNI /
tAbhireva caturabhyAsayuktAbhiH shroNI mAtavyau /
viMsheShu shaN^kuM nihatya tasmin paJNcikAM sAbhyAsaM paJNcaviMshatiM pratimucya paJNcadashikAM pratimucya tAbhiHshroNI viharet //


karavindIyA vyAkhyA.

darshapUrNamAsavediviharaNAnantaraM prakR^itau saumyavedivimAnamucyate /

(triMshatpadAni prakramA vA vedervij~nAyate)

triMshaditi //
triMshatpadAn.i pashcAttirashvI bhavatIti taittirIyakashrutiH /
triMshatprakrameti shAshAntarIyA, ato vikalpaH, yadyapi karmopateshaH prakramashabdena prAgvaMshasya madhyamAllAlATikAtrrIn prAcaH prakramAniti tatrApi shrutyorvaikalpikatvena pradarshanArthaH prakramashabdaH /
tatra prakramAyata iti prakramAshabdaH /
pashcAttirashvI pashcAttirya«bhAnI prAcI AyAmaH purastAstirashvI tirya«bhAnI vimAnamucyate //


(ShaTtriMshivaMsau)

ShaTtriMshikAyAmiti //
ShaTtriMshikA ShaTtriMshatpramANA rajjuH, tasyAmaShTAdashopasamasya saMyojyAparasmAt pashcimAdantAdArabhya dvAdashasu lakShaNamaMsArthaM, paJNcadashasu lakShaNaM shroNyarthaM, prAgvaMshasya madhyamAllAlATikAtrrin prAcaH prakramAnatItya tataH purastAt ShaTtriMshatpramANAM prAcIM lekhAmAlikheta sA pR^iShThyA tadantayoH shaN^ku nihatya tayoH pAshau pratimucya paJNcadashikena lakShaNena dakShiNApAyamya shaN^kuM nihanti sA dakShiNA shroNI, evamuttara to 'pAyamya shaN^kuH, sottarA shroNI, viparyastayAMsau viparyastapA shayAM'shau mAtavyau /
paJNcadashikenaivApAyamya dvAdashike shaN^kuH, dakShiNataH uttaratash ca tAvaMsau /
nanu "tadarthamabhyasyAparasmin' itya nenaiba viharaNenAsminviharaNe siddhe kimarthamiha punarvacanam, ucyate--saN^khyApUrvAgamArthamiti kecitpariharanti, anekarajjuvivakShayA ityanye, AyAmAbhyAseShu dvAdashasu lakShaNaM paJNcadashasu lakShaNaM saptaviMshatyAdau niraDhaJNjanamiti lakShaNabAhulyapratipAdanArthamityapare /
dIrghacaturashrANAM ca tatra viharaNamuktaM /
iha tu viShamadIrghacaturashrasyetyapare //


(tadekarajjvA viharaNam)

taditi //
ekA cAsau rajjushvetyekarajjuH, ekayaiva rajjvA shroNyaMsAnAM viharaNaM /
dvishaN^kunA trishaN^kunA paJNjashaN^kunA vA yogena yadviharaNamuktaM tadidamityuktamanubhAShate anekarajjuvidhitsayA //


(trikacatuShkayoH--paJNcikAkShNayArajjuH)

triketi //
trikA triprANA catuShkA catuShpramANA paJNcikA paJNcapramANA /
trikacatuShkayoriti AyAmAbhyAsaprAptamanUdyate, tadabhyAsena shroNyaMsavidhAnArthaM evamuttareShvabhyAseShu //


(tAbhistrirabhyastAbhiraMsau)

tAbhiH pR^ithakpR^ithakrirabhyastAbhiH trirupari nikSheptAbhiH, trikAt trirabhyastAt dvAdasha, catuShkAtrrirabhyastAt ShoDasha, paJNcakAttrirabhyastAt viMshatiH, tAbhiraMsau mAtavyau //


(caturabhyastAbhiHshroNI)

trikAccaturabhyastAt paJNcadasha, catuShkAdviMshatiH, paJNcakAt paJNcaviMshatiH, tAbhiHshroNyau mAtavyau /
yUpAvaTIyAcchaN^koH pashcAt ShoDashasu shaN^kuM nnihatya tasmiMstrirabhyastAM paJNcikAM caturabhyastAM pratimucya yUpAvaTIye trirabhyastAM trikAM caturabhyastAM pratimucya prathamanihitashaN^kau caturabhyastAM trikAMpratimucya tAbhyAM shroNyau, AyAmAbhyAsasiddhamidam /
AyAmadviguNAbhyAsasiddhaM vA //


sundararAjIyA vyAkhyA.

(triMshatpadAni prakramA vA vedervij~nAyate)

padaM ca dvividhamuktaM bodhAyanena--"dashAN^gulaM kShudrapadaM padaM paJNcadashAN^gulam' iti /
dvAdashAN^gulamiti kAtyAyanaH /
etAnitrividhAni padAni laukikena padena vikalpyante /
tathA vakShyati--"pade yuge 'radnau' ityAdi /
etAnyeva caturvindhAni padAni dviguNAni triguNAni ca prakramAH /
te ca saptavidhAH /
tatra sAgnicitye some padairvimAnaM na labhyate agnikShetrAsaMbhavAt /
evaM saptavidhe 'gnau viMshatyaN^gulasya nivR^ittir vyAkhyAtA, anagnicitye tu sarveShAmeva pradaprakramANAmicchayA vikalpa iti kecit /
anye punarevaM vyavasthAmicchanti--padaishcaturvidhairviMshatyaN^gulena vA prakrameNa mAnamanagnicitye /
ekavidhAgnau viMshatyaN^gulena, dvividhAdiShu paJNcavidhaparyanteShu caturviMshatyaN^gulena, ShaDvidhAdiShu dvAda shavidhaparyanteShu viMshatyaN^gulena laukikena vA dvipadena, trayodashavidhAdiShu ShaT triMshadaN^gulenetyAdi /
sarveShAmapi pakShe agnayaH paJNcacatvAriMshadaN^gulena prakrameNa saMbhavanti /
tatrAgnyanuguNA vede rvivR^iddhiH kartavyA /
yR^ipaiphAdashinyAM nyAyasya prakramAsthAnIyaH, ekashatavidhe ashItyaN^gula ityAdi /

athAsyA vederviMharaNamAha----

(ShaTtriMshikAyAMaviharaNam)

yAvadAyAm pramANamityuktasya mAnasyAyaM prapaJNcaH /

athAsyA eva vederanekarajjvA viharaNamAha--



(trikacatuShkayoHashroNI)

trikacatuShkayostiryakpAshvamAnyoH abhyastAbhiH upakShiptAbhiH, yathA-- trikA trirabhyastA dvAdashikA, catuShkA trirabhyastA ShoDAshekA, paJNcikA trirabhyastA viMshatikA /
etAbhistisR^ibhirabhyastAbhiraMsau mAtavyau /
etAbhireva caturabhyastAbhiH paJNcadashikayA viMshikayA ca shroNI mAtavye /
dvirabhyastAbhirapyetAbhiraMsau mAtuM shakyete /
sarvatra dvAdashikAM'sayoH /
tirya«bhAnI paJNcadashikA /
shroNyoritarA pR^iShThyAyAM pArshvamAnI evaM ShaDbhIrajjubhirviharaNam /
evamuttaratra //


kapardIyA bhAShyam.

prathamanihate shaN^kau trikaM sAbhyAsam /

dvAdashikApaJNcikayos trayodashikAkShNayArajjuH, tAbhir aMsau dvirabhyastAbhiH shroNI  || ˘p¡us_5.4 ||

yupAvaTIyAcchaN^koH pashcAtpaJNcasu shaN^kuM nihatya tasmin trayodashikAM pratimucya yUpAvaTIye paJNcikAM dvAdashikAM ca pratimucya tAbhiraMsau mAtavyau /
dvirabhyastAbhiHshroNI /

karavindIyA vyAkhyA.

(dvAdashikA rajjuH)

spaShTArthamidam //


(tAbhiHashroNI)

ardhAbhyAsaprAptamidamAyAmacaturguNAbhyAsaprAptaM vA //

etAvanti j~neyAni vediviharaNAni bhavanti  || ˘p¡us_5.6 ||

etAvantyeva shuddhamUlAni j~nAtuM shakyAni vediviharaNAni bhavanti /
anye shuddhamUlAH kalpayitumashakyAH /
tasmAdetAvantItyavadhAryante--



karavindIyA vyAkhyA.

(paJNcadashikA shroNI)

prathamanihatashaN^kau paJNcadashikA, tataH purastAdaShTAsu saptadashikA, tAbhyAM shroNyau /
AyAmatriguNAbhyAsaptAptamidaM AyAmatR^itIyadvikAbhyAsaptAptaM vA //


(dvAdashikA tAbiraMsau)

dvAdashiketi /
idamapi gatArtham /
yUpAvaTIye dvAdashikA, prathamanihatashaN^koH purastAtprakramamAtre shaN^kuM nihatya tasmin saptatriMshikA, tAbyAmaMsau, paJNcamadvayAbhyAsaprAptamidaM, paJNcaguNAbhyAsaptAptaM vA /



(etAvanti bhavanti)

etAvantIti //
shuddhamUlatay.A j~nAtuM shakyAni etAvantye vetyavadhAraNA /
etAvantyuktAni, anyAnyapi unneyAni, sacchedAbhiH rajjubhirnirhrAsavR^iddhibhyAM ca vediviharaNAni bhavantyeva, yadyapi idaM viharaNamekarajjvA dvisayogenaiva vyAkhyatam, tathA tri shaN^kupaJNcashaN^kubhtyAmapi nirhrAsavR^iddhibhyAM yathA yogaM vihartavyaH, itarathA tayorvidhAnasyAdR^iShTArthatvakalpanAprasaN^gAt, ato nidarshanametat sarvaviharaNAnAm /



sundararAjIyA.

(paJNcadashikA bhavanti)

chedarahitAnyetAvanti /

ardhadvAdashikArdhacaturthikayorardhatrayodashikAkShNayArajjuH, tAbhiraMsau /

aShTaviMshatyonaM padasahasraM mahAvediH  || ˘p¡us_5.7a ||

___________________________________________________________


navashatAni dvisaptatish ca (972) padakramANi prakramapramA NAni vA caturashrANi mahAvedeH /
mahadrahaNaM kimartham? padapramitAyAM mahAvedyAM sadohavirdhAnAdInAmapi padanevai mAnArthaM, prakramamitAyAmaratniprakramaireva navAratniH tirya«bhAnatyiratnimAnaM sadaso vihitam /
navAratni tiryagiti niyatapramANavidhAnAt aratninaina vidhAnamanumIyate /
tathA havirdhAnasya tryaratni vistAraM navAratnayAyAmamityanumIyate /
tatkathaM padena tayor mAnaM labhyate ityucyate, catvAriMshadadhikAni paJNcadashAN^gulamiti vacanAt /
sadasaH pashcAt paJNcacatvAriMshadaN^gulaM ShoDasAdhikaM shatadvayaM sadohavirdhAnayormadhyaM paJNcacatvAriMshadaN^gulaM ShoDashAdhikaM shatadvayaM sadohavirdhAnayormadhyaM paJNcacatvAriMshatsaMcaraH /
havirdhAnasya ShoDashAdhikaM shathadvayam /
avashiShTamaShTAdashAN^gulam /
tasmAduttaravedisadohavirdhAnAnAM antarvedyasaMbhavAt vR^iddhiH kalpanIyA /
aratnervA hrAsaH kalpanIyaH /
tadubhayamacoditaM bhavati /
atoyena vedirmitA tenaiva teShAM mAnArthaM pahadrahaNaM sthitam /



karavindIyA vyAkhyA.

(aShTAviMshatyUnaMamahAvediH)

dvisaptatiH navashatAni ca padaparimitAni kShetrANi mahAvodeH, prakramamAne 'pyevam /
padagrahaNaM kimarthaM, ucyate--padagrahaNamahadvrahaNAmyAmetat j~nAyate--vedyAH padena mAne sadohavirdhAnayo rapi padena mAnaM nAratnibhiH, uttaravedish ca yugamAtrI na sarvato dashapadeti prakramamitAyAM vedyAmaratnivihitayoHsadohavirdhAnayoHsarvato dashapadAyA uttaravedeshvAsaMbhavAt padenaiva sadohavirdhAna. yorvimAna yugamAtrottaravediriti siddham /
saMkhyAnaprayojanam vodantR^itIye yajata ityAdiShu /



sundararAjIyA.

aShTAviMshatyUnaMamahAvediH.

padagrahaNaM prakramasyApyupalakShaNam /



kapardikShAShyam

dakShiNasmAd aMsAd dvAdashasu dakShiNasyAM shroNyAM nipAtayet | chedaM viparyasyottarata upadadhyAt | sA dIrghA caturashrA | tathA yuktAM saMcakShIta  || ˘p¡us_5.7b ||

___________________________________________________________



dakShiNasmAdaMsAdArabhya dvAdashasveva shroNyAM vipAdayet /
trINi padAni shroNideshe, viparyasyottarasminnaMse manasA sthApayet /
evaM kR^ite saptaviMshativistArA ShaTtriMshadAyatA dIrghacaturashrA bhavati /
tathAbhUtAM vediM saptaviMshatiM ShaTtriMshatyA guNite sati aShTAviMshatyUnapadasahasraM bhavati /



___________________________________________________________


saumikyA veditR^itIyadeshe yajeteti sautrAmaNyA veder vij~nAyate  || ˘p¡us_5.8a ||

___________________________________________________________



veditR^itIye yajeteti dArshikapAshalakayorashaMbhavAtsaumikaM labhyate /
ataHsaumikyA ityuktam /

prakramAsya dvikaraNI prakramasthAnIyA bhavati trikaraNyA vA  || ˘p¡us_5.8b ||

___________________________________________________________



tR^itIyakaraNI prakramasthAnA, sthAnAntAdvibhASheti chapratyayaH /
tR^itIyakaraNIM prakramaM kR^itvA ShaTtriMshikAyAmityAdinA viharet /
tR^itIyakaraNyA vA vakShyamANena vidhinA /



___________________________________________________________


aShTikA dashiketi tirya«mAnyau | dvAdashikA pR^iShThayA  || ˘p¡us_5.8c ||

___________________________________________________________



aShTikA purastAttirya«bhAnI /
dvAdashikA pR^iShThayA /
dvAdashasu ShaDupasamasyAparasmAdantAtpaJNcasu lakShaNaM caturShu lakShaNaM kR^itvA pR^iShThayAntayorantau niyamya paJNcakena dakShiNA pasArya shaN^kuM nihanyAt /
evamuttarataste shroNI /
viparyastayAMsau /
paJNcakena dakShiNApAyamya caturShu shaN^kuM nihanyAt /
evamuttaratastAvaMsau bhavataH /

trINi caturviMshAni padashatAni sautrAmaNikI vediH  || ˘p¡us_5.9 ||

___________________________________________________________



dakShiNasmAdaMsAdArabhya caturShvava dakShiNasyAM shroNyAM vipAtya sheShaM viparyasyetyAdi pUrvAvat /
dvAdashapadavistArA dvAdashapadAyAmA bhavati evaM saMcakShIta //

dvistAvA vedir bhavatIty ashvamedhe vij~nAyate  || ˘p¡us_5.10 ||

___________________________________________________________


kasya dvistAvA? saumikyAH prakR^itatvAtprakR^ititvAcca /

iti paJNcamaHkhaNDaH.

----------



karavindIyA vyAkhyA.

kShetratR^itIyagrahaNaM na pramANamiti tR^itIyagrahaNamiti kathaM saMkhyAyAta ityata Aha--

dakShiNasmAdaMsA--saMcakShIta.

vedyA dakShiNasmAdaMsAdArabhya dvAdashasu dakShiNasyAM shroNyAM lekhA nipAtayedrajjuM vA tAM nipAtya tabdahishchindyAt /
lekhAyA bahirbhUtaM chedaM viparyasya--viparyAsaM kR^itvA itarataH--itarasmAt pArshve sthApayedevaM saptaviMshativistArA ShaTtriMshadAyatA dIrghacaturashrA vedirbhavati, tathA yuktAM tathA bhUtAM gaNayet /
etena viShamacaturashrANAM saMkhyAnaprakAro veditavyaH /

vediprasaN^gAdvikArA ucyante--

(saumikyA vij~nAyate.)

sutrAmadaivatyA sautrAmaNI, tasyA veditR^itIye yajeta iti shrUyate /
vedyAstR^itIyo deshaH veditR^itIyadeshaH, sa kasyAH, saumikyAH, kimodanaM shAlInAM saktvADhakaparimitAnAmiti vat //


(prakrama--pR^iShThayA.)

prakramatR^itIyakaraNI vyAkhyAtA prakramAsthAnIyA bhavati /
"sthAnAntAdvibhAShA' ityAdinA svArthe chapratyayaH /
tathA ShaTtriMshatikAyAmityAdinA kaumikavadvimAnaM trikaraNI coktA, aShTikAdashike tirya«bhAnyA dvAdashikA pR^iShThayA tatpakShe aShTapramANA purastAta tiryak, dashapramANA pashcAttiryak, dvAdashAyAmaH dvAdashikAyAM ShaDupasamasya catusR^iShu paJNcasu lakShaNaM paJNcasu shroNyA catasR^iShvaMsau /
veditR^itIyatvaM kShetrata ityAha- (triNi caturviMshAni padashatAni sautrAmaNikI vodiH.)

caturviMshatyadhikAni trINi shatAni sautrAmaNikI vediH /
dakShiNasmAdaMsAdityAdi saumikavat /
prakramasya tR^itIyakaraNIti darshanAt, atrApi padaprakramau vikalpitau /
prakamashabdenopakramya padashabdenopasaMhArAdanyatrApyaShTAsu prakrameShvityAdiShu padenApi vimAnaM labhyata iti sUcitam /

ddhistAvA vedirbhavatItyashvamedhe vij~nAyate.)

prakR^itatvAt prakR^ititvAcca saumikyA eva dvistAvA--dviguNA vedirashvamedhe bhavati, pashugaNasaMbandhAdyUpAnAM codakaprAptarathAkShamAtrAntarAlatA pratyakShavihitadvistAvavacanAt bAdhyate /
ato 'trayathA saMbhavAntarAlA eva ekaviMshatiyUpAH /
tristAvAnnItvA tripadakramaH dvistAvA /
yUpaikAdashinI pakShe vedivivR^iddhirbhavatItyeva /



sundararAjIyA vyAkhyA.

saMkhyAnopAyamAha----

(dakShiNasmAdaMasaMcakShIta.)

dakShiNasmAdaMsAdArabhyAparAnte pR^iShThacAyA dakShiNato dvAdashasu rajjuM nipAtayet /
taddakShiNatashchedaM dIrghaM trikoNaM manasA viparyasya uttarapArshva upadadhayAt, sA ShaTtriMshitprAcikA saptaviMshativyAsA dIrghacaturashrA bhavati, tathAbhUtAM gaNayet /
saptaviMshatiShaTtriMshatoHsaMvarge kR^ite nava shatAni dvisaptatish ca bhavanti /

(saumikyA bhavati.)

prakramAgrahaNaM padasyApyupalakShaNam, evaM padashatAnIti pada grahaNaM prakramasyopalakShaNamiti sheShaH //


(trikaraNyA vA pR^iShThayA.)

dashAN^gulapadasya trikaraNI saptadashAN^gulayaH ekAdasha tilAsh ca aM? 7 ti 11 dvAdashA N^gulasya viMshatyaN^gulayaH saptaviMshatitirAsh ca aM 20 ti 27 paJNcadashAN^gulasya tilonaShaDviMshatiraN^gulayaH /
evaM prakramANAmapi draShTavyam //


(trINi sautrAmaNikIvediH.)

kAThakAgnInAmapyeShA /

dvistAvA vedirbhavatatyishvamedhe vij~nAyate

iti paJNcamaHkhaNDaH

prakramasya dvikaraNI prakamasthAnIyA bhavati  || ˘p¡us_6.1 ||

___________________________________________________________



dvikaraNyA pramANatR^itIyena vardhayedityAdinA vardhitena tadeva viharaNam /


___________________________________________________________


prakramo dvipadastripado vA | prakrame yAthAkAmI shabdArthasya vishayitvAt  || ˘p¡us_6.2a ||

___________________________________________________________



dvipadastriMshadaN^gulaH /
tripadaH paJNcacatvAriMshadaN^gulaH /
padaM paJNcadashAN^gulamiti vacanAd /
kAma icchA /
yathAkAma eva yAthAkAmI yathecchA tathA gR^ihNIyAt /
prakrame 'dhyardhaprakramo viprakR^iShTaprakrama iti naivamanvarthasaMj~nA /
padAdhikasya mAnArthasya vAcako yathA yaugikaH tathA dvipadaM tripadaM vA vakti, krAmatyaneneti kramaH /
prakR^iShTaH kramaH iti nirUDhaH, kalpanArthadravye vacanAtpadAdhikaM prakrama iti shabdArthasya vishayitvAt vishayitvaM kalpitArthAnAmapi vAcakatvAdanekavAcakatvaM /
shabdArthAnAM vishayitvaM yataH, kasya padAdayo grahItavyAH ityAha--



___________________________________________________________


yajamAnasyAdhvaryorvA | eSha hi ceShTAnAM kartA bhavati  || ˘p¡us_6.2b ||

___________________________________________________________



yajamAnasya padaM grAhyaM svAmitvAt /
adhvaryorvA--vAshabdaH pakShavyAvR^ittau /
na yajamAnasya /
adhvaryureva kutaH? eSha hi ceShTAnAM kartA bhavati /
ceShTayanta iti ceShTAH karmANi /
sa karmaNAM kartA yataH hishabdo hetau /
tasmAdadhvaryoreva na yajamAnasya /



karavindIyA vyAkhyA.

(prakramasya bhavati)

dvistAvAyAM vedyAM ashvamedhe prakraprasya dvikariNI prakramasthAne bhavati pramANadvikaraNyA viharet /



(prakramo vishayitvAt).

padaM paJNcadashAN^gulam. dvipadaM triMshadaN^gulam. tripadaM paJNca catvAriMshadaN^gulam, dvipade tripade ca prakramavyavahArAdubhayamiha grAhyam /
athavA prakramaH padavikShepavAcI, padAdayo 'tra mAna sAdhanabhUtA gR^ihyante /
ato na vikShepamAtreNa prayojanam /
kinatu tatmaMbandhinA kenaciddravyoNa, ato vikShepaphalabhUtasaMyogavibhAgAbhyAmupalakShitadeshAntarAlaparimitarajjvAdinA prayojanam, gacchan hi sarvo janaH ekaM padaM vikShipya nidadhAti, tatra nirvikAraM saMgacchana samaH puruShaH, sthitanidhIyamAnayoH padayorantarAlaM yathA padaparimitaM bhavati tathA gacchati, ato vikShiptena padena padadvayaM vyAbtamiti dvipadaH prakramaH, sthitamapi padaM tatsahakArIti tAbhyAM padatrayavyAptestripadash ca bhavati /
prakrame yAthAkAmIkAma icchA, tadanatikramo yathAkAmam, tasya bhAvaH yathAkAmyam, yAtAkAmyameva yAthAkAmI--yatheShTamityarthaH, vividhaM sheta iti vishaya, ubhayatra prayogo dR^ishyata ityarthaH /
nanu prakrameShu vaiShamyamapi dR^ishyate, yathA caturo viShNukramAm prAcaH krAmatyuttaramuttaraM jyAyAMsamiti /
nAyaM doSha, tasya vacanasyotta rottaraM jyAyastvavidhiparatvAt, prakrame gR^ihyamANe dvipadameva tripadameva vA gR^ihNIyAt, na mishrayedityarthaH, caturo viShNukamAnityatra vAcanikatvAt kramavaiShamyasya na kramavaiShamyAnuyogaH /
ato visheShitaprakamavidhau dvitripadaprakamayorevAnyataraM kR^ihNIyAnna mishrayedityarthaH /
padAdisUtre vakShyamANaH padavikalpanibandhanaH prakramayorapi vikalpo bhavatItyeva /



(yajamAnasya bhavati).

cajamAnAdhvaryU prasiddhau, hi shabdo hetau, ceShTanta iti ceShTAH, karmANi /
ayamarthaH padAdayo yajamAnasya grAhyAH svAmitvAt, kutaH, yAthAkAmirvAt, tasya adhvaryorvA /
vAshabdo vikalpArthaH /
yasmAdeSho 'dhvaryushveShTAnAM kartA bhavati tasmAdasya padAdayo grAhyAH ceShTAkartR^itvAt, yajamAnasya prAptayarthaM vacanamadhvaryostu bAdhakavAdhanArthamato vikalpaH /



sundararAjIyA vyAkhyA.

(prakramasya vishayitvAt).

shabdArthasya--shabdapravR^ittinimittasya vishayitvaM--anekavR^ittitvam /
idaM prakame yAthAkAmyaM shabdArthasya vishayitvAduktamityarthaH /
"dvipadaH prakamaH' iti bodhAyanaH /
"tripadaH prakramaH' iti kAtyAyanaH /
ubhayamapyAcAryasyAnumatamiti vij~nAyate /



(yajamAnasyadhvAryorvA).

padenAN^gulibhirvA prakamo grAhyaH svAmitvAt /
kAraNamAha--

(eSha hi bhavati)



kapardikShAShyam.

___________________________________________________________


rathamAtrI nirUDhapashubandhasya vedir bhavatIti vij~nAyate  || ˘p¡us_6.3a ||

___________________________________________________________


rathapramANA niparUDhapashubandhasya vedirbhavatIti shrutiH /



___________________________________________________________


tasya khalvAhU rathAkShamAtrI pashcAt tiryag IShayA prAcI | vipathayugena purastAt  || ˘p¡us_6.3b ||

___________________________________________________________



khalushabdo 'laN^kAre /
tatra tasminnarthe rathapramANavido rathakArA AhuH /
rathAkShamAtrI pashcAt tiryagIShayA prAcI, vipathayugena purastAt, rathAkShaNAtrI pashcAttirya«nAnI /
rathagrahaNaM shakaTanivR^icyartham /
IShAmAtrI pR^iShThayA /
vipathayugena--vyAptaH panthA yena yugena tadvipathayugam /
abyantaraM yugachidrayorantarAlam /
tatpramANaM purastAttirya«bhAnI /



___________________________________________________________


yAvatA vA bAhye chidre  || ˘p¡us_6.3c ||

___________________________________________________________



yAvatA pramANena yugasya bAhye chidre bhavataH tAvadvA purastAttirya«bhAnI vedeH /



karavindIyA vyAkhyA.

(rathamAtrI bAhye chide)

rathamAtrI--rathapramANA nirUDhapashubandhasya vediriti shrutiH /
shrutyuktamabhiyuktoktayA darshayati /

khalushabdo vAkyAlaN^kArArthaH /
tatrAhurabhiyuktAH--rathAkShamAtrI rathapramANA pashcAttiryaktirashvI IShayA saMmitA prAcI /
vyAptaH panthA yena sa vipathaH cAraNaratha ityarthaH /
vipathasya yugo vipathayugaH /
tena saMmitA purastAttirashvI /
athavA yAvatA vA bAhye chidre yAvatA pramANena gR^ihIte bAhye cchidre bhavataH tAvatI vA purastAttiryak /



sundararAjIyA vyAkhyA.

(rathamAtrI bAhye chidre.)

ityAhurAcAryAH--pashcAttirya«bhAnI rathAkShamAtrI, IShAmAtrI prAcI, vipathayugamAtrI purastAttirya«nAnI /
vigataH panthA yasmAdyugAt tadvipathayugam /
bAhyacchidrasahitaM ShaDashItyaN^gulaM yugam /
yAvatA vA bAhye cchidre bAhyacchidrayorantarAlamashI tyaN^gulam /



kapardibhAShyam

___________________________________________________________


tadekarajjvoktam | paJNcadashikenaivApAyamyArdhAkSheNArdhayugena shroNyaMsAn nirharet  || ˘p¡us_6.4 ||

___________________________________________________________



tadekarajjuriti kiM saumikI gR^ihyate AhosvitprathamasaumikI gR^ihyate? paJNcadashikeneti darshanAt, tatra hi paJNcadashike lakShaNam, netaratra /
IShAmAtrI IShAM ShaTtriMshaddhA vibhajya ekaM bhAgaM prakramastAnIyaM kR^itvA saumikavatpaJNcadashikenAmAyamya ardhAkSheNa shroNa shroNIM minuyAt /
ardhayugenAsau minuyAditi kecit /
apare punaH prathamAmekarajjuM gR^ihNanti /
yadi saumikI gR^ihyate adR^iShTakalpanA prAptoti kathaM paJNcadashikeneti cet, lakShaNayA ShaTtriMshikAyAmaM yatpaJNcadashakaM tadapi ShaDbhAgonameva /
tasmAtpaJNcadashikeneti ShaDbhAgonAM lakShayituM na shakyate /
tenAdR^iShTakalpanAbhavati /
nanvanyatrApi lakShaNA? sA tu laukikI, kiM ca sAdhAraNatvAcca saivaikA rajjuHsAdhAraNI /
tasmAcca saiva grAhyA /
evamuttaratrApi yojanIyam /
ardhakShe ardhayuge ca lakShaNaM kR^itvA ShaDbhAgonenApAyamya ardhAkShe shroNI /
ardhayuge tvaMsau /



karavindIyA vyAkhyA.

(tadekarajjvA viharet)

etAdviharaNamekarajjuviharaNena vyAkhyAtam /
ekarajjuriti dvitripaJNcashaN^karajjvAdInAM grahaNaM, itarathA uttarayorvidhAnasyAdR^iShTArthatvakalpanAprasaN^gaditi saumikyAM vyAkhyAtam /
tathA paJNcadashikeneti ShaDbhAgone kR^italakShamasya grahaNam /
tacca niraJNcanamAtrapradarshanam /
itarathA adR^iShTArthatvaprasaN^gAditi tatrrevoktam, tatrAnekarajjubhirihApi viharaNasuktam, tadihApyavirodhAt gR^ihyata eva /
IShAmAtrA ShaTtriMshadbhAgaM prakramaM kR^itvA tenaiva viharet /



sundararAjIyA vyAkhyA.

(tadekarajjvA viharet)

"ShaTtriMshikAyAmaShTAdashopasamasya' ityAdinA ekarajjvA tanmAnamuktam /
IShAyAHShaTtriMsho bhAgaH paJNcAN^gulamardhAShTamatilAsh ca prakramasthAne draShTavyam /
yadvA ekarajjushabdena yAvadAyAmamiti viharaNamabhipretam /
atra pakShe paJNcadashikeneti lakShaNayA ShaDbhAgonatR^itIyamevocyate /
some tatpaJNcadashaprakramamabhUditi /
evamuttaratrApi bAhyacchidrAntarAlapakShe tadardhenAMsanirharaNam /



kapardibhAShyam

___________________________________________________________


athApyudAharanti  || ˘p¡us_6.5a ||

___________________________________________________________


athashabdaHsamuccaye /
evaM codAharanti rathapramANapido rathakArAH--



___________________________________________________________


aShTAshItishatamIShA tiryag akShashcatuHshatam | ShaDashItiyugaM cAsya rathashcAraNa ucyate iti rathaparimANam  || ˘p¡us_6.5b ||

___________________________________________________________


evaM rathaparimANaM sarvato mAnamudAharanti--bruvate /
sAmarthyasiddheshvAN^gulirgR^ihyate /
ratheShApramANaM aShTAshItyuttaramaN^gulashatam /
tiryakchabdaH pUraNArthaH /
akShapramANaM caturadhikaM shatam /
yugasya pramANaM ShaDasItiH /
evaMlakShaNo yo rathaHsa cAraNaH, caratyaneneti cAraNaH /
caraNa eva cAraNaH /
cAraNagrahaNaM krIDAdirathanivR^icyartham /
athavA asyashabdasya sthAne yasyashabdamadhyAhR^itya yojanIyam /
varNavyatyAsena vA /



___________________________________________________________


aratnibhir vA caturbhiH pashcAt ShaDbhiH prAcI tribhiH purastAt | tad ekarajjvoktaM paJNcadashikenaivApAyamya dvAbhyAm adhyardheneti shroNyaMsAn nirharet  || ˘p¡us_6.6 ||

___________________________________________________________



aratnibhirvA mAtavyamiti sheShaH /
caturbhiH pashcAttirya«bhAnI /
ShaDbhiH prAcI pR^iShThayA /
tribhiH purastAttirya«bhAnI /
tadekarajjvoktamityAdi--gatametat /



___________________________________________________________


yajamAnamAtrI catuHsraktir bhavatIti paitR^ikyA veder vij~nAyate, tadekarajjvoktaM paJNcadashikenaivApAyamyArdhena tataH shroNyaMsAn nirharet  || ˘p¡us_6.7 ||

___________________________________________________________



paitR^ikyA vedeH shrutiH--yathA dikShu sraktayo bhavanti tathA mAtavyA /
tadekarajjveti gatArtham /



karavindIyA vyAkhyA.

vedArthAvagamasya bahuvidyAntarAshrayatvAt /
takShashAstre gArgyA gastyAdibhiraN^gulisaMkhyayoktaM rathaparimANa shlokamudA harati--



(athApyu pramANam)

athApishabdau samuccaye, udAharanti munayaH, aShTashItish ca shataM cAShTAshItishataM, catvAri ca shataM ca catuHshatam, ShaTcAshItish ca ShaDashIti, AyodhanapuShyajaitracAraNAdibhedena rathasyAnekavidhatAmupanyasta tairuktaM aShTAshItishatamityAdi, asyArthaH--asya bahuvidhasya madhye yasya IShA aShTAshItishatamaN^gulayaH, caturadhikaM shatamakShaH, yugaM ca ShaDashItiH, evaMvidho rathashvAraNa ucyata iti /
evaM rathaparimANamudAharanti munayaH /



nanu akShasya tirya«bhAnItvamuktam, yugeShayoH kA prAcI kA tirashvIti na j~nAyate /
ucyate--akShasya tiryaktvavidhAnAdevayugeShayorapi yA drAghIyasI sA prAcI, yA hrasIyasI sA tirashvIti sAmarthyAdIShA prAcIti gamyata iti manyante /
chidrAntarAlapakShe ShoDashAN^gulahInA purastAttirashvI /

(aratnibhirvApurastAt) gatam /

(tadekarajjvA nirharet)

idamapi gatam /
atrAratnAvAratnidvaye ca lakShaNam /

(yajamAnamAtrI nirharet)

pitR^iNAmiyaM vediH--paitR^ikI mahApitR^iyaj~navediH /
codakaprApte 'pi yajamAnamAtre punarvacanaM vistArasyApi tathAtvA(ya)t /
(AyAmaH) pratidishaM sraktayaH mahAdikShukoNAH "sarvA hyanudishaH' iti darshanAt, atra prayogaH--agreNAnvAhAryapacanaM kiJNcidantaHsaJNcaramavashiShaya tasya purastAdyajamAnamAtraM dvikaramyA caturashraM saMpAdya tasya karaNImadhyeShu yathA sraktayo bhaveyuH tathA paJNcadashikenetyAdinA vihR^ityArdhena tataH tasya yajamAnamAtrasyArdhena shroNyaMsAnnirharettannimitto nirhrAso vivR^iddhirvetyuktayornirhrAsaH, mahAvedyAM padaJNcashikenaivApAyamya ardhayajamAnamAtre shaN^kuM nihanyAt dakShiNAprAcI vediH //


sundararAjIyA vyAkhyA.

(athApyudAharanti rathaparimANam)

aN^gulayaHsaMkhyeyAH /
aN^gulishvordhvabAhoH puruShasya viMshatishatatamo bhAga iti vakShyate /
"paJNcAratniH puruShaH, catuviMshatya N^gulayo 'ratniH

iti /
sA ca catustriMshatattiletyAcakShate /
yathoktaM bodhAyanena--

""aN^gulipramANaM caturdashANavaH catustriMshattilAH pR^ithusAMshliShTA ityaparam'' iti caturadhikaM shataM catuHshataM yugamiti vipathayugamucyate prastutatvAt /
anyattu yugaM shatAN^gulamiti takShashAstravidaH /
ShaNNavatyaN^gulamityAcAryapAdIyAH /
yathA'huH-- caturhasto dhanirdanDo dhanurdhanvantaraM yugam /

iti /
"hastashcaturviMshatiraN^gulayaH' iti ca /

(aratnibhirvA purastAt)

pashubandhavedItyeke /

(tadekara nirharet)

dvAbhyAM shroNI /
adhyardhenAMsau /

(yajamAnamAtrI vij~nAyate)

paJNcAratniH /

(tadekara nirharet)

tata iti ShaShThayantAttasil /
dakShiNAprAcI pR^iShThayA /
mahAdikShu shroNyaMsAH /
atra laghUpAyamAha kAtyAyanaH--

"paitR^ikyAM dvipuruShaM caturashraM kR^itvA karaNImadhyeShu shaN^kavaHsasamAdhiH' iti /
tatra prakAraH--puruShamAtradvikaraNyA dashatilonayA saptatishatAN^gulayA samacaturashraM kR^itvA karaNInAM madhyeShu shaN^kUnnihatya dashAratnayo rajjvoH pAshAna pUrvAparayoH pratimucya tayormadhye dakShiNottarayorniyamya vahiHspandamapacchindyAt /
etaM caturaratnamipi kecidicchanti /
tatra AjyaM puroDAshA AsAdayituM na shakyante /



kapardibhAshaShyam.

___________________________________________________________


dashapadottarA vedir bhavatIti some vij~nAyate | tad ekarajjvoktaM paJNcadashikenaivApAyamyArdhena tataH shroNyaMsAn nirharet  || ˘p¡us_6.8 ||

___________________________________________________________



padagrahaNaM pradarshanArtham /
prakamamitAyAM mahAnedyAM dashapadottaravediH sarvato dashapadA "pramANena pramANaM vidhIyata' iti vacanAt /
kShetrato vA dashapatA /
tadA ekapadavistAraM tripadAyAmaM dIrghacaturashraM kR^itvA tasyAkShNayA rajjuM gR^ihItvA caturashraM kuryAt /
prakrame 'pyekaprakramavistAraM triprakramAyAmaM caturashraM vihR^itya tasyAkShNayA rajjuM gR^ihItvA caturashraM kuryAt /
tadekarajjvoktaM--ardhena tataH--tasyetyarthaH ShaShThayarthe tasil /



___________________________________________________________


tAM yugena yajamAnasya vA padair vimAya shamyayA parimimIte  || ˘p¡us_6.9 ||

___________________________________________________________



yugenoktapamANena yajamAnasya vA padaiH /
yajamAnagrahaNAdadhvaryorna labhyate /
yajamAnagrahaNaM pradarshanArthamiti kecit /
tasmAdeva vacanAduttaravediryugamAtrI labhyate /
some padamAnAyAM mahAvedyAM uttaravediM yugena vA padairvA vimAya shaulbena mAnena pashcAcchamyayA mAnamadR^iShTArthaM kartavyam /
shamyayA parimimIta ityetadvacanamadR^iShTArthaM na pramANavidhiH iyuktaM bhavati /



karavindIyA vyAkhyA.

(dashapadotta vij~nAyate)

mahAvedyAM prathamanihatAcchaN^koH purastAtpaJNcaviMshatiShu shaN^kuM nihatya tatpurastAdR^ishasu shaN^kuM nihatya paJNcadashikenetyAdinA viharet //


(tadekara nirharet)

tator'dhena paJNcapadenetyarthaH /
"sarvato dashapadA' iti shatapathabrAhnaNe shrUyate "pramANena pramANaM vidhIyate shaturashramiti tadanirUpakShe trato dashapada

iti kAtyAyanaH /
asmin pakShe padavistAraM tripadAyAmaM dIrghacaturashraM vihR^itya tasyAkShNayArajjupramANottaravediH /
asminnapi pakShe etatkaraNyardhena shroNyaMsAnAM viharaNam //


(tAM yugena parimimIte )

tAmuttaravediM yugapramANena /
taduktaM "ShaDashItiryugam' iti /
tena vA yajamAnasya vA padairvimAya pashcAdadR^iShTArthaM shamyayA sarvato mimIte /
shamyApramANaM coktaM sUtrAntare "ShaTtriMshacchamyA' iti pashubandhe tvanyasyAbhAvAt parimANArthameva shamyAvidhAnam /
mAtraivAsyai seti liN^gAcca /
asmAdeva vacanAt saumikyuttaravediryugamAyapi labhyate (bhavati) //


sundararAjIyA vyAkhyA.

(dashapadottara nirharet)

dashapadA--sarvataH /
kShetrataHshatapadA /

(tAM yugena parimimIte)

yugamapi dashapadAyA eva mAnasAdhanaM veNuvat /
kecit tasyatantraM pramANamAhuH, atadvicAraNIyaM sUribhiH /
yajamAnagrahaNaM adhvaryunivR^icyartham /
shamyayA parimANamadR^iShTArtham /



kapardikShAShyam.

___________________________________________________________


pade yuge 'ratnAv iyati shamyAyAM ca mAnArtheShu yathAkAmI shabdArthasya vishayitvAt  || ˘p¡us_6.10 ||

___________________________________________________________



padAdiShu mAnArtheShu yathAkAmI--yathecchA tathA gR^ihNIyAt /
kimuktaM bhavati //


aNavashcaturdasha tilaH

catustriMshattilAH aN^gulaH (pR^ithutaHsaMspR^iShTA ityaparam)

dvAdashAN^gulAH prAdeshaH

trayodashAN^gulaH vitastiH

paJNcadashAN^gulaM padam

caturviMshatyaN^gulayaH aratniH

dvAtriMshadaN^gulayaH jAnuH

ShaTtriMshadaN^gulA shamyA

ShaDashItyaN^gulaM yugam

catuHshataM akShaH

viMshatyuttaraM shataM puruShaH

ityevamAdishulbAntaroktalakShaNamAnArtheShu pramANAvayavA gR^ihyeran /
lakShaNe vargeNa vimAya tatra yathAkAmI shabdArthasya vishayitvAt /
paJNcadashAN^gulaM padamapi bhavati /
yajamAnapadamapi /
tatrAnyataradgrAhyamityAdhAne /
iyaddvAdashavikrAmA iti /
tatra svasaMvittiM aparasaMvittiM lokaprasiddhiM shAstraprasiddhiM vA gR^ihNIyAdityarthaH /


___________________________________________________________


vimitAyAM purastAt pArshvamAnyA upasaMharet | shrutisAmarthyAt  || ˘p¡us_6.11 ||

___________________________________________________________



evaM caturashre ApAdite pArshvamAnyA purastAdu pasaMharet, shrutisAmarthyAt--""catuHshikhaNDe yuvatI kanIne'' iti yuvatisAdR^ishyAnuvAdaH sAmarthyam //


iti ShaShThaHkhaNDaH.

--------



karavindIyA vyAkhyA.

(pade yuge vishayitvAt)

pade yuge 'ratnAviyati prAdeshe prakrame shamyAyAM ceti hiraNyakoshishulbe bodhAyanIyashulbe ca /
athAN^gulIpramANaM caturdashANavaH catustriMshattilAH pR^ithusaMshliShTA ityaparam /
dashAN^gulaM kShudrapadam /
dvAdasha prAdeshaH /
pR^ithottarayuge trayodashike prakrAme ca (paJNca) dasha /
aShTAshItishatamIShA /
ShaDashItiryugam /
dvAtriMshajjAnuH ShaTtriMshacchamyA, bAhurddvipadaH prakAmaH, dvau prAdeshAvaratniriti /
tathA paJNcA ratniH puruShashcaturaratnirvA yAma iti ca /
tatraiva iyatyagre juhoti, iyatyagre harati, iyantaM gR^ihNAti, iyantaM karoti, iyadbhavatItyAdi brAhnaNavyAkhyAnAvasara evAcAryeNa jAnudaghnAdibhiH parimANairvyAkhyAtaH /
tatra padAdiShu mAnasAdhanavayA nirdiShTeShu yAthAkAmI syAdyathecchA tathA kuryAdityarthaH /
shabdArthasya vishayitvAditi gatam /
ayamarthaH--padAdiShu yajamAnasyAdhvaryorvAvayavabhUtAN^gulyA parikalpitAni aNutilaparikalpitAN^gulyA parikalpi tAni vA padAdIni gR^ihnIyAt /
padAdishabdArthasyobhayatrApi prayuktatvAditi /
aNavo dhAnyavisheShAH /
(AcAryeNaiva nirUDhapashau ratha parimANaj~nAnArthaM takShashAstroktAdaShTAshItishatamityudAharaNAt, shyenepaJNcAratniH puruSha ityAdeH klptishabdena pramANavidAM samayAnukathanAnna shAstrAntaraparigR^ihItAN^gulipadAdiparigrahAnuyogaH /
dvipadastripado veti prakramaprastAve yajamAnasyAdhvaryorveti vacanAnna kevalamavayavAdivimitAN^guliparicchinnapadAdigrahraNam) //


prAsAN^gukaM parisamApya prastutasheShaM brUte--

(vimitA sAmarththAt)

vyAkhyAtametaddArshikyAm /
iha tu shrutisAmarthyAt "catuHshikhaNDe yuvatI kanIne' idyasyAH shruterahIyasIM purastAdityeka ityupasaMhArAcca vikalpaH karmopadesha uktaH //


ShaShTha.khaNDaH.

--------



sundararAjIyA vyAkhyA.

(padayuge vishayatvAt)

padacAturvidhyamuktam /
yugatrauvidhyaM ca ShaDashItiShaNNavatishatAN^gulaiH /
aratnirdvividhaH--caturviMshatyaN^gulo hastash ceti /
iyAniti prAdesho 'bhipretaH /
sa ca dvividhaH--dvAdashAN^gulaH prasArite aN^guShThapredashinyAviti /
shamyA trividhA--"catvAro 'ShTadvAtriMshadaN^gulA shamyA, iti kAtyAyanaH /
"ShaTtriMshacchamyA' iti hodhAyanaH, laukikI tR^itIyA /
eShu mAneShu yAthA kAmyaM bhavati, shabdArthasyAnekatra vR^ittaiH /

(vimitAyAMasAmarthyAt)

aMhIyasI purastAditi asya vaikalpikatvaM prAgevoktam //


ShaShTha.khaNDuH

kapardibhAShyam.

navAratni tiryak saptaviMshatir udag Ayatam iti sadaso vij~nAyate  || ˘p¡us_7.1 ||

___________________________________________________________


___________________________________________________________


aShThAdashetyekeShAM  || ˘p¡us_7.2 ||

___________________________________________________________


___________________________________________________________


tadekarajjvoktaM paJNcadashikenaivApAyamyArdhapaJNcamaiH shroNyaMsAn nirharet  || ˘p¡us_7.3 ||

___________________________________________________________



navAratniH prAcI tirya«bhAnI, saptaviMshatirudIcI pArshvamAnI /
evaM mantavyamiti sadasaHshrutiH /
padena prakrameNa vA mAtavyam /
karaNamuktam /
prathamanihatAcchaN^kordakShiNataH prakrame shaN^kuM nihatya tasmin pAshaM pratimucya tasya purastAdardhAShTame pR^iShThayAyAM dakShimataH prakmashaN^guH /
tatsadaso madhyamaudumbarIsthAnam /
prathamanihatAcchaN^koH pR^iShTayAyAmeva purastAdardhAShTame shaN^kuM nihatya tasmin pAshaM pratimucyoparyupari shaN^kumudagapasAryArdhacaturdashe navasu vA shaN^kuM nihanyAt /
pR^iShThayAyAM yaHshaN^kuH tasmin pratimucyoparyuparyaudumbarIsthAnIyaM dakShiNApasAryArdhapaJNcadashe dashasu vA shaN^kuM nihanyAt /
sadasa AyAmaH /
taHsinnAyAme tadardhamabhyasya yathAsUtraM virahet /
saptaviMshatAvardhacaturdashamabhyasya dakShiNasmAdaMsAdekAdashasu padeShu nihaJNjanamardhapaJNcame lakShaNaM shroNyaM sAdardhamaShTAdashasu vA nava prakShipyArdhAShTame niraJNjanamardhapaJNcamalakShaNaM shroNyaMsArdhamAyAmayorantau niyamya niraJNjanam /
tena pashcAdapasAryArdhapaJNcame shaN^kuH /
purastAdapasAryArdhapaJNcame shaN^kuH /
te shroNI /
sadasaH viparyasyAMsau /
prAgvaMshamAnaM havirthAnam /
AgnIdhramAnaM cAnenAcAryeNa noktam. ataHshulbAntaroktaM grAhyaM vaikR^itatvAt /
sadasaH purastAttiShu prakrameShu dashaprakramavistAraM dvAdashAyAmaM havirdhAnaM minuyAt /
ekarajjvA paJNcashaN^kunA trishaN^kunA vA havirdhAnasya pAshvAtyamadhyamashaN^kau pAshaM pratimucyodagapasArya dvAdashaprakame shaN^kuH /
tadAgrIdhrAyatanam /
tayA rajjvA dakShiNApasArya dvAdashasu mArjAlIyam /
pR^iShThayAyAM sadasaH paurastyashaN^kau pAshaM pratimucyodagapasArya pAdonaikAdashasu shaN^kuM nihatya tasmAccottarataH ShaTsu shaN^kuH /
tAbhyAM ca purastAt ShaTsu prakameShu shaN^kuM nihanyAt /
evaM paJNcashaN^kunA vA samacaturashraM minuyAt /
aShTaprakamavistAraM dvAdashAyAmaM prAgvaMshaM minuyAt /
dvAdashavistAraM ShoDashAyAmamityanye /

karanindIyA yAkhyA.

(navAra ekeShAM)

tirya«nAnA navAratniH prAgbhavati udaksaptaviMshatirAyataM /
aShTAdashAyatamityekeShAM shAkhinAm /

(tadeka nirharet)

padavimitAyAM vedyAM sadohavirdhAnayorapi padenaiva mAnamityuktaM, prakramamAne tvaratnivimAnameva, havirdhAnasyAparimitaM vati karmopadesha uktaH, aparimitaM saptaviMshateH paraM sadovimAnamucyate, mahAvedeH pashcAttirashvayAH pR^iShThayAyA dakShiNato dashapadeShvArabhya yAvatpurastAt tirashvayAH tAvatIM leshAmAlikhet, rajjuM vA pAtayet, evaM pR^iShTayAyA uttarato 'pi aShTAsu padeShu pashcimAntAdArabhya tayoreva lekhayoH pUrvapashcimeShu dakShiNata Arabhya yAvaduttaraM udIcIM leshAmAlikhet, sA sadasaH pR^iShThayA bhavati /
aShTAdashikAyAM navopasamasyArdhapaJNcameShvardhAShTameShu lakShaNaM kR^itvA pR^iShThyAntayorityAdinA vihR^ityArdhapaJNcameShu shaN^kuM nnihanyAttatsado bhavati //
havirdhAnAgnIdhraprAgvaMshapramANAnIhAcAryeNAnupadiShTAnyapi shulbAntaropadiShTAni grAhyANi /
havirdhAnaM dashAyAmaM, dashavi stAramAgnIdhra, ShaDAyAmavistAramardhamantarvedyardhaM bahirvedirbhavati /
prAgvaMshaHShoDashAyAmo dvAdashavistAraH /
dvAdashAyAmo navavistAro vA /
prathamanihatAt shaN^koH purastAtpaJNcadashasu shabhkuH, tatpurastAt navAyAmavistAraM havirdhAnaM dashapadaM vA taddvishaN^kuprabhutInAmanyatame na kuryAt //


sundahahAjIyA vyAkhyA.

(navAra ekeShAM)

udagAyatamityeva /
navAratnireva prAcI /
tatra viMshaticatuviMshatyaN^gulaprakrameNa aShTAshAratniH /
uttareShu kratuShu saptaviMshatya rAtniH /
deshastu prayogakalpa evoktaH, "aparasmAdve dyaMsAt' ityAdinA /

(tadeka nirharet)

udIcI--pR^iShThyA /

kapardikShAShyAm.

___________________________________________________________


prAdeshamukhAH prAdeshAntarAlA bhavantIty uparavANAM vij~nAyate | aratnimAtraM caturashraM vihR^itya sraktiShu shaN^kUn nihatyArdhaprAdeshena taM taM parilikhec chrutisAmarthyAt  || ˘p¡us_7.4 ||

___________________________________________________________



uparavamAnamapi nigadavyAkhyAtam /
aratnIti gatArtham /

karavindIyA vyAkhyA.

(pradesha vij~nAyate)

abhiShavakAle grAvabhireShAmupari ra(ya)vanta ityuparavAH /
uparAH--grAvavisheShAH, tena tadvanta iti vA uparavA avaTavisheShAH /

(aratni marthyAt)

dakShiNasya havirdhAnasya dakShimasyAM shroNyAM dvishaN^kvAdInAmanyatamenAratnipramANaM caturashraM vihR^itya koNeShu shaN^kUn nihatyArdhaprAdeshena karkaTena rajjvA vA tAn shaN^kUn parito likhet /
evaM prAdeshamukhA anyonyataH prAdeshAntarAlA bhavanti /
eShA shrutirevamarthavatI bhavati /
padamAnena vediH //


atha devayajanadeshavimAnabhAgA ucyante--padamAne eka paJNcAshat prAcIM triMshattirashvIM devayajamAnayogyAM bhUmiM kR^itvA tanmadhye tadAyAmAM devayajanayogyAM bhUmiM kR^itvA ntamadhye tadAyAmAM prAcIM lekhAmAlikhya rajjuM prasArya tadantayoH shaN^kuM nikhAya prAgvaMshaprabhR^iti tadanurUpaM tatkratukAle kuryAt, pashcAdante prAgvaMshaM ShoDashAyAmaM dvAdashavistAraM dvAdashAyAmaM navavistAraM vA nirmAya tasya lAlATikAtrrIn prAca ityAdi tattraiva tacchaN^korArabhya tripadA vahirvedistadante shaN^kuH, tatastatpurastAt ShaTtriMshanmahAvediH prAcI, triMshatpashcAt tirashvI, caturviMshatiH purastAt tirashvI, evaM mahAvediM vimAya pashcimAnte tripadaHsaJNcaraH, tatpurastAtprAktvena navapadamudaktvenAShTAdashapadaM sadaH, dakShiNottaramaShTAdashAyAmaM tanmadhye pR^iShThyAyA dakShiNataH padamAtre bhavati /
tadoduMbarIsthAnaM, sadasaH pUrvArdhe purastAdardhaM padamAtraM saMcaramavashiShya tatpashcAtpR^iShThyAyAM hotrIyamityAdayo dhiShNyA aratnimAtrAH pishIlamAtrA vA /
teShAM ca tasya tasyottarataH visAMsthita saMcaraH sadasaH purastAt tripadaHsaMcaraH /
tatpurastAt navAyAmavistAraM havirdhAnaM, tryaratnivistAraM navAyAmamiti madhyamaM madhyame chatiShi tUShNImitare chadiShI iti darshanAt /
"dashAyAmavistAraM havirdhAnam' iti bodhAyanaH /
yUpAvaTIyAcchaN^koH pashcAtpadamAtraHsaMcaraH /
tatpashcAdyugamAtrottaravodiH /
uttaravedihavirdhAnayorantarAlamantarvediH /
pR^iShThyAyA dakShiNato dakShiNahavirdhAnaM, uttarata uttaraM havirdhAnaM, dakShiNahavirdhAnasya dakShiNashroNyAmuparavAH, havirdhAnasya pashcAd AgnIdhrasya (dAgnIdhrIyashva) bAhusamaM pR^iShThyAyA dakShiNato dvAdashasu pArjA lIyaH /
tathaiva tasyA evodak dvAdashasvAgnIdhrIyaH, sarvadhiShNiyAH pishIlamAtrAH sadasoM'sAdut tarataH pAdonatripade padonanavapade cashaN^kUH /
AgnIdhramaNTapasya te shroNI /
havirdhAnapashcimAntAdArabhya prAkrripadeShu pR^iShTyAyA uttarataH /
pAdonaikAdashasu pAdonasaptadashasu shaN^kU, tAvAgnIdhrapaNTapasyAMsau /
ShaDviMshikAyAH pashcAt pR^iShThyAyAH pUrvAnte ardhamantarvedyardhaM bahirvediH /
tripadaviShkambhastripadaparINAho yUpAvaTa iti bodhAyanaH /
uttarasmAdvedyaMsAdudakprakrame cAtvAla uttaravedisaMmitaH, cAtvAlamadhyo vedyaMsatulyaH /
ardhAnte cAtvAlAt pashcAddAdashasu tadbahirvedyutkaraH, vedyaN^kotkarayormadhye uttarataH ShoDashasu shAmitradhiShNyaH /
etatpadamAne /
prakramamAne tu sadohavirdhAnayoraratnimAnamagneruttaravedervA pashcAtrrIn pratIcaH prakramAnatItya tiryagahavirdhAnaM navAratnItyAdi yAvat /
saMbhavA yAmIvastAraM sadaH /
dhiShNyAH pishIlamAtrAH prakrameNaiva sarvamAnaM ShaTtriMshadaN^gulaparimitA uttaravedistu dashapadA yugamAtrI vA tatsthAne 'gnirvA /
anyatsarvaM prakramakR^itaM /
yUpaikAdashinIpekSha dasharathAkShAmekAdasho (parAM)paravAM rajjuM mItvA tasyAshcaturviMshena bhAgena vediMvimimIte /
prakramasthAnIyA bhavatItyukta (ktaM prAcyekAdashinyAM) mekAdashinyAM /
prAcyekAdashinIpakShe ardhaShaShThAni padAnyaMsau yUpArdhaM bedeH purastAt padArthamAtramaMsamapacchidya tatpurastAt prAJNcaM nidadhyAditi bodhAyanaH /
ekAdashaikAdIshanIpakShe ardhaShaShThAni padAnyaMsAvapacchidya tAnyekAdashadhA vibhajya pR^iShThyAntA pR^iShThyAdA dArabhya ekaM vibhAgaM madhye prAJNcannidadhyAt /
taddakShiNataH uttaratash ca paJNcapaJNca vibhAgAn prAJNco nidadhyAt /
agnivivR^iddhau mahAvedi vivR^iddhiH, prAgvaMshaHprAcI cAntarAlabahutve vivardhate /
alamati vistareNa //


sundararAjIyA.

(prAdesha sAmarthyAt)

deshastu darshita eva "dakShiNasya havirdhAnasya' ityA dinA /
sarvatrApi prakramairmAne aparasmAdvedyAntAt prakramatrayamavashiShya navArAtni sadaH /
uttaravedeH pashcAtprakramatrayamavashiShya navArAtni havirdhAnam /
padamAne tUktapramANAnAM sadohavirdhAnottaravedInAmasaMbhavAdvedyanuguNo nirdvAsaH kartavyaH /
cAtvAlastu shamyAmAtra eva sarvatrApi /
"shamyAmAtrashvAtvAlaH' iti bodhAyanavacanAt /
atra shlokAH----

mIyate saumikI vediH prakramairdvidashAN^gulaiH /

Adau triShu nava dvyekacandradvisharabhUdviShu // .1 //


ekaikadvisharaikeShu shaN^kavo dasha paJNca ca /

ShaTtriMshikA mAnarajjuH tasyA dvyAShTasu lakShaNam // .2 //


vimAne pAshayormadhye prakramA dvAdasha smR^itAH /

shroNI paJNcamoneShu sado 'nantaraturyayoH // .3 //


tatkoNaH paJNcamoneShu bhAskareShu dashasvapi /

tR^itIye dvyantarA dhiShNyAsteShAM prAdeshato bhramaH // .4 //


rudreShu saptadashasu shaN^kU pAdoniteShviha /

AgnIdhraM tatpaJNcame tu dhiShNyau dvAdashasu smR^itau // .5 //


ShaShThe syAtpaJNcake dhAnaM paJNcAshaddvitayAnvite /

saptame prAgvadAgnIdhraM navame manuShUtkaraH // .6 //


ekAdashe havirdhAnaM pAshau vyAtyasya pUrvavat /

ShoDashasvardhahIneShu shAmitro dvAdashe bhavet // .7 //


uttarArdhAttR^itIye tu trayodashacaturdashe /

shaN^koruttaravediHsyAddvayoHsArdhamupAntyayoH // .8 //


antime dvAdashasvaMsau cAtvAlalo 'sAdudakkrame /

puraH pashcAtsadodhAnAcyajetprakrama paJNcakam // .9 //


dakShiNe tu havirdhAne pashcActrIn prakramAMstyajet /

pArshvadvayo prakramau dvau aN^guladvayasaMyutau // .10 //


aratnimAtraM madhye coparavANAM tu lakShaNam /

evameva vimAMna syAtpadairapi caturvidhaiH // .11 //


padaM paJNcamasaMyuktaM dhiShNyaviShkambha iShyate /

shamyAmAtrastu cAtvAlo vyAktaM bodhAyano 'bravIt /

anyathAgnau virodhaHsyAt mAnaM cAnyanna vidyate // .11 //


kapardikShAShyam.

tatpramANaM gArhapatyaciteH /

karaNaM vyAyAmasya tR^itIyAyAmaM saptamavyAsaM kArayet  || ˘p¡us_7.7 ||

___________________________________________________________



caturashrAyAM karaNamucyate /
vyAyAmatR^itIyA pArshvamAnI vyAyAmasaptamI tirya«nAnI /
evaM karaNaM kArayet /
kuryAditi vaktavye kArayediti vacanAdanyaistakShAdibhiH pravINairnAdhvaryuNetyavagamyate /
kiyante 'neneShTakA iti karaNaM dArumayam /

tA ekaviMshatir bhavanti  || ˘p¡us_7.8 ||

___________________________________________________________



tena karaNena kR^itA iShTakAH ekaviMshatiH tasyAM gArhapatyacitau bhavantIti sheShaH /

karavindIyA vyAkhyA.

(vyAyAma vij~nAyate)

vyAyAmashcaturarAtniH //


(caturashre  ekeShAM)

ekeShAM shAkhinAmubhayamapi bhavati /

(karaNaMarbhavanti)

kriyante 'neneShTakA iti karaNam, tacca dArumayaM lohamayaM vA /
dvAtriMshadaN^gula AyAmaH, trayodashAN^gulayashcaturviMshatitilAsh ca vyAsaH /
utsedhash ca jAnoH paJNcamabhAgaH /
ekaviMshatiriti shaN^khyAsapattiM brUte /
paJNcacitIkamityAdiShu samudAyasaMkhyAvagatyarthaM //


sundararAjIyA vyAkhyA.

athAgnicityAyAM----

(vyAyAma bij~nAyate)

caturarAtnirvyAyAmaH /

(catura keShAM)

tatra caturashrAyAm--

(karaNaMarbhavanti)

prAgAyAmAH prathame prastAre 'parasminn udagAyAmAH  || ˘p¡us_7.9 ||

___________________________________________________________



prAgAyAmAH--prAgAyatAH prathame prastAre /
udagAyAmAH--udagAyatAH dvitIye prastAre /
evasupahite bhedo na bhavati /
anena j~nAyate sarvatra bhedo varjanIya iti /
shabdenaivoktaM bhagavatA bodhAyanena ""sarvatra bhedo varjanIyaH'' iti /
adharottarayoH parshvasaMsthAnaM bheda ityupadishantIti /
anenAcAryeNoktametat "vyatyAsaM cinuyAt' iti /

karavindIyA vyAkhyA.

(prAgAyamAprathame prastAre)

upadhIyamAne prAgAyAmAH syuH /

(aparasminnudagAyAmAH)

aparasmin dvitIye tu udagAyatA bhaveyuH bhedAbhAvAya /
uktaM ca bodhAyanena "sarvatra bhedAnvarjayeta' iti /

sundahahAjIyA vyAkhyA.

(prAgAyA gAyAmAH)

iShTakA upadheyAH /

maNDalAyAM mR^ido dehaM kR^itvA madhye shaN^kuM nihatyArdhavyAyAmena saha maNDalaM parilikhet  || ˘p¡us_7.10a ||

___________________________________________________________


yadi maNDalA gArhapatyacitiH mR^ido bhR^ittikAyAH "ha' iti nipAtaH atretyetasminnarthe /
ullekhanaM kR^itveti dehabimbaM shlakShNIkR^itya tanmadhye shaN^kuM nihatyArdhavyAyAmena maNDalaM parilikhet /
tadvyAyAmamAtraM NaNDalaM bhavati /
kecidatra sahashabdashravaNAdatIyeneti varNayanti /
kShetrasamatvAya tadanI psitamihAcAryasya ardhavyAyAmeneti vadataH /
yadIpsita mabhaviShyat mR^ido dehaM kR^itvA maNDalaM kuryAdityevAvakShyat /
uktaM tvAdeshAdanyaditi /
tAvatIM bhUmimiti vakShyAti ca /
kathaM sahetyucyate? yo maNDalaM cikIrShet sa evaM kR^itvAr'dhavyAyAmena parilikhet /
ha iti nipAtaH /
evamadhyAhR^itya yojanIyam /
athavA shrutireveyamevaMbhUtA /

___________________________________________________________


tasmiMsh caturashram avadadhyAd yAvat sambhavet tan navadhA vyavalikhya traidham ekaikaM pradhikaM vibhajet  || ˘p¡us_7.10b ||

___________________________________________________________



tasminniti maNDalaM parAmR^isyate /
tasminmaNDale caturashraM yAvacchete tAvaccaturashraM likhet /
samapariNAhaM caturdhA vibhajya avAntaradikShu lakShaNaM kR^itvA teShu sraktayo yathA bhavanti tathA caturashramAlikhet /
dikShu catvAri dhanuHsamAH /
taccaturashraM navadhA vyavalikhya ekasya pramANena samacaturashraM karaNaM kArayet /
traidhamekaikaM pradhikaM vibhajen /
gamanAya pradhIyata iti pradhikam /
tacca pArshvadhanuH /
tatpratikR^ititvAt pradhikamityucyate /
ekaikaM pradhikaM tridhA kR^itvA karaNAni kArayet /
caturbhistilairUnAHShTyaN^gulAshcaturashrapramANam /
NaNDalamadhye tasya tR^itIyenaikaM karaNaM pradhikamadhyaM dvAviMshatitrayodashAbhyAM kArayet /
triMshadaN^gulena tvekaM takShayet //
yath.A dhanurAkAraM yathA jyAphalakayormadhye tilonamaN^gulaM bhavati tathonaM tribhistrayodashAN^gulamekaM karaNaM aratnimAtraM tilAbhyAmekaM saptaviMshatyaN^gulamaShTabhistilairUnamekaM takShet /
pUrvamaN^guladvayaM agniphalakAbhyAM saha madhye yathA bhavati tathA tR^itIyena karaNena viparyasyAnyamevamiShTakAH kArayet /

upadhAne caturashrasyAvAntaradeshAn prati sraktIH sampAdayet  || ˘p¡us_7.11a ||

___________________________________________________________



upadhAnakAle prathame prastAre avAntaradeshAn koNadeshAn prati caturashrasya sraktIHsampAdeyat saMyojayet /
caturashre nArdheShTakAHsharate /
caturashre naveShTakAHsherate /
pradhikeShu dvAdasha /
navasu dvAdashasu ca ekaviMshatirbhavanti /

madhyAnItarasminprastAre  || ˘p¡us_7.11b ||
