dvitIye prastAre madhyAni caturashre madhyAni avAntaradeshaM pratisampAdayet /

___________________________________________________________


vyatyAsaM cinuyAd yAvataH prastArAMsh cikIrShet  || ˘p¡us_7.11c ||

___________________________________________________________


yAvataH prastArAnkartumicchet tAvadyvatyAsaM cinuyAt /
yaH prathamaHsa tR^itIyaH /
paJNcamash ca yo dvitIyaHsa caturthaH /



___________________________________________________________


pishIlamAtrA bhavantIti dhiShNyAnAM vij~nAyate  || ˘p¡us_7.12 ||

___________________________________________________________


___________________________________________________________


caturashrA ityekeShAM parimaNDalA ityekeShAm  || ˘p¡us_7.13 ||

___________________________________________________________



bAhvorantarAlaM pishIlamiti kecit /
muShTikR^ito 'ratniH pishIlamityanyo /
prAdeshaH pishIlamityapare /
caturashrA dhiShNyA ityekeShAM shrutiH /
parimaNDalA ityekeShAm /

___________________________________________________________


mR^ido dehAn kR^itvAgnIdhrIyaM navadhA vyavalikhya, ekasyAH sthAne 'shmAnam upapadhyAt  || ˘p¡us_7.14 ||

___________________________________________________________


___________________________________________________________


yathAsaN^khyam itarA vyavalikhya yathAyogam upadadhyAt  || ˘p¡us_7.15 ||

___________________________________________________________



----------------

mR^ido dehAniti pradarshanaM tasmin caturashramityAdeH /
ashmanavamA iti siddhe ' pyekasyAH sthAna iti vacanaM dravyeShTakAnAmavaTeShUpadhAnasya j~nApanArtham /
vyaktamuktaM bodhAyanena /
lokabAdhAni dravyANyavaTeShUpadheyAni /
yathAyogamupadadhyAt agnikalpe yAvatsaN^khyAkA dhiShNiyA AmnAtAH tAvatsa«raShyAkA tA vyavalikhya karaNAni kR^itvA yathAyogaM yathA yujyate tatho padadhyAt //


iti saptamaHkhaNDaH.

ityApastambasUtravivaraNe kapardisvAmibhAShye shulbAkhyaprashne

dvitIyaH paTalaH.

----------

karavindIyA vyAkhyA.

maNDalAyAM gArhapatyacityAM karaNaM bahuprayAsasAdhyamiti prakArAntareNeShTakAsampattiM brUte /

(maNDa likhet)

same shucau kacidbhUtale vyAyAmamAtrAdhikavistAraM jAnupaJNcamordhvapramANaM saMsarjanIyairdravyaiHsaMsR^iShTAyAH saMprakR^iShTAyA mR^ido biMmbaM kR^itvA tanmadhye vyAyAmacaturashrakShetraM maNDalaM kR^itvA tanmadhye shaN^kuM nikhAya ardhavyAyAmena saha atishayatR^itIyena saha maNDalaM parilikhet //


(tasminabhavet)

tasminmaNDale yAvat pramANaM caturashraM kartuM shakyaM tAvallikhet, evaM kR^ite maNDalamadhye samacaturashraM ekaM, tatpArshveShu catvAri dhanurAkArANi bhavanti, tAni pradhaya ityucyante /
pradhirnAma rathacakrAvayavaH /
pradhIyate pradhAvyate vAneneti pradhiH /
tatsArUpyAt maNDalAvayavA api pradhaya ityucyante //


(tannavadhA vibhajet)

taccaturashraM navadhA vibhajeta /
tribhAgAvalekhanena navadhA vibhajya pradhiM tvekaikaM traidhaM vibhajet /
caturashraM naveShTakaM catvAraH pradhayaH tridhA vibhaktA dvAdashamAcyaH ekaviMshatiriShTakAH /
maNDalamadhye caturashrakaraNo 'yaM prayogaH /
maNDalamadhye prAcyudIcIM sampAdya maNDalalekhAyAH parINAhaM caturdhA saMbhujya saMbhogeShu tatra lakShaNAni kR^itvA lakShaNAllakShaNaM likhet /
evaM kR^ite maNDalamadhye caturashraM bhavati /
tatra viShkambhArdhaM catuH paJNcadashAN^gulayor'dhadvAviMshatitilAsh ca madhyacaturashrakaraNI /
(sapta) saptatiraN^gulayo 'ShTatilAsh ca tasyAsya tR^itIyo bhAgaH /
paJNcaviMshatiraN^gulayaH paJNcaviMshatitilAsh ca karaNAni kuryata, tAnyucyante--sarvataH paJNcaviMshatitilasahitaM paJNcaviMshatyaN^gulamekaM karaNaM pradhiShu /
trINi karaNAni /
pradhimadhyAshcaturbhiH /
tasya pArshve caturdashAN^gulayaH saptasaptadasha tilAsh ca /
pR^iShThaM paJNcaviMshatitilasahitaM paJNcaviMshatyaN^gulamukham /
ekonatriMshadaN^gulaM (pAdonatriMshaduN^galaM) taM viShkambhArdhapramANayA rajjvA karkaTena vA vilikhya takShayet /
pradhyantayostadevapArshvaM paTaShThaM ca /
mukhaM tu ShaTtriMshadaN^gulaM, dakShiNasya dakShiNaM pArshvaM savyasyottaram /
etAnyeva caturNAM pradhInAM karaNAni /
evaM catuShkaraNI maNDalacitiH //


(upadhAne prastAre)

maNDalAyAmupadhAnakAle prayamaprastAre caturashrasya sraktIH koTIH avAntaradeshAna koNadishaH prati saMyojayet /
dvitIye prastAre caturashrasya madhyAni avAntaradeshAn prati saMyojeyat /
evaM bhedo na syAt /
bhedo nAma prastArAnvayagatAnAmiShTakAnAM prAnteShu sAmyaM, tatsarvatra pariharaNIyamiti tatra tatra vyAkhyAnavacanAt j~nAyate /
vacanamapyasti sarvatra bhedAnvarjayediti //


(vyatyAsaM cinuyAdyAvataH prastArAn cikIrShet)

vyatyasya vyatyasyetyarthaH /
prastArA iShTakAHsaMghAtavi sheShAH /
te paJNcacitIkaM cinvIteti vihitA yAvantaHsyuH tAvanto vyAtyasya vyatyasya cinuyAditi asmAdevAvadhAraNAt j~nAyate, agnidharmA iShTakAyatanordhvapramANAdayo 'tra prApnuvantIti prastAreShu prathamatR^itoyapaJNcamAHsamAH /
dvitIyacaturthau samau nanu kathaM labhyate atishayatR^itIyeneti /
ucyate--saha shabda sAmarthyAccaturashrasya maNDalakaraNe atishayatR^itIyasya karaNIsheShatvavidhAnAccAtishayatR^itIyena saha viShkambArdhena maNDalakaraNam /
etasyA eva gArhapatyaciteH caturashramaNDalatayA prApte kShetrasya sAmyavabhimatamiti caturashramaNDalakaraNanyAyo 'nusartavyaH /
caturashrapUrvakatvaM cAsya maNDalakaraNasya dR^ishyate /
tato 'pi sa evAnusartavyaH /

kecittu saheti dvipadaM kR^itvA sArdhavyAyAmena sambandhayanti /
teShAmanayoH padayoH prayojanavisheShAnnaiva pashyAmaH /
tasmAtsUktamatishatR^itIyena saheti //


(pishIla vij~nAyate)

tripadaM pishIlaM, muShTIkR^itoratniH pishIlamityeke /
bAhvorantarAlaM pishIlamiti bodhAyanaH /
dhiShNyA agnayaH "agnayo vA atha dhiShNiyAH' iti darshanAt, tacchabdena tadAyatanAni lakShyante /
agnInAmAyatanabhuvaH pishIlamAtrANi bhavanti /
apavAdAbhAve AkArabhede 'pi kShetrasya sAmyaM bhavatyeva //


(caturashrA letyekeShAm)

gatametat /
atra sAgnicitye kratau visheShamAha /

(mR^ido dadhyAt)

mudo dehAn kR^itvA mR^itsambandhino dahAnupacayAn bimbAni kR^ityA AgnIdhrIyamekaM navadhA prAktvenodaktevana ca tridhA vyavalikhya madhyasthamekamekenAshmAnA upadadhyAt /
anyAMstatpramANAbiraShTakAbiritarAn hotrIyAdInAM mR^ido dehAn yathA sahkhyaM yasyayasya dhiShNiyAgneH yAyA saN^khyA dvAdasha ShoDasha ekaviMshatiM caturviMshatimityAdyA tayA saMkhyayA taM taM vyavalikhya yathAyogaM yatrayatra deshe yAyA iShTakA yujyate tatratatra tAM tAM iShTakAmupadadhyAt /
dvAdasha ShoDasha ekaviMshatiM caturviMshatiM vA hotrIye, ekAdasha brAhnaNAcchaMsIye, ShaT mArjAlIye, aShTAvaShTAvanyoShu dhiShNiyeShUpadadhAtIti vij~nAyate iti /
anyadhiShNyAH prashAstrIyapotrIyaneShTIyAcchAvAkIyacAtvAlashAmitrAvabhR^ithAH /
karaNAni vA kR^itveShTakAH kuryAt /
caturashrapakShe sarvataH prAdeshAH hotrIyasya, dvAdashapakShe prAdeshe dve navAN^gule dve, ShoDashapakShe sarbato navakAni, ekaniMshatipakShe navake dve saptAN^gulayaH saptatilAsh ca dve, tadekaM sarvataH saptatilAHsaptAN^gulaya ekaM, atra caturashramekataH paJNcadhA vibhajya caturo bhAgAn prathamena caturdhA vibhajet /
dvitIyenaikaM paJNcadhA /
caturviMshatipakShe 'yete eva karaNe /
tatra pUrvavat paJNcadhA vibhajya caturo bhAgAn saptatilasaptAN^gulena paJNcadhA vibhajet /
itareNaikaM caturdhA /
brAhnaNAcchaMsIyasyAShTau hotrIye dvAdashyaH, tisra AgnIdhrIyAH, mArjAlIyaHsyaikataH prAdeshAH, anyato 'dhyardhAH ShaT /
anyeShAM potrUyAdInAM AgnIdhrIyeShTakAH ShaNmArjAlIye aShTake dve /
maNDalapakShe karaNabAhulyaprasaN^gAdyavalekhanamevocyate /
AgnIdhrIyasya prAkcodakca tredhA vibhAgaH /
hotrUyasya dvAdashapakShe ekatastridhA vibhAgo 'nyatashcaturdhA /
ShoDashapakShe sarvatashcaturdhA /
ekaviMshatipakShe tvekataH paJNcadhA kR^itvA caturo bhAgAMshcaturdhA vibhajya caturo bhAgAn paJNcadhA kR^itvAnyaMbhAgaM caturdhA vibhajet /
ekAdashapakShe tvekatashvaturdhA vibhajya trIna trodhA kR^itvA anyaM dvidhA vibhajet /
ShaTpakShe tvekatastridhA kR^itvAnyato dvidhA vibhajet /
aShTapakShe caikatastridhA vibhajya dvau bhAgau tridhA kR^itvAnyaM dvidhA kuryAt /
dhiShNyAnAmekacitIkatvAt sukaratvA ccaiSha eva prakAro varamityAcAryo manyate /
tatra shlokaH //


vyAyAmamAtre citye 'gnau karaNaM dAravaM bhavet /

laihe vA taccaturbhiHsyAt phalakAbhistaducyate //


dvAtriMshadaN^gulAyAmamaN^gulyaHsyustrayodasha /

caturviMshatitila vistAraH karaNe bhavet //


maNDalAtmani tatra syAtkaraNaM ca caturvidham /

madhyamekaM pR^ithau trINi tAnyucyante yathAkramam //


sapaJNcaviMshatitilA aN^gulyaH paJNcaviMshatiH /

sarvataH karaNaM tvekaM madhye 'ne(te)neShTakAkR^itiH //


pradhiShu trINi tAni syuH pradhyante karaNaM tribhiH /

phalakaiH prati(dhi)madhyIyaM caturbhiH karaNaM bhavet //


pR^iShThaM paJNcatilopetA aN^gulyaH paJNcaviMshatiH /

pArshve caturdashAN^gulyaH tilasaptadashAnvitAH //


sapAdonatilastriM(triM)shadekonatriMshadaN^gulam /

mukhaM syAtpradhimadhyIya karaNasyAntayorapi //


pR^iShThapArshveShu tatreme mukhaM ShaTtriMshadaN^gulam /

antayoryatra yasya syAtpArshvaM nAnyasya tatra tat //


karaNAnAM mukhAnyatra viShkambArdhapramANayA /

Alikhya takShayedrajjvA karkaTenAthavA likhet //


ShaTtriMshadaN^gulAyAmA dhiShmayAHsarvataHsamAH /

tatratatra yathAsaN^khyAmucyante karaNAnyatha //


prAdeshamekato yasmAdanyato 'ShTAdashAN^gulam /

mArjAlIyenena kR^itA dhiShNiye ShaTsyuriShTakAH //


prAdeshaHsarvato yasmAdAgnIdhrIye tu tatkR^itAH /

dvAdashAN^gulamekatra yasyAnyatra navAN^gulam //


hotrIye dvAdashopetA tatkR^itA dvAdasheShTakAH //


navAN^gulaM sarvataHsyAddhotrIye tena ShoDasha //


tilapaJNcakasaMyuktAHsaptAN^gulaya ekataH /

navAN^gulaM cAnyataHsyAtkaraNaM tvekaviMshatau (kau) //


tilasapta(paJNca)kasaMyuktA aN^galyaHsapta sarvataH /

idamatraikaviMshe syAccturviMshe 'pyubhe ime //


prathame caikaviMshe syuH ShoDashAnyena paJNcakam /

caturviMshe dvitIyena viMshatistvanyadanyataH //


yAH prAdeshe(sha)nuvAN^galyastvaShTau tAstisra eva ca /

prAdeshAbrAhnaNAcchaMsidhiShNiye tvekayugdasha //


prAdoshAH ShaTpadAdhyardhedvece....tyaShTake vidhiH /

potriyAdau yathAyogamupadhAnaM tu sarvataH //


ekacityAdhiShNiyAnAM bhedasyAnavakAshataH /

vaiShamyeNaiva sahkhyAnAM karaNAnekatA bha(ve)yAt //


vyavalikhya yathAsaN^kyamupadadhyAdiheShTakAH /

yathAyogamiti tvevamAcAryo maNDale 'bravIt //


adhikAMshena karNasya hR^ine karNayuge bhuvA /

hR^ite phalena (phalone) hInAyA yujo vA yadbhuvo daram //


tasya varge 'sya karNasya vargAttu parishodhite /

parishiShTasya mUlaM tu lambakaM tadvido viduH //


vadiprAcImitAM rajjumantarAloktayA vR^itA /

dakShiNottaramAyamya vedeH pUrvAparArdhayoH //


vi(dvi)dR^itIyau tu vij~neyA prAgudvedi rutkaraH (ttaram) /

madhyadeshotrimadhyaM tu vahneH prAcyapratIcyayoH //


lakShaNena nimittArthaM (dvi) vikR^itIye tvapAyate /

pashcime cottaratrApi nimittaM syAdapAyate //


viparyasya tu pUrvatra nimitte dakShiNottare /

kR^itvA viShkambha turye syAdubhayasyApi lakShaNam //


tayorlakShaNayortekhAM rajjuM vA prA«nipAtayet /

lekhAyA dakShiNaM grAhyaM maNDalArthaM tyajedudak //


pariNAhe caturthA ShaTsaMbhugne bhugnalAJNchane /

aN^kAdaN^kagatA rekhA caturashrasya sAdhikA //


viShkambhArdhIyavargasya dviguNasyaiSha mUlataH /

maNDale caturashrasya karaNI parikalpanA ( kalpitA) //


yadvA viShkambhamUlArdha (vargArdha) mUlena karaNIkR^itiH /

maNDale catushrasya yAvatsaMbhavajanmanaH //


akShNayAvasthitAM rajjuM yAvatsaMbhavajanmanaH /

caturashrasya viShkambhaM maNDalasya vadanti hi //


viShkambhasyAntarA varge viShkambhArdhasya vargataH /

shodhite parishiShTasya mUlaM syAddalalakShaNam //


viShkambhasyAddalagrastacApajyArdhAsya vargake /

pUrvajyAdalavarge tu viShkambhArdhasya vargataH //


shodhite parishiShTasya mUlaM taddhanuShaHshiraH /

sajyAvargaHShaDguNeShu vargashvApasya vargakaH //


sharAhatastu kodaNDo dalito dhanuShaH phalam //


viShkambha AtmadviguNena('pi)yojyaH sa cAtmaviMshena sa paJNcamAkhyAm /

sapaJNcaviMshena ca tau sametau vyAsena saiShA pariNAhallaptiH //


nemidvirekAdashavAtrakAryas tadbhAga ekash ca tathA dvidhA ca /

vyAsaHsvarAMshAH paridheHsaha syur bhAgAMshaturyeNa sa saptamena //


ityApastambasUtravivaraNe karavindIyabhAShye shulbAkhyaprashne

dvitIyaH paTalaH.

---- /
----



sundahahAjIyA vyAkhyA.

maNDalAyAM tu karaNAnAM vahuvaktavyatvAt tairvinaiveShTakopAyamAha----

maNDa vibhajet

deha--upacayaHShaDuN^galotsedhaH /
saheti nipAto vAkyAlaM kAre /
sa iti vA cchedaH /
"ardhavyAyAmena maNDalaM parilikhet' ityeva satyAShADhaH /
caturashraM savisheSheNa viShkambhArdhena catustilonenAShTaShaShTyaN^gulenAvadadhyAt /
caturashraM navadhA kR^itvA prathikAn tredhA vibhajhet /
prathireva prathikaH /
prathishvakraparyantaH /
athavA karaNaireveShTakAH kuryAt /
trINi karaNAni--samacaturashraM prathimadhyaM prathyantamiti /
atra samacaturashraM dvAviMshatyaN^gulaM saikaviMshatitilam /
prathimadhyasya pArshvamAnyAH pramANametadeva /
tirya«nAnyA dashatilonatrayodashAhgule ekaM pArshvaM phalakaM dhanurAkAraM takShet /
yathA aN^guliH dvAdashatilAsh ca sharapramANaM bhavati /
prathyantaM tu pramANam /
tasyApi caturashravadekaM pArshvaM, trayodashAN^gulaM dashatilonamaparaM, ShaDviMshakaM tiladvayonamaparaM, taddhanuriva takShet, yathA aN^guliH saptaviMshatish ca tilAHsharo bhavati //


upadhAne shcikIrShet

maNDalacaturashrayoHsAdhAraNamidaM bhedaparihArAya, anenaiva j~nAyate sarvatra bhedo varjanIya iti /
tathAca bodhAyanaH------

bhedAn varjayedadharottarayoH pArshvasaMdhAnaM bheda ityAcakShate, tadAdyAnteShu na vidyate--iti /

pishIla vij~nAyate

vishIlaM paJNcadhA varNayanti--bAhvorantarAlamityekam, kR^itamu ShTimaratniM(kR^itamuShTirara tniH) dvitIyam /
akR^itamuShTimaratniM tR^itIyaM, dvAtriMshadaN^gulaM caturthaM, ShaTtriMshadaN^gulaM paJNcamamiti /

caturashrAn kR^itvA

tAn kuryAditi sheShaH /

AgnIdhro dadhyAt

itarAn dhiShNiyAn yathAsaMkhyaM vyavalikhya dvAdasha ShoDashetyAdi hotrIye, ekAdasha brAhnaNAcchaMsIye, ShaNmArjAlIye, aShTAvaShTAvanyoShviti /
teShAM ca yathAsaMbhavaM vibhAgA iti kecidAhuH /
sama catuhashrANAM dhiShNiyAnAM samacaturashrA eveShTakAH kAryAH caturashramAdeshAdanyaditi /
tavAratnIviShkambhANAM dhiShNiyAnA miShTakA aShTAN^gulA AgnIdhrIyasya /
hotrIyasya dvAdashakasya madhye catasrashcaturaN^gulAH /
parito 'ShTAN^gulAH /
ShoDashike ShaDaN^gulAHsarvAH /
ekaviMshakasya madhye nava caturaN^gulAH, parito dvAdasha ShaDaN^gulA /
caturviMshakasya koNe 'pvaShTAN^gulAH, sheSho viMshatishcaturaN^gulAH /
vlAhnaNAcchaMsIye sapta ShaDaN^gulA, catasro navAN^gulAH /
mArjAlIye paJNcAShTAN^gulAH /
anye tvAhuH--yathAsaMkhyamitarAniti vacanAt sarvA iShTakAstulyakShetrA eva /
tatra samacaturakShANAmeva kartumashakyatvAddIrghacaturashrA api kriyeranniti /
tanmate 'pyAgnIdhrI yasya pUrvavat /
hotrIyasya dvAdashakasyeShTakA aShTAN^gulAyAmAH ShaDaN^gulavyAsAH /
ShoDashakasya pUrvavadeva /
ekaviMshakasya tu aShTAN^gulAyAmA aratnisa(pta)mavyAsAH /
(caturviMshakasya ShaDaN^gulA yAmAshcaturaN^gulavyAsAH /
mArjAlIyasya prAdeshAyAmA aShTAN^gulir vyAsAH aShTakAnAM prAdeshAyAmAHShaDaN^gulavyAsAH) /
brAhnaNAcchaMsIyasya dve saraNe aShTAN^gulAyAmaM sAShTAdashatilaShaDaN^gulavyAsamekaM karaNam /
tena tisra iShTakAHShaDaN^gulavyAsA bhavanti /
navatilonanavAN^gulAyAmamaparam /
tena aShTAviShTakAH /
anyeShu pishIlamAtreShvetadanusAreNeShTakA draShTavyAH //


atha parimaNDalAnAM ShaTtriMshadaN^gulaviShkambAnAM AgnIdhrIyasya madhye prAdeshavyAsaM parimaNDalamashmAnaM nidhAya parito 'ShTAviShTakAstAsAM karaNaM, pArshve dvAdashAN^gule, caturdashAN^gulamaShTatilonamekaM tiryakphalakaM, taddhanuriva takShet, yathA aN^guliH dvAdashatilAsh ca sharo bhavati /
saviMshatitilaM caturaN^gulamanyattiryakphalakaM, tacca dhanuriva takShet, antarvakraM tu bhavati yathA paJNcadashatilAHsharaH /
evamiShTakA anyeShAM dhiShNiyAnAM trINi karaNAni /
sarveShAM ca dveTve phalake aShTAdashAN^gule /
hotrIyasya dvAdashakasya tR^itIyaM phalake navAN^gulaM saikAdashatilaM, taddhanuriva takShet, yathaika viMshatitilAHsharaH evaM ShoDashakAdInAM ca draShTavyam /
brAhnaNAcchaMsIyasya tR^itIyaM phalakaM dashAN^gulaM sapaJNcadashatilaM, taddhanurivatakSheta, paJNcaviMshatitilAHshAraH, saptatilamiti vkacit /
mArjA lIyasya tR^itIyamapyaShTAdashAN^gulaM, tadardhadhanuriva takShet, vdyaN^gulaM caturdashatilAHsharaH /
aShTakAnAM tR^itIyaphalakaM caturdashAN^gulamaShTatilonaM, taddhanuriva takShet, aN^gulirdvAdashatilAsh ca sharaH /
anyeShAM ca pishIlAnAmetadanusAreNa draShTavyam //


// it.i saptamaH khaNDaH //


iti sundahahAjIye ApastambashulbasUtravyAkhyAne shulbapradIpe

dvitIyaH paTalaH.

---- /
----



kapardikShAShyam

uktAni haviryaj~nAnAM viharaNani /
saumikAni ca sAgnicityasya kratoragnikShetramAnamiShTakAnAM karaNAni upadhAnavi dhish ca noktaH /
tadvaktukAmaH prastauti--

bhavatIva khalu vA eSha yo 'gniM cinute iti vij~nAyate | vayasAM vA eSha pratimayA cIyata ityAkR^iticodanAt | pratyakShavidhAnAdvA  || ˘p¡us_8.1 ||

___________________________________________________________


yAvadAmnAnena veNunA caturashre Atmani puruShAn avamimote  || ˘p¡us_8.2a ||

___________________________________________________________



prastAvamAtramanayA shrutyA kiyate na phalanidhAnaM /
vidhivibhakterabhAvAt /
nityo 'gniruttaravedivat /
"agniShToma uttaravediruttareShu kratuShvagniH' iti nityavacanAt /
yadi prastAvo 'nayA shrutyA svIkriyate gArhapatyaciteH pUrvameva prastAvo na kartavyaH /
satyametat /
iha prastAvavacanasyedaM prayojanam-- vakShyamANAni dhamArNi mahAgnereva yathA syuriti /
kAni punastAni? jAnudaghrAjo mahAgneveti kAtyAyanIye shulbe mahAgnanerevaite dharmA iti spaShTamuktam /
kiM cAshcehAgnishabdena nirupapadena coditA dharmA yathA syuriti /
yathA--"taM vA etaM yajamAna eva cinvIta' iti yajamAno mahAgnereva kartA na gArhapatyAdeH /
gArhapatyadhiShNayAnAmadhvaryureva kartA /
pashcAdvidhAtavyAnAM dhiShNiyAnAM pUrvaM vidhAnasyaitatprayojanam /
yo 'gneshvetA sa bhavatyeva /
yadyapi bahavo bhrAtR^ivyA iti kriyate 'nayA shrutyA /
vayasAM--pakShiNAM eSho 'gniH pratimayA prakR^ityA cetavya iti AkR^iteHsvarUpasya vidhAnaM kriyate /
sa cotpatatAM chAyayetyartha iti bodhAyanenoktam /
vaishabdo nishvaye /
asAvapyAcAryo vakShyati "vakrapuccho vyastapakSha' iti /
tasmAcchyenacideva prathamaH /
shulbAntare coktaM "shyenacidagnInAM prathamo 'gniH' iti /
yadi shyeno nityaH kathaM svargakAma iti ? yUpadravyavat /
yathA khAdiraM svargakAmasyeti khAdirasya nityatvaM kAmyatvaM ca /
pratyakShavidhAnAdyAvadAmrAyena /
vAshabdaH pakShavyAvR^ittau /
tena naiShApR^iticodanApi shyenaH prakR^itiH /
kutaH? pratyakShavidhAnAt /
pratyakShamevAtra vidhIyate /
pakShIbhavatItyArabhya pakShapucchAnAmapi pramANaM vihitam /
tena virodhAt /
nanktamAkR^iticodaneti, naiShA codanA; nApi vidhiH; vidhivibhakterabhAvAt /
cIyata iti nirdishyate; na cinuyAccetavyamiti vA /
vidhyantarasheShabhUtatvAcca pashyAmo na vidhAyiketi /
"brahnavAdino vadanti nya««agnishvetavyA 3 uttAnA 3 ityArabhya prAcInamuttAnaM purUShashIrShamupadadhAti' iti puruShashirasaH upadhAnaM vidhIyate /
tasya sheShabhUtamidaM na vidhAyakam /
shyenacidagnInAM prathama iti piThakashyenamadhikR^ityaitaduktaM puruShamAtrapakShapucchasya samAkhyA shyena iti /
tasmAdavirodhaH /
yAvadAmnAnaM tAvadeva sArUpyaM /
pakShapucchavattathA sArUpyaM gR^ihItvA vayaHshabdo vartate /
tasmAtpuruShamAtrapakShapucchavAnagniriti tAmeva prakR^itiM nishvitya anye AkR^itivisheShA vakrapakShAdayaH kAmyA iti siddham /
vakShyati "kAmyA guNavikArA' iti /
veNunA caturashra Atmani puruShAnavamimIte--agnikalpe uktalakShaNena veNunA mimIte--minoti sthaNDulArdhaM kShetraM vakShyamANena mAgaiNa sarvato dvipuruSha AtmA dvAbhyAM catvArIti vacanAccatavAri ca puruShakShetrANyAtmani----

prAdeshena vitastyA vA pashcAtpuccham  || ˘p¡us_8.2d ||

dvAdashAN^gulena trayodashAN^gulena vA pashcAtpucchaM vardhayediti sheShaH /
evamardhAShTamAni ShuruShakShetrANi bhavanti /

karavindIyA vyAkhyA

agnyAdheyaprabhR^iti somAntAnAM kevalavihArA uktAH /
idAnIM sAgnicityeShu kratuShu vihAravisheShavidhitsayAgneshvayanavidhAyikAM shrutiM paThati //


bhavatI yate

bhavatiHsamR^iddhyarthe /
ivakhaluvaishabdo nipAtasamudAyo vAkyAlaN^kArAdau vartate /
"rasa iva khaluvai tat yo 'rgni cinute--agniM cayanena saMskaroti sa samR^iddho bhavatIti vij~nAyate //
nan.u mantrasya vidheH stAvakatayAr'thavAdo 'yaM /
cinuta iti vartamAnanirdeshaH /
ataH kathameShA agrisaMskArabhUtasya cayanasya vidhAyikA shrutiH kalpyate /
satyaM, taittirIyake asyA eva shrutermukhyatvAdaprAptArthatvenAnuvAdatvAsaMbhavAccayanamAtrasyaiShA vidhAyikA shrutiH kalpyate /
akAmasaMbandhAnnityeti ca /
nanu cayanavadbhavatyartho 'pi vidheyaH /
na vidheyaH, kuta, cayanasyAgnisaMskAratvena tatphalAnuvAdAsaMbhavAt //


vayasAMadanA

vayAMsi--pakShiNaH shyenAdayaH /
pratimA -- pratikR^itiHsAdR^ishyamAkR^itirUpaM codayatIti codanA vidhIyakA shrutiH /
eSho 'gniryathA shyenAkR^itirbhavati tathA yetavya ityarthaH /
shulbAntare ca -- shyenacidagnInAM prathamo 'gnirityuktaM /
vakShyati ca shyenaM prakR^itya vakrapakSho vyastapuccho bhavatIti /
tasmAdvakapakShAdivishiShTashyeno 'gniH prakR^ititvena kAryaH /
sa nityaH /
yUpaprakR^itibhUtakhAdirAdikat svargakAmasyApi bhaviShyati /

pratya nena

vAshabdaH pakShavyAvR^ittau /
naitadasti vayasAM vA eSha pratimayA cAyate iti eShA shyenAdyAkR^itivisheShacodaneti /
kutaH, pratyakShavidhAnAt /
yataH pakShI bhavatItyAdinA vAkyena vyAyAmamAtrapakShapucchavadAkR^itiH pratyakShamevAgnervidhIyate /
ataH vayasAM vA eSha pratimayA cIyata iti vayaHsAdR^ishyamAtramabhidadhAti, naiShA shyainAkR^itiyodanA bhavitumarhati /
kiJNca cIyata iti vartamAnArtha nirdeshAdasya vAkyasya puruShashIrShopadhAnavidhivAkyasheShatvAcca naiShA vidhAyikA /

yaccoktaM shulbAntare -- "shyenacidagninAM prathamo 'gnirityuktamiti' nAyaM doShaH /
tatra hi vyAyAmamAtrapakShapuccho 'gnirityapi shyena ityucyate /
tasmAdAmnAnena vedena vyAyAmamAtrapakShapucchavattAyA yAvatsAdR^ishyaM vihitaM tAvadeva saMpAdayitavyaM /
tasmAtpuruShamAtrapakShapucchavAnagniH prakR^itirnityash ceti sthitam /
asyA gneHsvarUpamAha /

veNunA cchaM vakShyamANaprakAreNa veNunA'tmani caturaH puruShAnavamimIte /
avamAnamapi vimAnameva /
iyati shakShyAmIti tvA avamAya yajanta iti darshanAt /
sarvato dvipuruSha AtmA tAbhyAM catvAri puruShakShetrANyAtmA bhavati /
evaM vakShayoH pucche ca puruShasaMmitAni trINi /
evaM sapta puruShakShetrANi aratninA dakShiNato dakShiNaM pakShaM pravardhayati dakShiNato -- dIrghaM kuryAt /
evamuttarata uttaramapi pakShamuttarato dIrghaM kuryAt /
prAdeshena nitastyA vA pashcAtpucchaM /
prAdeshoN^guShThapradeshinIbhyAM parimitaH vitastiraN^guShThakaniShThikAbhyAM tayoranyatareNa pucchaM pratIcInaM vardhayet /
evamardhAShTamAni puruShakShetrANyagneH kShetraM bhavati /

sundararAjIyA vyAkhyA.

vedervimAnaM saumikyAH kramairdvidvAdashAN^gulaiH /

Aditrisaptasu dvitricandradviyugabhUmiShu // .1 //


bhUtribhUdvisharaikeShu shaN^kavo dasha paJNca ca /

saShaTtilAratniShaShThonAShTAtriMshadaratnikA // .2 //


vimAnarajjushvihnaM syAttasyAHsaptadashasvatha /

pAshau kAryau tayormadhye praktamA dvAdasha smR^itAH // .3 //


ShaTtriMshikA vA rajjuHsyAdvimAne vdyaShTalakShaNA /

shroNI paJNcadashasvAdye sado 'nantaraturyayoH // .4 //


dashasvaShTasu tatkoNAstR^itIye 'ratnimAtrakAH /

dhiShNyAH prAdeshAntarAlA AgnIdhraM tu turIyake // .5 //


rudreShu saptadashasu shaN^kU pAdoniteShviha /

kAryau hi paJNcamer'keShu mArjAlAgnIdhradhiShNiyau // .6 //


saptame prAgvadAgnIdhre dhAnaM sArdhacatuShTaye /

utkaro dashame shaN^kau manuShUttarataH krame // .7 //


UvathyagohakhananasthAnamekAdashe punaH /

havirdhAnaM prAgvadatra pAshayorvyatyato 'dhikaH // .8 //


ShoDashasvardhahIneShu shAmitro dvAdashe bhavet /

shaN^kvoruttaravediHsyAddvayoHsArdha upAntyayoH // .9 //


antime dvAdashasvaMsau cAtvAloM'sAdudakkrame /

pashubandho 'stu cAtvAlaHsome 'pItyavadhAryate // .10 //


mAnAntaramanuktvaiva vyAkhyAta iti kIrtanAt /

shamyAmAtrastu sarvatra vyaktaM bodhAyano 'bravIt // .11 //


anyathAgnau virodhaHsyAnmAnaM cAnyanna vidyAte /

uttareM'se mahAvedyAmAstAvaH parikIrtitaH // .12 //


dakShiNe tu havirdhAne pashcAttIn prakramAMstyajet /

pAdonadvitayaM pArshve 'ratnau tUparavAHsmR^itAH // .13 //


ardhaprAdeshatasteShAM bhramaNaM koNashaN^kuShu /

agreNoparavAMstyaktvA pAdonaprakramatrayam // .14 //


shamyAmAtrashvatuHsraktiH kharashliShTastu saJNcaraH /

audumbarasadomadhye pR^iShThyA dakShiNataH krame // .15 //


bhavatIva codanA

pratimayA vayasAM utpatatAM chAyayA /
tathA ca bodhAyanaH--

"vayasAmutpatatAM chAyayetyarthaH'

iti /
anena shyenacitirnityoti j~nAyate /
mantravarNAsh ca bhavanti, "suparNo 'si garutmAn' ityAdIni /
liN^gAni ca pucchAcchi ro 'dhikR^iShati shirasi pakShayorityAdIni /
na hi caturashre shirosta /

pratya dvA

pakShIbhavati vyAmamAtrau pakShau ca pucchaM ca bhavatItyAdi pratyakShavidhAnAdvA AkR^itiH pratyetavyA /
anena caturashro 'gnirvi dhIyate /
sa ca sarvAgnInAM prakR^itiriti /
tameva tAvadAha --

yAva ttare

yAvadAmnAnena yathAsamnAtena puruShamAtreNa vakShyamANena paJNcAratninA /
evaM kevalasaptavidhAgnermAnamuktaM, pakShAntaramAha --

aratninA cchaM vitastirdvAdashAN^gulA /
yathoktaM kAtyAyanena --

(120)

"paJNcAratnanirdashavitastirviMshatishatAN^gulayaH puruShaH'

iti /
vitastirdvidashAN^guletyeva naighaNTukAH /
prAdeshenetyasya vyAkhyAnaM vitastyeti /
prAdeshashabdArthasya vishayisvAt vitastirevAtra prAdasheshabdena grAhyA, natu prasArite aN^guShThapradeshinyAvityarthaH /
athavA vAjasaneyake "vitastyA pucchaM' iti shrutatvA dvitastishabdasyaiva prasiddhatareNa prAdeshashabdenana vyAkhyAnam /
vAshabdo vAkyArthe 'vasaMbadhyate /
tena sarvamidaM vikalpyate /
tathAhi -- pucchavR^iddhestAvadvaikalpikatvamavagatam, taittirIyake pravR^iddheranuktatvAt /
vyanakti ca kAtyAyanastathA "aratninA pakShau drAghIyAgaMsau bhavataH' ityuktvA iti drAghIyastvamuktvA "vyAmamAtrau pakShau ca pucchaM ca bhavati' iti puruShamAtrasyaiva nigamanAt /
rupaShTa

yati caitadbodhAyanaH --

puruShamAtraiNa veNunA sapakShapucchamaratninA vA pakShau drAghIyAgaMsau bhavataH /

iti /
kecittu vitastiM trayodashAMN^gulAM manvAnA dvAdashAN^gulena prAdeshena vikalpayantaH pakShapucchAnAmaratnanyAdipravR^iddhiM nityAmAhuH /
teShAmaShTavidhaprabhR^itInAM yadanyatsaptadhA vibhajya vidhAsaptamakaraNImityAdi na saMgacchate /
tattyodashAN^gulavitastyabhyupagame pucche viMshatishatAN^gulamAtraM kShetramupadhAtuM na shakyate /

tatra kashvidAha -- purISheNa pUryatAmiti, tatsUtrakAro na sahate /
yadAha "ardhAntaratvAt purIShasya' iti "yatpacyamAnAnAM pratihraseta' iti ca /
kiJNca purISheNa cetsarvasya nyUnasya pUrtiH; kimiti mahatA granthena iShTakApramANArdhamadhunA prayatyate /
tasmAnna kiJNci detatrrayodashAN^gulA vitastiriti /
anye manyante -- dvAdashAN^gula yoreva vitastiprAdeshayoH AmikShApayasyayoriva bidhibhedAcchabdabhedaH /
tayosh ca parasparaM vikalpa iti /
teShAmapi pUrvoktAsaMgatiH spaShTaiva /
brAhnaNavirodhash ca /
taittirIyake hi pucchasya pravR^iddhiH pAkShikatvenApi noktA /
tasmAdaratnaniprAdeshAnAM pAkShikatvameva jyAyo manyAmahe /
kiJNca yadeveShTakAnAmaShTAN^gulAnAM paJNcamaM karaNaM tadapyasminnardhe liN^gaM katham? tatra hi prathamatR^itIyakaraNAbhyAmeva upadhAne shakye anyAni trINi karaNAni bhedaparihArArthAni /
tatra paJNcamena vinApyupadhAnaM sukaram /
saratnyAdipravR^iddhau nityAyAM tatprakArash ca darshito bhagavatA bodhAyanena --

"uradhAne pUrvAparayoH pakShapArshvayoH' /


ityAdi /
anyash ca prakAraH -- Atmani purastAt dashArdheShTakAH /
udagAyatAH paJNcadasha /
pakShAgraryormadhye tisrastisraH prAcyaH /
pucchApArshvayoH paJNcapaJNca /
pucchAgrakoNayordve prAdeshamAtryau /
tAbhyAmadhyardhe 'ShTake udIcyau /
pakShAgrakoNeShvekaikA adhyardhA udagAyatA /
apyayosh ca paJNcapaJNca yathAsUtraM /
pucchAgramadhye dve prAcyau /
sheShe paJNcamyaH /
eSha dvishataH prastAraH /
aparasmiMstu pakShapArshvayoHShaTShaDardheShTakA udIcyaH /
Atmani dakShiNata uttaratash ca ShaT ShaT prAcyaH /
shroNyaMseShu dvedve adhyardhe udIcyau /
pucchApyaye paJNca prAgAyatAH AtmAnamaratnaninopetAH /
sheShe paJNcamyaH /
pucchAgreShu madhyamAmuddhR^itya dve ardhe 'ShTake udIcyau /
eSha dvishataH prastAraH /
evaM caturbhiH karaNairupadhAne siddhe yatpaJNcamaM karaNaM tadaratnaniprAdeshAbhAve 'pi bhedaparihAreNa dvishatapUraNArtham /
nirUpaNIyaM caitatsarvaM sUribhirityuparamyate //

ekaH puruSho yasminniti ekavidhaH, ekapuruShAdekottaraM cinvIteti prathamAtikrame kAraNAbhAvAditi prathama ekapuruShavidhA iShTakA asminvidhIyante iti agnikShetram /

abhividhAvA« /

tad u ha vai saptavidham eva cinvIta | saptavidho vAva prAkR^ito 'gniH | tata Urdhvam ekottarAn iti vij~nAyate  || ˘p¡us_8.4 ||

___________________________________________________________


nipAtasamUhaH pakShavyAvR^ittau /
ekavidhAdayo na cetavyA iti /
vAvetyavadhAraNe /
saptavidha eva prAkR^ito 'gniH -- prakR^itirityarthaH /
svArtha eva taddhita /
saptavidhAdUrdhvaM ekottarAniti vAjasane yinAM shrutiH /
saptArtha eva prathamaH prakR^itish ca puruShamAtreNetyArabhya saptArdhasya vidhAnAdupadhAnavidhau dakShiNe pakShe upadadhAtIti shrUyate /
tata UrdhvamekottarAniti ekapuruShAdhikAH paramiti, dvitIye prayoge ardhanavamaM, tR^itIyer'dhadashamamityevaM draShTavyam /

karavindIyA vyAkhyA

ekavidhaH pra tivij~nAyate

saptavidhasya prakR^ititvamAshaN^kya tenaiva prakR^ititvaM pratipAdayitumAha vidhIyate mIyata iti vidhA agnanivimAnaM, puruShamAtreNa veNunA puruShakShetrANi ekaikasho 'tra mIyanta iti vidhAshabdaH puruShakShetravAcI /
ekA vidhA yasyAgneH sa ekavidhaH /
prathamAtikrame kAraNAbhAvAt prathama ekavidhaHsa eva prakR^itiH, itare vikR^itayaH, te cAgnaya evamekapuruShavR^iddhyA udyanti adhikA bhavanti -- vardhanta ityarthaH /
A ekashatavidhAt /
AN^gAbhividhau /
kathaM vidhAshabdasya vimA naparyAyatvaM, ucyate -- vidadhAti karotItyarthaH /
karaNIvyApAreShu vimAneShu karotiH tatratatrad dashyate /
ato vidhAvimA nayoH paryAyatvam /
tasmAdekavidhaH prathamaH /
sa ekavidhaH prakR^itish ca /
dvividhAdayastadvikArA iti /
taduhavai saptavidhameva cinvIta -- taduhavA iti nipAtasamudAyaH pakShavyAvR^ittau /
naitadastyekavidhaH prathama iti /
kiM? tasmin saptavidhameva prathamaM cinvIteti /
kutaH? saptavidho vAva prAkR^ito 'gniH /
vAva ityavadhAraNe /
"eSha vAva sarvato rAjA' ityAdau darshanAt /
prakR^itireva prAkR^itaH svArthe taddhitaH, tasmAtsaptavidha eva prakR^itibhUto 'gniH /
tasmAtsaptavidha eva prathamaM cetavyaH, naikavidhaH tasminneva pakShapucchAdyaN^gAnAmupadeshAdityabhiprAyaH /
saptavidha ityardhAShTama evocyate /
yAvAnagniHsAratniprAdeshaHsaptavidhaHsaMpadyata iti vakShyamANatvAt /
tata UrdhvaM tataHsaptavidhAdUrdhvamekottarAnekenAdhikAnagnIMshvinvIteti shrutiH /
agnirbaloktaM vAjasaneyakamiti /
tasmAddvitIyAdyAhAreShu

saptavidhameva cinvItetyetadashamaH ityevamekottaravidhatvaM ekashatavidhAt draShTavyam /

sundararAjIyA vyAkhyA.

ekavidhaHavidhAt

vidhIyata iti vidhA -- puruShamAtraM kShetram /
prathamAhAre ekavidhaH /
evaM dvividhAdi /
ekashatatama AhAre ekashatapuruShaH /

taduhavai vij~nAyate

pakShAntaramAha -- prakR^itireva prAkR^itaH praj~nAdyaN /
saptavidhAdUrdhvamekottarAnekashatavidhAt /
sarvatrAradniprAdeshAnAM na vR^iddhiH, vidhAnAmeva vR^iddhivacanAt /
"ekaviMshe puruShAbhyAso nAratnaniprAde shAnAm' iti liN^gAcca /
vyaktoktametadbodhAyanena -- "ardhAShTamAH puruShAH prathamo 'gniH ardhanavamA dvitIyor'dhadashamAstR^itIyaH' ityAdi /
yastvekavidhAdikrameNAharate tasya saptavidhAdiShvapyara tniprAdeshAnAmabhAvaH, ekottaratvAvirodhAt sAratniprAdeshe saptavidha AhR^ite uttare 'pi nAratniprAdeshAH /

kapardikShAShyam

vAjasaneyikamiti agnivikalpavidhAnAt vikalpaM saptArdhamapi dvitIye vihAre cinvItetyetadapi labhyate /

ekavidhaprabhR^itInAM na pakShapucchAni bhavanti | saptavidhavAkyasheShatvAc chrutivipratiShedhAc ca  || ˘p¡us_8.5 ||

___________________________________________________________



itash ca pashyAmaH saptArdhavidha eva cetavya iti /
yasmAdekavidhaprabhR^itInAM ShaDvidhaparyantAnAM na pakShapucchAni bhavanti /
kimuktaM bhavati? yataH pakShapucchAni na bhavanti teShu na sherata ityarthaH /
kuta ityAha -- sapteti /
saptavidhamagniM prakutya vidhIyanta ityarthaH /
rathantaraM dakShiNe pakShe upadadhAti bR^ihaduttarapakSha ityevamAdayo na viyujyante /
tasmAnna cetavyA ekavidhAdayaH /
saptavidha eva cetavyaH /
teShveva pakShapucchAni kimiti na kriyerannityata Aha -- shrutIti /
virodho -- vipratiShedhaH /
yadyekavidhasyapakShapucchAtmanAM vibhAgaH kriyate; pakShapucchatmanAM vyAyAmamAtratA hIyate /
athaiSha doSho na bhavediti vyAyAmamAtratA pakShapucchAtmanAM gR^ihyeta; tadaikavidhatvaM hIyeta /
tasmAdvirodhaH /
atash ca viro dhAnna kartavyA ekavidhAdayaH ShaDvidhaparyantAH /
kathamaShTavidhAdayo mAtavyA ityata Aha --

aShTavidhaprabhR^itInAM yad anyat saptabhyas tat saptadhA vibhajya pratipuruSham Aveshayet  || ˘p¡us_8.6a ||

___________________________________________________________



aShTavidhaprabhR^itInAM ekashatavidhaparyantAnAM yadanyatsaptabhyaH saptArdhebhyaH tatsaptadhA saptArdhadhA yadanyatsaptArdhebhyaH prakSheptavyamAsIt tatsaptArdhadhA vibhajya saptArdhebhya iti kuta etallabhyate? saptavidha ityukter'dhAShTama eva gR^ihyate /
aratniprAdeshAnAM tadantargatatvAt /
vakShyati saptavidha iti /
aShTavidha ekaH prakSheptavyaH navavidhe dvau /
dashavidhe traya ityevaM draShTavyamekashatavidhAt puruShAt /
puruShaM saptArdhadhA vibhaktaM kR^itvA pratipuruShameko bhAgaH kSheptavyaH /
saptAsvardhapaJNcAratniprAdesheShu puruShe triMshatpaJNcadashabhAgIyAH /
ardha puruShe paJNcadasha /
evamekasminpuruShakShetre dve shate paJNcaviMshatish ca paJNcadashabhAgIyAHsherate /
aShTavidhe tAH prakSheptavyAH /
ekasminpuruShakShetre triMshatpaJNcadashabhAgIyAH /
tAsu prAkShiptAsu paJNcapaJNcAshadadhikashatadvayamApadyate /
ShoDashAnAM vargaM ShaTpaJNcAshadadhikam /
taccaturashrAccaturashramityanena nyAyena ekasminpaJNcadashabhAgayikShetre 'panIte yA rajjuH sA puruShasthAnIyA /
tasyAH paJNcamo bhAgo 'ratnisthAnIyaH /
tena mAnena kR^ite sarvapuruShakShetraM liptaM bhavati /
evaM navavidhAdiShu draShTavyam /

___________________________________________________________


AkR^itivikArasyAshrutatvAt  || ˘p¡us_8.6b ||

___________________________________________________________



___________________________________________________________


puruShamAtreNa vimimIte' veNunA vimimIte, iti vij~nAyate  || ˘p¡us_8.7 ||

___________________________________________________________



yadi puruShakShetramekatra kShipyate, vikriyetAkR^itiH /
na vidyate shrutiryasyAHsA ashrutiH /
AkR^itivikArasya shruterabhAvAt ityarthaH /
puruShamAtreNeti dravyamapekShate /
veNuneti ca mAtrAmapekShate /
tayornaShTAshvadagdharathavatsaMbandhaH /
puruShamAtreNa veNunA minoti /

___________________________________________________________


yAvAn yajamAna UrdhvabAhus tAvad antarAle veNosh chidre karoti madhye tR^itIyam  || ˘p¡us_8.8 ||

___________________________________________________________



yajamAnagrahaNAdadhvaryupramANo veNurna gR^ihyate /
chidrayorantarAlaM yajamAnamAtraM yathA bhavati tathA chidre karoti /
tayormadhye veNoshchidramekaM karotIti sheShaH /

___________________________________________________________


apareNa yUpAvaTadesham anupR^iShThyaM veNuM nidhAya chidreShu shaN^kUn nihatyonmucyAparAbhyAM dakShiNAprAk parilikhed AntAt  || ˘p¡us_8.9 ||

___________________________________________________________



saJNcarasya pashcAdanupR^iShThyaM pR^iShThyA yathA tathA veNuM nidhAya triShu chidreShu shaN^kuM nihatya aparAbhyAM shaN^kubhyAmunmucya dakShiNAprAksavyaM parilikhedAntAt agnikShetrAt /

___________________________________________________________


unmucya pUrvasmAd aparasmin pratimucya dakShiNA pratyakparilikhed AntAt  || ˘p¡us_8.10 ||

___________________________________________________________



purvasmAcchaN^koH pratimucyAparasmin pratimucya dakShiNApratyakparilikhedAntAt /

aShTamaH khaNDaH

------

karavindIyA vyAkhyA

saptavidho 'gniH prakR^itiH,. anye 'gnayo vikR^itaya ityuktam, tatraikavidhAdInAM ShaNNAM visheShamAha --

ekavidhAdInAMabhavanti

na bhaveyuH /
kutaH? saptavidhavAkyasheShutvAcchutivipratiShedhAcca /
pakShIbhavatItyAdipucchavidhAyakavAkyasya saptavidhaprakaraNapAThAttaccheShatvAvagateH /
kiJNcaikavidhe pakShAdivibhAgakaraNe vyAyAmamAtratAhAniH vyAyAmamAtrapakShAdikaraNaikavidhatAhAniriti vyAyAmamAtrapakShapucchaikavidhatvavidhAyakayoH shrutyorvirodhAnnaikavidhAdInAM pakShAdayo bhaveyuH /
teShAM karaNopadhAnAdIni ekavidhaprabhR^itInAmityatra vakShyati /
nanu sapakShapuccheShu vidhAbhyAse 'pacaye ca visaptamakaraNIM puruShasthAnIyAM kR^itvA viharedityaShTavidhAdyupacayamate ekavidhAdau apacaye 'pisaptadhA vibhAgaM darshayati /
tatpakShapucchavibhAgArthaM /
itarathA apacayaviShaye 'pacayasyad daShTArthatvaprasaN^gAt /
tenaikavidhAnAmapi bhavatIti gamyate /
tatkathaM teShAM tAni na bhavantIti /
ucyate -- ekavidhaH prathamo 'gniH, taduhavai saptavidhameva cinvItetyevamAdyorvi ruddhArthAbhidhAyinyoHshrutyoHsamucchayAbhAvAdvikalpa evAvakalpate /
tasmAdekavidho vA prathamaH saptavidho vA prathamaH /
tatra yadaikavidhaH prathamaH prakR^itishva; tadA dvitIyAdyahAreShu ekottarA eva dvividhAdayaH prayoktavyAH /
prakR^itibhUtaikavidhe pakShapucchA nAmanAmnAnAdekavidhAdInAM ShaNNAM pakShapucchAni na bhavanti /
saptavidhe tu vidyanta eva /
evamaShTavidhAdInAM tadvikAratvAtteShu ca vidyanta eva /
yadA saptavidhaH prakR^itiH, itare tadvikarArAH tadaikavidhAdayo 'pyaShTavidhavat sapakShapucchA eva bhaveyuH, evaM vidhApacayoktaH saptavidhavibhAgo 'rthavAn bhaviShyati, tatrAtirAtravadvikR^iterapi kadAcit prathamato 'nuShThAnaM ekavidhasya labhyata eva /
asminnapi pakShe ekottaraniyamo 'styeva /
yadaikavidhaH prakR^iti /
prathamamAhAraH, tadAsAvapakShapucchAH /
dvitIyAdiShvAhAreShu dvividhAdayo yAvatsaptavidhamapakShapucchA eva /
saptavidhAdayaHsapakShapucchA eva /
yadaikavidho vikR^itiH prathamAhAraH, tadAsau sapakShapucchaH /
dvitI yAdiShvAhAreShu dvividhAdayaHsarve sapakShapucchA eva /
yadA saptavidhaH prakR^itirvA vikR^itirvA prathamaH, tadA tata UrdhvamaShTavidhAdayaHsaptavidhA eva /
tasmAdekavidhAdInAM ShaNNAmapakShapucchatvaM sapakShapuvchatvamubhayamapyastyeveti sarvamupapannam /
aShTavidhAdiShvekottareShu kathamatiriktasya vibhAga ityata Aha --

aShTavi yeta

asyArthaH -- aShTavidhAdiShvardhAShTamebhyo yadanyadadhikamAgantu tatsaptadhA saptArdhadhA vibhajya pratipuruShaM -- puruShe ShuruShe bhAgamekaikamAveshayet /
ardhamardhe yAvAnagniHsAratniprAdeshaHsaptavidha iti liN^gAl, kutaH? AkR^itivikArasyAshrutatvAt -- shruterabhAvAt pramANAbhAvAdityarthaH /
tatraikasmin puruShakShetre paJNcaviMshatirdve shate ca paJNcadasha bhAgIyAHsherate, AsAM triMshatrriMshatpaJNcadashabhAgIyAH puruShepuruShe prakSheptavyAH /
ardhe paJNcadasha, ayamarthaH -- prakSheptavyaM paJNcadashadhA vibhajya tasya dvibhAga hitaM, puruShaM yaM karoti AkR^iteravikAratvAya sA tasya puruShasya karaNI grahyA /
tAvAnveNurbhavatItyarthaH /

idAnIM vimAnamucyate ----

puru yate

shrutidvayamidam /
atrrekA shrutirdravyApekShaNI, anyA parimANApekShaNI /
tayoH naShTAshvAdagdharathavatsaMprayogaH /
puruShamAtreNa veNunetyarthaH /
yAvAn -- yatparimANo yajamAna UrdhvabhUtabAhuH tatparimANaM yathA chidrayorantarAlaM bhavati tathA veNuchidre kuryAt /
paJNcAratniH puruSha iti vakShyati /
sa caitaddhetukaH /
yUpAvaTasya pashcAt saJNcaramavashiShyAnupR^iShThyaM pR^iShThyAyAM veNuM nidhAya chidreShu shaN^kuM nihatyAparAbhyAM shaN^kubhyAM veNumunmucyAparasmin chidre kIlaM pratikShipya pUrvasmin shaN^kau pratimucya tenaivAparashaN^kumUlAdAramya dakShiNAprAgAntAt parilikhet /
antastasyAH stasyA disho 'ntaH veNunA'rabdhA rekhA yAvaddigantarAbhimukhI bhavati tAvatparili khedityarthaH /


unmucya pUrvasmAc chaN^kor aparasmin shaN^kau pratimucya dakShiNA pratyakpUrvavat parilikhet /



sundararAjIyA vyAkhyA.

ekavidha cca

shrutivipratiShedho vyAmamAtrau pakShau ca pucchaM ca bhavatIti /
caturashraviShayaM caitat /
shyenacidAdayastu sapakShapucchA eva bhavanti, tadAkR^itereva vidheyatvAt /

aShTavidha yet

yadadhikaM saptabhyaH puruShakShetrAN^gulayash ca caturdashasahasrANi catvAri shatAni 14400 /
tAHsaptabhyo 'dhikaiH puruShairhatvA saptabhirvibhajya labdhaM puruShakShetrAN^guliShu saMyojayet /
tAstatra puruShakShetrAN^gulayo j~neyAH /
yathA aShTavidhe purukShetrAN^gulayaH caturdasha sahasrANi catvAri shatAni ca saptabhyo 'dhikenaikena puruSheNa hatvA saptabhirvibhajya labdhaM dve sahasre saptapaJNcAshaccAN^gulayaH paJNcatilayuktAH /
etAH puruShAN^guliShu saMyojayet /
tAstatra puruShakShetrAN^gulayaH ShoDashasahasrANi catvAri shatAni saptapaJNcAshaccAN^gulayaH paJNcatilAdhikAH 16457 ti 5. asya mUlaM aShTAviMshatishatamaN^gulayaH, dashatilAdikAH 128 ti 10. /
etatpuruShasthAnIyasya veNoH pramANamiti hetoH vakShyate /
"vidhAsaptamakaraNIM puruShasthAnIyAM kR^itvA viharediti' /
evaM navavidhe puruShAN^gulIH 14400 dvAbhyAM hatvA saptabhirvibhajya labdhaM catvari sahasrANi shataM caturdashAN^gulayaH dashatilAdhikAH /
tadyuktAH puruShAN^gulayaH aShTAdashA sahasrANi paJNca shatAni caturdasha dashatilAdhikAH 18514 ti 10 tasya mUlaM ShaTtriMshacchatamaN^gulayo dvau tilau 136 ti 2. evaM navavidhe puruShapramANam /
evameva dashAvidhAdiShu draShTavyam /

anyaH prakAraH -- yAvanto 'gneH puruShAH tatsaMkhyayA puruShAN^gulIrhatvA saptabhirvibhajya labdhaM puruShAN^gulayaH pUrvoktA eva ShoDashasahasrANi catvAri shatAni saptapaJNcAshacca paJNcatilAdhikAH 16457 ti 5. /
evaM navavidhAdiShu /
ekasmiMshvAN^gulikShetre tilAHShaTapaJNcAshat shataM sahasraM ca 1156 /
evamaratniprAdesharahitAnAM sapakShapucchAgnonAM puruShaveNush ca /
atra caturashrAgneH prastAvAdekavidhAgnInAM caturashrANAM apakShapucchatvAdaShTavidhaprabhR^itInAmityuktam /
yadA tu shyenacidAdividheHsAdhAraNatvAt "vayasAM vA eSha pratimayA cIyate' ityAkR^itivavidhAnAcca shyenAdyAkAratvena sapakShapucchamakavidhAdInAm /
tadA yannayUnaM saptabhyastatsaptadhA viyajya pratipuruShaM jahyAditi draShTavyam /
tatra vyakta eva vimAgaprakAraH /
tathA sati ekavidhashyenaciti dve sahasre saptapaJNcAshacca paJNcatilayuktAH puruShAN^gulayaH 2057 ti 5 /
tanmUlaM paJNcacatvAriMshadaN^gulayo dvAdasha tilAsh ca /
puruShadvividhe tu puruShAMN^gulayashvatvAri sahasrANi shataM caturdasha ca triMshattilasaMyuktAH /
puruShaveNustu catustilAdhikAshvatuHShaShTiraN^gulayaH /
evaM trividhAdiShu draShTavyam /
yo yatrAgnau purupasthAnIyaH tatra tasya viMshatitamo bhAgo viharaNe iShTakAnAM cAN^guliH kalpyA /
tilAsh ca tasyAshvatustriMshAH /
tatra shlokAH --

vyomAkAshAbdhivedaikAdabhIShTaiH puruShairhatAt /

hareta saptabhirbhAgaM tanmUlaM puruSho bhavet // .1 //


caturashrashyenacitoH prAdeshAratnihInayoH /

tatratatrAN^guliH kalpyA tatra viMshashatAMshataH /
// .2 //


sAratniprAdeshe tu bodhAyanenokto vibhAgaH --

"yadanyatprakR^itestatpaJNcadashabhAgAn kR^itvA vidhAyAM vidhAyAM dvaudvau bhAgau samasyet, tAbhirardhAShTamAbhiragniM cinuyAt' //


ityAdi /
tatra prakAraH -- ardhAShTamebhyo 'dhikaiH puruShaiH puruShAN^gulIshvadurhashasahasrANi catvAri ca shatAni hatvA paJNcadashabhirvibhajya labdhaM dviguNIkR^itya puruShAMN^gulIShu saMyojayet /
tAstatra puruShAN^gulayaH /
yathA ardhanavame puruSheShu puruShAN^gulIrekena hatvA paJNcadashabhirvibhajya labdhaM nava shatAni ShaShTishvAN^gulayaH, tA dviguNAH puruShAN^gulIShu saMyojya dR^iShTAH puruShAN^gulyaH ShoDashasahasrANi trINi shatAni viMshatish ca 16320. tanmUlaM tatra puruShapramANaM pAdonAShTaviMshatishatamaN^gulayaH /
evamardhadashapuruShe aShTAdasha sahasrANi dve shate catvAriMshacca puruShakShetrAN^gulayaH /
puruShaveNush ca paJNcatriMshacchatAN^gulayaH tiladvayAdhikA ityAdi draShTavyam /
ye tvapakShapucchAH praugacidAdayaH teShvaratniprAdeshairyukteShu viyukteShu caivameva puruShamAnIya tasya viMshatishatatamabhAgamaN^guliM prakalpya viharaNamiShTakAsh ca /
yathA praugaciti -- 14400. ekavidhe ekaM sahasraM catushvatvAriMshacchatAN^gulayaH ShaTtilonAH puruShaH, tasya viMshatishatatamo bhAgaH tatrAN^gulirityAdi /
tatra shlokau ------

khAkAshashrutivedaikAt ShuruShairdviguNairhatAt /

hareta tithibhirbhAgaM tanmUlaM puruSho bhavet // .1 //


caturashrashyenacitoH prAdeshAratniyuktayoH /

praugAdiShu caivaM syAtpuruShAN^gulaklTaptaye // .2 //


ye tvaratniprAdeshavR^iddhiM nityAmAhuH teShAmetatsUtre bodhAyanenokter'the kleshena yojayitavyaM syAt -- saptabhyaHsArdhasaptabhya iti, evaM saptavidhA ardhAShTamavidheti, evamuttaratra vidhAsaptamakaraNImiti /
atrAdhikAnAM puruShANAM pratipuruShamAveshanamuktam /
tatra hetumAha --

AkR^iti tvAt

prakR^ityA anyAkR^itervikArasya shrutyabhAvAt /
yadi tvadhikAH puruShAH kacidevaikasmin pradeshe Atmani pakShe vA nidhIyeran /
prakR^itirhyagnyAkR^itirvikriyate /

puruSha yate

puruShamAtreNa -- yAvAn puruSha UrdhvabAhustAvatA veNunAgniM vimimIta iti shrutidvayasyArthaH /

yAvAnatIyam

bAhyacchidrAbhbhAM bahiHsasasaukaryArthamupAhriyate chidrayosh ca bAhyArthe /

apareNa dAntAt

apareNa yUpAvaTadeshaM saJNcaramavashiShyaiva veNunidhAnam /
AntAdarvAkcakShurnimitAccaturashrapUrvAntAdunmucya pUrvasmAdaparasmin pratimucya dakShiNA pratyakparilikhedAntAt /

aShTamaH khaNDaH.

--------

kapardikShAShyam

___________________________________________________________


unmucya veNuM madhyame shaN^kAv antyaM veNosh chidraM pratimucyoparyupari lekhAsamaraM dakShiNA veNuM nidhAyAntye chidre shaN^kuM nihatya tasmin madhyamaM veNosh chidraM pratimucya lekhAntayor itare pratiShThApya chidrayoH shaN^kU nihanti  || ˘p¡us_9.1a ||

___________________________________________________________



dakShiNe shaN^kau anyataraM veNoshchidraM pratimucyoparyuparilekhAsambhedaM dakShiNAgraM veNuM nidhAya antye chidre shaN^kuM nihatya tamin shN^kakakakau

madhyamaM veNoshchidraM pratimucya lekhAntarayorantara chidrepratiShThApya chidrayorlekhAntayoreva shaN^kU nihanti /


___________________________________________________________


sa puruShash caturashraH  || ˘p¡us_9.1b ||

___________________________________________________________



sa caturashraH puruShaH //


___________________________________________________________


evaM puradakShiNaM catura Atmani puruShAnavamimIte  || ˘p¡us_9.2a ||

___________________________________________________________



evaM catvAri puruShakShetrANi Atmani yathA bhavanti tathA pradakShiNaM minuyAt /


___________________________________________________________


puruShaM dakShiNe pakShe | puruShaM pucche puruSham uttare  || ˘p¡us_9.2b ||

___________________________________________________________



dakShiNe pakShe -- dakShiNe pArshve /
madhyameShu triShu veNuM pratimucya aparAbhyAmityAdi pUrvavaccaturashraH puruShaH /
evamuttarapakShe uttarapArshve, madhyameShveva triShu pratimucya uttaram /
pucche tu pAshvAtyamadhayamashaN^kau madhyamaM veNocchidraM pratimucya tiryagveNuM nidhAya chidrayoHshaN^kU nihatyonmucyottarAbhyAM prasavyaM parilikhet /
dakShiNasmAdunmucyottarasmin puruShamAtre shaN^kau pratimucyAntyacchidrashaN^kuprabhR^iti pradakShiNaM parilikhet /
unmucya veNuM madhyame pratimucya uparyupari lekhAsambhedaM pashcAdveNuM nidhAya antya ityAdi samAnaM tatpuccham /


___________________________________________________________


aratninA dakShiNato dakShiNam ity uktam  || ˘p¡us_9.2c ||

___________________________________________________________



evaM vimitasya dakShiNapakShasya dakShiNataH uttarasyottarataH aratninA vardhayet, pakShayostirya«bhAnI sAratnanipuruShamAtrA pArshva mAnI ca puruShamAtraM, evaM pucchasya pashcAdapi prAdeshena vitastyA vA vardhayet, tattatsupArshvamAnI sa prAdeshaH puruShaH, puruShamAtre tirya«bhAnI //


___________________________________________________________


pR^iShThyAto vA puruShamAtrasyAkShNayA veNuM nidhAya pUrvasminn itaram | tAbhyAM dakShiNaM aMsaM nirharet | viparyasya shroNI  || ˘p¡us_9.3a ||

___________________________________________________________



aparasmin shaN^kau puruShamAtra pratimucya dakShiNAM shroNiM udagapasAryottarAmeva shroNiM viharet /


___________________________________________________________


pUrvavad uttaram aMsam  || ˘p¡us_9.3b ||

___________________________________________________________


gatametat /

karavindIyA vyAkhyA

aparasmAdunmucya veNuM madhyame shaN^kAvanyaM veNoshchidraM pratimucya uparyuparilekhAsamaraM veNuM nidhAya /
lekhAsamaraH -- lekhAyAHsaMpAtaH /
tasyopariShTAt sannikR^iShTaM nidhAyAntyachidre shaN^kUnnihatya tasmin madhyamaM veNoshchidraM pratimucya lekhAntayoritare chidre pratiShThApya chidrayoHshaN^kuM niranti sa caturashraH puruShasaMj~no bhavati, evaM pradakShiNaM caturaH puruShAnAtmani kuryAt /
pashcime shahkAvevaM veNoshchidraM pratimucya pashcAdanupR^iShThyaM veNuM nidhAya pashcimayorapi chidrayorapi shaN^kuM nikhAya pUrvavaddvitIyaM puruShaM kuryAdevamuttarato 'pi uttarApratyaguttarAprAkcAlikhya puruShadvayaM vimimIte /
apareNa yUpAvaTateshaM saJNcaramavashiShya pR^iShThyAyAM shaN^kuM nihatya tasmin veNoshchidraM pratimucya pR^iShThyAyAM veNuM nipAtya chidrayordvai shaN^kU /
pashcime shaN^kau veNoH chidraM pratimucya pR^iShThyAyAmeva pashcAnnanipAtya dvau shaN^kU /
evaM paJNca shaN^kavaH /
madhyamapUrvayoHsha«vkoH pratimucya ullikhya pUrvavatpuruSha dvayaM kuryAt /
udakShimata upAntyayoH chidraM pratimucya ullikhya dakShiNapakShe puruShaM uttarata upAntyayoH pratimucya uttarapakShe puruShaNTapucche tu pashcime shaN^kau veNormadhyamachidraM pratimucya dakShiNottaraM veNuM nidhAya chidrayoHshaN^kuM nihatya tayoshchidraM pratimucya pashcimottaraM pashcimadakShiNaM cAlikhya puruShaM kuryAt /
evaM kR^itvA AratnaninA dakShiNato dakShiNaM pakShaM pravardhayati /
uttaramapi pakShamuttarato 'ratninaiva prAdeshena vitastyA vA pashcAt pucchaM pravardhayati //


pR^iShThyA masaM vA shabdo vikalpArthaH /
evamiha veNumAnam /
dvau tAvadveNU bhavataH /
tayorakeH puruShamAtraH /
anyaH puruShamAtrasyAkShNayA rajjusamaH /
tAbhyAM vimAnamapareNa yupAvaTadeshaM saJNcaramavashiShyate /
pR^iShThyAyAM shaN^kuH /
tataH pashcAt tAvanmAtre shaN^kuH /
madhyamashaN^kAvakShNayAmAtraM veNuM pratimucya pUrvasmin puruShamAtraM prati mucya tAbhyAM dakShiNamaMsaM nirharet /
puruShamAtraM pUrvasmAdunmucyAparasmin pratismin pratimucyottaramaMsaM dAkShaNottarapashcimamadhyamashaN^kUnAM pArshvadvayeShvarddhapuruShamAtreShu shaN^kuM nihatya pukShapucchapuruShAnapyevameva kuryAt //


unmucya nihanti

samaraH -- saN^gamaH pUrvApare chidre lekhayoryatra nipatatastAveva lekhAntau /

sa vamimIte

pR^iShThyAyAM pUrvayoshcaturashrayoH pAshvAtyashaN^kuH aparayoH paurastyaH /

puruShaMapakShe

dAkShiNAtyAnAM paJNcAnAM shaN^kUnAM madhyameShu triShu veNuMpratimucya aparAbhyAmityAdi /

puruShaM pacche

pAshvAtyAnAM trayANAM dakShiNayorantye chidre pratimucya madhyame chidre shaN^kuM nihanyAt /
evamuttarayorevaM sthitAnAM paJNcAnAM madhye madhyameShu triShu veNuM pratimucyottarAbhyAmityAdi draShTavyam /

puruShamuttare

dakShiNapakShavat /

aratninA tyuktam

veNoH paJNcame lakShaNaM kR^itvA tena pakShau pravardhayet, evaM dashame lakShaNaM kR^itvA /
pucchaM prakArAntaramAha ----

pR^iShThyAnto maMsaM dvAvatra veNU ubhyatashchidau, puruShamAtraHsavisheShash ca /
pR^iShThyAyAM puruShAntarAlAn trIn shaN^kUnnihatya madhyame savisheShaM pratimucya pUrvasminnitaraM tayorantye cchidre yatra saMpatataHsa dakShiNAMsaH /

viparyasya puruShamAtraM pAshvAtye pratimucya shroNI pUrvavaduttarAMsaH /
evaM pakShapuccheShvapi /
savisheSho veNuHsaptatishatamaN^gulayo dashatilonAH /

rajjvA vA vimAyottaravedinyAyena veNunA vimimIte  || ˘p¡us_9.4 ||

sapakShapuccheShu vidhAbhyAse 'pacaye ca vidhAsaptamakaraNIM puruShasthAnIyAM kR^itvA viharet  || ˘p¡us_9.5 ||

___________________________________________________________



vidhAbhyAse 'ShTavidhaprabhR^itayaH /
vidhApacaye ekavidhAdayaH /
teShvekavidhAdiShu vidhAsaptamakaraNI yena veNunA vimimIte tadardhAShTamaM bhavati /
sa puruShasthAnIyaH /
evaM caturashraM kR^itvA pUrvavadvibhajya viharet /
sapakShapuccheShviti vacanamekavidhAnArtham /
eteShvekavidhA diShu shyenAdiShu kriyamANeShu yadyekavidhA tatpaJNcadashadhA vibhajya dvau bhAgau samasya caturashraM kR^itvA tasya mAnena veNunA gR^ihNIyAt /
sa puruShasthAnIyaH /
evaM sarvatra /
yAvadvidhaM tatkShetraM samacaturashraM kR^itvA tasya pramANaM gR^ihNIyAt; yathA catvAri sahasrANyashItitilAH (4080) puruShaH /
teShAM vargaH-ekA koTiH ShaTShaShTirniyutAni catvAryayutAni ShaTsahasrANi catvAri shatAni (16646400) yadyaShTavidhaH aShTabhirguNayitvA pUrvArdhaM saMyojya paJNcadashalabdhaM dviguNIkR^itya mUlaM gR^ihNIyAt /
sa tasya puruSho bhavati /
apacaye tvardhasaMyogo nAsti /
aratripAdeshAbhAvAt /
anyatsarvamuvacayena tulyam /
ardhatilena vA UnAdhike vA doSho na bhavati visheShA darshanAt /
tatra shlokaH --

AkAshavasvambaraveda (4080) varga

miShTapravR^iddhaM tithibhirvibhaktam /

labdhasya vR^iddhasya yamena mUlaM vR^iddhau kShaye tatpuruShasya mAnam //


sadA bhavetsApacayeca vR^iddhau ...... //


iti /

nanvekavidhAdayaH shyenAdayo vakrapakShapucchAH kartavyA iti pratipAditam /
tasmAtkiM mahatA prayatnena hetUnAM darshanena? satyametat! kartavyA ekavidhAdaya iti kR^itvA vkacitteShu yadyekavidhAdayaH kartavyAH tadA kratvarthakatayopAdIyante /
tadA shyenAdaya AkR^itivikArAH puruShAtmakAH santaH tadvikR^ityAdhishayeran /
yathA puruShamAtratAM vikR^itya pakShapucchAnAM saptArdhavidhe shyenAdayaH pravartante evaM puruShaM vikR^itya ekavidhAdiShu nivisheran /
tatra yadA sapakShapucchatvamekavidhAdInAM tadAyaM vidhiriti aShTavidhaprabhR^itInAmapi mArgAntareNa vidhAnAdadoShaH /
sapakShapucchoShviti vidhAnAt /
praugAdiShvekavidhAdayo na santi /
aShTavidhAdayash ceti kecit /
vakShyati ca "yAvAnAgniHsAratniprAdesha' iti /
apare punarekavidhAdiShu na santi nApacayeShviti varNayanti /
sAratriprAdesha iti vacanAt //


karavindIyA vyAkhyA

(rajjvA mimIte)

athavA ekarajjvAdInAmanyatamayA rajvAgniM vimAya pashcAdadR^iShTArthaM veNunA vimimIte /
uttaravedinyAyena yathottaravediryugenayajamAnasya vA padairvimAya shamyayA parimimIte adR^iShTArthaM; evamatrApi rajjvA vimAya veNunA mAnamadR^iShTArthaM syAt, tathottaravedivikAratvAdagneH rajjvA vimAya veNunA shamyayA cAdR^iShTArthaM vimAnaM bhavediti //


sapakSha -- ret

sapakShapuccheShu praugAdivyatirikteShvagniShvabhyAse 'ShTavidhAdAvapacaye caikavidhAdau caikavidhAdau vidhAvidhAnaM karaNInAmucyate vidhAsaptamakaraNIM puruShasthAnIyAM kR^itvA viharet /
yAvatyo 'gnervidhAHsanti tAsAM saptamaM yA karoti sA vidhA saptamakaraNI tAM puruShasthAnIyAM kR^itvA tayA'tmapakShapucchAni viharediti /
ayamarthaH -- yadyekavidho 'gniH ; tamekavidhaM paJNcadashadhA vibhajya dvau bhAgau samasya samacaturashraM kR^itvA tasya pramANaM puruShakthAne kR^itvA anenAtmapakShapucchAni viharediti /
evameva dvividhAdiShu kuryAt /
catvAri sahasrANyashItish ca tilAH puruShaH /
teShAM varga ekA koTiH ShaTprayutAni ShaNNiyutAni catvAryayutAni ShaTsasrANi catvAri shatAni (16646400) yadyaShTavidhaM puruShavargamaShTabhirguNitvA pUrvarAshyarghena ca saMyojya tatpaJNcadashabhirvibhajya labdhaM dviguNIkR^itya mUle gR^ihIte sa tasya puruSho bhavati /
apacaye tvaratniprAdeshAnAmabhAvAt nArdhasaMyogaH //
itaradupacayavat. /
nanvekavidhaprabhR^itInAM na prakShapucchAni bhavantItyuktaM satyamuktam /
tadvyAyAmamAtrarUpatvena ekavidhAdau na ghaTata ityevamarthamidamiti tatraiva vyAkhyAtam /
ekavidhaprakR^ititvapratipAdanAya ca /
tasmAnnAtyantaniShedhaH, ekavidhaprabhR^itInAmapi pakShapucchAni bhavantyeva //


atra shlokamudAharanti --

AkAshavasvambaravedavarga

miShTapravR^iddhaM tithimirvibhaktam /

tasya pravR^iddhasya yamena mUlaM sambhAvayetsApacaye ca vR^iddhau //


iti ----

sundararAjIyA vyAkhyA

rajjvA mimIte

Asmin pakShe shamyAmAnavadadR^iShTArthaM veNumAnam /
athAShTavidhAdInAmekavidhAdInAM ca viharaNamAha //


sapakSha ret

sapakShapucchA agnayaH caturashrashyenakaN^kacidalajacitash ca /
tatrAShTavidhAdiShu vidhAnAmabhyAsaH /
ekavidhAdiShvapacayaH /
vidhAnAM (ekIbhUtAnAM) samastAnAM saptamasya karaNI vidhAsaptamakaraNI /
cIyamAnasyAgneryoM'shaH tasya karaNI puruShasthAnIyA /
sA cAShTavidhaprabhR^itInAmityatraiva pradarshitA /
atrApi sArAtniprAdeshapakShe vidhArdhAShTamakaraNImiti draShTavyam /
apacayavacanaM shyenacidAdyartham /
caturashrANAmekavidhAdInAmapakShapucchatvAt /
pUrvatra puruShAveshanamuktaM, idAnIM tasya viharaNamucyate ityato na punaruktiH /
yadvA pUrvasUtramaShTavidhAdiviShayaM caturashraviShayaM ca /
DadamekavidhAdInAM shyenAdInAM ca sAdhAraNamityasti visheShaH /
idaM cAnena j~nAyate -- shyenacidAdayo guNavikArAHsaptavidhAdivadekavidhAdiShvapi bhavanti /
shakhAntarIyatvaM ca tasya pUrvamevoktam /
ata eva tasya pakShasya yatnasAdhyatvAt tatraivopadhAna prakAro vakShyate -- "yAvAnagniHsAratniprAdeshaH' ityAdi /

kapardibhAShyam

tAsAmeveShTakAnAM (katipayA) ekato 'dhyardhA ardhenAdhikAstAsAM karaNaM tR^itIyaM triprAdeshA pArshvamAnI aratnimAtrA tirya«bhAnI dvitIyasya karaNasya /

sarvataH prAdeshas tac caturtham | samacaturashrAH paJNcadashabhAgIyAs tat paJNcamam  || ˘p¡us_9.6c ||

___________________________________________________________


aShTAN^gulena kArikAstatpaJNcamaM karaNam /
samacaturashrA iti kimarthamiha saN^guhaNam? yasminnagnau samacaturashrA eveShTakAH tatrApyAsAM pravesho yathA syAdityevamartham /
vakShyati ca "aNUkAH paJNcadashabhAgIyAnAM sthAna' iti /
aNUkapaJNcadashabhAgIyayorekaviShayatvam /

karavindIyA vyAkhyA

(karaNAni kArayet)

idAnImiShTakAnAM karaNAnyucyante -- pAribhAShikaH puruShaH paJNcAratniH /
tasya paJNcamenAratninA /
paJNcamenoti jAtAvekavacanam /
paJNcamairityarthaH /
kArayetkushalaiH /
tairaratnibhishcaturbhiH prathamaM karaNam

tAsA -- tIyam

tAsAM paJNcamakR^itAnAmeveShTakAnAM yA ekataH -- ekasmin bhAge 'dhyarthAratnayAyAmAH tAsAM karaNaM cattaddvitIyaM kArayet /
tAsAmeveti sarvatra saMbadhyate //


puru -- tIyam

yAsAmekasmin pArshve caturviMshatyaN^gulayaH ekato dvAdashAN^gulayastAsAM yatkaraNaM tattR^itIyam /

sarvar -- tham

yAsAM sarvataH prAdeshaH pramANaM tAsAM yatkaraNaM taccatirtham /
sarvato grahaNaM prAdeshagrahaNena vkacidghuhaNaM sUcayati /

sama -- JNcamam

puruShasya paJNcadashabhAgo 'ShTAN^gulayaH /
tena parimitAH paJNcadashabhAgIyA iShTakAH ITR^ishAHsamacaturashrAH, tAsAM yatkaraNaM tatpaJNcamam /
samacaturashragrahaNAdeva paJNcadashabhAgIyAnAM kAryeNUkAdayaH prAptAH /
tatra prAgudakpashcimeShu caturashratvaniyamo nAstIti j~nAyate /
dvitIyAdivyavahAraH kimarthaH? adR^irShTArthameva /
tathopadhAnAdiShu darshanAt /

sundararAjIyA vyAkhyA

athaivaM vimitasyAgneriShTakAkaraNAnyAha --

karaNAni kArayet

ekamidaM karaNaM aratnimAtraM samacaturashram /

tAsA tIyaM ShaTtriMshikA pArshvamAnI, tirya«bhAnI catuviMshikaiva /

puruShya tIyaM evamardheShTakAH /

(sarvataHatpaJNcam)

aShTAN^gulAH /

yat pacyamAnAnAM pratihrasIta purISheNa tat sampUrayed aniyataparimANatvAt purIShasya  || ˘p¡us_9.8 ||

pacyamAnAnAmiShTakAnAmutsedhatash ca parimANatash ca pratihrAso bhavettatpurISheNa pUrayet /
kuta ityAha -- aniyataparimANatvAtpurIShasya -- niyataparimANA iShTakAH aniyataparimANaM purISham /

karavindIyA vyAkhyA

Urdhva -- yet

sarvAsAmiShTakAnAmUrthvApramANamutsedhaM jAnupaJNcamena kArayet /
aN^gulyadhikAre dvAtriMshajjAnuriti bodhAyanaH /
tasya paJNcamaM ShaDaN^gulayaH ardhacaturadashAstilAsh ca /
tena saMmitamiShTakAnAm UrdhvapramANaM bhavati /
jAnudaghnaM cinvIta prathamaM cinvAnaH, paJNca citayo bhavantIti shrutyoHsamAveshAdUrdhvapramANe samaM syAdashrutatvAditi jAnupaJNcamA iShTakA bhaveyuH /
jAnudviguNA nAbhiH /
jAnutriguNamAsyam /
jAnudaghne sahasrA iShTakAH nAbhidaghne dvisAhasrA dviprastArAsh ca /
Asyadaghne triShAhasrAH triprastArAsh ca /
tatra sarvatra visheShAshravaNAt jAnupaJNcamamevordhvapramANamiShTakAnAm /
iShTakAnAM kArayediti ihAnuvartamAne punarapi tayorgrahaNaM gArhapatyadhiShNayeShTakAnAmapi jAnupaJNcamatvAya /

ardhena -- Shasya

ardhena paJNcacArdhenana kArayedityeva /
nAkasadashvUDopadhAnamantravisheShAH /
tairupadheyAH /
paJNcapaDhceShTakA jAnupa§vramasyordhena kAryAH uttarA "nAkasadbhaya upadadhAti' /
ityekasmin prastAre tAsAmuttarAdharabhAvadarshanAt /
iShTakAbhirakeva jAnudaghnAdisAmpAdanAt, purIShopadhAnImaShTakA samIkaraNArthe citervR^iddhayarthaM ca /

yatpacya Shasya

karaNaparik ptAnAM iShTakAnAM pAkavashAt pratihrAsaH -- kShaya upajAyate /
tatpurISheNa pUrayet, anenShTakA na duShyanti avarjanIyatvAt, tasya "mitraitAM paceti' liN^gAt, vAtAtapAbhyAmapi shoShaNaM pAka eva /
ata eva pAkavashAddhInamiShTakAyAmavistArobhayamupadhAnakAle purISheNa pUrayet /
kutaH? aniyataparimANatvAt purIShasya /
na hyetAvat purIShaM prakShepaNIyamiti niyamaH /
tasmAtpAkavashAddhInasya purISheNa pUraNameva /
jalArdrA mR^it purIShaM /
teneShTakAnAM hrAsaM pUrayet /

sundararAjIyA vyAkhyA

Urdhva kArayet

"triMshadaN^gulaM jAnuH, ityAgniveshyaH /
tasya paJNcamaM ShaDaN^gulam, "ShaDaN^gulotsedhA, ityeva kAtyAyanaH /

ardhena ca

trayaN^gulena /

yatpacya Shasya

shuShyamANAnAM sarveShAmetadupalkShaNam /

upadhAne 'dhyardhA dasha purastAt pratIcIr Atmany upadadhAti | dasha pashcAt prAcIH  || ˘p¡us_10.1a ||

Atpranyeva pashcAdbhAge tA eveShTakAH tatsaMkhyAkAH prAcIH -- prAgAyatAH /

paJNcapaJNca pakShAgrayoH | pakShApyayayosh ca vishayAs tAsAm ardheShTakAmAtrANi pakShayor bhavanti  || ˘p¡us_10.1b ||

___________________________________________________________



paJNcapaJNca pakShAgrayordakShiNAyatAH udagAyatAsh ca /
vishayAsh ca paJNca codagAyatAH dakShiNAyatAsh ca /

paJNcapaJNca pucchapArshvayor dakShiNA udIcIsh ca  || ˘p¡us_10.1c ||

___________________________________________________________



paJNcapaJNcadhyardhA dakShiNAyatA udagAyatAsh ca yathA samIpe pradeshamAtramavashiShyate tathopadheyAH /

karavindIyA vyAkhyA

upa cIH

upadhAnakAlo dvatIyakaraNotpannA iShTakAH Atmani pUrvAnte dashopadadhyAt /
pratIcIH pratyagAyAtAH udIcIriti /
tA eva esha pashcAt prAcIH Atmani pashcimAnte prAgAyAtAH tA eva /

paJNca yAH

tA eva prAcyau rItyau /
pakShApyayayosh ca vishayAH /
pakShApyayaH -- pakShamUlaM vividhamAtmani pakShe ca sherata iti vishayAH /

tAsAM kiyadAtmani kiyatpakSha ityAha --

tAsAManti

AtmAnamaratninA pradeshena pakShamityarthaH /
prAcyau rItyau //


paJNca cIsh ca

pucchapArshvayoH paJNcapaJNca uttarA dakShiNAmukhAH dakShiNA uttarAmukhAH prAcyau rItyau! uttarasUtre bhedAmAvAya pucchAgraprAdeshasyApR^ithaggrItitA pratipAdayiShyate /
ata etA agraprabhR^ityupadheyAH //

pratIcIH pratyagAyatAH /

___________________________________________________________


pucche prAdesham upadhAya sarvam agniM paJNcamabhAgIyAbhiH pracchAdayet  || ˘p¡us_10.2 ||

___________________________________________________________


___________________________________________________________


paJNcadashabhAgIyAbhiH saN^khyAM pUrayet  || ˘p¡us_10.3 ||

___________________________________________________________



pucche prAdeshamupadhAya AtmasamIpe yadavashiShTaM tatprAdeshamatrArdheShTakAdvayaM madhye abhitaH prAdeshAH ShaT /
ShaTsu vitastyA ca virdhanamuktaM kathaM prAdeshamAtramupadhAyeti? ucyate -- yadyapi vitastyA vardhanamuktaM, tathApi karaNAntarasya vidhAnAt prAdeshakShetrameveShTakAbhishvetavyamiti yadaN^gulimAtraM parigR^ihItaM tatpuraShiNe pUrayitavyam /
amumevArtaM pradarshayituM prAdeshamupadhAyetyuktam /
sarvamagnimiti -- paJNcAshadadhyardhaH sUtroktAH pUccher'dheShTakAdvayaM pracchAdayet /
dashettaraM shataM paJNcamabhAgIyaH sherate /
pUrvAbhiHsahAShTaShaShTayadhikaM shatam /
paJNcadasheti -- ekasminpaJNcamabhAgIyAkShetre nava paJNcadashabhAgIyAHsherate /
catasraH paJNcamabAgIyA navadhA vibhajya yatra vkApi paJNcadashabhAgIyAH kSheptavyAH tatrApi mantrepadhAnasaukaryArthaM prAdesha ucyate /
Atmani dvitIyarItyAM madhye dvayamapahAyAShTAdasha /
aShTamyAM ca rItyAM aShTAdasha /
evaM dvishataH prastAraH //


karavindIyA vyAkhyA

pucche dayet

pucche yatpuruShAdhikaM prAdeshakShetraM tadupadhAya sarvamagniM paJNcamabhAgIyAbhiH pracchAdayet /
ayamAshayaH -- Atmapat pucche ca purastAtprabhR^iti paJNcamabAgIyAbhiH pracchAdyamAne 'gre prAdeshamavishiShyate /
asmin yogAbhiriShTakAbhirupahite pucche ca bahavo bhedA bhavantIti matvA AcAryaH tatparihArAyAgramArabhya pucche prAdeshopadhAnapUrvakaM pracchAdayediti /
yadvA -- prAdeshaM pucche upadhAya -- pucche saMyojya yathA prAdeshaM pucchAt pR^ithaggrIti na bhavati tathA kR^itvetyarthaH /
yadvA prAdeshaM puccha upadhAya pucche nidhAya sthApayitvA, "tAsAM ShaTTapradhA upadhAyoti' vat /
yadvAgragataM prAdeshaM pucchamUle nidadhyAt /
bhedaM viparyasye tarata upadadhyAditi /
tadayamarthaH -- yAvatA vacanavyaktiH sarvathA bhedAbhAvAya pucchAgraM pucchAt pR^ithagrItiM na kuryAt iti tAtparyArtha iti /
sarveShu pakSheShu atiriktaM prAdeshaM pucchapUle 'nupahitamavashiShyate /
tadabhitaH prAdeshAbhirardheShTakAbhirupadadhayAt /
kiJNca uparitanaprastAre "yathA prathame prastAre pakShau tathA pucchamiti' vacanAt pucchamUle 'tideshaprAptAnAmadhyardhAnAM vaiparItyaM vakShyati -- "viparItA apyayA' iti /
taccaivamupadhAne samaJNjajasaM syAt /
itarathA viruddhArthamanartaM ca syAt /
tasmAt



pucche prAdeshamupadhAyetyasya bhAgasyAyamevArtho grAhyaH /
nanu kathaM sarvasyAgneH paJNcadashabhAgIyAbhiH pracchAdanam? ucyate -- atropahitAnAmiShTakAnAmabAdhena sarvasminnagnau paJNcamabhAgIyAbhiH pracchAdyAmAne tadekadeshe tAsAmasambhave satyAkhyAtAnAmarthaM bruvatAM shaktiH sahakAriNI nahi vacanashatenApyashaN^kanIyArthaHshakyo vidhAtumiti caturashrAbhiH pracchAdayitumashakyatvAt prathamapratItasarvashabdAnurodhena jaghanyaH paJNcamabhAgIyAshabdo bAhulyAbhiprAyo varNanIyaH /
tena tattatsahakAriNIbhiratratyAbhiH sambhavantIbhirapi pracchAdanaM kAryamityevamarthaM prAdeshAnAmatra prAptiH /
eSha nyAyastatrAN^gIkaraNIyaH /
tatratyAbhiranuraktAbhirapi pracchAdane kiM vAr'dheShTakAH karaNenotpannAH na kutracidviniyuktAH /
tAsAmupadeshabalAdeva atra saMkhyApUraNe pracchAdane ca yathAyogaM viniyogaH kAryaH /
kiJNca yaccaturashraM trayashri vA sampadyetArdheShTakAbhiH pAdeShTakAbhirvA pracchAdayediti paribhAShAM vakShyati /
tathA vAtra samupadhAnaM syAt /
atrAtmani sandhyantarAle catvAriMshat paJNcamabhAgIyAstAsAM purastAddasha pashcAcca dasha /
pakShayorviMshatiH pucche dasha /
tA etA dashottarashataM paJNcamabhAgIyAH, paJNcAshadardhAshcatasror'dhAH dvau prAdeshAviti ShaTShaShThiH shataM ceShTakAH /
"sAhasraM cinvIta prathamaM cinvAna' ityAdibhirvAkyaiH pratyagnIShTakAnAM sAhasrAdayaHsaMkhyA vidhAsyante /
tAsh ca praticiti pratiprastAraM ca bhidyAnta iti ca tatraiva pratipAdayiShyate /
sA sahasrasaMkhyA kathamatra sampAdyetyAha //


paJNca rayet

paJNcadashabhAgIyAbhiraShTAN^gulAbhiHsaMkhyA pUrayet /
kA saMkhyAtra pUryate? kiM samudAyagatA? uta prastAragatA avisheShAt? na samudAyagatA AnantaryAt, pratiprastAraM shatadvayaniyamAcca, prastAragataiva saMkhyA tatra pUryate, asya vacanasya sAmarthyAdavasIyate saMkhyApUraNaM upadhAnAya pracchAdikAsu kAsAMciduddharaNaM pracAlanaM vA yathAyogaM nyAyyamiti /
atra prastArashatadvayasampattaye catustriMshatsaMkhyAsampAdyA /
sA ca pracchAditAsu kAshviduddhR^itya yogneShTakopadhAnena bhavati /
tatraikasmin paJNcamabhAgIyAkShetre nava paJNcadashabhAgIyAHsherata iti /
tatratatropadhAne deshAniyame taduddharaNena tAsAmupadhAne kArye mantropadhAnasaukaryAya uddharaNopadhAnadeshaniyama ucyate /
tatrAsmani prAcyo dasha rItayaH, tatra madhyamarItyoH dvitIye uddhR^itya tatra aShTAdasha paJNcadashabhAgIyA Avapet /
tayoreva rItyorupAnte uddhR^ityAShTAdasha Avapet /
pucche catasnaH prAcyo rItyaH, tatra madhyamayoranta uddhR^itya catasror'dheShTakA udIcIrupadadhyAt /
evaM dvishataH prastAraH pUryate /
atraike pucchAgre dasha prAdeshAnupadhAya paJNcamabhAgIyAbhiH pracchAdayanti, teShAM ca viparItavacanAnarthakyaprasaN^go maidaprasaN^gash ca bhavatIti tathA nopadheyAH /
kiJNca -- yadi pucchAgre prAdeshAnAmupadhAnamapIShTamabhaviShyattarhi pAdeShTakAshcaturmAgIyAnAM pakShAgrayoH paJNcadasha pucchAgra iti ca spaShTataraM pucchAgra ityevAvakShyat /
na caivamuktaM /
tasmAduktavidha evopadhAnakrama iti sthitam //


sundararAjIyA vyAkhyA

pucchAdavashiShTaM prAdeshakShetraM yAmiriShTakAbhirmedaparihAreNopadhAtuM shakyate tAbhirupadadhyAt /
tatra pArshvayordve prAdeshamAtrayau madhye catasror'dheShTakA udagAyatAH /
etadeva prAdeshakaraNasya prayojanam /
ataH prAdeshAbhAvena kiyate /
shiShTAgnau paJNcamabhAgIyAbhiH pracchAdite ShaTShaShTishatamiShTakA bhavanti /
aratniprAdesharahite paJNcAshacchataM iShTakA bhavanti /
tatra AtmanyudIcye nava rItayaH /
tatra Atmani madhyamAyAM madhyamAshcatasra uddhR^itya catuHpaJNcAshannidheyAH /
ubhayatrApi pucchAgre dve paJNcamyAvuddhR^itya catasror'dheShTakA upadheyA udagAyatAH /
evaM dvishataH prastAraH //


kapardibAShTam

___________________________________________________________


aparasmin prastAre 'dhyardhA dasha dakShiNata udIcIr Atmany upadadhAti | dashottarato dakShiNAH  || ˘p¡us_10.4a ||

___________________________________________________________



Atmani dakShiNata utIcIrudagAyatAH dashAdhyardhAH upadadhAti AtmanyevottarataH dashadhyardhAH dakShiNAyatAH /

___________________________________________________________


yathA prathame prastAre pakShau tathA puccham | yathA pucchaM tathA pakShau viparItA apyaye  || ˘p¡us_10.4b ||

___________________________________________________________


pucchAgre pashcAdadhyardhAH prAgAyatAH /
dakShiNe pakShe pashcAt paJNca prAgAyatAH purastAcc paJNca /
ShaTpratyagAyatAH /
uttarapakShe caivaM prAgAyatAH

pratyagAyatAsh ca /
pucchApyaye 'dhyardhAH paJNca prAgAyatAH pratyagAyatAsh ca /
pucchApyaye 'dhyarthAH paJNca prAgAyatAH /
tAsAmardheShTakAmAtrA Atmani bhavanti /
evaM viparItA apyaye /
tAsAM purastAtpaJNcArdheShTakA udIcyaH /

___________________________________________________________


sarvam agniM paJNcamabhAgIyAbhiH pracchAdayet  || ˘p¡us_10.5 ||

___________________________________________________________


___________________________________________________________


paJNcadashabhAgIyAbiH saN^khyAM pUrayet  || ˘p¡us_10.6a ||

___________________________________________________________



gatametat /
pUrvavaddvishataH prastAraH /

karavindIyA vyAkhyA

apara NAH

dvitIye prastAre 'dhyardhA Atmano dakShiNe bhAge dashopadadhyAduttare dasha //


yathApra kShau

prathamaprastAre yathA pakShAvupahitau tathA pucche /
yathA pucchamupahitaM tathA pakShayoH /
etaduktaM bhavati -- pucchAgre pucchAgrasandhau paJNca paJNcAdhyardhA upadheyAH /
pakShayostu pArshvayoH adhyardhA upadheyAH, tatra visheShamAha --

viparItA  pyaye

pucchApyaye pakShApyayavadatideshaprAptAnAmadhyardhAnAM Atmani aratni mAtratvaM puccher'dheShTakAmAtratvaM ca prAptotItyata Aha /
atra viparItA bhaveyurardheShTakA mAtrANyAtmani bhaveyuraradnanimAtrANi puccha ityarthaH /
asya ca bhedAbhAvaH prayojanamiti pUrvasminneva prastAra uktaM /

sarvama yet

atra purastAt prabhR^ityAtmani pracchAdyamAne pucchApyayavishayAnAM purataH puruShamAtre prAdesho 'vashiShyate /
tatra paJNcamabhAgIyAnAmasambhavAt bhedAbhAvAya paJNcArdheShTakA udIcya upadheyAH, tAsAmupadhAne heturuktaH /
atrAtmanyadhyardhAnAM madhye paJNcaShaShTiH paJNcama

karavindIyA vyAkhyA

bhAgIyAH paJNca cArdhAH, pakShayordvAdasha dvAdasha paJNcamabhAgIyAH, pucche paJNcadasha tA etAH caturuttarashataM paJNcamabAgIyAH, paJNcacArdhAH, catuHpaJNcAghadadhyardhAH /
tA etAH triShaShTiH shataM ca, atra saptatriMshatsaMkhyA sampAdyA //


paJNca yet

atra pakShayorAtmani pucche catasraH paJNcamabhAgIyA uddhR^itya ShTtriMshataM paJNcadashabhAgIyA upadadhyAt /
atmani pUrvasyAM rItyAM madhye paJNcoddhatya dashArdheShTakA udIcIrupadadhyAdevaM dvishataH prastAraH //


sundararAjIyA vyAkhyA

aparasminatathApuccham

atrApyayayoH paJNcapaJNcAdhyardhAH /
pArshveShu paJNcapaJNcAdhyardhAH, aratnanivR^iddhau ShaTShaDiti draShTavyam /
pucchApyaye yA upadhIyante tAsAmardheShTakAmAtrANyAtmani bhavanti /
pucche 'ratnimAtrANi /
etacca prAdeshavR^iddhau /
itarathA ardheShTakAmAtrANyeva pucche /

sarvamagniMapUrayet

pUrvavadAtmani madhye catasraHShaDvoddhR^itya ekaikasya sthAne navanavAShTAN^gulAH /
sAratniprAdeshapakShe pucchApyayasthAbhyaH prAkpaJNcArdheShTakA udagAyatA upadheyAH /
Atmani pUrvarItyAM madhyamAH paJNcod dhR^itya dashArdheShTakA udagAyatA upadadhyAt /
evaM dvishataH /
aratniprAdashAbhAve tu catu paJNcAshatA paJNcatashabhAgIyAbhiH dvayUnaM dvishataM bhavati /
pucchapArshvayorevaikaikAM paJNcamImapohya catasror'dheShTakAH prAgAyatAH /
evaM dvishataH /

kapardibhAShyam
