___________________________________________________________


vyatyAsaM cinuyAd yAvataH prastArAMsh cikIrShet  || ˘p¡us_10.6b ||

___________________________________________________________


gatametat /

___________________________________________________________


paJNca citayo bhavanti | paJNcabhiH purIShair abhyUhatIti purIShAntA citir arthAntaratvAt purIShasya  || ˘p¡us_10.7 ||

___________________________________________________________



iShTakAsandhAnArthaM purISham /
tasmAttadantA citiH /
tadarthatvAttadghareNa gR^ihyate /

___________________________________________________________


jAnudaghnIM sAhasraM cinvIta prathamaM cinvAnaH  || ˘p¡us_10.8a ||

___________________________________________________________



yaH prathamaM cinoti sa jAnudaghnIM cinuyAt sahasrasaN^khyAyutaM ca /
mahAgnimevAdhikR^itya vidhAnAnna shAlAmukhIyadhiShNIyAnAM sahasrasaN^khyAyAmantarbhAvaH /
nApi jAnudaghnItA //


___________________________________________________________


nAbhidaghnIM dviShAhasraM dvitIyam AsyadaghnIM triShAhasraM tR^itIyam uttaram uttaraM jyAyAmsam  || ˘p¡us_10.8b ||

___________________________________________________________



nAbhipramANamutsedhataH dviShAhsraM dvitIyaM cinvAnaH /
AsyapramANaM tR^itIyaM cinvAnaH /
triShAhasraM tR^itIyamuttaramuttaraM jyAyAmsaM //


nAbhipramANamutsedhataH dviShAhsraM dvalitIyaM cinvAnaH /
AsyapramANaM tR^itIyaM cinvAnaH /
triShAhasraM ca grIvadaghnamityasmadIyA shrutiH /

___________________________________________________________


mahAntaM bR^ihantam aparimitaM svargakAmash cinvIteti vij~nAyate  || ˘p¡us_10.8c ||

___________________________________________________________


uttaramuttaramAhAramAharet /
jyAyAn vidhAbhyAsena /
mahAnutsedhataH /
bR^ihatparimANataH /
aparimitaM sahasrAdibhyaH /
"svargakAma' iti vacanAdAgnikalpe "vAjisaneyikamiti' pacanAcca vikalpaH /

karavimandIyA vyAkhyA

vyatyA rShet

gataM /

nanu vyatyAse nAma yasmin prastAre yatra yAdR^ishAnAmupadhAnaM kR^itaM tadanantare prastAre tatrAnyATR^ishAnAmupadhAnaM tAdR^ishAnAmevAnyato dIrghANAm /
naca bhedAbhAvaH prayojanam; sa cehAcAryapravR^icyaiva siddhaH, tatkimarthamidamucyate vyatyAsaM cinuyAditi? ucyate -- anyaprastAradvaye sUtrakArasya vyatyAsopadhAnavidheruparyupari prastAreShvaniyamAshaN^kA mandadhiyAM na bhavediti vyatyAsavacanam /
kiJNca mantropadhAnottaramapi prAmAdika bhedadarshane tatparijihIrShayA lokavadupahitAnAmeva pracAlanAdiprAptau ""sa indra iShTakAmAvR^ihat /
te vA kIryanteti'' doShadarshanAdayAlanAya shulbopadhAnasamaya eva shulbakushalairniyatadeshAnAmabhAdhena bhedAbhAgavaH pariharaNIya ityevamarthaM vyatyAsavacanam /

paJNca Shasya

jalAdrA pR^it -- purISham /
abhyUhanamupalepaH /
upadhAyApedhAya tAM tAM citiM jalArdrayA mR^idopalimpet /
dvAbhyAM vAkyAbhyAmekA citiH purIShopadhAnaparyantA j~neyA /
na kevaletyarthaH /
arthAntaratvAt purIShasya, arthaH -- prayojanaM /
antarA -- bhedaH /
prayojanAnyatvAdityarthaH /
citInAmanyatprayojanaM purIShANAM cAnyat /
citInAM prayojanabhUtAt jAnudaghnavadutsedhakaraNAdanyat prayojanaM purIShasya /
tacceShTakAnAM shoShapAkAgalahrAsapUraNaM parasparasaM shleShash ca /
ata eva cAniyataparimANaM purISham /
naca etAvadbhiH purIShairhrAsaparihAraH parasparasaMshleShash ca bhavatIti pramANamasti /
tasmAdaniyatapramANaM purISham /
ata uktaM purIShAntA citiriti /
tathAca shrUyate -- "purISheNAbhyUhati /
tasmAnmAMsenAsthi cchannamiti' /
ayamarthaH -- yathA sharIrAvayavabhUtAnyasthIni mAMsaishchannAnyeva sharIrakArye prabhavanti /
evamavayavabhUteShTakAH sarvataH purIShaishchannA evAgnikArye prabhavanti /
tasmAdabhyUhanaparyantA citiH /
kiJNcayadi purIShopadAnaM svArthaM tadA jAnudaghnAdyatiriktapramANatAgneH syAt /
ataH uktameva prayojanam /
anena "dasha sampadyante dvAdasha sampadyanta' iti cArthavAdadarshanena citipurIShayorminnArthatAshaN^kA mAbhUditi ekArthatA pratipaditA /

jAnu yate

atra "jAnudaghnaM cinvIta prathamaM cinvAna' ityAdyA utsedhavidhAyikA stisraHshrutayaH /
tathA "sahasraM cinvIte' tyAdyA agneriShTakAsaN^khyAvidhAyikAstisraHshrutayaH /
jAnudaghnaM jAnupramANaM, nAbhidaghnaM nAbhipramANaM AsyadaghnamAsyapramANam /
sAhasraM sahasrasaN^khyA parimitaM /

dviShAhasraM dvAbhyAM sahasrAbhyAM parimitam /
triShashAhasraM tribhiHsahasraiH parimitam /
utsedhavidhayaH tatsampAdanApekShAH /
saN^khyAvidhayaH tadAshrayApekShAH /
teShAM yathAkramaM naShTAshvadagdharathavat parasparApekShayA melanena paThitAH /
jyAyAMsamutkR^iShTairmardanAdikalpaiH utkR^iShTaish ca saMsarjanIyaiH; mahAntamutsedhataH; bR^ihantaM parimANataH; aparimitaM saN^khyAta uktaM /
saMkhyAdikamaparimitaM parimitAt parimANAt bhUyaH pramANe sAhasraM shAstraM pramANamiti kAtyAyanaH /
svargakAmasya tu visheShataH /
akAmasya tu nitya eva /
svargakAmasye tyukteH agnikalpe "vAjasaneyikamiti' vacanAcca dviShAhasrAdInAM vikalpaH /
grIvadaghnamiti taittirIyake shrUyate /
ubhayamapyekArthameva /
iShTakotsedhakaraNAntarAvidhAnAt /
"samAnaM hishirogrIvamiti' brAhnaNadarshanAcca /
(kiJNca grIvAsyayoH paryAyatvadarshanAcca) /
kiJNca grIvAsyayoH paryAytvaM loke ca dR^ishyate -- dashAsyo dashagrIva iti /
tasmAcchutyorekArthatA /

sundararAjIyA vyAkhyA

vyatyAsaMapurIShasya

iShTakAHsthaNDilArthAH, tatsandhAnArthaM purIShaM /
ato bhinnaprayojanatvAtsakhyAntaraM nAvagAhate /

jAnudaghnIMajyAyAMsaM sAhasraM sahasraparimANam /
dviShAhasraM triShAhasramiti "pUrvapadAditi' Shatvam /
uttaramuttaraM caturthaprabhR^iti /

atra brAhnaNaM pramANatvenAha --

mahAntaMavij~nAyate

mahAntaM vidhAbhyAsena /
aparimitaM bR^ihantaM UrvapramANena /
atra bodhAyanaH -- UrdhvapramANAbhyAsaM jAnoH paJNcamasya caturviMshenaike samAmananti /

kapardibhAShyam

___________________________________________________________


dviShAhasre dviprastArAsh citayo bhavanti | triShAhasra triprastArAsh caturthaprabhR^itiShv AhAreShu nityam iShTakAparimANam  || ˘p¡us_10.9 ||

___________________________________________________________



___________________________________________________________


vij~nAyate ca ˛na jyAyAMsaM citvA kanIyAMsaM cinvIteti'  || ˘p¡us_10.10 ||

___________________________________________________________



nigadavyAkhyAtametat /
caturthoti -- iShTakAparimANamiha triShAhasramityucyate /
triShAhasrameva niyataM /
nocyeta anIkavadAvR^ittiHsyAt /
anyasyAvidhAnAt /
amumevArthaM darshayituM shrutiM darshayati -- vij~nAyata iti /
jyAyAMsaM -- dviShAhasraM triShAhasraM vA citvA kanIyAMsaM -- sAhasraM na cinuyAditi pratiShedhaH /
tathAr'dhAShTamamardhanavamaM vA citvA ekavidhAptArghavidhaparyantA na cetavyAH /

ityApastambasUtra vivaraNe kapardisvAmibhAShye

shulbAkhyaprashne tR^itIyaH paTalaH.

----------------

karavindIyA vyAkhyA

utsedhAdhikyaM ca prastArAnekatve na bhavatItyAha --

dviShA stArAH

dviShAhasre 'gnau dviprastArAH tUShNIM purIShAbhyUhanam /
" tAsu purIShamabhyUhatIti 'gap  nAkSha anye ca citidharmAH /

catu mANam

AhareShu -- prayogeShu /
caturthapabrabhR^itiShu prayogeShvanantaroktaM triShAhasraM nityaM; na nyUnAdikamityarthaH /
nanvanantarArthAdeva triShAhasraM caturthaprabhR^itiShu nityaM bhaviShyati kimarthamidamucyate? ucyateyadItaM nocyate, tarhi anIkavadAvR^ittiH prasajyeta /
yadvA dvitIyatR^itIyanimittA vivR^iddhiriti caturthAdiShu sAhasrameva vA prasajyet /
ata idamucyate -- "nityamiShTakAparimANamiti' /
amumevArthaM shrutyA prathayati --

vij~nA te

jyAyAMsamadhikapramANaM kaniyAMsamalpapramANam /
dviShAhasraM triShAhasraM vA kR^itvA na sAhasraM cinvIta /
tatrriShAhasrameva cinvIta //
tatr.a shlokAH --

yadatra pucche prAdeshamupadhAyeti sUtritam /

tadabhedAya pucchAgre pR^ithaggrItiniShedhakam //


agrasya rItibhede syurbahvayaH pucche bhidA yataH /

ataH pucchAdanArambhaH pucchAgraprabhR^itirbhavet //


tathopadhAne tanmUle yatkShetramatiricyate /

caturbhirardhaiH prAdeshasahitaishchAdayettataH //


apyaye viparItoktirevamarthavatI bhavet /

prAdeshamAtrA nAgre syustathA bahubhidA yataH //


chAdane viniyuktAnAM sAmarthyeM nAsti yatra tu /

tatrAnyAbhiHsamarthAbistatratyAbishchadirbhavet //


pracchAdayeti vacanaM sarvAgniviShayaM yataH /

ataH paJNcamabhAgIyA pANibAhu yahetukA //


vyatyAsenopadhAnasya vyatyAsavacanasya ca /

punaHkriyA tatra tatra bhedAbhAvaikahetukA //


vyatyAse lokataHsiddhe tatrAsau yatate yataH /

teneShTakA mA6bhedo 'pyamR^iShya iti gamyate //


saMkhyAmAtramanUdyeha pUraNaM vidadhAti yat /

tena manyAmahe sAmyaM sarvaprastAragocaram //


nyUne tu pUrayeduktaiH sAmyasyAyatanIsthateH /

atireke kramAbhAvAt prastArAHsarvataHsamAH //


iti karavindasvAmikR^itAyAM shulbadIpikAyAM tR^itIyaH paTalaH

----------------------

sundararAjIyA vyAkhyA

dviShAhasre triprastArAH

pratiprastAraM saMdhAnArtaM purIShaM bhavati /
cityante mantrataH /

caturthaprabhR^iti parimANam

nityamuttaraM triShAhasrameva --

vij~nAyate cinvIteti

sarevatrAgniShu dakShiNottare pArshve sadR^ishe evopadheye /
tathA pAshvAtyapaurastye /
yadevamAha -- "adyardhA dasha purastAddasha pashcAt aShTAvaShTau pAdeShTakAH pakShAgrayosvatasrashvalatasraH pakShAgrIyAH, ityAdi /
tadAha bodhAyanaH -- "pashudharmA ha vA agniryathA vai pashordakShiNeShamasthnaM yaddakShiNaM taduttareShAmuttaram, ityAdi /
etacca sati saMbhave; yadAha -- "dvitIyacaturthayosvAnyatarataH pratisaMhitAmekaikAM triMshatShaShTayaH, ekaM paJNcamIm' iti ca /
dvishatA eva sarve prastArAH. pratiprastAraM saMkhyApUraNavacanAt rathacakre dvishatayoreva prastArayorvacanAt eSha dvishataH prastAra iti shyenaciti vacanAcca /
atashvoDA nAkasadashvaikIkR^itya saMkhyeyAH /
bodhAyanastvAha -- "paJNcamyAM vA citau saMkhyApUrtirdvishatAH prastArAH /
paJNcacoDAbhirnAkasadaHsamAnasaMkhyAH pratIyAt' iti //


dashamaH khaNDaH

iti sundararAjIye ApastambashulbasUtravyAkhyAne

shulbapradIpe tR^itIyaH paTalaH

--------------

kapardibhAShyam

atha caturthaH paTalaH


___________________________________________________________


caturashrAbhir agniM cinuta iti vij~nAyata | samacaturashrA anupapadatvAc chabdasya  || ˘p¡us_11.1 ||

___________________________________________________________



asyAHshrulerarthastarkyate -- kiM samAnAnAM caturashrANAM cAvisheShagrahaNaM Ahosvit samAnAmAmeveti? kutaH? visheShAgrahaNAt /
na kashvidvisheShaH shrUyate /
tasmAdavisheSheNeti prApte ucyate -- samacaturashrA eva grAhyAH /
kutaH anupapadatvAcchabdasya /
yatropapadaM na shrUyate dIrgho viShama iti vA tatra samacaturashrANAmeva mukhyatvAt mukhyerthe prathamaM pratyayo bhavati; yataH pratIyate tasyArtho bhavati /
itaratra gauNaH /
tasmAtsapacaturashrAbhirevopA dhAtavyaH /
nAdhyardhAbhiriti sthitam /

___________________________________________________________


pAdamAtrayo bhavanti aratnimAtrayo bhavanty UrvasthimAtrayo bhavanty aNUkamAtrayo bhavantIti vij~nAyate  || ˘p¡us_11.2 ||

___________________________________________________________



catasra etAHshrutayaH /
tAsAsAvayameva vyAcaShTe --

___________________________________________________________


caturbhAgIyamaNUkam | paJNcamabhAgIyAratniH | tathorvasthi  || ˘p¡us_11.3a ||

___________________________________________________________



aNUkashabdaH puruShacaturthasya vAcasaH /
aratniH paJNcamasya /
tathA -- tenaiva prakAreNa Urvasthi ShaShThasya /
ShaDbhAgIyA iti shulbAntare /

___________________________________________________________


pAdeShTakA pAdamAtrI  || ˘p¡us_11.3b ||

___________________________________________________________


___________________________________________________________


tatra yathAkAmI shabdArthasya vishayitvAt  || ˘p¡us_11.4 ||

___________________________________________________________



caturbhAgIyaH pAda iti saMj~nA vihitA shAstrAntare /
pAda shabdena pramANacaturbhAgo gR^ihyate kShetracaturbhAgash ca /
pAdaH pramANamasyAH pAdamAtrI /
pAdashabdasya saMbandhashabdatvAt puruShacaturbhAgo 'pi gR^ihyate aNUkAdicaturbhAgash ca sannihitatvAt /
teShAM pAdeShTakAbhirityukte puruShacaturbhAgA aNUkAdicaturbhAgAsh ca pratIyante /
kutaH? shabdArthasya viSha(sha)yitvAta /
vakShyati ca -- aNUkAH paJNcadashabhAgIyAnAM sthAna iti /
saN^khyApUraNe 'NUkAnAM praveshaM darshayati /
UrvasthayaratnayoH ekArthatvaM kecidicchanti /
te paJNcadashabhAgIyAbhiHsaN^khyApUraNaM kurvate /
teShAM darshane prastArA na yujyante /
sahasrasaN^khyA tu pUryate pratiprastAramiti vacanamanarthakamApadyeta /
ye prastArA te dvishatA iti vajanAni na yujyante /
tasmAtpUrvokta evArtho grahyaH /
sarvavacanAnAmarthavacvAya /

karavindIyA vyAkhyA

atha caturthaH paTalaH

catura yate

catuShkoNAbiriShTakAbhiragniM cinute /
kIdR^ishyo grAhyA ityata Aha --

sanaca bdasya

tA iShTakA adIrghaviShamAH samacaturashrA grahyAH /
kutaH? anupapadatvAcchabdasya /
na hyatropapadaM shrUyate dIrghAbhiriShTakAbirviShamAbhirveti /
ataH "samaM syAdashrutatvAditi' nyAyena samA eva syuH /
pUrvasminnagnau dIrghAsh ca santi /
ato vidhibhedAdvA vikalpaH pUrveNAgninA /
nityashvAkAmashruteH /

agnikalpasyaiva shravaNaM pradarshanArtam /
AsAM shrutyaiva darshayannAha --

pAda yate

etAshratasraHshrutayaH iShTakAnAM pramANaM vidavati /
sambhavAcca tAsAM samuccayaH /
pAdamAtrayaH -- pAda pramANAH /
pAdashabdasvaraNacaturthabhAgAdau vartate /
iha caturmAgavAcI /
sa caturbhAgo 'NUkAdInAM grAhya ityuttarasUtre pratipAdayiShyate /
pAdapraNANAH pAdamAtrayaH /
aratniH sakaniShThikaH karaH /
sa ca puruShasya paJNcamabAgaH /
vakShyati ca paJNcAratniH puruvaH caturviMshatyaN^gulayoratniriti /
tatpramANA aratnimAtrayaH /
urvasthi -- Urvorasthi /
aNUkaM pR^iShThavaMshaH /
tA UrvasthijAnvAsthinAmptayornANUkasyetyatra vyAkhyAnAt /
puruShasyaH ShTho bhAga -- urvasthi /
caturtho bhAgo 'NUkaH /
etacca uttarasUtre spaShTaM vakShyati /
tatpramANA UrvasthimAtrayaH /
aNUkAmAtrayash ca /

A(tA)somavadikapamANavashena saMj~nAvisheShavidhAnArthamAha --

caturmi trI

aNUkAratnayUrvasthishabdaiH tanmAtraya iShTakA gR^ihyante /
upasaMhAre pAdamAtrIShTaketi darshanAt /
saMj~nAsu strIlihganirddeshAcca /
kiJNcANUkAdishabdairapIShTakAnAM vyavahArA dR^ishyante /
"aNUkAH paJNcadashabhAgIyAnAM sthAne sandhyantarAle paJNcamabAgIyAHsapAdAHtA Atmani caturdashabhiH pAdairyathAyogaM paryupadadhyAt' ityAdiShu aNUkamAtrI caturbhAgIyA tatsaMj~nA bhavatItyarthaH /
paJNcamabhAgIyArAtniH -- aratnimAtrI paJNcamabhAgIyAkhyA /
tathorvasthi -- urvasthimAtrI ShaDbAgIyAkhyA /
pAdeShTakA -- pAdamAtrI /
nanu kathametallabhyate ShaDbhAgIyorvasthIti? tatheti prakArAtideshAt /
kathamatideshaH? yathAratnimAtrIsaN^khyA sannikarSheNa svapUrvoktAratnimAtrIpramA(Ne)NAnyUnAnantaraparimANavacana saMj~nA syAditi tathorvasthimA6yapi saMkhyA tatsannikarSheNa svapUrvoktAratnimAtrI pramANAnyUnAnantaraparimANavacanasaMj~nA syAditi /
kiJNca ShaDbAgIyorvasthIti vaktavya tathetyayamatideshaH prakR^itapuruShAvayavapramANaprakArasamAptisUcanArthaH /
tenorvasthayantAnAmevAvayavapramANaparimANatvaM na pAdamAtrINAmiti j~nAyate /
ataHsvavAkyasannihitatvAt "upadhAne 'ShTAvaShTau pAdeShTakAH caturbhAgIyAnAM pakShAgrayornidadhyAt /
sandhyantarAle paJNcamabhAgIyAHsapAdAHtA Atmani caturdashabhiH pAdairyathAyogaM paryupadadhyAt' iti darshanAcca /
aNUkArdAnAM pAdA iha pAdatvena gR^ihyante na caraNAdayaH /
kiJNcashvutidR^iShTamapahAyANUkAdInAM vyutkrameNa pAThapaurvAparye pUrvasya pramANAdhikyaj~nApanArthaH /
tenorvasthipramANAnAmaratnimAtrIbhyo nyUnapramANatvaM pAdamAtrINAmaNUkAratnacUrvAsthimAtrIbhyo nyUnapramANatvaM ca j~nApitaM bhavati /
etacca sarvamuktaM bhagavatA bodhAyanena "samacaturashrAbhiragniM' cinuta "ityupakramya tasyeShTakAH kArayet /
puruShasya caturthena paJNcamenaH ShThena dashemana ca' itivadatA /
ato 'NUkAdipAdA iha pAdatvena gR^ihyante /
te ca teShAmardhena grAhyAH /
ardhapramANena pAdapramANaM vidhIyata iti nyAyAt /
ataH paJNcadashAN^gulANUkapAdAH dvAdashAN^gulAratnipAdAH dashAN^gulA UrvAsthipAdAH /
teneha ShaDvidhA iShTakAH /
tAdR^ishaiH karaNaiH kAryAH /
nanvaNUkAdishabdairAsAM parimANaj~nAne vyavahAre ca siddhe kimarthaM mahatyaH saMj~nAH kriyante? ucyate -- shrautanAmaNUkAdishabdAnAM pUruShacaturbhAgAdimAtraparimANaparatvaj~nApanena tasya tasya puruShasya caturbhAgAdiparimANairiShTakAnirmANArtham /
tathAhi -- loke dvividhAH puruShAH samAsh ca viShamAsh ca /
tatra samAHsAmudrIyAsheShalakShaNopetAH /
katipayairvihInA viShamAH /
samAHsAmudrIyAsheShalakShaNopetAH /
katipayairvihInA viShamAH /
samAnAmaNUkAdayaH /
tadapekShayA niyataparimANatvAnmukhyatayA gR^ihItAH /
itareShAM tu garbhAdhAnAdikAlastitaprAkR^itAdR^iShTAdivashena nyUnAdhikavakrAdyaneka rUpAN^gatayANUkAdiShu caturbhAgAdiniyamavyabhicArAttatpramANairutpAditAnAmiShTakAnAM upadhAnakAle tatsaMkhyAkAnAM tAsAM tatra tatropadhAne tAbhistAbhistaddeshapUraNaM nyUnAbhirvA pUraNam /
bhinnajAtIyAnAM tatratyAnAM tatra tatra saN^ghaTTanamityevamAdayo mahAnto doShAstatra sambhIvaShyantIti /
ataHshrutigatANUkAdishabdaistadvaiShamyaparihArAya puruShacaturmAgAdayo lakShyanta ityasyArthasya pratipAdanAyAnvarthA mahatyaHsaMj~nAH kiyante /
tenAyamarthaHsaMpadyate -- UrdhvabAhoH puruShasya pramANaM gR^ihItvAtsya caturthena paJNcamenaH ShThena vA teShAM ardheShTakAH kArayediti /
atra kecidvarvashthyaratvayorekArthatAmicchInta /
teShAM mate 'gnikalpe tathorvasti shabdasyAratnishabdasya vA pR^ithagupAdAnaM punarupAdAnaM shrutidarshanaM ca sUtrakArasya pramAdakR^itamevAvatiShThate /

tatra yA yitvAt

gataM /
ayamarthaH -- caturbhAgAdayaH puruShacaturbhAgaparimitAH syuH /
puruShakalpanAnurUpAH syuriti caturbhAgIyAstriMshadaN^gulAH paJNcabhAgIyAshcaturviMshatyaN^gulAH ShaDbhAgIyAH viMshatyaN^gulAH /
tAsAM pAdAstadarthamitAH paJNcadashadvAdashAN^gulAsh ceti /

sundararAjIyA vyAkhyA

atha caturthaH paTalaH

athaitameva caturashvaM prakArAntareNopadhAtumAha ----

caturashrAbhi tvAcchabdasya

anupapadatvaM dIrghAdibhiriti visheShaNAbhAvaH /

pAdamAtrayo vij~nAyate

eShAM pAdAdInAM pramANamAha --

caturbhAgIyANUkam

puruShasya caturbhAgIyA triMshadaN^gulA aNUkamAtrItyucyate /

paJNcamabhAgIyArAtniH

caturviMshatyaN^gulA /

tathorvasthi

tathA tenaiva mArgeNorvasthi j~nAtavyaM, tacca ShaDhbhAgIyaM viMshatyaN^gulam /
kecidUrvasthItyapi paJNcamabhAgIyAmevAhuH, tadayuktam /
"kulmimAtro 'ratniprAdesha UrvasthIti' bhedena nirdeshAt /
"iShTakAH karoti prAdeshamAtrayo 'ratnimAtraya UrvasthimAtra' iti prayogakalpe pR^ithagvacanAt tadUrvasthItyAdivacanAcca /
vyaktoktatvAcca bodhAyanena -- "tasyeShTakAH kArayet puruShasya caturthena paJNcamena ShaShThena dashamena' iti /

pAdeShTakA pAdamAtri

pAdashvAvisheShAdaNUkAdInAM ca sarvAsAM ca bhavati /

tatra yathAkAmIshabdArthasya vishayitvAt

loke pAdashabdashcaturbhAgavacanaH prasiddhaH /
vkacidekadeshamAtre /
"kR^icch pAdaH prakIrtita' iti "R^icaM pAdagrahaNa' iti R^ikShu ca /
vede tvekadeshamAtre dR^ishyate -- "tripadA gAyatrI paJNcapadA pAN^ktirH ,capapadA shavkarI' iti /
iha tadubhayaM grAhyaM /
shabdArthasyobhayatra vR^itteH /
atra ca pAdashabdArthanirUpaNaM kriyate ekavidhAdyartham /
asmiM stvagnau caturbhAgavacane 'pi pAde na kashviddoShaH /
ye tu ShaDbhAgIyAnnecchanti teShAmevopayogaH, aNUkAratnipAdatvena dashAN^gulAShTAN^gulAnAM grAhyatvAt /

kapardibhAShyam

___________________________________________________________


upadhAne 'ShTAvaShTau pAdeShTakAsh caturbhAgIyAnAM pakShAgrayor nidadhyAt | sandhyosh ca tadvad AtmAnaM ShaDaN^gulApetAH  || ˘p¡us_11.5a ||

___________________________________________________________



upadhAnakAle aShTAvaShTau caturbhAgIyAnAM pAdeShTakAH pakShAgrayorUpadadhAyAt /
aShTAvaShTAviti vishayAH /
atmAnaM ShaDaN^gulamAtramavetAH avagatA vyAptA iti yAvata /
navAN^gulamAtraM pakShayoH /

___________________________________________________________


shroNyaMseShu cAShTau prAcIH pratIcish ca  || ˘p¡us_11.5b ||

___________________________________________________________


shroNyaMsayosvatasrashcatasraH /
tAH pAdAH /
pracIHshroNyoH /
aMsayoH ptIcIH /
evaM caturbhAgIyapAdA aShTAcatvAriMshat /


___________________________________________________________


sandhyantarAle paJNcabhAgIyAH sapAdAH  || ˘p¡us_11.6 ||

___________________________________________________________


pakShasandhyorantarAle paJNcamabhAgIyAH pAdasahitAH /
madhye pAdAH /
dasha pratIciH /
tAsAM dakShiNataH paThcaviMshatiH paJNcamabhAgIyAH /
uttarato viMshatiH /

evaM sandhyantarAle paJNcapaJNcAshadiShTakAH upadheyAH /

___________________________________________________________


pucche prAdeshamupadhAya sarvam agniM caturbhAgIyAbhiH pracchAdayet  || ˘p¡us_11.7 ||

___________________________________________________________


prAdeshashabdena kiM kShetramabhidhIyate? pucche yatprAdeshamiti? athavA iShTakAH prAdeshena kAritAH? yadi kShetramabhidhIyeta prAdeshapaN^ktirevopadhAtavyA syAt /
tathA sati bhidyetAgniH /
itarasminpakShe yathA na bhidyate tathA prAdesheShTakA bhaveyuH /
prAdeshamiti jAtAvekavacanam /
prAdesheShTakAbhiHsahANUkA na sherate /
sherate tu paJNcabhAgIyAstAbhiHsaha /
atashcatasrashcatasraH shroNyoH pAdeShTakAstrayodasha paJNcamabhAgIyAH /
pUrvArdhe 'ShTAvaNUkAH /
evamekonatriMshatpucche /
apare punarevaM varNayanti -- yasya vitastayA vardhanaM kR^itaM tatrApi caturashrashrutisAmarthyAt prAdesha eveShTakAbhirvyApyata iti /
evamarthaM prAdeshagrahaNamiti /
tasminnapi pakShe ukta upadhAnakramaH /
sarvamiti dvAtriMshat /
aShTAviMshatirAtmanyuktAH /
pucchapUrvArdhe 'ShTau //


___________________________________________________________


pAdeShTakAbhiH saMkhyAM pUrayet  || ˘p¡us_11.8 ||

___________________________________________________________



paJNcadashabhAgIyAbhiHsaMkhyAM pUrayet /
Atmani dvitIyAyAM rItyAM madhyamAM caturbhAgIyAM madhyame dvishataH prastAraH //


karavindIyA vyAkhyA

upadhA dhyAt

upadhAnakAle paJNcadashAN^gulA aShTAvaShTau pakShAgrayornidadhyAt /
pakShAtmasandhayosh ca tadvadAtmani ShaDaN^gulAvetAH /
pakShAtmasandhyoshvAShTAvaShTau /
tAHShaDaN^gulAHshyenAtmani praviShTAHshroNyaMseShu ca /
cakAreNa tadvadityAkR^iShya sAmarthyAdvishayAbhAvaH /
shroNyaMseShucatasrashcatasraH /
visheShamAha -- aShTAvaShTau prAcIH pratIcIsh ca /
shroNyoH prAcIH aMsayoH pratIcIH /
nanu aShTAvaShTAviti vIpsayA prAptAnAM sthAnacatuShTayanirddeshe pratisthAnamaShTAvaShTau kathaM na syuH? ucyate -- "aShTau prAcIH pratisthAnamaShTAvaShTau kathaM na syuH? ucyate --"aShTau prAcIH praticIshveti' vacanasAmarthyAt prAcInAM pratIcInAM cAShTatvamavagamyate na pratyekaM catasra eveti /
shroNyoHprAcyau rItyAvaMsayoHpratIcyau /
tA etA aShTAcatvAriMshat caturbhAgIyAH pAdAHsandhyantarAle paJNcamabhAgIyAHsapAdAH pakShasandhyormadhye Atmani paJNcamabAgIyAHsapAdAH sAmarthyAt svapAdaiHsahitA nidadhyAt /
atra dakShiNabhAge vishayAnAmuttarataH paJNcaviMshatiH paJNcamabhAgIyAH /
uttarabhAge vishayAnAM dakShiNato viMshatiH paJNcamabhAgIyAH /
madhye dasha pradeshAH /
evametAHsandhyantarAle paJNcapaJNcAshadiShTakAH //


pucche yet

gatametat /
pUrvAgnau pucchAgrapradeshe pR^ithagrItitve bhedaprasaN^gena tatparihArAyAyaM yatnaH /
atra tu mUlapradesharaya pR^ithagrItitve uparitanaprastAre vakShyamANavishayapaJNcamabhAgIyAvidherbhedaH prasajyeteti gamyate /
sa cApi parihArya eva /
tatashcaturbhAgIyAbhirAtmasheShaM pakShasheShaM ca pracchAdya pucche tu pUrvArdhe 'ShTau caturbhAgIyA upadhAya pashcArdhe bhedAbhAvAya paJNcadasha paJNcamabAgIyA upadadhyAt /
uktaM cAbhiyuktaiH --

avAdhaH k ptadeshAnAM stAre stAre ca pUraNam /

bhedabhAvo 'pi cAgnInAmAcAryANAM parAyaNAm //


iti /
caturbhAgIyAshabdo bAhuyAbhiprAyaH /
pracchAdane pracchAdana shabdasyApi pUrvoktameva prayojanam /
atra prAdeshapR^ithagrItitve bhedaprasaN^gAt sarvAgneH pracchAdanarya vihitatvAccaturbhAgIyAnAM cAsambhavAduktAnAmasambhave bhedAbhAvAya ca tatratatroktAnAmasambhave tatratyAbhiHsambhavantIbhiranyAbhiH pracchAdanaM kAryamiti pUrvamevoktam /
tatra dakShiNe pakShe pAdAnAM madhye ShoDashacaturbhAgIyAH /
uttare ca tAH ShoDasha /
Atmani sandhyorantarAlaraca purataH purataH pAdAnAM madhye catUrdasha /
tAH pashcimatashvapAdAnAM madhye caturdasha /
aShTau puccharaya pUrvArdhe /
aparArdhe paJNcadasha paJNcamabhAgIyAH /
sandhyantarAle paJNcacatvAriMshat paJNcamabhAgIyAH tatra ShaShTiraNUkAH /
ShaShTiH paJNcamabhAgIyAH /
aShTAcatvAriMshadaNUkApAdAH dasha paJNcamabAgIyAH pAdAH /
tA etAHShaDashItishatam /

atra caturdashasaMkhyA sampAdyA /
tatsampAdanamAha --

pAde yet

gatam /
Atmamadhye paJNcamyAM rItyAM upAntyAM caturbhAgIyAmuddhrR^itya nava ShaDbhAgIyAn pAdAnupadadhyAt /
pucchashroNyorekaikAM paJNcamabhAgIyAmuddhR^itya

caturastatpAdAnupadadhyAt /
evaM dvishataH prastAraH /
Atmani prAcyo rItayaH /
pakShayordakShiNottarayoH pucche codIcyo rItayaH //


sundararAjIyA vyAkhyA

upAdhAne 'ShTAvaShTau dadhyAt

caturbhAgIyAnAM pAdeShTakAH paJNcadashAhgulAH //


sandhyoshva--vetAH

sandhyoH pakShApyayayoH tadvat pakShAgravadaShTAvaShTau //


tAshvAtmAnaM ShaDaN^gulena prAptAH, navAN^gulena pakShau //


shoNyaMseShu -- cIsh ca

ekaikatra catasrashcatasraH, evaM ShoDasha prAcIH pratIcIriti pAdAH aShTAvityatra vIpsArtho draShTavyaH /
athavA anena sUtreNa shroNyaMseShvaShTAveva vidhIyante, "anyA aShTau pAdeShTakAbhiHsaMkhyAM pUreyat' ityanena /
sarvathA tAvat ShoDashaivopadheyAH /

sandhyantarAle -- pAdAH

pakShApyayayorantarAle paJNcamabAgIyAH paJNcacatvAriMshat /
AsAM madhye dasha prAdeshamAtrayaH /
pAdashabdena ca sannihitatvAt paJNcamabAgIyAnAM pAdA ucyante /
tAsAM pAdeShTakAnAM dakShiNato viMshatiH paJNcamabhAgIyAH, uttarataH paJNcaviMshatiH, viparItA vA //


puccheprAdeshamupadhAya

pucchAgre yatpravR^iddhaM prAdeshakShetraM tadupadadhyAt sAmarthayAddashabhiH prAdeshaiH //


sarvamagniM -- dayet

evaM pracchAdite ekonanavatishataM (189 ) iShTakA bhavanti /

pAdeShTa -- yet

pucchasyAparArdhe pArshveyoshcatasrashcatasraH paJNcadashAN^gulAH /
evaM kR^ite paJNconadvishataM bhavati /
tataH pucchasya pUrvArdhe pArshveyormadhye tisrastisraHShaDbhAgIyAH pracIrupadadhyAt /
evaM dvishataH prastAraH //


kapardibhAShyam

___________________________________________________________


aparasmin prastAre pucchApyaye paJNcamabhAgIyA vishayAH  || ˘p¡us_11.9a ||

___________________________________________________________


dvitIye prastAre pucchApyaye pucchAtmasandhau vishayA ubhayasthAH paJNcamabhAgIyA upadheyAH /

___________________________________________________________


tA Atmani caturdashabhiH pAdair yathAyogaM paryupadadhyAt  || ˘p¡us_11.9b ||

___________________________________________________________



tAsAneva pAdeShTakAbhiH vishayAsaMsR^iShTAbhiH caturdashabhirupadadhyAt /
Atmani yathA yujyante /
iha ShaDbhAgIyAnAM karaNamuktam /
upadhAnaM noktam yathA pUrvatrArdheShTakAnAM purastAccopadheyAH pucchasya pUrvArdhe pArshvayostisrastisraH ShaDbhAgIyAH madhye catasraH /
shiShTe dvAdasha caturbhAgIyAH /

___________________________________________________________


sarvam agniM paJNcamabhAgIyAbhiH pracchAdayet  || ˘p¡us_11.10 ||

___________________________________________________________


___________________________________________________________


pAdeShTakAkShiH saN^khyAM pUrayet  || ˘p¡us_11.11a ||

___________________________________________________________



iha pAdeShTakAshabdena puruShasya pUrayitavyasya caturbhAgakArikA aNUkA gR^ihyante /
paJNcamabhAgIyAsh ca kR^itA upadheyA ityucyante /
dvAdasha caturbhAgIyA Atmani /
prathamA rItiH paJNcamabhAgIyAnAm /
dvitIyA rItishcaturbhAgIyAnAm /
ShaShThI prAdeshAnAm /
navamI caturbhAgIyAnAm /
shiShTe paJNcamabhAgIyAH /
eSha prastAro dvishataH /
atra kecana yAj~nikAH anupAshitaguravaH AcAryAbhiprAyamajAnantaH UnAddUya(hya)dhikaprastAraM kurvanti /
asya tu sUtrakArasya pratiprastAraM pUrayediti vadatastadanabhipretameva /
yadyevamabhimatamabhaviShyat sarvatra pratiprastAraM saMkhyAM pUrayediti nAvakShyat /
uktaM ca; tasmAddvishataH prastAraH

kartavyaH /

tatra shlokaH --

aShTau shroNyaMsayosh ca syuH pAdAH sUtrakR^iteritAH /

tAsAM madhye caturthyaHsyuH caturdasha caturdasha //


sandhyantarAle paJNcamyAH pAdaish ca dashbhiHsaha /

tAsAM madhye dasha proktAH prAcyasyuHshulbakarmaNi //


aShTau pucchasya pUrvArdhe caturthyaHshiShTa eva tu /

dvitIyA navamI caiva catturthI nAma vAtmani //


udIcya eva nityaM syurmadhyAH paJNcamapAdakaiH /

kR^itAbhishcaturashrAbhiraNUkovira .... tnibhiH //


asyA eva sapAdAbhiH prastAro dvishataH kR^itaH //


iti //


karavindIyA vyAkhyA

apara yAH

dvitIye prastAre pucchApyaye evaM paJNcapaJNcamabhAgIyA upadheyAH /
avisheShAdAtmapucchayoHsamaM praviShTAH //


tA A dhyAt

tA vishayAshcaturdashabhiH pAdaiH prakR^itatvAt paJNcamabhAgIyAnAM yathA yogaM paritaHsarvataH upadadhyAt /
vishayAnAM purastAddasha /

sarva yet

pakShayostriMshattriMshacpaJNcamabhAgIyAH purastAtprabhR^ityAtmani pracchAdyamAne udagAyatAH paJNcamabhAgIyAnAM nava rItayaH /
caturdashIyAnAM pAdAnAM dakShiNato dve paJNcamabhAgIye uttaratash ca dve /
pucche tu yathoktAbhiH pracchAdyAmAne bahubhedaprasaN^gAt ShaDbhAgIyA utpannA api na yuktA iti ShaDbhAgIyAstisrastisro vishayAnAM pashcAt pucchapArshvayoH pratIcIrupadadhAti ""tAsAM pArshve dvedve caturbhAgIye pratIcyau upadhAya tAsAM madhye tisraH ShaDbhAgIyAH pratIcIrupadadhthAt /
aparArdhe cAShTAvaNUkeShTakA upadadhyAt /
evamAtmani vishayAbhiH saha ekonashataM paJNcamabhAgIyAshcaturdashaprAdeshAH pakShayostriMshattiMshat paJNcamabhAgIyAH pucche dvAdasha caturbhAgIyA nava ShaDbhAgIyAH /
tA etAH ShaDUnaM dvishatam /
tatra ShaTsaMkhyA sampAdyA''

pAde yet

atra navapaJNcamabhAgIyArItInAM madhyasthAmekAM paJNcamabhAgIyArItimuddhR^itya madhye viMshatiprAdesheShTakA udIcIrupadadhyAt /
atra catuHsaMkhyAtiricyate /
atireke adhikapramANopadhAnena saMkhyApUraNasyAnyAyyatvAdaNUkAH paJNcamabhAgIyAnAM sthAna iti paribhAShayANUkopadhAnena saMkhyApUraNasya nyAyyatvAcca /
tataH prAdesharotyA pUrvarItiH yathA saMshliShTA bhavati tathA kR^itvA pUrvAntarItimuddhR^itya tatrAShTAvaNUkA upadadhyAt /
evaM prAdesharItyAH paritastisro rItIH pracyAvya dvitIyAM rItimuddhtyAShTAvaNUkA upadadhyAt /
evaM dvishataH prastAraH /
atra kecita -- prathame prastAre pucchAgre dashaprAdeshAnupadhAya pAdeShTakAshvAnAdR^itya paJNcadashabhAgIyAbhiHsaMkhyAM pUrayanti /
bhedamapi sahante /
prathame 'pi prathame 'pi prastAre sandhyantarAle 'NUkAstatpAdAshvopadadhAti /
tathopadhAne prayojanaM mR^igyam /
kecitu pracchAdanakAle saMkhyApUrakANAM sthAnamavashiShya pracchAdya saMkhyApUrakA upadadhati /
tatra tu sUtrAJNjasyamasti vA naveti cintyam //
tatr.a shlokAH /

UrvarsthishabdasaMyuktA shrutirmukhyAtra yA kR^itA /
AcAryeNaiva sUtrANAM ShaDbhAgIyA kR^ite tu sA /
AkyAtamarthaM cAcAryaistathorvasthIti sUtritam /
ShaDbhAgIyApadaM taddvadapyanyaiHsUtrritaM paraiH /
hiraNyakeshinAM shulbe tathorvasthIti sUtritam /
vyAkhyAtAro 'pi tatraitat ShaDbhIgAyAparaM viduH /
bodhAyanash ca bhagavAn same tu caturashrake /
turyapaJNcamaShaShThaish ca sapAdaiH karaNaM vyadhAt /
urvasthinAmadheyAnAmupadeshabalAdiha /
pracchAditAnAmAbhistadbAdhaHsUtrakR^iteShTate /
aratnayo 'pyaNUkAsh ca chAdane syurviparyayAt /
pUrvasminnaparasmiMsh ca prastAre saMbhavo na hi /
na paJNcadashabhAgIyA shrUyate tra dvitIyake /
shrUyante tAstu pUrvAgnau na tatpUrvo dvitIyakaH /
prakR^ititvAddvayoragnayoH nityatvAcca dvayorapi /
atastAsaM dvitIye 'gnau kathaM prAptirvimR^ishyatAm /
kintu tAsAM tu yatkAryaM tatrANUkAstu bodhitAH /
prathamAgnerato 'nyatra tatsthAne syuraNUkikAH /



ye tvatra paJNcadashabhAgIyAbhiHsaMkhyApUraNaM kurvanti te kimupadeshato vA prAptaM manvate? atideshato vA? ubhayathApi na yujyate /
dvayoH prakR^ititvAt prakR^itivikArAbhAvAcca /
nanvaNUkAH paJNcadashabhAgIyAnAM sthAna iti vacanasAmarthyAttAsAM prAptirbhaviShyati //
it.i cenna; paJNcadashabhAgIyAnAM sthAna iti vacanaM tatkArye saMkhyApUraNo 'NkAnAM prApakam /
na tu saMkhyApUraNamAtre tAsAmapyu padhAyakam /
tasmAccintyamidam /
sathamarthamidamAcAryeNoktaM? ucyate -- upadhIyamAnAnAmiShTakAnAM saMkhyAyAHsthAne /
na ca prastArai saMkhyAsampattau yadiShTakAbhedAdavayavabhedaHsyAt sa marShaNIya iti manyamAnenoktam /
tadetaddvitIyashyene pratipAdayiShyate /
kecittu yAj~nikA nyUnAdhikaprastAramagnau kurvanti samudAye saMkhyAsampattiM manyamAnAH /
tadayuktam /
paJNcadashaprabhR^itibhiH prastAreH sahasrAdi saMkhyAyAM sampAdyamAnAyAM visheShAshravaNe "samaM syAdashrutatvAt' iti prastArANAM dvishatatvasyaiva nyAyyatvAt /
rathacakrAgnau tasya karaNyA dvAdashenetyAdinA dvishatAnAmevotpAdanAcca /
nanu yatra yatra prastAre pUrayediti vacanAntaramasti tatra prastAre saMkhyApUraNamastu /
tadyatra nAsti tatra samudAyasaMkhyA pUraNasaMkhyA itarathA pUraNavacanasyAnarthakyaprasaN^gAt /
ucyate -- na tatrAnarthakyaprasaN^gaH /
kathaM? tatra hi nyAyaprAptaM saMkhyApUraNaM tatsAdhanatvena paJNcadashabhAgIyAnAM vidhAnAt /
yadi sarve prastArA dvishatAH kimarthameSha dvishata prastAra ityucyate? siddhe satyArambhamAtroddeshena sarveShAM prastArANAM dvishatatvasampAdanArtham /
yathaikavidhaprastAro dvishataH evamanye 'pi sarve prastArA dvishatasaMkhyAH kAryAH /
pUraNavacanA bhAve 'pIti nyAyaprAptamevArthaM anuvAdena draDhayitumayaM yatnaH /
tasmAtsarve prastArA dvishatAH kAryA iti na nyUnAdhikA iti siddhaM sarvaprastArANAM dvishatatvam /
prakR^itibhUtaHsaptavidha uktaH /
idAnIM nityA vikR^itaya ucyante -- ekavidheti /
ekavidhAdInAM ShaDvidhaparyantAnAM ShaNNAmagnInAM tasyatasyAgneH karaNInAM dvAdashabhAgena trayodashabhAgena ca iShTakAH kArayet /
atraikavidhasya karaNI shataM viMshatiH (120) aN^gulayaH /
dvividhasya ekonasaptatishataM aN^gulayaH catuviMshatitilAsh ca /
(169 2 /
3 4 /
4) trividhasya dve shate sapta N^gulayaH ekonatriMshattilAsh ca (207 2 /
3 9 /
4) caturvidhasya dve shate catvAriMshaccAN^gulayaH (240) paJNcavidhasya dve shate ShaShThiraN^gulayaH ekAdasha tilAsh ca (260 1 /
3 1 /
4) ShaDvidhasya dve shate trinavatiraN^gulayaH ekatriMshattilAsh ca (293 3 /
3 1 /
4) /
etAsAM karaNInAM sarvato dvAdashenaikaM karaNam /
sarvatastrayodashenaikaM karaNam /
tayoH pAdeShTakAnAM karaNaM cakArAdardheShTakAnAmapi ShaDvidhaM navavidhaM vA karaNam /
upadhAnamucyate -- abhitaH pAdAstisro rItyo dvAdashyaH /
tataH paJNcarItyastrayodashyaH /
tata ekA trayodashIpAdAH /
tata ekA trayodashyaH /
tatastisro 'bhitaH pAdA dvAdashyaH iti trayodasha rItyaH /
tatra dvitIyAyAM rItyAM dvAdashyAM caturthImaShTamIM ceShTakAmuddhR^itya dvedver'dheShTake upadadhyAt /
tatraiva copAntye uddhR^itya catasror'dheShTakAH /
dvishata eva prastAraH /
dvitIye prastAre dve rItyau trayodashyaH /
tata ekA 6yodashIpAdA /
tata ekAbhitaH pAdA trayodashyaH /
tatashcatasro rItyo dvAdashyaH /
tata ekAbhitaH pAdA dvAdashyaH /
tatastisro rItyastrayodashyaH iti trayodasha rItyaH /
atra madhyamAyAM vA ShaDuddhR^itya pAdA upadadhyAt /
prastAro dvishataH /
athavA prathamaprastAre dvAdashabhiH dvitIyastrayodashabhistathocyate /
kR^itsnadvAdashI pakShe dIrghA pAdeShTakA ardheShTakAsh ca tatratatra prathamaprastAre prAcyaHsaptadasha rItayaH /
tAHsarvA dvAdasheShTakAH /
tAsAM sarvAsAM dakShiNA ardheShTakAbhiH /
tata ekA pAdAbhistatastisro dvAdashIbhistata ekA pAdAbhistata ekArdhAbhiH /
tata ekA pAdAbhistatastisro dvAdashIbhiH /
antyArdhAbhirevaM saptadasha rItayaH /
tatra ShaJNcamIShaShThIsaptamInAM rItInAmantyAstisra uddhR^itya ekAM dvAdashImupadadhyAt /
athaikAdashI dvAdashI trayodashInAmantyAH tisra uddhR^itya ekAdashImupadadhyAt /
evaM dvishataH /
yaddvitIyaM trayodashabhirudIcyo rItayashcaturdasha tAsAM prathamArdhAbhirdvAdashItrayodashIbhirantyArdhAbhiH tAshcaturdasha rItayaH /
evaM dvAdasha shatamiShTakAH /
tatra pUrvArdhe trayodashIH ShaDuddhR^itya caturviMshatiM pAdA upadadhyAt /
evaM dvishataH /
yadi sarve prastArA dvAdashIbhiH tadA pUrvoktaprakAreNa prathamaM prastAramupadhAya dvitIyaprastArata eva rItIrudIcIrupadadhyAt /
eSha dvishataH /
yadi sarve trayodashIbhiH, tadA dvitIyaprastAroktA rItiH prathame prastAre prAcIrupadhAya pashcArdhe trayodashIruddhR^itya pAdA upadhAyAparasmin prastAre tA udIcIrupadadhyAt /
eSha dvishataH /
yadyekatra trayodashAnyato dvAdasha tadA prAgAyatA iShTakA udIcyaH trayodasha rItayaH /
tAHShaTpaJNcAshacchataM ca pUrvasyAM rItyAM paJNcamyAM cAShTAvaShTAvuddhR^ityAShTAviMshatiM pAdAH dve dve cArdhe /
evaM dvishataM /
dvitIye prastAre tA eva prAcyo rItayaH /
yatra dakShiNataH uttaratashvAShTAvaShTAvuddhR^itya pUrvavat pAdA ardhAshvopadadhyAdevaM dvishataH /
evameva praugAdiShvapi karaNAni dvAdashabhAgIyAbhistrayodashabhAgIyAbhirvA yathAyogamupadhAya pAdeShTakAbhirardheShTakAbhish ca saMkhyAM pUrayet /
alamatiprasaN^gena //


sundararAjIyA vyAkhyA

ubhayatra prAdeshamAtramavisheShAt /
tataH purastAddasha prAdeshAH pArshvayordvaidvau /

sarvamagniMapUrayet

Atmani vishayAbhiHsaha udIcyo dasha rItayaH, tAsAM dvitIyAM navamIM caturthIbhirupadadhAyAt, ShaShThIM prAdeshaiH /
AtmasheShe pakShayosh ca paJNcamabhAgIyAH /
pucchasyAparArdhe pArshvayormadhyato nava ShaDbhAgIyAH prAcyaH /
pucchasheShe dvAdashANUkAH /
evaM dvishataH prastAraH /

vyatyAsaM cinuyAd yAvataH prastArAMsh cikIrShet  || ˘p¡us_11.11b ||

___________________________________________________________



gatametat /

ekAdashaH khaNDaH.

kapardibhAShyam

kratvarthenopAdIyamAnAmAmekavidhAdInAM pakShapucchatvaM pratipAditam /
tathA teShAmupadhAnavidhiH kathaM bhavatItyucyate ----

___________________________________________________________


ekavidhaprabhR^itInAM karaNInAM dvAdashena trayodashenetIShTakAH kArayet  || ˘p¡us_12.1a ||

___________________________________________________________



karaNAnAM dvAdashena trayodashena kR^itaiHsamacaturashraiH iShTakAH kArayet /
sarvato dvAdashenaikaM karaNaM sarvatastrayodashena dvitIyam /

___________________________________________________________


pAdeShTakAsh ca vyatyAsaM cinuyAd yAvataH prastArAMsh cikIrShet  || ˘p¡us_12.1b ||

___________________________________________________________


pAdeShTakAsh ca dvAdashIvadhAstrayodashavidhAshvArdheShTakAsh ceti shulbAntaram /
asmAkamapi prauger'dheShTakAH kAryAH /
ekavidhAdiShvapi yadi prathamaprastAro dvAdashabhiH dvitIyastrayodashabhirityasminpAkSher'dheShTakAH kAryAH /
itarathA sa«dhayA na pUryata eva /

tatra shlokAH --

dvividhe mAnikA rajjuHsaptatyA ca shatena ca /

aN^gulInAM mitA sA syAdUnAgnerdashamistilaiH //


trividhe mAnikA rajjuraShTottarashatadvayam /

ShaDbhireva tilairUnA gaNakaiH parikalpitA //


vidhaspApi caturthasya mAnikA rajjurucyate /

mitA shatadvayenAtha catvAriMshAdhikena ca //


vidhasya paJNcamasyeyamaShTaShaShTiHshatadvayI /

ekAdashatilairyuktAM mAnikAM gaNakA viduH //


caturbhish ca navatyA ca shatAbhyAM ca mitA bhavet /

tribhireva tilairUnA ShaDhvidhasya vidhAnikA //


upadhAne 'bhitaH pAdAstisro rItyo 'tha dvAdashyaH /
tataH paJNca trayodashyaH /
tata ekA trayodashI /
pAdarItiH tata ekA trayodashI tatastisro 'bhitaH pAdA rItyAM dvAdashyaH /
dvitIyasyAM ekA caturthI ca tebhyo 'nyo 'ShTamI /
eSha prastAraH /
aparasmin prastAre dve rItyau trayodashyekA trayodashI pAdA tata ekAbhihitapAdA trayodashI /
tatashcatasro dvAdashyaH /
atha madhyamAHShaDiShTakAH caturbhedAH, eSha dvishataH prattAraH //


vyatyAsamiti -- gatametat //


___________________________________________________________


ekavidhaprabhR^itInAM prathamAhAreNa dvitIyena tR^itIyeneti yo yujyeta | sarveShAM yathA shrutisaN^khyA tathordhvapramANam  || ˘p¡us_12.2 ||

___________________________________________________________



ekavidhaprabhR^itInAM ShaDvidhaparyantAnAM sarveShAM prathamAhAre dvitIyAhAre ca yathA saN^khyAH shrUyante /
kimuktaM bhavati? yadi prathamAhAraHsahasrasaN^khyA jAnudaghnatA ca /
atha dvitIya ete yuktA eva /
te dharmAH saptArdhasvarUpayuktA eveti /
tacca vacanaM saptArdhaprakR^ititvaj~nApanArtham //


karavindIyA vyAkhyA

vyatyA rShet

gataM /
vikR^itiShu punarvyatyAse vacanaM kimartham? ucyate -- prakR^itau citInAM prastArANAM ca vaiShamyAt kimayaM vyatyAsaH prastAradharmaH citidharma iti kasyacitsandehaHsyAt /
vikR^itau tu dviprastArAshvitaya iti prastArayorvaiShamyemAyaM vyatyAsaH kasya dharma iti sandehe yAvantaH prastArAstAvato vyatyasya cinuyAt bhedAbhAvAya /
vyatyAsasya prastAradharmatApratipAdanAya punarvacanaM vyatyAsasya /

ekavi mANam

ekavidhaprabhR^itiShaDvidhaparyantAnAM prathamAhAraH prathamaprayogaH yo yujyeta bhR^ishaM yukto bhavati /
yathAshrutisaN^khyA shrutyuktena prakAreNa saN^khyA sahasrAdiH yathA bhR^ishaM yujyate tathordhvapramANaM jAnudaghnAdi ca yoyujyeteti ca sambandhaH /
ekavidhaprabhR^itiShaDvidhaparyantAnAM sarveShAM prathamAhAreNa dvitIyAhAreNa tR^itIyAhAreNa "sAhasraM cinvIta prathamaM cinvAnaH' ityAdyAH shrUyamANAH sAhasrAdisaN^khyAjAnudaghnAdiparimANAshvaiteShu sampAdyatayopadishyante /
etena ekavidhasya

prakR^ititve dvividhAdInAM tatprakR^ititve ca sAhasrAdisaN^khyAjAnudaghnAdi parimANatvaM siddhaM bhavati /
ekavidhAdayo 'pi nityA eva akAmasambandhAt /
prakR^itayo vikR^itayash ca nityA uktAH /
itAnIM kAmyAH praugAdaya ucyante /


___________________________________________________________


kAmyA guNavikArAH guNashAstratvAt  || ˘p¡us_12.3 ||

___________________________________________________________



nityasya saptavidhAgnervikArAH praugAdyAkR^itivisheSheNa guNena vikR^itAH /
kutaH? guNashAstratvAt /
guNaM shAsti vidadhAtIti guNashAstram /
"praugacitaM cinvIta' iti vakShyamANaM vAkyaM praugasyAgneshvayanamanUdya tatra bhAtR^ivyApanodanaphalArthaM praugAdyAkR^itivisheShaM guNaM vidhatte /
tasmAtkAmyAH praugAdayaH /
godohanAdivannityasyAgnerguNavikArAH na nityAH naiva prakR^itaya iti /

sundararAjIyA vyAkhyA

(vyatyA rShet)

"sandhyantarAle paJNcamabhAgIyAHsapAdAH' ityasyAparA vyAkhyApAdashabdena prastutA evANUkApAdA gR^ihyante /
prastutAsh ca pAdA aShTasaMkhyA iti tathaiveha grAhyAH /
tatraivamupadhAnam -- prathame prastAre sandhyantarAle pArshvayostriMshadaN^gulaM parishiShya madhyame paJNcatriMshatpaJNcamabhAgIyAH, parishiShTayostriMshadaN^gulayoH pashcAtpurastAcca dvedve paJNcadashAN^gule udIcyau, madhye tasrastisro 'NUkAH, paJNcamIbhiH pUrayitumashakyatvAtpucchasya pArshvayoH purataHShaTShaTpaJNcadashAN^gulAH /
pucchasheShe trayodashANUkAH, evaM kR^ite aShTonadvishataM bhavati /
pucchamadhye 'NUkAmekAmuddhR^itya dashAN^gulA navopadadhyAt /
Atmani dvitIye madhye vA mantropadhAnasaukaryArtham /
evaM dvishataH prastAraH /
aparasmin pucchavarjaM yathAsUtramevAtmani prAcyo dasha rItyaH /
tatra dakShiNasyAM madhye paJNcamIM nidhAya tataH prAkpashcAcca dvedve prAdeshamAyau /
evamuttarasyAM pucchasyAparArdhe pArshvayormadhye ca tisrastisraHShaDbhAgIyAH prAcyaH, pucchasheShe dvAdashANUkAH /
ye tu ShaDbhAgIyA necchanti teShAmapi pucchavarjamevamevopadhAnam /
tatra pucche prAdeshamupadhAyetyasya prAdesheShTakAmupadhAyetyevaM varNayanti /
anyathA bhedaprasaN^gAt /
prAdeshAshcaturbhAgIyAbhiHsaha na sherata iti sAmarthyAt paJNcamabhAgIyAnAmAkShepaH /
tatraivamupadhAnam -- pucchasyapUrvArdhe pArshvayoshcatasraH paJNcadashAhgulAH /
madhye ShaDaNUkAH /
aparArdhe paJNcadasha paJNcamyaH /
pucchAgre madhyamA abhito dve uddhR^ityAShTau prAdesheShTakA upadheyAH /
evamaShTonadvishataM bhavati /
tataH pUrvavadekAM catuthIM paJNcamIM voddhR^itya dashAN^gulA vAShTAN^gulA vopadadhyAt /
dvishataH prastAraH /
dvitIye prastAre pucche ShoDashANUkAH, AtmanyuttarasyAM rItyAM catasR^ibhyaH paJNcamIbhyaH prAktisro 'ShTAhgulA udIcyaH tata ekA paJNcamI /
tatastisro 'ShTAN^gulAH /
tatastisraH paJNcamyaH /
dakShiNArItiH pUrvavadeva /
dvishataH prastAraH /
evaM sAratniprAdeshasyopadhAnamuktamAcAryeNa /
tadrahitasyocyate -- pakShAgrayostisrastisro 'NUkAH /
tAsAM pasvAtpurastAcca dvedve paJNcadashAN^gule /
evamnyayorapyAtmAnaM pradeshenopetAH pArshvayoH ShaTShaT prAdeshAH /
pakShasheShe paJNcamyaH /
sandhyantarAle catvAriMshatpaJNcamabhAgIyA AtmasheShaH pUrvoktavadeva /
pucchasya pUrvArdhe pArshvayoraShTau paJNcadashAN^gulAH, padhye ShaDaNUkAH /
aparArdhe ShaDbhAgIyAbhirudIcyastisro rItayaH /
tAsu pUrvasyAM pArshvayordvedve dashAN^gule /
pucchasya pUrvArdhe ShaDbhAgIyA aShTAdasha /
aparArdhe pR^iShThayAmabhitaH paJNcamyAkuddhR^itya aShTau pAdeShTakA upadadhyAt /
Atmani pUrvarItau madhye paJNcamIM nidhAyAbhitashcatasraH pAdeShTakA upadadhyAt /
evaM dvishataH prastAraH /
athAtrApi ShaDbhAgIyAmanicchatAM pucchasya pArshvayoH purataHShaTShaT paJNcadashAN^gulAH /
pucchasheShe trayodashANUkAH /
pakShAgrayoshcatasrashcatasro 'NUkAH /
sheShaM pUrvoktavadeva /
evaM kR^ite caturashItishatamiShTakA bhavanti /
tatrAtmani pR^iShThayAnte caturthyau paJNcamyAvuddhR^ityAShTAdashAN^gulA aShTAN^gulA vopadadhyAt /
dvishataH prastAraH /
anyasmin prastAre pucchApyaye paJNcamabhAgIyA ityAdi yathAsUtram /
AtmanaH pUrvarItiH pUrvoktavat /
pucchasya pUrvArdhe 'ShTAvaNUkAH aparArdhe paJNcamyAvR^iddhR^ityAShTaN^gulA upadadhyAt /
dvishataH prastAraH /
evamupadhAnasyAnekaprakArA uktAH /
tatra yuktataraH prakAro vidvadbhirAdaraNIyaH /
sarveShveva prakAreShu pucchApyaye pakShApyaye vA anyataratra vishayA iShTakA upadhIyanta ityanusandhAtavyam //


ekAdashaH khaNDaH.

--------

ekavidhaprabhR^itInAMatpAdeShTakAshva.

vyAdhikaraNaHShThayau /
ekavidhaprabhR^itInAM ShaDvidhaparyantAnAM yAH karaNyaH tAsAM dvAdashena trayodasheneti samacaturashrA iShTakAH kArayet pAdeShTakAsh ca /

tAshcaturbAgIyA navamyash ceti dvividhAH /

tatra shlokAH --

aN^gulyo viMshatishataM karaNyekavidhe bhavet /

dvividhe saptatishataM j~neyaM dashatilonitam //


trividhe dve shate cAShTau cAN^gulyaSh,TtilonitAH /

caturvidhasya karaNI catvalAriMshacchatadvayam //


aShTaShaShTiH paJNcavidhe saikAdashatile shate /

ShaDvidhe trishatAcyAjyAHShaDaN^gulyastilAvapi //


ekavidhasya tAvat karaNyA dvAdashena dashAN^gulenaikaM karaNam /
tadardhena paJNcAN^gulena dvitIyaM pAdeShTakArUpam /
tR^itIyena ca saikAdashatilena tryaN^gulena tR^itIyam /
sA navamItyucyate /
evaM trayodashena sAShTatilena navAN^gulenaikam /
tadardhena tatpAdyAH /
caturaN^gulA saikaviMshatitilA /
tR^itIyena ca navamI tryaN^gulA satilatrayA /
evaM dvividhAdiShu draShTavyam /

vyatyAsaMashcikIrShet

tatra prastArayoranuktatvAt dvAdashItrayodashInAmeva sAvayavAnAM prastAreShu vyatyAsaH /
dvAdashIbhiHsAvayavabhirekaH prastAraH trayodashIbhirapara iti /
saMkAlitopadhAnaM tu na bhavatyavacanAt etadatidiShTapraugacityasambhavAcca /
tatra prathame prastAre agnimadhye navadvAdashInAM navamyashcaturashrIkR^itAH /
tAH paritaHShaShTiH pAdyAH /
tAH parito 'ShTAviMshatishataM dvAdashyaH /
uttarAMsa ekAmuddhR^itya cataslaH pAdyAH /
dvishataH prastAraH /
aparasmin trayodashabhiH pracchAdite navaShaShTishatamiShTakA bhavanti /
agnimadhyasthamuddhatya catasraH pAdyAH /
pratikoNaM catasrashcatasraH pAdyAH pR^iShThayAyAM pashcAtpurastAccaikaikAmuddhR^itya navanava navamyaH /
dvishataH prastAraH /

ekavidha rdhvapramANaM ekavidhAdInAmapi sahasrAdisaMkhyA /
UrdhvapramANaM ca jAnudaghnAdisaptavidhAdipadbhavatyeva /
kShetrApacaye 'pi saMkhyordhvapramANayornApacaya ityarthaH //


kapardibhAShyam

kAmyA guNavikArAH guNashAsratvAt // .3 //


kAmyAH praugAdayaH guNena vikR^itAH -- kimuktaM bhavati? guNasiddhirnAgneH /
kutaH? guNashAsratvAt /
shAstIti shAsram /
guNo 'tra shiShyate nAgniH /
tasmAdguNashAstratvAt godohanAdiva, dguNaphalAnyotAni //


___________________________________________________________


praugacitaM cinvIta bhrAtR^ivyavAn iti vij~nAyate  || ˘p¡us_12.4 ||

___________________________________________________________



praugaH shakaTapurvabhAgaH /
tadAkAraM cinvIta bhrAtR^ivyavAnyasya bahavaH bhrAtR^ivyAH sa evaM cinvIta /

___________________________________________________________


yAvAnagniH sAratniprAdesho dvistAvatIM bhUmiM caturashrAM kR^itvA pUrvasyAH karaNyA ardhAc chroNIM pratyAlikhet | sA nityA praugam  || ˘p¡us_12.5 ||

___________________________________________________________



___________________________________________________________


karANAni cayanam ity ekavidhoktam  || ˘p¡us_12.6a ||

___________________________________________________________



etacca vacanaM saptArdhasya prakR^ititvaj~nApanArtham /
paJNcadashabhiraN^gulairnavabhish ca tilaiH antarA catuHpuruShA rajjuH dvistAvatIM karoti /
tathA caturashraM vihR^itya sUtroktena mArgeNa shroNIM parilikhet /
karaNAni ca kArayet /
dvAdashena trayodashena sapAdena ca praugAkAraH //


___________________________________________________________


praugA iShTakAH kArayet  || ˘p¡us_12.6b ||

___________________________________________________________


catuHpuruShAratninA ca paJNcadashabhiraN^gulaistilairekaviMshatyA parimitA rajjurIShAmAtrI bhavati vAkShayoH pramANam /
tasyA dvAdashena ca trayodashena ca karaNAni ca kArayet /
dvAdashyA prathame prastAre praugamukhyaH /
catuHShaShTiH pAdeShTakAH catasrashcatasraHshroNyoH /
evaM caturviMshottaraM shataM /
catasror'dheShTakAHshroNyoreva /

anyasmin prastAre trayodashyaH shroNyoH pAdAshvatvAriMshat dvAvardhau aShTapaJNcAshadadhikashataM trayodashyaH /
prastAro dvishataH /
evaM vyatyAsaM cinuyAt /
tatra shlokAH --

ekonaviMshatyaratnibhiraN^gulIbhiHsahAShTabhiH /

tilAnAM paJNcaviMshatyA mitA pashcAdvimAnikA //


ekaviMshatyaratnibhiraN^gulInAM tripaJNcakaiH /

tilAnAmekaviMshatyA mitA tvekA vimAnikA //


kurvanti praugamagnimetAstisraHsamIkR^itAH /

AsAmeva yathAsUtraM karaNAni prakalpayet //


karavindIyA vyAkhyA

praugaMayate

praugaH shakaTasya pUrvabhAgaH /
tadAkR^itimagniM cinvIta /
bhrAdR^ivyavAnbhrAtR^ivyaishrAtrubhirbAdhyamAnaH /
tena bhrAtR^ivyAn praNudata eva //


yAvAna -- ugam.

yAvAnaratniprAdeshAbhyAM sahitaHsaptavidhaH tAvaddviguNAM samacaturashrAM bhUmiM kR^itvA tasya caturashrasya pUrvasyAH karaNyA madhyAdArabhya shroNI pratyakShNayA likhet /
saptArdhavidhasya dvistAvatI bhUmiH paJNcadashapuruShAH /
tasyAH karaNI trayaHpuruShAshcaturadhikashatAN^gulayaH paJNcaviMshatitilAsh ca /
tayApareNa yUpAvaTadeshaM saJNcaramavashiShyAnupraShTyaM samacaturashraM vihR^itya pUrvasyAH karaNyA ardhAcchoNI pratyAlikhet /
sA bhUmiHsaptavidhaparimitapraugAkR^itirbhavati //


kara -- yet

atra karaNI karaNInAM dvAdashatrayodashakR^itAni /
tAbhish ca yanaM prastAravyatyAsa ityevamAdyekavidhavat grAhyamityarthaH /
visheShastu praugA iShTakAH kArayet /
karaNAni praugAkR^itIni bhaveyuH /
tA dvAdashatrayodashabhAgIyAH pAdA ardhAsh ca praugAkR^itIni bhaveyuH /
tA dvAdashatrayodashabhAgIyAH pAdA ardhAsh ca praugAkArA grAhyAH /
catvAraH puruShA ekonacatvAriMshadaN^gulayaH ekaviMshatitilAsh ca praugasyaiShA mAtrA /
sA praugasya pArshvamAnI /
tasyAH dvAdashena trayodashena ca karaNAni kArayet /
pAdA ardhAsh ca dvAdasha bhAgIyAnAmaShTatriMshadahgulayaH paJNcaviMshatitilAsh ca /
eShAmAtrI tanmukham /
pArshvamAnyau tricatvAriMshadaN^gulayaH dashatilAsh ca /
argheShTakAnAmekApArshvamAnI /
saiva anyA aShTatriMshadaN^gulayaH paJNcaviMshatitilAsh ca /
ekonaviMshatiraN^gulayor'dhatrayodashatilAsh ca mukham /
pAdeShTakAnAmekonaviMshatiraN^gulayaH dvAviMshatitilAsh ca /
atha trayodashabhAgIyAnAM tAsAM paJNcatriMshadaN^gulayaH paJNcaviMshatitilAshcaikaM mukham /
pArshvamAnyau tilonacatvAriMshadaN^gulayaH /
ardheShTakAnAmapi saivaikA pArshvamAnI /
anyAH paJNcatriMshadaN^gulayaH paJNcaviMshatitilAsh ca /
saptadashAhgulayaH ekonatriMshattilAsh ca tilArdhAshvaikaM mukham /
pAdeShTakAnAM saptadashAN^gulaya ekonatriMshattilAshvaikaM mukham /
pArshvamAnyau viMshatiraN^gulayor'dhatilonAH /
upadhAne prathamaprastAre praugamukhe catuHShaShTiH pAdeShTakA upadadhyAt /
shroNyoshcatasrashcaturviMshottaraM shataM dvAdashyaH catasror'dheShTakAH /
eSha dvishataH prastAraH /
aparasmin shroNyorviMshativishatistrayodashapAdAH dvAvardhAvaShTapaJNcAshadadhikashataM trayodashyaH /
eSha dvishataH prastAraH /
vyatyAsash ca kAryaH //


sundararAjIyA vyAkhyA

kAmyAHaguNashAsratvAt

kAmyAH chandashvitprabhR^itayo 'gnayo nityasya caturashrasya guNavikArA, tasyaivAgneNamAtreNa vikR^itatvAt guNaphalaM svaphalaM ca sAdhayanti /
yathA agniShTomasya guNavikArA ukthyAdayaH /

praugacitaMavij~nAyate

praugaM shakaTasya mukhaM trikoNaM, tadvaccIyata iti praugacit /
"karmaNyagnayAkhyAyAm' iti vkip /

tasyAgnermAnamAha --

yAvAna likhet

sAratniprAdeshasya saptavidhasya karaNI trINi shatAnyaShTAviMshatishvAN^gulayor'dhadvAdashatilAH /
tasyA dvikaraNI pAdonapaJNcaShaShTicatuHshatAN^gulayaH dvistAvatyAH paJNcadashapuruShAyAshcaturashrIkR^itAyA bhUmeH karaNI /
praNagasya pArshvamAnI catvAraH puruSha ekonacatvAriMshadaN^gulaya ekaviMshatitilAsh ca /
yAvAnagnirityeva siddhe sAratniprAdeshagrahaNaM tasya pakShasya shAkhAntarIya tvena yatnasAdhyatvAt ekavidhAdiShvekashataparyanteShu kevaleShu kAratnipradesheShu ca yathAkAmaM guNavikArA bhavantyeveti pUrvameva pratipAditam /
tatra pakShapuccharahitAnAM praugacidAdInAM khAkAshashrutivedaikAmityAdinA AnItasya puruShasya viMshatishatatamo bhAgo 'N^guliH kalpyA /
tasyAshvatustriMsho bhAgastilaH /

sA praugaM nityA prakR^ityeva /
sA bhUmirevaM kR^ite praugaM bhavati /

karaNAni thoktaM karaNaM dvAdashena trayodashenetyAdinA /

praugAHarayet

dvAdashyAH pArshve tricatvAriMshadaN^gule sapAdadashItalayukte navatilonaM navatriMshadaN^gulamaparam /
teShAmardhaiH pAdyAH /
tR^itIyairnavamyaH /
trayodashyAstu catvAriMshadaN^gule tilone pArshve tripAdonaShATtriMshadaN^gulamaparam /
eteShAmardhaiH pAdyAH /
tR^itIyaish ca navamyaH /
upAdAne prathame prastAre catushvatvAriMshacchatena dvAdashIbhirudIcyo dvAdasha rItayaH /
madhyamarIticatuShTaye madhyo ShoDashoddhR^itya catuHShaShTiH pAdyAH /
praugamukhyAmud dhR^itya nava navamyaH /
dvishataH prastAraH /
aparasmin prastAre trayodashIbiH navaShaShTishatena trayodasha rItayaH /
tAsu dashamyAM sapteShTakA uddhR^itya viMshatiH pAdyAH /
aShTAdashanavamyash ca nidheyAH /
evaM dvishataH /

kapardibhAShyam

ubhayayaH praugaM cinvIta yaH kAmayeta prajAtAn bhrAtR^ivyAn nudeya pratijaniShyamANAn iti vij~nAyate  || ˘p¡us_12.7 ||

ubhayataHshakaTameva cinvIta yaH kAmayetotpannAnutpatsyamAnAMsh ca shatrUn bAdheyeti /

___________________________________________________________


yathA vimukhe shakaTe  || ˘p¡us_12.8 ||

___________________________________________________________


___________________________________________________________


tAvad eva tIrghaM caturashraM vihR^itya pUrvAparayoH karaNyor ardhAt tAvati dakShiNottarayor nipAtayet | sA nityobhabhayataH praugam  || ˘p¡us_12.9 ||

___________________________________________________________


___________________________________________________________


praugacitoktIH (-ktaM) | ubhayataH praugA iShTakAH kArayet  || ˘p¡us_12.10 ||

___________________________________________________________


tAvadeva saptAdhesya dviguNam /
iha tu dIrghacaturashrasya dviguNAyAmapramANavistAraH /
puruShadvayena tribiraradnibhiH ShoDashabhiraN^gulaiH sArdhaikaviMshatyA tilaiH mitA tirya«mAnImadhye ca shaN^kUnnihatya shaN^kuShu rajjvA veShTayitvA bAhyatastyajet /
saptaShashaShThishatatrayamaN^gulInAM caturdashabhistilaiHsArdhayIShAprAmANyam /
AsAM dvAdashena karaNAni kArayet /
praugacitobhayataH praugeShTakAH kArayet /
ubhayataH praughAkArAH iShTakAH pAdAshvobhayataH praughIbhUtAH /
cayanavidhiruktaH prauge /
tatra shlokaH --

trisaptakaistilairyuktAM sAShTAviMshashatatrayIm /

praugasyottarasyAgneH tirya«bhAnIM vidurbudhAH //


tiryagdviguNitAyAme caturashre havirbhujaH /

shaN^gUnnihatya madhyeShu karaNeShu caturShvapi //


rajjuM shahguShu saMyojya shroNyoraMsAn parityajet /

shiShTaM saptArdhameva syAcchakaTe vimukhe yathA //


caturdashatilairyuktaM saptaShaShTishatatrayam /

praughasyottarasyaitadIShAmAtraM prakalpitam //


IShAdvAdashabhAgena tathA bhAgottareNa cca /

ubhyataH praugIbhUtAH sapAdAH kArayediha //


karavindIyA vyAkhyA

ubha -- te

ubhayataH praugaM -- ubhayataH shakaTamukhaM /
prajAtAn shatrUna praNudeyaM janiShyamANAMsh ca praNudeyaM yathA na jAyante tathA karavANItyarthaH /

shrutipadaM vyAcaShTe ----

yathAvi -- toktAH

vimukhe -- nAnAmukhaghe shakaTe yathA pR^iShThai saMhite tiShThete tAdR^igAkAramubhayatra praugaM tathA cinvItetyarthaH /
tAvadeva pUrvoktaM sAratniprAdeshash ca saptavidhasya dviyuNaM dIrghaM caturashraM vihR^itya tirya«nAnIpArshvamAnInAM madhye shaN^kuM nihatya pUrvasmAcchaN^koH dakShiNaM shaN^kuM pratyakShNayA lisheddakShiNataH pashcimaM pashcimataH uttaramuttarataH pUrvaM, evaM lishedubhayataH praugAkR^itikShetraM bhavati /
vistAradviguNAyAmaM dIrghaM paJNcapuruShAH saptadashAN^gulAsvAyAmaH, dvau puruShAvaShTaShaShTiraN^gulaya ekaviMshatitilAsh ca tirya«bhAnI dIrghacaturashrasya //


ubhaya -- yet

karaNAni cayanavidhish ca praugavat /
visheShastUbhayataH praugAH iShTakAH /
trayaH puruShAHsapta cAN^gulayaH saptadasha tilAsh ca eShAM pramANam /
asya dvAdasho bhAgastriMshadaN^gulayaH paJNcaviMshatitilAsh ca /
trayodasho bhAgo 'ShTAviMshatiraN^gulayaH tribhAgonA nava tilAsh ca /
shatadvayaM aShTAviMshatiraN^gulayaH ekaviMshatitilAshvobhayataH praugasya tirya«bhAnI /
tasyA dvAdashabhAgena trayodashabhAgena parimitaM karaNaM yathA bhavati tathA bhavet karaNam /
ardheShTakA dvAdashabhAgIyAbhistrayodashabhAgIyAbhisva AyAmatastulyAH vistAratastadardhavistArAH /
pAdeShTakA AyAmato vistAratashvArdhAH /
prathame prastAre yAHpAdA upahitAH te dvitIye tadanyatropadheyAH /
dvAdashabhAgIyApakShe catasror'deShTakAH trayodashabhAgIyApakShe dve //


sundararAjIyA vyAkhyA

ubhayataHashakaTe

vimukhe -- viparyastamukhe prAkpashcAnmukhe yathA shakaTabhAge tAdR^igeSho 'gnirbhavati /

tAva yet

dvistAvadagnikShetravistAradviguNAyAmaM dIrghacaturashraM viharet /
trINi shatAnyaShTAviMshatishvAN^gulayo dvAviMshatitilAsh ca tirya«bhAnI /
dviguNA pArshvamAnI /
evaM vihR^itya pUrvAparayoH karaNyormadhyAt dakShiNottarayorNadhye nipAdayet /
bahiShpandyamapacchindyAt /

sutoktaH

ekavidhokta iShTakAdiH /

ubha rayet

dvAdashyAshvatvAri phalakAni triMshadaN^gulAni saikaviMshatitilAni /
ekAkShNayA saptaviMshatyaN^gulA trayodashatilayuktA /
dviguNAnyA /
eShAmardhaiH pAdyAstR^itIyairnavamyaH /
trayodashyAshvatvAri phalakAni sapAdShTAviMshatyaN^gulAni, ityekaH karNarajjuH /
eka vidhavadevopadhAMnam /
rItayastu koNAdimukhAH /
dvitIyaprastAre madhye viMshatiH pAdyAH, aShTAdasha navamyaH /
tA api madhyasthapAdAnAM pashcAtpuraktAcca vidheyAH //


kapardibhAShyam

rathacakracitaM cinvIta bhrAtR^ivyavAn iti vij~nAyate  || ˘p¡us_12.11 ||

yAvAn agniH sAratniprAdeshas tAvatIM bhUmiM parimaNDalAM kR^itvA tasmiMsh caturashram avadadhyAd yAvatsambhavet  || ˘p¡us_12.12 ||

___________________________________________________________



shulbAntare rathacakradvayamuktam; anenAcAryeNaikamevoktam; tasmAttadevocyate /
yAvAnagniHsAratniprAdesho dvistAvatIM bhUmiM parimaNDalAM kR^itvA ubhayataH praugasya yA tirya«bhAnI tayA caturashraM karaNaM kR^itvA teneShTakAH kArayet /
tAshcaturashre catushvatvA riMshadadhikashatamupadhAya tAsAM caturashramavadadhyAdyAvatsambhavet /

iti dvAdashaH khaNDaH

----------

___________________________________________________________


tasya karaNyA dvAdasheneShTakAH kArayet  || ˘p¡us_13.1 ||

___________________________________________________________



___________________________________________________________


tAsAM ShaT pradhAv upadhAya sheSham aShTadhA vibhajet  || ˘p¡us_13.2 ||

___________________________________________________________



pradhikAshvatvAraH /
teShu pradhikenaShu ShaDiShTakA dvAdashena kAritAH upadhAya sheShaM pradhikamaShTadhA vibhajet /
aShTabhirapadadhyAt /
tAsAM karaNaM vakShyAmaH -- trayastriMshadaN^gulamaShTabhistilairUnamekaM, ekatriMshadaN^gulaM dvAdashabhistilairUnamekaM, aShTAviMshatyaN^gulamekaM aShTAviMshatyaN^gulaM tilAbhyAM sahaikaM, etaishcaturbhiH phalakaiH ekaM karaNaM; tasya caturthaM phalakaM takShet /
yathA dhanurAkAraM bhavati yathA sharamaShTAdashatilamAtraM bhavati /
tathA ekatriMshadaN^gulaM dvAdashabhiktilairUnaM, ekaviMshatyaN^gulaM ekAdashabhiktilairUnamekaM, aShTAtriMshadaN^gulaM tribhistilaiHsahaikaM, navatriMshadaN^gulaM dvAdashatilaiH sahaikaM, etaishcaturbhiH dvitIyaM kararaNam /
asya caturthaM pUrvavattakShet /
sharapramANaM tilAbhyAM sahaikaM bhavati tathA takShet /
catvAriMshadahgulaM dashabhistilairUnamekaM, trayastrishadaN^gulaM dashabhistilairUnamekaM, dvAtriMshadaN^gulaM tilena sahaikaM, dvAtriMshadaN^gulaM dvAdashabhistilaiHsahaikaM, aShTAviMshatyaN^gulaM ekAdashabhistilaiHsahaikaM, paJNcacatvAriMshadaN^gulaM caturbhistilairUnamekaM, etaishcaturbhishcaturthaM karaNam /
tasya caturthaM takShet /
pUrvavacca pramANadvayaN^gulaM tribhistilairUnam -- tatra shlokau bhavataH ----

rajjuH kR^itAnyataH pAshA saptAshItishatAN^gulA /

vimAnaM rathacakrasya karotyoShA tu maNDalam /

caturashrakaraNI rajjuH catuHShaShTishatadvayI /

tilaistrayodashairyuktA rathacakre havirbhuji //


karavindIyA vyAkhyA

rathaca te

rathacakraM maNDalAkAraM brAtR^ivyavAn tairbAdhyamAnaH tAn jetum //


yAvA bhavet.

aratniprAdeshasahitasya karaNI dvau puruShAvaShTAshItirahgulayaH viShkambhArdhaM ekarvishatitilAsh ca /
tasya madhye yAvatsambhavaM caturashraM vihR^itya vilikhya //


tasya yet.

caturashrasya karaNI dve shate catuHShaShTishvAN^gulayaH trayodashatilAsh ca /
tasyA dvAdashabhAgaH satilA dvAviMshatilaN^gulayaH /
caturbhiH dvAdashabhAgIyAnAM karaNI /
tanmadhye catushvatvAriMshacchatamiShTacakAH tAsAM dvAdashabhAgIyAnAM ShaDiShTakA ekaikasmin pradhavupadhAya sampAdya sheShaM pradhisheShamaShTadhA vibhajet /
tatra pUrvasmin pradhau dakShiNArdhe catturashrakaraNIsamIpe dakShiNottarAstisraH dvAdashabhAgIyAH /
uttarato vyavalikhya shaSheM pradhyardhaM caturdhA vibhaje dekaikasmin bhAge ekaikaM karaNaM tisR^iNAM dvAdashabhAgIyAnAM purastAddvau bhAgau /
tasmin dakShiNato dvau bhAgau /
evaM vibhAge caturNAM vibhAgAnAM pashcattirya«mAnI trayastriMshadaN^gulayaH

ekatilam /
tatra dakShiNabhAgasya karaNaM tribhiH phalakairbhavati /
tatra tirya«bhAnyuktA caturNAM sameti pArshvamAnyekaiva /
sA ca ShaDvintiraN^gulayaH dvAdashatilAsh ca /
dvitIyaM vaktavyaM dvicatvAriMshadaN^galayaH sArdhapaJNcaviMshatitilAsh ca /
tadviShkambhArdhapramA NayA rajjvA karkaTena va''likhya takShayet /
dvitIyadakShiNapArshvamAnI saiva yA dakShiNasyottarA /
tirya«nAnI coktA /
uttarapArshvamAnI dvicatvAriMshadaN^gulayaH paJNcaviMshatitilAsh ca /
mukhaJNcatustriMshadaN^gulayaH dasha tilAsh ca /
tatpUrvaM takShayet /
tAnyeva viparItAnyuttarArdhe karaNAni /
eShaivottarArdhe vibhAgakalpanA /
tatra sarvaShAM saiva pashcAttirashvI /
dakShAttirashvI /
dakShiNamuttareShAM dakShiNaM bhavati /
tAnyeva tAnyeva mukhAni /
atra caturthavat paJNcamaM /
tR^itIyavat ShaShTham /
dvitIyavat saptamam /
prathamavadaShTamam /
evaM dakShiNottarapashcimapradhiShu dakShiNottarapashcimamukhAnyetAni karaNAni bhavanti //


sundararAjIyA vyAkhyA

rathacakra tsaMbhavet

viShkambho maNDalavidhAveva prapaJNcitaH /
madhye shaN^kuM nihatya paJNcAshItishatAN^gulena caturdashatilayuktena parimaNDalaM bhramayet /
tasya pariNAhastilanyUnaM paJNcaShaShThayadhikashatottarasahasrAN^gulayaH /
tasya madhye viShkambhArdhadvikaraNyA dviShaShTishatadvayAN^gulayA saptatilasahitayA samacaturashramavadadhyAt /
caturashrAdbahishvatvAraH pradhayaH //


iti dvAdashaH khaNDaH

----------

tasya kAreyet

dvAviMshatyaN^gulena paJNcatilonena samacaturashrakaraNam /
caturashramadhye catushvatvAriMshacchatamiShTakAHsherate /

tAsAM -- vibhajet.

pradhimadhye ShaT caturashrA upadhAya tasya pradheHsheShamaShTadhA vibhajet /
upahitAnAM ShaNNAM pArshvayordvedve mukhe catasra udIritAH /
tAsAM catvAri karaNAni /
trikoNamAdyam /
tasya tilatrayayuktaM ShaDviMshatyaN^gulamekaM tiryakphalakam /
sArdhasaptatilahInaM trayastriMshadaN^gulaM dvitIyam /
ekAdashatilayuktadvicatvAriMshadaN^gulaM tR^itI yam /
karNarUpaM taddhanuriva takShet /
yathA ShaTtilayuktAN^guliHsharo bhavati /
dvitIyasya ShaDviMshatyaN^gulaM tilatrayayuktaM tiryakphalakamekam /
ekAdashatilayuktaM dvicatvAriMshadaN^gulamaparam /
saptatilonaM trayastriMshadaN^gulamekaM pArshvam /
ShaTtriMshakaM saviMshatitilaM pArshvAntaram /
taddhanuriva takShet /
yathA tilatrayonAN^guliHsharo bhavati /
tR^itIyasya sArdhaviMshatyaN^gulamekaM tiryakphalakam /
triMshakaM ShoDashatilahInaM dvitIyam /
saptatilonaM trayastrishakamekaM pArshvAntaram, taddhanuriva takShet /
paJNcaviMshatitilAstasya sharaH /
etAnyeva catvAri karaNAni anyasmin pradhyardhe viparyAsena bhavanti /
eva meva catvAraH pradhayaH //


kapardibhAShyam

___________________________________________________________


upadhAne caturashrasyAvAntaradeshAn prati sraktIH sampAdayet | madhyAnItarasmin prastAre | vyatyAsaM cinuyAd yAvataH prastArAMsh cikIrShet  || ˘p¡us_13.3 ||

___________________________________________________________



gatametat /
eSha eva prastAro maNDale shmashAne droNe ca /

___________________________________________________________


droNacitaM cinvItAnnakAma iti vij~nAyate  || ˘p¡us_13.4 ||

___________________________________________________________



annakAmasya droNaciditi shrutiH /

___________________________________________________________


dvayAni tu khalu droNAni, caturashrANi parimaNDalAni ca  || ˘p¡us_13.5 ||

___________________________________________________________



___________________________________________________________


tatra yathAkAmI shabdArthasya vishayitvAt  || ˘p¡us_13.6 ||

___________________________________________________________



droNashabdo jalAdhArasya vartulAkArasya vAcakaH /
dArumayasya satsarukasya caturashrasya ca /
tatraikataro gR^ihyata ityucyate /
yathAkAmI caturashraM parimaNDalaM vA /
agR^ihyamANatvAdvisheShasya caturashraM parimaNDalaM vA cinuyAt /
ubhayashabdapravR^iteH //


___________________________________________________________


caturashraM vA yasya guNashAstram  || ˘p¡us_13.7 ||

___________________________________________________________



___________________________________________________________


sa caturashraH  || ˘p¡us_13.8 ||

___________________________________________________________



___________________________________________________________


pashcAt tsarur bhavaty anurUpatvAyeti vij~nAyate  || ˘p¡us_13.9 ||

___________________________________________________________



vAshabdaH pakShavyAvR^ittau /
na vikalpArthaH /
naiSha maNDalAkArashvetavyaH; caturashra eva cetavyaH /
yasya guNashAstraM "droNe vA annaM bhriyate' iti /
taccaturashre yujyate na vartulAkAradroNe /
ato guNasambandhAccaturashra eva nishvIyeta /
tasmAccaturashra eva cetavyaH /
pashcAtpucchasthAnetsarurbhavati anurupatva shruteH, tathAkArasaMpAdanAya /

karavindIyA vyAkhyA

upadhAr -- Shet.

gatam.

droNa -- te.

annAdhAraM pAtraM droNamityucyate /
tadAkAraM cinvIta annakAmaH /

dvayAni -- ca.

tushabdo bhede /
na praugAdivadekaprakArANi droNAni kintu dviprakArANi catushrANi parimaNDalAni ca /
khalushabdaH prasiddhau //


yA -- tvAt --

gatam.

ubhayatra droNashabdaprayogAdubhayaprakArau grAhyau //


catura -- shraH

caturashrANyeva grAhyANi /
kutaH? yasyedaM guNashAstraM sa caturashraH, prAkR^itaM caturashraM agnimanUdyAnnakAmAya droNAkAraM vidhIyate /
ata idamapi caturashrameva grAhyamityarthaH //


pashcA -- te.

AtmanaH pashcAt pucchasthAnetsarurbhavati /
tsarurmuShTiH /
prA«bhukhAvasthitastha puruShasya pashcAt sthitaH droNo 'pi pashcAnmuShTirbhaviShyati /
evamihApItyarthaH //


sundararAjIyA vyAkhyA

upAdhAne -- caturashraM vA.

tatra hetumAha --

yasya -- sa caturashraH.

guNaprApakaHsamacaturashraH /
yasya -- agneH /

pashcAstaru -- vij~nAyate /

pashcAtsaruryasya sa tathoktaH /
asamAso vA /
tsarushbada ubhayaliN^gaH /
"tsaruH pumAna' iti naighaNTukaH pramAdaH /

"dashamaMtsaru' iti nirdeshAt /
anurUpatvaM droNAnurUpyam /

etacca maNDalacaturashrayoHsamAnam /
tathAha bhAradvAjaH --

droNicitaM cinvItAnnakAmashcaturashraM parimaNDalaM vA pashcAtsarurbhavati /
iti /
spaShTamevAha kAtyAyanaH --

"dashamabhAgo vR^ittaH pashcAtpurastAdvA paNDale 'pyevameva' iti /

kapardibhAShyam

___________________________________________________________


sarvasyA bhUmer dashamaM tsarus tasya pucchena nirhAra uktaH  || ˘p¡us_13.10 ||

___________________________________________________________



___________________________________________________________


tasya karaNyA dvAdasheneShTakAH kArayet | adhyardhAH pAdeShTakAsh ca  || ˘p¡us_13.11 ||

___________________________________________________________



dvAdashacaturbhAgIyAkShetraM sAratniprAdeshasya dashamoM'shaH /
ShaShThayaN^gulapramANaM tirya«bhAnI tasya dvikaraNI pArshvamAnI /
tasyA kShNayA rajjvA kR^ite caturashre dvAdashacaturbhAgIyA kShetraM bhavati /
yacsaroH pramANam /
tayaiva triguNIkR^itayA droNaH /

tasya pucchena nirhAra uktaH -- pucchenaiva mAnamArgo vyAkhyAtaH /
tasya karaNyA dvAdasheShTakAH kArayot tasyeti droNaH parAmR^ishyate natsaruH sa ca trikoNa samadeshena caturbhAgIyenetyarthaH /
adhyardhAH pAdeShTekAsh ca atra vipratipannA yAj~nikAH akShNayA pAdamicchanti kecit /
keciddIrghapadapAdamardheShTakAH kartavyAH tAbhirvinA saMkhyApUraNasyAshakyatvAt /
vktamuktaM shulbAntare "ardheShTakAsveti /
ihApi cakArAdardheShTakAshceti /
karaNAni ca ShTtriMshadaN^gulaM tilonamekaM karaNaJNca; ekato 'dhyardhaM dvitIyaM; prathamakaraNamubhayato 'bhNayA caturdhA dIrghaM,' tena pAdAnAM tR^itIyaM karaNaM, tR^itIyenaiva karaNena dIrgheNa vAr'dheShTakAnAM karaNaM caturtham /

___________________________________________________________


upadhAne 'dhyardhAH purastAt pratIcIr Atmany upadadhAti | tsarvarge shroNyosh ca prAcIH  || ˘p¡us_13.12 ||

___________________________________________________________



___________________________________________________________


sarvam agniM caturashrAbhiH pracchAdayet  || ˘p¡us_13.13 ||

___________________________________________________________



___________________________________________________________


pAdeShTakAbhiH saN^khyAM pUrayet  || ˘p¡us_13.14 ||

___________________________________________________________



___________________________________________________________


aparasmin prastAre 'dhyardhA dakShiNata udIcIr Atmany upadadhAty uttaratash ca dakShiNAs tsarupArshvayor dakShiNA utIcIsh ca  || ˘p¡us_13.15 ||

___________________________________________________________



___________________________________________________________


sarvamagniM caturashrAbhiH pracchAdayet  || ˘p¡us_13.16 ||

___________________________________________________________



___________________________________________________________


pAdeShTakAkShiH saN^kyAM pUrayet  || ˘p¡us_13.17 ||

___________________________________________________________



___________________________________________________________


vyatyAsaM cinuyAd yAvataH prastArAMshcikIrShet  || ˘p¡us_13.18 ||

___________________________________________________________



iti trayodashaH khaNDaH

----------

upAdhAne yathAsUtramadhyardhA upadhAya pUrvArdhe saptadasheShTakA akShNayA chindyAt dvAvar dhau /
yadi dIrghAshvet pAdA uttarasyAM rItyAM nevaShTakAH chindyAt yathA prAcIH prapAdAH yathA dakShiNasyAmaShTau tathaiva prAcIrekAdvidhA /
tatra tathaiva pUrNaH prastAraH /
aparasminprastAre pashcAdAtmanyaShTAdasheShTakAH karaNe chindyAt /
dve dve iShTake dvidhAkaraNenaiva /
yadi dIrghAH pAdAH pUrvasyAM rItyAM naveShTakA bhindyAt /
yathA vA udIcyAHshroNyA dve dvetsaroH pashcAdevAgrataH pAshamadhyer'dhAH pAdAshvodIcyaH /
evaM prastAro dvishataH /
tatra shlokA bhavanti ----

mitAstribhistilairUnA caturbhish ca shatena ca /

droNasyaiShAtsarormAtrA tasya triguNutaiva sA //


pAdA ardhAsh ca bhedAsyuH karaNAni vibhAvasau /

droNAkhye tu smashAne ca caturashre havirbhuji //


prastAre prathame pAdA yatra syustatra nottare /

dvAvardhau prathamastAre catasra stUttare stare //


nidhAya cottare stAre adhyardhatvavipUrvake /

adhyardhA yatra tatra syuH pAdA dIrghA yadi tvatha //


prAcyasyuH prathame stAre udIcyastUttare stare /

abhitaH pAdamadhyardhA rItayasapta cottare //
it.i //


karavindIyA vyAkhyA

sarva -- ktaH

sarvasyAgnikShetrasya dashamaushaHtsaruH /
chAndasonapuMsakaliMN^ganirdeshaH /
sAratnipradeshasya dashamobhAgo dvAdashabhAgIyAkShetram /
tasyatsarornirhAraH samudAyAt pR^ithak karaNaM pucchena pucchapradeshena bhavet /
sa ukto nirhAraH caturashrAccaturashraM nijihIrShanniti /
caturashrasyAtmanaH karaNI shatatrayamekAdashAN^gulayaH ShaDviMshatitilAsh ca /
tsarostutryadhikaM shatamaN^kulayaH ekatriMshattilAsh ca //


karaNyaH kA tasya -- ka sh ca

tasyadroNasya karaNI dashakI ShaDviMshatirahgulayaH tilonAH /
dvAdashabhIgIyAnAM karaNI ekataHShaDviMshatiraN^gulayaH tilonAH anyatraikonacatvAriMshadaN^gulayaH adhyardhatilonAH dvitIyaM karaNaM pAdeShTakA dvAdashabhAgIyAnAmeva /
cakArAdardheShTakAsh ca /
tAbhirvinAsaN^khyApUraNAshakteH uktaJNca shulbAntare pAdeShTakA ardheShTakAsh ceti prathamakaraNamakShNayA bhindyAt //


sApAdeShTakA athavA dvAdashabhAgA pArshvamAnikA /
tatturIyaM /
tiryakmAnikA pAdeShTakA //


upadhAne prAcIH

Atmani pUrvabhAge dvAdasheShTakAH pratIcIrupadadhAti /
tsarvarge catasraH /
shroNyoH pratyekaJNcatasraH /
evaM caturviMshati radhyardhAH //


sarva -- yet

shiShTamagnikShetraM dvAdashabhAgIyAbhiH pracchAdayet pucche caturiShTake dve rItyau dvayoH purastAr pucchApya ya vishayarUpaikAH caturiShTakAsh ca /
tasyAH purastAddishyekA /
atmani dvAdasheShTakAH udIcyonavarItayaH /
ekaviMshati shataM caturashrAH /
caturviMshatiradhyardhAH /
uttarasminpArshva navacaturashrA udhR^itya ShaTtriMshataM dIrghAH pAdAH pratIcIrupadadhyAt /
dakShiNasmin pArshveca navoddhR^ityaShTtriMshataMpAdAH /
ShUrvasyAM dishi dvAdhashabhAgIyAnAmupAntye uddhR^ityadveddve cArde upadadhyAt /
akShNayApAdAshvet pUrvArdhe 'ShTAdashacaturashrA udhR^ityadvisaptatipAdAH dve iShTake uddhR^itya dve dve cArdhe /
dvishataH eSha prastAraH //


aparasmin -- udIcIsh ca

Asmani dakShiNatodvAdasha /
tathaivottarataH /
pucchapArshvayoshcatasrashcatasraH /
prAcyorItayaH dvAtriMshat //


sarva -- yet

pucche catasrashcaturashrA Atmani dvAdasheShTakAH prAcyonavarItayaH /
tAdvAdashashatam /
pashcAdAtmani /
dashacaturashrA uddhR^itya dvAtriMshatamakShNayApAdA upadadhyAt /
catasrashvArvAH dIrghAshvet pAdAH pUrvasyAM rItyAM naveShTakA uddhR^itya ShaTatriMshataM pAdA utIcya upadadhyAt /
pashcAdAtmanyaShTAdasha caturashrAH navapAdA utIcIrupadhAya tAsAM purastAdabhito dvipAdAH saptArdhAH upadhAyatAsAM purastAdaShTAdashArdA upadhAyatAsAM purastAnnavapAdA upadadhyAt /
dvishata eShaprastAraH /

sundararAjIyA vyAkhyA

sarvasyA uktaH

pucchamivAtmano vahirbhUtaM pashcAnminuyAdityarthaH ta6 caturashradroNacit dvAdhashatrishatAN^gulenAShThatilonena samacaturashraH tasya pashcAnmadhyadeshe karaNItR^itIyenatsarusamacaturashram /

tasya karaNya kArayet

AtmakaraNyA dvAdashena ShaDviMshatyaN^gulenaikatilonena samacaturashrAH /

adhyardhAH -- pAdeShTakAsh ca

tR^itIyena ca navamyaH pUrvavat /

upAdAne -- dadhAti

dvAdashIbhirudIcI rItiH //


tsarvargre -- prAcIH

tsarvargre catasro 'dhyardhAH, shroNyash ca catasrashcatasraH /
evaM dvAdasha /

sarvamagniM -- pracchAdayet

dvAdhashIbhirevaM pracchAdite 'ShTAcatvAriMshacchataM bhavati /

pAdeShTakAbhiH -- pUrayet

Atmani prAcyo dvAdasharItayaH /
tatra dadiNasyAM pashcAddvayaM hitvA pUrvAstisro navamya udIcyaH /
tato dvAdasha pAdyAH /
tatastisro navamyaH /
tataH prAkapAdyA dvAdasha /
tatastisro navamyaH udIcyaH /
tataH prAgdvAdashyadhyardhe /
evameva dvAdashIrItiH /
evaM dvishataH prastAraH //


aparasmin -- ucIcIsh ca

dvAdasha dvAdasha /
dakShiNeti dvitIyAvahuvacanasvIkAraH /
tsarupArshvayordakShiNA udIcIshcatasrashcatasraH /

sarvamagniM -- pracchAdayet

catushvatvAriMshacchataM bhavati //


pAdeShTakAbhi'-- pUrayet

AtmanyudIcyo dvAdasha rItayaH /
atrAparasyAM dakShiNAdhyardhAyA udaktisro navamyaH prAcyaH /
tato 'ShTau pAdyAH /
tatastisro navamyaH /
tato dvAdashI tatastisro navamyaH /
tato 'ShTau pAdyAH tatastisro navamyaH /
tatodvAdashI /
tatastisro navamyaH /
tato 'dhyardhA /
evaM pUrvA rItiH /
dvishataH prastAraH /

vyatyAsaM ---- cikIrShet

atha parimaNDalasya droNaciteH prakAro vakShyate /

ShaTsaptatishatA N^gulashtrayastilono veNurubhayatAshchidraH /
madhyeshaN^kuM nihatya tasmin veNoshchidraM pratimucya chidrAntareNa parimaNlaM parilikhet /
madhyashaN^koH pashcAdaShTaShaShTishatAN^gule satiladvaye shaN^kuH /
tasya pashcAtsaruH /
samacarashraM tiladvayonacatuHshatAN^gulaM kuryAt /
maNDalamadhyashaN^koH pashcAccatuHshatAN^gule tilatrayone shaN^kaM nihatya tasmin veNochidraM pratimucyAnyena cchidreNatsaruNo dakShiNAparakoNAdArabhya uttarAparakoNAdAlikhet, yathAtsarvagraM pradhyAkAraM bhavati /
maNDalabhramaNetsarupurvAnter'dhe yAvaddhriyate tAvatpashcAdAgacchati /
tato maNjalamadhye pUrvavaccaturashraM navacatvAriMshad dvishatAN^gulamaShTatilonamavadadhyAt /
tasya karaNyA dvAdasheneShTakAH ekaviMshatyaN^gulA navItalonAH caturashramadhye catushvatvAriMshacchatamiShTakAHsherate /
tato dIrghamekaM karaNam /
tasya tilonaShaDviMshatyahgulA tilashvI /
catustriMshakaM dvAviMshatitilaM pArshvam /
tAH pradhimUlamadhye catasrashcatasro nidheyAH pUrvAparayoH prAgAyatA dakShiNottarayorudagAyatAH /
pradhisheSheShu saptasapteShTakAH /
catasR^iNAM mukheShu tisraH /
pArshvayordvedve iti tAsAM catvari karaNAni /
trikoNamAdyaM, tasya ShaTtilonamaShTAviMshatyaN^gulamekaM phalakaM /
ShaTtriMshakam saptatilonaM dvitIyam /
tryaMshonitaM ShaTcatvAriMshadaN^gulaM tR^itIyaM karNarUpaM, taddhanuriva takShet, yathAdhyardhAN^guliHsharo bhavet /
dvidIyasya ShaTtilonamaShTAviMshakamekaM tilyakphalakam /
tryaMshonacatushvatvAriMshadaN^gulamanyat /
saptatilaM ShaTtriMshakamekaM pArshvam /
sAShTAdashatilaM navatriMshakaM pArshvAntaram /
taddhanuriva takShet, yathA sa catustilAN^guliHsharaH /
tR^itIyasya satilaM navakamekaM tiryakphalakamekam /
satilaM ShoDashAhgulamanyat /
dvAdashatilonaM paJNcatriMshadaN^gulamekaM pArshvaM dvAdashatilayuktaM paJNcatriMshakaM pArshvAntaram, taddhanuriva takShet /
triMshattilAHsharaH /
caturthasya satile ShoDashike tirashvayau pArshve ca dashatilonepaJNcatriMshake /
ephaM pArshvaM dhanuriva takShet /
ekAnnatriMshattilAHsharaH /
eShA iShTakA pradhimadhye sthApyA, abhitastisrastisraH pUrvoktAH kramotkrameNa /
evaM maNDalakShetre aShTAshItishatamiShTakA bhavanti /

tato 'parapradhermadhyAstisra uddhR^ityatsarvagre nidadhyAt /
tsarusheShe dvAdasha dIrgheShTakAH /
dvishataH prastAraH /
evamevAparaH prastAraH /
caturashrasraktayastu mahAdikShu bhavanti /
tsaruNastvanye dve karaNe /
tatraikasya tilone ShaDviMshatyaN^gule tilyakphalake /
catvAriMshadaN^gule tryaMshe pArshvai /
ekAkShNayArajhjustricatvAriMshadaN^gulA ShaTtilayuktA /
anyA tvekapaJNcAshadahgulA sadashatilA /
ekaM pArshvaphalakaM dhanuriva takShet /
sa catustilAN^guliHsharaH /
anyadapi pArshvamevameva /
antashvApaM tu bhavati yathaivamiShTakArUpaM, etA iShTakAHtsarupArshvayoshcatasrashcatasra udagAyatAH /
athAnyattilonaShaDviMshakaM samacaturashraM tasyaikaM tilyakphalaM dhanuriva takShet yathA ShoDashatilAHsharo bhavati /
evamevAnyattiryakphalakaM. antashvAvIM tu bhavati /
yathaivamiShTakAHtsarumadhye etAshcatasraH prastAro dvishataH /

vyatyasaM cinuyAdyavataH prastArAMshvitIShont //


iti trayodashaH khaNDaH

----------

kapardikShAShyam

samUhanneveShTakA upadadhAti  || ˘p¡us_14.2 ||
