___________________________________________________________


dikShu cAtvAlA bhavanti | tebhyaH puraShimabhyudUhatIti vij~nAyate  || ˘p¡us_14.3 ||

___________________________________________________________



samUhyaM ityupadhAnaprakAravisheSho nAkR^itivisheShaH /
prakR^itAvevAyaM vidhiH nAkR^itivikAreShu /
agnikShetrasya parita iShTakAH sthApayitvA yathA samUhanaM kriyate tathopadadhAti sarvata upAdAyopadadhAtIti yAvat /
sa evopadhAnavidhiH -- "pratidishaM cAtvAlA bhAvanti bahirvedi /
tebhyashvAtvAlebhyaH purIShaM pAMshUnabhyudR^ihatIti' shrutiH /

___________________________________________________________


paricAyyaM cinvIta grAmakAma iti vij~nAyate  || ˘p¡us_14.4 ||

___________________________________________________________



ayamapyupadhAnavidhiH //


___________________________________________________________


madhyamAM svayamAtR^iNNAM pradakShiNamiShTakAgaNaiH paricinoti | sa pariyAyyaH  || ˘p¡us_14.5 ||

___________________________________________________________



tR^itIyasyAM citau svayamAtR^iNNAmupadhAya iShTakAgaNaiH pradakShiNaM tAM svayamAtR^iNNAM parita upadadhAti /
sa paricAyyaH /

___________________________________________________________


upacAyyaM cinvIta grAmakAma iti vij~nAyate  || ˘p¡us_14.6 ||

___________________________________________________________



___________________________________________________________


paricAyyenoktaH  || ˘p¡us_14.7 ||

___________________________________________________________



pUrvavatparicAyyena vyatyAsaH /

karavindIyA vyAkhyA

samU -- te

samUhanamatra guNo nAkR^itivisheShaH /
tametamagniM cinvIta pashukAmaH /
samUhyashabdasya pravR^ittinimittamAha----

samUha dhAti

samUhanniva upadhAna itti parito 'gnikShetramiShTakAHsthApayitvA samUhan -- sampAdayanniva yathAyathA bAhyAbhyantarA iShTakAH unnatA bhaveyuH tathAtathopadadhyAt /
ayamarthaH -- yathA sarvamagnikShetramantarata unnataM bahirninataM bhavati tathA puriSheNa kR^itvA tatreShTakA upadhAya sapurIShAbiH kShetrapUraNaM kuryAditi //


dikShucA -- yate.

dikShu catR^isR^iShvapi cAtvAlAH /
purIShANAM vAhulyAccAtvAlabAhulayaM dikShvekaikaM cAtvAlaM shamyayA vimAya kAla eva prakR^itivaduttaravediShu yavayati /
tebhyaH

sarvebhyaH purIShANyAdAya citimabhyUhayediti /
prakR^itAnyeva vimAnakaraNopadhAnAni //


paricata -- te

paricayanamatra guNaH /
kShutyarthaM vyAcaShTe --

madhyamA -- yyaH.

tR^itIyasyAM citAvAkramaNAdisvayamAtR^iNNAntamupadhAya hiraNyeShTakAbhirgaNaiH pradakShiNaiH pradakShiNaM svayamAtR^iNNAM paricinuyAt /
prAkR^itAnAM sthAnAnAM vAdhakaM paricayanam /
eSha dvishataH /

upa -- ktaH

upacayanamapi guNaH /
upacayanaM samIte cayanam /
tAnyeva vimAnakaraNopadhAnAni /
sarvaM paricAyyavat /
ayaM bhedaH -- Adyasya bahirArabhya svayamAtR^iNNAsamIpe samAptiH /
dvitIyasya svayamAtR^iNNAsamIpa Arabhya vahiHsamAptiH /

sundararAjIyA vyAkhyA

atha caturdashaH khaNDaH

samU dhAti

agnanikShetraM parita iShTakAHsthApayitvA samUhan ekatra rAshIkUrvannivopadadhAti //


dikShu cAtvAlA sa paricAyyaH

svayamAtR^iNNAmupadhAyAnyAHsarvA iShTakAHsvayamAtR^iNNAM parita upadadhAti /
na tu prAcIH pratIcIrityAdayo visheShAH /
pUrvaHpUrvo gaNaHsavayamAtR^iNNAsamIpe /
tatastato bahiruttarauttaraH /
anayoHsamUhyaparicAyyayoH prakR^itivadeva rUpaM iShTakAsh ca visheShAvacanAt /
athavA samUhasya paritaHsthitvA samUhane kriyamANe maNDalarUpa iShTakAcayo bhavatItyarthAnmaNDalarUpatvamagnerbhavati /
paricAyyasyApi svayamAtR^iNNAparicayanaM maNDalarUpa evAgnAvupapadyate iti arthAdeva maNDalarUpatvaM /
tathAca bodhAyanaH -- samUhyaparicAyyau pUrveNa rathacakracitA vyAkhyAtAviti /

upacA -- kraH

pUrvasyaivedaM shAkAntarIyaM saMj~nAntaramityarthaH /

kapardibhAShTam

___________________________________________________________


shmashAnacitaM cinvIta yaH kAmayet pitR^iloka R^idhnuyAmiti vij~nAyate  || ˘p¡us_14.8 ||

___________________________________________________________



pitR^iloke R^idhyAsamiti yaH kAmayet sa evaM cinuyAt /

___________________________________________________________


dvayAni khalu shmamashAnAni caturashrANi parimaNDalAni ca  || ˘p¡us_14.9 ||

___________________________________________________________



___________________________________________________________


tatra yathAkAmI shabdArthasya vishayitvAt  || ˘p¡us_14.10 ||

___________________________________________________________



___________________________________________________________


caturashraM vA | yasya guNashAstram  || ˘p¡us_14.11 ||

___________________________________________________________



___________________________________________________________


sa caturashraH | tsaruvarjaM droNacitoktaH  || ˘p¡us_14.12 ||

___________________________________________________________



caturashrAkArANi santi shmashAnAni parimaNDalAkArANi ca /
tatrecchAtaH pravR^ittiH shabdasyobhayapravR^itteH /
yadi vartulAkAraH rathacakravat /
caturashraM veti -- gatametat // .//
yasya guNashAstraM pitR^ilokasambaddhaM taccaturashre shmashAne na vartule /
khAlA hi tatra nikShipyante /
yeShu paitR^imedhikakriyA teShAM pitÃNAM samvandhaH R^idhyA ca /
tasmAccaturashra eva cetavyaH yadi caturashrastadAtsaruvarjaM droNacitoktaH -- tatsarvaM droNacityeva vyAkhyAtam //


___________________________________________________________


chandashcitaM cinvIta pashukAma iti vij~nAyate  || ˘p¡us_14.13 ||

___________________________________________________________



chandobhireva yatreShTakAsvIyante taM chandasvivaM pashukAmashvinuyAdityasyAH shruterarthaM shrutidvayena vyAcaShTe --

___________________________________________________________


sarvaish chandobish cinuyAd ity ekam | prAkR^itair ity aparam  || ˘p¡us_14.14 ||

___________________________________________________________



caturdashaH khaNDaH

------

sarvaishchandobhirdAshatayibhishvetavya ityekA shrutiH /
prAkR^itaiH -- prakR^itau yAni chandAMsi agrirmUrdhetyAdIni tairevetyaparA shrutiH //


ityApastambasUtravivaraNe shulbAkhyaprashne kapardisvAmibhAShye

caturthaH paTalaH

karavindIyA vyAkhyA

shmashA -- te

shmashAnamiva cinvIta pitR^iloke vR^iddhiM kAmayamAnaH /

dvayAni -- yitvAt

gataM /
agnayAyatanaprakArarUpANi dvayAnyapi shmashAnAni loke dR^ishyante caturashrANi parimaNDalAni ca /

caturashaH -- shraH

prakR^ititvAccaturashrameva cinvIta na maNDalamiti samAsa uktaH /
shmashAnAni droNacitetivat kartavyAni /
tsaruM varjayedanyatsarvaM droNavat vimAnAni /
dvAdashabAgIyA adhyardhAH ardhAH pAdAsh ca dvAdashabhAgIyAHsaptaviMshatiraN^gulayaH trayodashatilAsh ca /
adhyardhA ekatastAdR^ishAH anyata ekacatvAriMshadaN^gulayaH trayash ca tilAH ardhAH pAdAH ekato dvAdashabhAgIyAsadR^ishAH anyatastadardhAH /
pAdA ekato dvAdashabhAgIyAsadR^ishAH anyato navAN^gulayaH sAdhikAshvatvArastilAsh ca /
upadhAne prathamaprastAre purastAt pashcAccAdhyardhAH caturashrAbhaiH pracchAdanaM /
pAdAbhirar dhAbhish ca saMkhyApUraNaM /
dvitIye dakShiNata uttaratashvAdhyardhAbhishcaturashrAbhiH pracchAdanAdi pUrvavat //


chanda -- te

chantobhiH R^igbhishvIyate iti cchandashvit etAvAneva visheShaH /
anyat sarvaM prakR^itireva //


sarvai -- kam

savairndashatayIgataishchantobhishvinuyAt /
tAni sahasradhA vibhajya teShAmekaikena bhAgenaikaikAmiShTakAmupadadhyAt /
yajuShAM sthAne chandAMsi bhaveyuH /
tatra yAvatyaH yajuShmatyaH iShTakAH tAvatyashchandAMsi vibhajya teShAmekaikena vibhAgenaikaikAmiShTakAM yajuShmatIrUpadadhyAt /
laukampR^iNAstu pUrvavadevana /
athavA dashatayIgataiHsarvaishchandobhirgAyatrIbhIstriShTubbhirjagatIbhiranuShTubbhirvR^ihatIbhiruShNigbhiH paN^ktibhirakSharapaN^ktibhirviShurupAbhistredhA vibhaktAbhiraticchandobhistridhA vibhaktaisarvAbhirddvipadAbhish ca purastAdAramya yAj~nasenIbhirupadadhyAt //


prAkR^i -- nAm

prAkR^itaiH agnikANDagataiH agnirmUrdhetyanuvAkasthairgAyatrayAdibhiH na dashatayIbhirityaparam /
nAsmAtparaM vibhajyata iti siddhAntitam /
atra shlokAH --

ekaikavR^iddhA ekaikadhA hyagnayaH kramasha ekashatam /

paTale tR^itiya uditAsteShAM bhedAshcaturtAdau //


prakR^itistvavahNInAmekavidhA vAtha saptavidhAH /

ekavidhaprakR^ititve tadA ShaNNAM na pakShapucchAni //


saptavidhaprakR^ititve bhavati ca teShAM sapakShapucchatvam /

saptavidhaprabhR^itInAM saiva bhavetprakR^itirekashatavidhAt //


karaNInAM dvAdashAMshaiH tairuktAMshayutAyutaiH /

pR^ithagutpannarUpAbhiriShTakAbhistridhopadheH //


traidhamekavidhAdInAM cAturvidhyaM sapakShataH /

evaM praugayugmasya traidhaM nAnyadapakShataH //


dvau caturashrau praugau rathacakradroNacitsamUhyash ca /

paryupapUrvau cAntyau shmashAnacicchandashvitishyenau /

ka«cidalajau saptavidhAH paJNcar pUvavaddashadahanAH //


praugacidubhayapraugo rathacakro droNacichshmashAnAgniH /

ete tvapakShapucchAH kUrmacidAdyAH paroktAsh ca /

anye sapakShapucchA agnaya uktAH pravakShyamaNAsh ca //


shyenapramukhAnanalAn vyAkhyAsye paTalayorihottarayoH //


iti karavindasvAmi kR^itAyAM shulbapradIpikAyAM caturthaH ShaTalaH

sundararAjIyA vyAkhyA

(shmasha -- yate) (dvayA -- tvAt) (catu) ktaH /

atra caturashratve trINi shatAnyaShTAviMshatishvAN^gulAH ekavintitilAsh ca karaNI /
tasyA dvAdashena saptaviMshatyaN^gulena trayodashatilayuktena dvAdashabhAgIyAH /
tadardhena pAdyAH tR^itIyena ca navamyaH /
adhArsh ca pUrvavat /
upAdhAne 'dhyardhA dvAdashapurastAtpratIcyaH /

pasvAddvAdasha prAcyaH /
sheShaM droNateva /
tatra sarvAbhAvAt ShoDasheShTakA hIyante /
ato'gnimadhye dve uddhR^ityAShTAdashanavamyo nidheyAH /
dvishataH prastAraH /
evamevAparaH /

prAcyudIcyostu viparyAsaH /
maNDale shmashAnIcadrathacakracitA vyAkhyAtaH

chandaHayate

chandobhishvIyat iti chandashvit /
chAndasaH karaNa upapade vkip /
anyatra karmaNyagnayAkhyAyAmiti /

sarvaiH paraM tatra sarvairgAyatrayAdibhi shcaturuttaraiH atidhR^iti paryantaiH caturdashabhirutkR^itiparyantairvaikaviMshatyA trivR^itkakubhAdivisheShayuktairdAshatayIbhya AhR^itaishchantaubiH sarvA iShTakAshvinuyAdityekaM mataM /
prAkR^itairagnir mUrdhetyanuvAkAdhItairyAj~nasenyarthaiH punaH punarabhyastairityaparaM mataM /
asyAgreH prakR^itivadeva rUpaM /
kecitu vayasAM vA eSha pratimayetyasyApi nityatvAdvayasa AkAramapIcchanti /
yathAha -- vodhAyanaH -- tasya rUpaM shyenAkR^itirbhavatIti //


iti shrImatsundahahAjakR^itAyAM shulbapradIpikAyAM caturthaH paTalaH

___________________________________________________________


shyenacitaM cinvIta suvargakAma iti vij~nAyate  || ˘p¡us_15.1 ||

___________________________________________________________



___________________________________________________________


vakrapakSho vyastapuccho bhavati  || ˘p¡us_15.2a ||

___________________________________________________________



shyena iva cetavyaH shyanacit tadAkAraM cinvIta /
AkR^ityAH phalamAkArasaMpAdanaM svayameva vakShyati /
anR^ijupakShaH vyastapuccho 'saN^kocitapucchaH /

kathaM vakratA? --

___________________________________________________________


pashcAt prA« udUhati |  purastAtpratya«« udUhati | evam iva hi vayasAM madhye pakShanirNAmo bhavatIti vij~nAyate  || ˘p¡us_15.2b ||

___________________________________________________________



unnayati purastAtpratya«« unnayati /
evameva vakrAH pakShA yasya sa vakrapakShaH /
hishabdaH prasiddhau /
evamiva -- evameva vayasAmutpatatAM madhye pakShanirNAmo namanaM bhavatIti shrutiH //


___________________________________________________________


yAvAn agniH sAratniprAdeshaH saptavidhaH saMpadyate | prAdeshaM caturtham Atmanash caturbhAgIyAsh cAShTau | tAsAM tisraH shira itarat pakShayor vibhajet  || ˘p¡us_15.3 ||

___________________________________________________________



aradninA prAdeshena ca virdhito 'gniH prAkR^ito yAvAn saMpadyate prAdesha iti gR^ihNIyAditi sheShaH /
sAratniprAdeshAgnau yatprAdeshaM pucche Atmani caturtaM puruShakShetraM caturbhAgIyAshvAShTau shiShTe puruShe 'ShTau caturbhAgIyAH kShetraM ca gR^ihItvA tAsAM caturbhAgIyAnAM disrashcaturbAgIyAHshirasi nidhAtavyAH /
itaratsarvaM pakShayorvibhajya kShipet /
ShaDaN^gulamAtraM prAdeshe /
ShaShTayaN^gulaM puruShe /
caturbhAgIyAsu paJNcasu pAdonaM navadashAN^gulam /
etadevaikaikasmina pakShe kShaipet /

___________________________________________________________


paJNcAratniH puruShaH | caturaratniH vyAyAmaH | caturviMshatyaN^gulayo 'ratniH | tadardhaM prAdesha iti k ptiH  || ˘p¡us_15.4 ||

___________________________________________________________


paJNceti -- etatpuruShasya pramANam /
caturiti -- etadaratnipramANam /
k ptiH -- evaM kalpanA /
itishabdaH prakAre /
anenana mArgeNa kalpayedityarthaH /
triMshadaN^gulaM caturbhAgIyam /

karavindIyA vyAkhyA

shyena -- te

shyenaH -- pakShivisheShaH /
tadAkAramagniM cinvIta svargakAmaH /
vayasAM vA eSha pratimayA cIyata iti vayomAtrasadR^ishaH prAkR^ito 'gniH /
ayaM tu shyenasadR^ishaH /
kIdR^ishaH shyena ityAha --

vakra -- te.

vakrau -- anR^ijU pakShau yasya sa vakrapakShaH /
vyastaM vistIrNaM pucchaM yasya mUlAdArabhya uparyupari vistIrNaM saH /
pashcAt prA«udUtIti udUhanamunnayanaM prathamapakShArdhaM mUlAdArabya pashcAtprabhR^iti prAgunnayet /
purastAtpratya««udUhati /
dvayaM pakShArdhaM madhyAdArabya purastAt prabhR^iti pratyagunnayet /
evamivahIti nipAdasamudAyaH prasiddhau /
vayasAM madhye -- shyenAnAM pakShayormadhye /
nirNAmaH -- nirNamanaM nirgatya prahvIbhAvaH /
vij~nAyate -- shrUyate dR^ishyat vA /
pakShanirNAma iti vacanasAmarthyAt pakShayormadhye nirNAmaH dR^ishyate -- pakShiNAM dR^ishyate iti //


yAvAna -- jet.

prAkR^itamagnimAtmapakShapucchashiraHsu vibhajet /
kAn vibAgAnityAha -- pucchAt prAdeshakShetramAtmanashvatuShpuruShAdekapuruShakShetrama (ShTau) ShTAdashacaturbhAgIyAH yAvati kShetre upadhIyante tAvaccAtmakShetraM saMgR^ihya tAsAM caturbAgIyAnAM tisro(gneH)gre shiraH kuryAt /
avashiShTapaJNca dasha(viMshati)caturbAgIyAH puruShaH prAdeshashvaprAkR^itayoH adhyaratnipuruShayoH pakShayorvibhajet -- kShipedityarthaH /
evaM satyardhadashamA aratnayashcaturbhAgonAN^gulishvaikaikaH pakShaH /
ardhatR^itIyapuruSha AtmA /
puruShamAtraM pucchaM /
tisrashcaturbhagIyAHshiraH //


paJNcAra -- k ptiH.

"paJNcAratniragnau puruShaH /
yAvAn puruSha UrdhvabAhustAvAna bhavatIti puruShapramANavisheShavidheH /
anyatra caturaradniH /
caturviMshatiraN^gulayo 'ratniH /
tadardhaM prAdeshaH /
sa ca dvAdashAhgulaH /
k ptiH-- acAryasya samayaH //


sundararAjIyA vyAkhyA

shyena yate

taittirIyake kAmyaprakaraNe paThito 'pyayaM shyenacit nitya eva svargaphalakatvAt caturashrAgnivattasyApi svargaphalakatvaM /
"suvargAya vA eSha lokAya cIyate /
yadagniH' iti liN^gAni cAtra prAgeva darshitAni /

vakra yate

shrutyanataranidaM shyenacidvAkyasya she,bhUtaM /
tatra vakratA pakShamadhye /
vyAsaH pucchAgre /
pakShayorvakrIkaraNaprakAramapi shrutirevAha ----

pasvAtprA«UdUhati pakShamadhye /
purastAtmatyu««udUhati pakShAgrApyayayoH /

evamiva hi vayasAM pakShasya madhye madhyapakShaM nirNAmo vakratA /
madhyepakShanirNAmaH -- vayasAmutpatatAM pakShamadhye nirNAma evamiva hi dR^ishyata ityarthaH /

yAvA te

sAratniprodashashcaturashro 'gniryAvAn sampadyate tAvAnevAyaM shyenaciddhavati /
sAratniprAdeshagrahaNasya prayojanamuktameva /

tatra --

prAde ShTau

AdadhIteti sheShaH pucche puruShAdadhikaM prAdeshamAtmanashcaturthaM puruShaM caturbhAgIyAshvAShTau Atmana evAdadhIta /
shiShTa AtmA /
ardhatR^itIyaH puruShaH /
pucchaM puruShapramANa(mAtra)meva /

tA -- shiraH

tAsAM tisrashcaturbhAgIyAH shiraH prakalpayet /

itara jet.

pucchAdAtmanashvAtra sheShaM dvedhA vibhajya pakShayornidadhyAt /
ekaikasmin pakShe prAdeshArdhaM ShaDaN^gulaM AtmacaturthAdardhaM ShaShTirahgulayaH /
paJNcAnAM caturbhAgIyAnAM madhye puruShAyAme pakShe nyaste pAdenA ekAnnatriMshatirahgulayaH prAkR^itaH pakShaH /
catushvatvAriMshadadhikashatAN^gulayaH /
ebhiH sahitaH pAdonaikAnnatriMshacchatadvayAN^gulaH sampadyate /
tadetadvakShyati ardhadashamA aratnaya ityAdi /

paJNcA k ptiH /

kaparhibhAShyam

___________________________________________________________


ardhadashamA aratnayo 'N^gulayash ca caturbhAgonAH pakShAyAmaH  || ˘p¡us_15.5 ||

___________________________________________________________



prAdeshadashamA aratnayo 'N^gulayash ca caturbhAgonAH pakShAyAmaH -- pakShayorAyamaH /
prAkR^itAH ShaDaratnayaH ardhapuruShe prAdeshasahitAratnidvayamaShTAdashAhgulAshcaturbhAgonAsh ca prAdeshe ShaDN^gulAH /
tA aShTAdashabhiHsahAratniH sarvaM sambhUyArdhadashamA aratnayo 'hgulAsva caturbhAgonAH /
eSha pakShayorAyAmaH /

___________________________________________________________


dvipuruShAM rajjum ubhayataHpAshAM karoti | madhye lakShaNam | pakShasyAparayoH koTyor antau niyamya lakShaNena prAcInam Ayacched evaM purastAt | sa nirNAmaH  || ˘p¡us_15.6 ||

etenottaraH pakSho vyAkhyAtaH  || ˘p¡us_15.7 ||

dvipuruShapramANAM rajjumubhayataH pAshAM kR^itvA madhye lakShaNaM; kuryAditi sheShaH /
anenaiva mArgeNottarasyApi pakShasya namanaM vyAkhyAtam /
eShA pakShayorvakratA // .7 //

AtmA dvipuruShAyAmo 'dhyardhapuruShavyAsaH  || ˘p¡us_15.8 ||

___________________________________________________________


pucche 'rdhapuruShavyAsaM puruShaM pratIcInam Ayacchet | tasya dakShiNato 'nyam uttaratash ca  || ˘p¡us_15.9a ||

___________________________________________________________



dvipjaruShAyAma AtmA adhdhardhapuruShavyAsaH /
evaM dIrghacaturashraM vihR^itya pucchasthAner'dhapuruShA tirya«bhAnI puruShapramANA pArshvamAnI bhavati yathA tathA yacchet -- kuryAdityarthaH /
tasya caturashrasya dakShiNapArshve 'nyaM tAdR^igvidhaM caturashramuttaratashvAnyam /
evaM trINi caturashrANi ardhapuruShavyAsAni /

___________________________________________________________


tAvakShNayA vyavalikhet | yathArdhapuruSho 'pyaye syAt  || ˘p¡us_15.9b ||

___________________________________________________________


___________________________________________________________


shirasy ardhapuruSheNa caturashraM kR^itvA pUrvasyAH karaNyA ardhAt tAvati dakShiNayor nipAtayet  || ˘p¡us_15.10 ||

___________________________________________________________



iti paJNcadashaH khaNDaH

----------

tau caturashrau yau pArshvasthau /
tAvakShNayA karNena Alikhet; yathApyaye Atmapucchasandhau ardhapuruShamAtraM kR^itaM pUrvasya bhavati /
prAcyamiva dakShiNaM prAcyamivottaram /
evaM kR^ite 'pyayer'dhapuruShamAtraM bhavati /
shiraHsthAner'dhaShuruShapramANena caturashraM kR^itvA pUrvasyAH karaNyA ardhAdArabya tAvatyevArdhe madhye nipAtayet -- Alikhet /
tisraH parishiShyanta ityuparitane vakShyati /
atrApi tisraH shirasItyuktam /

paJNcadashaH khaNDaH.

--------

karavindIyA vyAkhyA

ardhada -- yAmaH

apareNa yUpAvaTadeshaM saMcaramavashiShyetyAdi vimAya pakShApyayeShu shaN^kuM nihatya dakShiNottarayA rajjvA navAratnIn prAdeshamaN^gulaM caturbhAgonAM cAyAmaM kR^itvA pakShAgreShu shaN^kuM nihanyAt /
evamekAdashabhiraN^gulIbhiH prAdeshena ca puruSho hIyate /
tatrArdhAShTamAbhiraN^gulIbhirekA caturbhAgIyA bhavati /
tadardhenArdhadvipuruShAyAmAM rajjumubhayataH pAshAM kR^itvA madhye lakShaNaM kR^itvA pakShasyAparakoTishaN^kvoH pratimucya lakShaNena prAcImapasArya shaN^kuM nihanyAt /
evaM tasyaiva pUrvayoH koTyoH pratimucya lakShaNena pratIcImapasArya tatra shaN^kuH /
evaM kR^ite pashcimapArshvamAnyAH purastAt pakShmadhye caturviMshatyaN^gule sArdhasaptatile lakShaNaM nipatati puratashvaivaM /
sa nirNAmaH -- nirNamanaM pakShasya /
ardhadashamA ityAdi sa nirNAma ityantenottaramapi pakShaM kuryAt //


Atmadvi -- vyAsaH

AtmAnaM prAktvena dvipuruShAyAmamudaktvenAdhyardhapuruShamanupR^iShThayaM minuyAt //


pucche -- yesyAt

pucche puruShAyAmAni tadardhavistArANi pratyagAyatAni trINi caturashrANi dakShiNottarANi vihR^itya dakShiNaM caturashraM dakShiNAparakoTiM pratyakShNayAlikhet /
evamuttarAparakoTiM prati /
evaM kR^ite pucchamUler'dhapuruShavistAramagre 'dhyardhapuruShavistAraM puruShamAtrAyAmaM caturashraM bhavati //


shiraH -- yet

AtmanaH pUrvakaraNImadhye pucchavadardhAyAmavistAraM caturashraM kR^itvA tatpUrvakaraNImadhyAd dakShiNottarakaraNyormadhye rekhAM nipAtayeta -- rekhayorbahistyajet //


paJNcadashaH khaNDaH.

------

sundararAjIyA vyAkhyA

ardhada -- yAmaH

vyAsaH puruShamAtra eva /
atha tasya nirNAmaH --

dvipur -- NAmaH

koTayoragrApyayayorevaM purastAtpUrvayoH koTayorantau niyamya yatpashcAdapacchidyate tatpurastAdAgacchati /

etena -- khyAtaH AtmA -- vyAsaH

evamevAtmani trayaH puruShAH sthitAH /

pucche -- yet

AtmanaH purastAcchiraH /

iti paJNcadashaH khaNDaH

----------

kapardibhAShyam

___________________________________________________________


apyayAn prati shroNyaMsAn apacchindyAt  || ˘p¡us_16.1a ||

___________________________________________________________



apyayashabdena pakShapucchashirasAM sandhiruktaH /
tAnpratyapacchi ndyAt -- shroNyaMsAcyajet /
shiraso 'pyayAdArabhya pakShApyayaM prati /
evaM shroNyoraMse ca /
evaM dve dve caturbhAgIye niraste bhavataH /
vakShyati catvAriMshatparishipyanta iti //


___________________________________________________________


evam iva hi shyenaH  || ˘p¡us_16.1b ||

___________________________________________________________



prasiddhaH /
vakShyati ca "yAvadAmnAnasArUpyam' iti /

___________________________________________________________


karaNaM puruShasya paJNcamAyAmaM ShaShThavyAsaM kArayed yathAyoganataM tatprathamam  || ˘p¡us_16.2 ||

___________________________________________________________



puruShapaJNcamAyAmaM puruShaShaShThavyAsaM -- aratnimAtrI pArshvamAnI ShaDbhAgA tirya«bhAnI yathA yujyate tathA nataH; natashabdena prajambhanamucyate /
tathA prajambhayet /
ekAmakShNayAdIrghAM kuryAt /
yathA yujyata iti yathAyogaH /
tatprathamaM karaNam /
prathamamityasya saMj~nA /

___________________________________________________________


te dve prAcI saMhite | tad dvitIyam  || ˘p¡us_16.3 ||

___________________________________________________________



te dve viparyaste upasR^itya madhyamaphalake saMsR^iShTe yathA tiShThataH tathAvidhaM karaNaM dvitIyam /

___________________________________________________________


prathamasya ShaDbhAgam aShTabhAgena vardhayet | yathAyoganataM tat tR^itIyam  || ˘p¡us_16.4 ||

___________________________________________________________



prathamasya ShaDbAgakaraNamaShTabhAgeva vardhayeddIrghaM kuryAt /
mAtrA? tamakShNayA chindyAt /
chinnA yathA yujyate namanaM tatA yogaH /
yathA pakShanamane 'dhyarghaM yujyate tathA nataM vakraM tR^itIyakaraNam /

___________________________________________________________


caturbhAgIyAdhyardhA | tasyAsh caturbhAgIyAmAtram akShNayA chindyAt | tac caturtham  || ˘p¡us_16.5 ||

___________________________________________________________



caturbhAgIyAdhyardhaM bhUmAvAlikya caturbAgIyAM na tyajet /
tathAbhUteShTakA yena karaNena kiyate taccaturthaM karaNam /
ShoDashIM catubhiriti vakShyati /
tadetatkaraNam //


karavindIyA vyAkhyA

apya -- shyenaH

apyayashavdenAtmanaH pakShupacchashirasAM sandhirucyate /
shiraso 'pyayAdArabhya ApakShApyayAt pucchApyayAdArabhya ApakShA pyayAt /
evamivahIti gatam //


kara -- prathamam

puruShasya paJNcamaM caturviMshatiraN^gulaya ekataH /
anyatoviMshatiraN^gulayaH prathamaM karaNam /
yathAyoganataM bhavet -- upadhAne yathAyujyate tathA kuryAt /
namanaprakArashvopari shyene vakShyate /
prathamAdayaHshabdA vyavahArasaukaryAya //


tedve -- yam

prathamakaraNe prAgAyate dakShiNamekamuttaramekamiti saMhite caturviMshatyaN^gule pArshvamAnyau catvAriMshadaN^gule tirya«nAnyau /
tayorekAnamanavidhinA madhye nirNatA ekapArshve unnatA /
taddvitIyaM karaNam /

prathamakaraNasya ShaDbhAgo viMshatyaN^gulamaShTabhAgena paJNcadashAN^gulena yathAyoganatena vardhayet; yathA ShaDbAgaH pabhAnurodhI vakraHsyAdaShTamabAga AtmAnurUpa R^ijurbhavettattR^itIyaM karaNam //


caturbhA rthaM caturbhAgIyANUkAkhyA /
sAdhyardA kAryA /
tasyAshcaturbhAgIyAmAtramakShNayAmAtramakShNayA chindyAt /
etadR^iktaM bhavati--paJNcacatvAriMshadaN^gulAyAmaM triMshadahgulavyAsaM kR^itvA triMshadaN^gulamakShNayA chindyAt /
evamekA pArshvamAnI /
paJNcacatvAriMshadaN^gulayaH ekA tirya«bhAnI triMshadahgulayaH ekAkShNayA sthitA dvicatvAriMshadaN^gulayaH caturdasha tilAH /
etaccaturtaM karaNam //


sundararAjIyA vyAkhyA

apya -- chindyAt

pakShapucchashiro 'pyayebhyaH anyonyaM pratyakShNayA paricchindyAt /
evamAtmanor'dhapuruSho nirasto bhavati /

evamiva -- prathamam

caturviMshatyaN^gulaM /
pArshvaphalakam /
viMshatyaN^gulaM tiryakphalakam /
yathAyoganataM yathA yujyate pakShe tathA natam /
tasyaikAkShNayArajjuH paJNcatriMshikA viMshatitilayuktA /
aparA ShaDviMshikA ShaTtilayuktA /
evaM kR^ite pakShAyAmasya dvAdashabhAgaH ekAnnaviMshatirahgulayaH tilau ca iShTakAvyAso bhavati /
tadetatprathamaM karaNam /
aratniprAdesharahitaprakR^itike pakShAyAmasya triMshadaN^gulahAniH /
tadanuguNaM ceShTakAnAM namanaM bhavati /
tatra karNau ekaviMshakaikAnnatriMshakau tilatrayayuktau /

tedve -- dvitIyam

yathA ShaDashrI bhavati tathA saMhite /

pratha -- tR^itIyam

paJNcadashAN^gulavyAsaM aratnayAyAmaM samakarNaM dIrghacaturashraM prAgAyataM mUmau likhitvA prathamena prAgAyatena yuJNjayAttattR^itIyam /
R^ijvavasthitameva prathamApekShayA natamityucyate yathAyoganatamiti /

caturbhAga -- caturtham

ekA pArsvamAnI paJNcadashAN^gulA /
anyA paJNcacatvAriMshadaN^gulA /
ekA tirya«nAnI triMshadaN^gulA /
anyA dvicatvAriMshadaN^gulA sacaturdashatilA /

kapardibhAShyam

___________________________________________________________


caturbAgIyArdhaM paJNcamam  || ˘p¡us_16.6 ||

___________________________________________________________



ekatastriMshadaN^gulamanyataH paJNcadashAN^gulaM tatpaJNcamam /

___________________________________________________________


tasyAkShNayA bhedaH ShaShTham  || ˘p¡us_16.7 ||

___________________________________________________________



tasya paJNcamasyAkShNayA karNena vibhajyata iti bhedaHShaShTham /

___________________________________________________________


puruShasya paJNcamabhAgaM dashabhAgavyAsaM pratIcInam Ayacchet | tasya dakShiNato 'nyam uttaratash ca | tAv akShNayA dakShiNAoarayoH koTyor Alikhet | tat saptamam  || ˘p¡us_16.8 ||

___________________________________________________________



aratnimAtrAyAmaM prAdeshavyAsaM pratIcInaM pratyagAyatamAyacchet /
bhUmau dakShiNapArshve 'nyaM tathAvidhamuttaratashvAnyaM tathAvidham /

tAvakShNayA karNena dakShiNAvarayoH koTyorArabhya srucyavadAlikhet /
tatsaptamam //


___________________________________________________________


evamanyat | uttaraM tUttarasyAH koTyAlikhet tad aShTamam  || ˘p¡us_16.9 ||

___________________________________________________________



evameva kR^itvottaraM caturashramuttarasyAH koTyA Arabhya dakShiNAM koTiM pratyAlikhet srauvavattadaShTamam /

___________________________________________________________


caturbhAgIyAkShNayobhayato bhedo navamam  || ˘p¡us_16.10 ||

___________________________________________________________



akShNayA ubhayataH karNena bhedanaM khaNDanaM tasyAshcaturbhAgIyAyAstathAvidhaM navamaM karaNam /
pAdamAtraM pAdeShTakA tribhiriti //


___________________________________________________________


upadhAne ShaShTiHShaShTiH pakShayoH prathamA udIcIrnir upadadhyAt  || ˘p¡us_16.11 ||

___________________________________________________________



___________________________________________________________


pucchapArshvayor aShTAvaShTau ShaThyayas tisro 'gre tata ekAn tatas tisraH tata ekA  || ˘p¡us_16.12 ||

___________________________________________________________



___________________________________________________________


pucchApyaye caturthyau vishaye | tayos tu pashcAt paJNcamyAv anIkasaMhite  || ˘p¡us_16.12 ||

___________________________________________________________



upadhAnakAle ekasmin pakShe ShaShTiH prathamA udIcIrudagAyatA nidadhyAt -- upadadhyAt triMshatrriMshadviparyasya kAritAH /
evamuttarapakShe 'pi /
pucchasya pArshvayorubhayoHShaShTayaH aShTAvekasmin pArshve 'parasmiMshvAShTau /
kathamityAha -- pucchAgre tisraH tAsAM purastAdekAm /
evamuttarasmin pArshve viparyasya kAritAH /
pucche cAtmani ca sthite tiryak -- tayosh ceti tayoH pashcAtpucche anIkasaMhite -- mukhasahinte meShayUthavat /

ShoDashaH khaNDaH

------

karavindIyA vyAkhyA

catu -- mam

triMshadaN^gulAyAmaM paJNcadashavyAsaM yattatpaJNcamaM karaNam //


tasyA -- ShaShTham

paJNcamasyAkShNayA bhedaM kR^itvA ShaShThaM karaNaM bhavati sA pAdeShTakA /
tasyaikatriMshadaN^gulamanyat paJNcadashAN^gulamanyadakShNayA ekonaviMshatitilAdhikaM trayastriMshadaN^gulam /
etat ShaShThaM karaNam //


puruSha -- mam

caturviMshatyaN^gulAyAmaM tadardhavistAraM caturashraM kR^itvA tasya dakShiNata uttaratash ca tAdR^ishe caturashre /
evaM trINi caturashrANi kR^itvA dakShiNottaracaturashre dakShiNAparakoTI pratyAlikhet /
evaM pArshvamAnyau ShaDviMshatyaN^gule aShTAviMshatitilAdhike /
tirya«bhAnyau catuviMshatyaN^gule /
etatsaptamaM karaNam //


evama -- ShTamam

saptamavatrrINi caturashrANi kR^itvA dakShiNaM dakShiNAparakoTiM pratyAlikheduttaramuttarAparakoTiM prati /
evamapi te eva pArshvamAnyau pUrvaM pArshvaM dvAdashAN^gulaM pashcimaM tu ShaTtriMshadaN^gulaM /
yadeva tadaShTamaM karaNam //


caturbha -- mam

caturbhAgIyAyA ubhayato bhedo 'kShNayAbhavet /
iyamapi pAdeShTakA /
pArshvamAnyau akShNayA ekaviMshatyaN^gule saptatilasahite tiryagekaM triMshadaN^gulam /
evaM navamaM karaNam /

athopadhAnamucyate--

upa -- dhyAt

upadhAnakAle dakShiNe pakShe ShaShTiH prathamA udIcIrnidadhyAt /
uttare ca ShaShTim /
chAndaso vibhaktivyatyayaH /

puccha -- ShThayAH

ShaShThakaraNotpannA aShTAvaShTau pucchapArshvayoH /

upadhAnaprakAramAha ----

tisro -- kAm

pucchapArshvayorityeva /
tisro 'gre pucchasya dakShiNashroNyAmekA prAcI bAhyavisheShA /
tasyA uttarato dve nAnAgre visheShasahite /
tayoH purastAdekA bAhyavisheShA

prAgagrA /
tasyAH purastAtpUrvavattisraH /
tAsAM purastAt pUrvavadekA /
evamudakpArshve 'pi //


pucchA -- ye

pucchAtmasandhau dve caturthyau vishaye /
avisheShAdAtmani pucchaM ca same //


tayo -- hite

tayosh ca pashAvat dve paJNcamyAvartheShTake /
anIkaM mukham /
tena saMhite meShayuddhavat //


ShoDashaH khaNDaH

------

sundararAjIyA vyAkhyA

catu -- paJNcamam

triMshadaN^gulAyAmaM paJNcadashAhgulavyAsaM /
samakarNaM dIrghacaturashram /

tasyA -- ShaShTham

puruSha -- mam

yathA purastAtprAdeshastirya«bhAnI pashcAttu prAdeshatrayam /
saptamAShTamayorubhayorapi pArshvaphalakAni saptaviMshakAni ShaTtilonAni /

catu -- mam

caturbhAgIyAmubhayato 'kShNayAbhinnAyAM catvAro navamA bhavanti trikoNAH /
teShAmekaM karaNaM navamaM /
tasyaikaM phalakaM triMshadaN^gulaM /
anye ekavishake saptatile /

upa -- dhyAt

prathamAH prathamakaraNakR^itAH /
evaM ShaShTaya ityAdiShu udIcIrudagAyatAH //


puccha -- ShaShTayaH

prAgAyatA etAH /
AsAmupadhAnaprakAramAha --

tisra -- kAH

tisR^iNAM dve prAgagre /
ekA pratyagagrA /

pucchA -- ye

udagagrA dakShiNAgrA ca /
te AtmAnaM pucchaM ca paJNcadashAN^gulAvete /

tayo -- hite

anIkasaMhite mukhasaMhite /
udagAyate /

ShoDashaH khaNDaH

kapardibhAShyam

___________________________________________________________


sheShe dasha caturthyaH shroNyaMseShu cAShTau prAcIH pratIcIsh ca  || ˘p¡us_17.1 ||

___________________________________________________________



pucchasheShe caturthyo dasha tiryagAyatAH /
shroNyaMseShu cAShTau shroNyAshcatasraH prAgAyatAH /
uttarasyAM dakShiNasyAM ca viparyasya kAritAH /
aMsayoshvaivam /

___________________________________________________________


sheShe ca ShaDviMshatir aShTau ShaShTayash catasraH paJNcamyaH  || ˘p¡us_17.2 ||

___________________________________________________________


Atmani sheShe shiShTe deshe ShaDviMshatishcaturthyaH /
aShTau catasraH paJNcamyaH /
tAsAmupadhAnamArga ucyate -- vishayAnAM mArge tiryagAtmani caturdasha caturthyaH /
tAsAM pArshvayordve dve prAcyau ca viparyasya kArite /
uttare pArshve caturdashAnAmeva pArshvayormadhye dve dve tiryak /
etAHShaDviMshatishcaturthya upahitAH /
catasrashcaturbhAgIyAkoNeShu sthitAH /
tAsu catasraH paJNcamyaH tiryak /
ShaShTayashvAShTau tiryageva //


___________________________________________________________


shirasi caturthyau vishaye | tayosh ca purastAt prAcyau  || ˘p¡us_17.3 ||

___________________________________________________________



___________________________________________________________


eSha dvishataH prastAraH  || ˘p¡us_17.4 ||

___________________________________________________________



tayorvishayayoH purastAtprAcyau caturthyau viparyasya kAritA dakShiNataH /
eSheti /
kirmathamidam yAvatA dvishata eva? paribhASheyam /
yo 'yaM prastAro dvishata(Hsa) iti paribhAShyate /
saN^khyAM pUrayedityukte dvishata eva pUryate /
itarathA kA saMkhyA pUrayitavyeti na j~nAyate /
asti sahasrasaMkhyeti cenna /
pratiprastAraM pUrayediti vacanamanarthaN^kaM sampadyate /
tasmAtparibhASheyamiti //


___________________________________________________________


aparasmin prastAre paJNcapaJNca nirNAmayordvitIyAH | apyayayosh ca tR^itIyA AtmAnam aShTabhAgAvetAH  || ˘p¡us_17.5a ||

___________________________________________________________



dvitIyA vakrIbhUtAH /
nirNAmo vakrapradeshaH /
tasmin pradeshe paJNcapaJNca dvitIyAH /
apyayayosh ca tR^itIyAH -- pakShApyayayoshtR^itIyA AtmAnamaShTabhAgAvetA vyAptAH /
caturbhAgIyeShTakAmAtramAtmani sthitAH /
paJNchapaJNca viparyasya kAritA uttare pakShApyaye /

___________________________________________________________


sheShe paJNcacatvAriMshat prathamAH prAcIH  || ˘p¡us_17.5b ||

___________________________________________________________


dakShiNe pArshve paJNcaviMshatiH /
dakShiNe pakShe uttare pArshve paJNcaviMshatiruttare pakSheviMshatiH /


___________________________________________________________


pucchapArshvayoH paJNcapaJNca saptamyaH  || ˘p¡us_17.6a ||

___________________________________________________________


uttare pArshve viparyasya kAritAH /

___________________________________________________________


dvitIyacaturthosh cAnyatarataH pratisaMhitAm ekaikAm  || ˘p¡us_17.6b ||

___________________________________________________________



dvitIyAyAM rItyAM catutharyAM ca rItyAM anyasminpArshve ekaikA saptamI /
ekA dakShiNe pArshve viparyasya kAritA /
aparA uttare pArshve //


___________________________________________________________


sheShe trayodashAShTamyaH  || ˘p¡us_17.6c ||

___________________________________________________________


pucchadeshe trayodashAShTamyaHsherate /

___________________________________________________________


shroNyaMseShu cAShTau caturthyo dakShiNA udIcIsh ca  || ˘p¡us_17.7a ||

___________________________________________________________



dakShiNasyAM dakShiNAyate viparyasya kArite /
uttarasyAM shroNyAM udagAyate /
dakShiNeM'se udagAyate viparyasya kArite //


___________________________________________________________


sheShe ca viMshatis triMshat ShaShThayaH ekAM paJNcamIm  || ˘p¡us_17.7b ||

___________________________________________________________



cakAreNa caturthyo 'nukR^iShyante /
triMshat ShaShThayaH ekA ca paJNcamI /
tAsAmupAdhAnadesha ucyate -- Atmano dakShiNe pArshve dasha catur thyaH /
paJNca prAcIH paJNca pratIcIH evamuttare pArshve /
madhye triMshat ShaShThayaH prAcIH ekA ca paJNcamI /
tAsAM paJNcadasha prAcIH //


___________________________________________________________


shirasi caturthyau tayosh ca purastAccatasro navamyaH  || ˘p¡us_17.8 ||

___________________________________________________________



___________________________________________________________


eSha dvishataprastAraH  || ˘p¡us_17.9 ||

___________________________________________________________



___________________________________________________________


vyatyAsaM cinuyAd yAvataH prastArAMsh cikIrShet  || ˘p¡us_17.10 ||

___________________________________________________________


navamyashcatasraH purastAt /
eSheti -- gatametat /
kimarthamidam? niyamArtham /
kimatra niyamyate? viShamadvishataprastAro niyamyate nopari shyenaH /
shyena eva niyamyate nAnyaH /
kathamavagamyate nAnya iti? prastArapUraNavacanAt -- tatrApi vyatyAsaM cinuyAdityetadevoktaM na pUraNavacanam /
tasmAdanye dvishataprastArAH /
atraiva paribhAShitatvAt /
iShTakAkaraNe paJNcacatvAriMshadaN^gulaM dakShiNena gR^ihItvA caturthIH kArayet /
viparyastAH savye /
vyatyAsaM cinuyAdyAvataH prastArAMshcikIrShet iti /
gatametat /
atra shlokA bhavanti --

ekonaviMshatistiryagaN^gulaM satiladvayam /

yathA bhavettathA kAryA yathAyoganataM tu tat //


yathodIcyeva ShaDbhAge ShaShThabhAgena vardhanam /

karaNasya tR^itIyasya yathAyoganataM bhavet //


sa visheShashcaturthasya dvicatvAriMshadaN^gulam /

caturdashatilairyuktaM karaNasya bhaviShyati //


ShaShThasya karNaphalakaM syAtrrayastriMshadaN^gulam /

aShTAdashatilairyuktaM itare sUtracedite //


pArshvasthAH saptamasyeyaM viMshatyaH saha saptabhiH /

ShaDhbhireva tilairUnaM phalake 'ShTAShTamasya ca //


prathamena tR^itIyena viparyasya punaH punaH /

tathA saptamaShaShThAbhyAM kArayediShTakAH kratau //


paJNcatriMshadviparyasya caturthenApi kArayet /

etAvadeva kushalAH iShTakAkaraNe viduH //


pucche tirya«nidhAtavyAH catutharyA dasha coditAH /

yoshvAntarA tiryak caturthyaHsyushcaturdasha //


caturthyaH pArshvayostAsAM ShaTShaTtiryaktu madhyamAH /

koNeShu tiryak paJNcamyaH ShaShThashvAShTau tathAvidhAH /

ApucchasyApyayAttadvat shirasi triMshadiShyate /

prAcyashvaiva pratIcyash ca prAcIShveva ca paJNcamI //


caturthyaH pArshvayostAsAM tathA shiShTe ca viMshatiH /

anyatsarvaM yathAsUtraM prastAro dvishataH kratau //


shroNyA caiva tathaivAMsau ShaTsu tveva tatAvidhA /

caturthyo ................... dakShiNa na paitAH //


shroNyordakShiNa vij~neyaM tathA caivAMsa uttare //


ityApastamba sUtravivaraNe kapardisvAmibhAShye shulbAkhyaprashne

paJNcamaH paTalaH.

------

karavindIyA vyAkhyA

sheSher -- thyaH

pucche dasha caturthakaraNaniShpannAH tiryagAyatAH //


shroNyaM -- sh ca

evaM shroNyoshcatasraH uttarapArshve viparyasya kAritAH //


sheShe -- myaH

sheShe ceti cakArAccaturthyo 'nuShajyante /
AtmasheShe ShaDviMshatishcaturthyaH /
aShTau ca ShaShTayaH /
catasraH paJNcamyaH /
tA etA aShTAtriMshat /
asAmupadhAnamucyate --

shirasi -- stA

pucchagatavishayAnAM madhye tiryagAtmani caturdasha caturthyaH prAcyo rItayaH /
tAsAM pArshvayoH pashcAddvedve purastA dvedve dakShiNata uttaratash ca /
tA aShTau /
aShTAnAM catasraH prAcyashcatasraH pratIcyaH /
caturdashAnAmeva pArshvayormadhye dakShiNata uttaratash ca dvedve /
tAshcatasraH /
evaM ShaDviMshatishcaturthyaH /
atrAnupahitAH koNek /
catvArashvatu rbhAgIyAdeshAH /
teShu catasraH paJNcamyaH tiryak /
ShaShTishvAShTau tiryageva /
shirasi pratyekaM dakShiNottarataH prAcyau tayorviMshayayoH purataH prAcyau caturthyau /
evaM bAhyavisheShe //


eSha dvishataH prastAraH

upadAnavidhigatadeshAdi saMkhyAsamudAyavashena prastAre shatadvaye siddhe 'pi dvishataH prastAra iti vacanaM prastAre dvishatatvasiddhikaraNAya //


apa -- kriyAH

nirNAmaH pakShayormadhye vakrapradesha ityuktam /
tasmin dvitIyAH dakShiNottarapakShayoH paJNcapaJNca nirNAmAnurUpamupadheyAH //


apya -- vetAH

tR^itIyakaraNAvetAH paJNcapaJNcaivAShTabhAgena vardhitenAtmAnamavagatAH ShaDbhAgena pakSham //


sheShe -- prAcIH

dakShiNapakShasya dakShiNabhAge paJNcaviMshatiH /
uttarapakShasya uttarabhAge paJNcaviMshatiH dakShiNe viMshatiH //


puccha -- myaH

pucchasya dakShiNe pArshve paJNca saptamyaH /
uttare paJNca prAcyo rItayaH //


dvitI -- kAm

anenAnyayoH saptamyorupadhAnamucyate /
pucchapArshvagatasaptamIrItyoranyatarasyAM rItyAM dvitIyA /
pratisaMhitAmekAmanyasyAM caturthIpratisaMhitAM caikAM saptamImupadadhyAt /
evaM dvAdasha saptamya upahitA bhavanti //


sheShe -- ShTamyAH

pucchasheShe aShTamakaraNotpannAH trayodashodIcyaH paJNca rItayaH /
pucchAgre pArshvagatayoHsaptamyormadhye paJNcAShTamyau /
nanAgrA dvitIyAyAm /
tisR^iNAM saptamInAM madhye tisro 'ShTamyaH /
tR^itIyAyAM ca tisraH /
caturtharItyAM tisR^iNAM saptamInAM madhye ekA /
paJNcamarItyAM saptamyormadhye ekA /
evaM trayodashAShTamyaH yathAyogaM prAgagrAH pratyagagrAsh ca bhaveyuH //


shroNyaMsebhyash ca shroNyaM -- sh ca

shroNyoshcatasraH pratyekaM dvedve dakShiNayordakShiNA uttarayoruttarAH /
sarvA bAhyavisheShAH //


sheShe -- mIm

AtmasheShe viMshatiH /
cakAreNa vacanAbhAve shirasicaturthyau /
tayosh ca purastAt catasro navamyaH //


eSha dvishataH prastAraH

prastArashatadvayAniyamashaN^ktAnirAkaraNAya dvishatavacanam //


vyatyAsarM -- Shet

gatam //


atha phalakAnAM prajambhanamucyate -- prathamakaraNasya viMshatyaN^gulA tirya«mAnI prajambhite yathaikonaviMshatiraN^gulayaHsAShTAdashatiladvayaM ca R^ijvavasthitA bhavati, tathA karaNaM prajambhayet /
vakShyamANaprakAreNa dvitIyasya karaNasya pakShanamnI caturviMshatyaN^gulA sArdhasaptatilA /
tasyAHShaShTho bhAgashcatasro 'hgulayaH

sapAdatilash ca /
tena dvitIyakaraNasya dIrghatayA catvAriMshadahgulayoH phalakayormadhye catuviMshatyaN^gule ekasminnunnatiM ca kuryAt; yathA tasya bhAgadvayamekaikashaH pUrvakarNasadR^ishaM bhavati tatheti /
dR^itIyasya tu ShaShThAShTabhAgasandhau namanaM /
ShaShThaM bhAgaM pUrvavannamayet /
aShTamasya tu namanamAtmAnurUpaM R^ijvavasthAnameva /
tasminnamanaM ShaShThApekShayA /

tatra shlokAH ----

shyene prathama Adyasya karaNasya prajambhanam /

dvitIyasya tR^itIyasya cocyate phalakAnatiH //


asmin shyene tvAdimsya karaNasya prajambhanam /

pucchasya pakShakaraNI ShaShThasyAsau yathArjavam //


dvitIyasya tR^itIyasya pakShakANAM nateH phalam /

vyAsasya pakShakaraNIM ShaShThatAnAdime natiH //


ekonaviMshatyaN^gulyaHsAShTAMshaM ca tiladvayam /

tirya«bhAnI yatA sA syAttathA rajjvA prajambhayet //


sapAdatilasaMyuktacaturaN^gulamAtrataH /

pakShasya namanI ShaShThaH tena syAtphalakAnatiH //


evaM dvitIyashyenoktamArgeNonnIya jambhanam /

karaNasya vidhAtavyaM phalakAnamanaM tathA //


iti karavindasvAmikR^itAyAM shulbapratIpikAyAM paJNcamaH paTalaH

------

sundararAjIyA vyAkhyA

sheSher ---- thyaH

puccha udagAyatAH /

shroNyaMash ca

AtmanaH shroNyaMseShu dvedve bAhyavisheShe /

sheShe paJNcamyaH

AtmasheShe ShaDviMshaticaturthyaH prAcyaH pratIcyaH /
tatra madhyarItyoH saptasaptodagagrA dakShiNAgrAsh ca /
dvitIyapaJNcamarItyoH paJNcapaJNca matAH /
samamadhye dakShiNottare anyAH prAkpratIcyaH /
AdyantarItyormadhye ekaikacaturthyau dakShiNottarayoH pashcAtpurastAcca dvedve ShaShThayau /
tAshvAShTau dakShiNottarAH /
tadrItyoH sheShe catasraH paJNcamya udagAyatAH /

shirasi caturthyau vishaye

apyaye pucchApyayavat /

tayo cyau

bAhyavisheShe caturthyau /

eSha stAraH

ato 'tra saMkhyApUraNAya kartavyo yatna ityarthaH /

apara tAmekaikAm

anyatarataH dakShiNe pArshve uttare vA dvitIyacaturthIbhyAM saptamIbhyAM saMhitAmekAM saptamImantarupadadhyAt //


sheShe ShTamyaH

Shuccha sheShe /

shroNyaMacIsh ca

dvedve bAhyavisheShe /

sheShe paJNcamI

AtmasheShe viMshatishcaturthyaH prAgAyatAH /
madhye prAgAyatAbhiH ShaShThIbhirdvAtriMshatA dve rItI /
tayordakShiNasyAM dve uddhR^itya ekAM paJNcamIM nidadhyAt //


shirasi caturthyau

udagAyate //


tayo myaH

udagAyatAH //


eSha stAraH -- vyatyA rShet

iti shrI sundararAjakR^itAyAM shulbapradIpikAyAM paJNcamaH paTalaH

------

shyenacitaM cinvIta suvargakAma iti vij~nAyate  || ˘p¡us_18.1 ||

___________________________________________________________


vakrapakSho vyastapuccho bhavati | pashcAt prA« udUhati | purastAt pratya« udUhati | evam iva hi vayasAM madhye pakShanirNAmo bhavatIti vij~nAyate  || ˘p¡us_18.2 ||

___________________________________________________________



asyAH shruteH punarupanyAso mArgAntaraM pratipAdayitum /
athavA anyaivaiShA shrutiH /
iyamevAkAramArgatA /
vakreti -- gatametat /

___________________________________________________________


puruShasya ShoDashabhir viMshaM shataM sAratniprAdeshaH saptavidhaH saMpadyate | tAsAM catvAriMshadAtmani tisraH shirasi paJNcadasha puccha ekatriMshad dakShiNe pakShe tathottare  || ˘p¡us_18.3 ||

___________________________________________________________



puruShasya ShoDashamAgaH ShoDashI /
tAbhirviMshottaraM shataM saMpadyate /
parigaNanAyAM kriyamANAyAM etAvatyaH ShoDashyaH saptArdhe sherate /
sapta sthApayitvA ShoDashIbhirguNite dvAdashottaraM shatam /
ardhapuruShe dvAdashasu aShTau /
kShipte viMshatiH /
evaM viMshottaraM shataM sampannam /
tAsAmiti -- tAsAM ShoDashInAM catvAriMshadAtmanyupadheyAH; tisraHshirasi; sarvatra nidheyA iti sheShaH /
paJNcadasha pucche /
dakShiNe pakShe ekatriMshat tathottare /
ekatriMshaduttare pakShe /
kathametA nidheyA ityucyate --

___________________________________________________________


adhyardhapuruShas tiryag dvAv AyAmata iti dIrghaM caturashraM vihR^itya shroNyaMsebhyo dve dve ShoDasyau nirasyet | catvAriMshat parishiShyante | sa AtmA  || ˘p¡us_18.4 ||

___________________________________________________________



adhyardhapuruShA tirya«bhAnI dvipuruShA pArshvamAnI /
evaM dIrghacaturashraM vihR^itya shroNIbhyAmaMsAbhyAM ca dve dve ShoDashyau pratyekaM nirasyet -- tyajet /
akShNayA .... yathA shroNyaMseShu catvAri caturashrANi ardhapuruShapramANAni kR^itvA akShNayAnyArdhAni nirasyet /
shiShTaM catvAriMshat /
sa AtmA //


___________________________________________________________


shirasyardhapuruSheNa caturashraM kR^itvA pUrvasyAH karaNyA ardhAt tAvati dakShiNottarayor nipAtayet  || ˘p¡us_18.5a ||

___________________________________________________________



gatametat --

___________________________________________________________


tisraH parishiShyante | tac chiraH  || ˘p¡us_18.5b ||

___________________________________________________________


tisraHshiShTAH /
tacchiraH /

___________________________________________________________


puruShas tiryag dvAv AyAmataH ShoDashabhAgash ca dakShiNaH pakShaH | tathottaraH  || ˘p¡us_18.6 ||

___________________________________________________________



puruShamAtrA tirya«bAnI /
dvipuruShA pArshvamAnI /
puruShaShoDashamAgAshvArdhenAShTAhgulamAtraM dakShiNe pakShe cAmAmaH /
tadvadevottarapakShaH //


___________________________________________________________


pakShAgrepakShAgre puruShacaturthena catvAri caturashrANi kR^itvA tAny akShNayA vyavalikhyArdhAni nirasyet | ekatriMshat parishiShyante  || ˘p¡us_18.7 ||

___________________________________________________________



pakShayoragre pratyekaM puruShacaturthapramANena catvAri caturashrANi kR^itvA tAnyakShNayA karNemAlikhya ardhAni nirasyet /
sucyavaddakShiNapakShAgrANi bahirbhUtAni nirasyet /
dvipuruShAyAme dvAtriMshat ShoDashyo bhavanti /
ShoDashabhAgena caikA /
tAsu dvayostyaktayoH ekatriMshatparishiShyante //


___________________________________________________________


pakShAgram utsR^ijya madhye pakShasya prAcIM lekhAm Alikhet  || ˘p¡us_18.8a ||

___________________________________________________________



pakShAgramiti puruShacaturthena kR^itAni caturashrANi lakShyante /
pakShAyAme puruShacaturbhAgArdhamutsR^ijyetyarthaH /
madhye pakShasya pragAyatAM lekhAmAlikhet //


___________________________________________________________


pakShApyaye puruShaM niyamya lekhAyAM puruShAnte nitodantukuryAt | nitodAt prAcInaM puruShAnte nitodaM nitodayor nAnAntAv Alikhet | tatpakShinamanam | etenottaraH pakSho vyAkhyAtaH  || ˘p¡us_18.8b ||

___________________________________________________________



AtmapakShasandhau puruShamAtraM veNuM niyamya lekhAyAmeva puruShasyAnte veNorante lakShaNaM kuryAt /
tasmAnnitodAtpAgAyataM prAcInaM veNuM lekhAyAmeva nidhAyAntye chidre shaN^kuM lakShaNaM vA nihatya nitodayorantau nAnA Alikhet /
aparasmAnnitodAdA rabhyAparAntamAlikhet /
pUrvasmAnnitodAccArabhya pUrvAntamiti /
tatpakShanamanaM pakShasya vakratA /
eteneti uttarapakShanamanamapyevaM kuryAt //


aShTAdashaH khaNDaH

--------

___________________________________________________________


dvipuruShaM pascAdardhapuruShaM purastAc caturbhAgonaH puruSha AyAmo 'ShTAdashakaraNyo pArshvayos tAH paJNcadashaparigR^ihNanti | tat puccham  || ˘p¡us_19.1 ||

___________________________________________________________



pashcAttirya«bhAnI dvipuruShA /
purastAdardhapuruShA /
pAdonapuruShAyAmA /
pArshvayoraShTAdashaShoDashIH karoti /
aShTAdashakaraNI sA pArshvayoH /
tA etAH paJNcadashaShoDashIH parigR^ihranti /
kathamardhapuruShavyAsA pAdonapuruShAyAmA ShaTkaroti? tasyAbhiyo dve caturashre same sarvataH pAdonapuruShamAtre /
tAvakShNayA likhet /
ekaikamardhaM tyajet /
shiShTaM pratyekamardhapaJNcamaM karoti /
ardhapaJNcamaM ardhapaJNcamaM nava /
navasu ShaTsu kShipteShu paJNcadasha /
tatpuccham //


karavindIyA vyAkhyA

shyenA -- yate

dvitIyashyenamupadeShTuM saiva shrutiH punarapi paThitA /
tatra visheShamAha ------

puruShasya --t tare

ShoDashIH -- ShoDashabhAgaparimitAH /
tAbhiH ShoDashIbiH /
sAratniprAdeshaHsaptavidho 'gnirviMshatishataM saMpadyate /
tathAhi -- sapta sthApayitvA ShoDashIbirguNite dvAdashottaraM shataM bhavati /
ardhe ShoDashIbhirguNite aShTau /
teShvaShTasu kShipteShu viMshatyuttaraM shataM ShoDashyo bhavanti /
tAsAM catvAriMshadAtmani catvAriMshat ShoDashinIkShetrANyAtmetyarthaH /
tisrAHshirasi ShoDashyaHsyuH /
paJNcadasha pucche /
paJNcadashaShoDashyaH pucchakShetram /
ekatriMshaddakShiNe pakShe /
tathottare pakShe /
ekAtriMshat ShoDashIkShetraM dakShiNaH pakSha uttarash ca /
evaM vibhajya vimAnamAha ----

adhya -- tmA

anupR^iShThayaM catvAriMshaddve shate cAN^gulaya AyAmaH /
vistAro 'shItishatamaN^gulyastiryak /
evaM dIrghaM caturashraM vihR^itya shroNyaMseShvardhapuruShapramANAni catvAri caturashrANi kR^itvA tAnyAtmapArshvamAnIniShThakoNataH tirya«bhAnIniShThakoNaM pratyakShNayAlikhet /
lekhAnAM bahirbhUtAstyajet /
catvAriMshadavashiShyante /
sa AtmA bhavati /
katham? AyAmato 'ShTau ShoDashyaH /
tiryak ShaT /
aShTau ShaDguNitA aShTAcatvAriMshat /
tatra shroNyaMsebhyo dvedve nirasyAShTau nirastA

bhavanti /
shiShTacAshvatvAriMshadAtmani bhavanti //


shirasya -- cchiraH

shiraH pradeshe AtmanoM'sayoH purataH pR^iShThayAyAmardhapuruSheNa caturashraM kR^itvA pUrvasyAH karaNyAH ityAdikR^ite tisraH parishiShyante /
tacchiro bhavati //


puru --t taraH

puruShamAtraM tiryagAyAmaH /
dvipuruShamAtramardhAShTamAN^gulayash ca /
evaM dakShiNe pakShe dIrghacaturashraM kR^itvA /
tathottare 'pi //


pakShAgre -- nte

pakShsyAgre puruShacaturthena triMshadaN^gulena catvAri caturashrANi kR^itvA tAni pratyekaM dakShiNApratyagvyavalikhya pUrvANyardhAni nirasyet /
evamekatriMshat ShoDashyaH parishiShyante /
sa dakShiNaH pakShaH /
kathaM? pakShe dvAtriMshatShoDashyaH /
ShoDasho bhAgashvaikaH /
tAstrayastriMshat /
tAbhyAM caturShvardheShu nirasteShu ekatriMshatparishiShyante /
evamevottaraH pakShaH /
tatra caturakShANyuttarApratyAgakShNayAvilikhya pUrvArdhAni nirasyet //


pakShAgra -- manam

pakShAgramutsR^ijya triMshadaN^gulamapahAya madhye pakShasya prAcIM lekhAmAlikhet /
pakShAgre utsR^iShTe sheShaH pakShaH ardhatR^itIyAN^gulonaviMshatyadhikashatadvayAN^gulam /
tasya madhye sapAdAN^gulonadashAdhikashatAN^gulena pashcAdArabhya pragAyatAM lekhAM pakShamatItyAlikhet /
pashcime pakShApyaye puruShamAtraM veNuM nidhAya niyamyAparaM veNorantaraM dakShiNAprAk lekhAyAM nipAtayet /
sa pashcima pakShAntAt prAkpaJNcAshadaN^gule paJNcaviMshatitilAdhike nipatati /
tatra nitodaM--binduM kuryAt /
tasmAcca prAcInalekhAyAmeva puruShamAtre dvitIyaM nitodaM kuryAta /
nitodayoH nAnAntAvAlikhet /
nitodayorArabhya pakShAntAvabhi nAnApR^ithak Alikhet /
pashcimAnnitodAdArabhya pashcimapakShAgraM pakShApyayaM ca pratyagAlikhet /
tatpakShanamanaM -- tadetatpakShasya namanaM bhavati /
pUrvasmannitodAdArabhya pUrvaM pakShAgraM pakShApyayaM ca pratyagalikhet /
tat pakShanamanaM -- pakShasya namanaM bhavati /

ete -- taH

R^ijuH //


dvipu -- ccham

pucchasyAgraM dvipuruShapramANam /
tasya mUlamardhapuruShapramANaM /
AyAmashcaturbhAgonaH puruShaH /
aShTAdashakaraNyau pArshvayoH /
aShTAdasha karotItyaShTAdashakaraNI /
ShoDashInAM prakR^itatvAttAsAM aShTAdashAnAM karaNI /
te khalu triShoDashIpramANanavatyaN^gulasamacaturashrasyAkShNayAbhUte /
tathAhi -- pucchamUlAddakShiNataH uttaratash ca pArshvamAnI tirya«bhAnI caturbhAgonapuruShapramANopetA /
tribhirnaveti navaShoDashIkShetrasyAkShNayArajjubhUte /
atra caturashrasyAkShNayArajjuH dvistAvatIM bhUmiM karotIti te 'ShTAdashakaraNyau ShoDashInAm /
tA etAshcatasraH karaNyaH /
dviShoDashikAShTaShoDashike tirya«bhAnyAvaShTA dashakaraNyau pArshvamAnyau paJNcadasha ShoDashIH parigaTahNanti /
katham? ardhapuruShavyAsA pAdonapuruShAyAmA ShaTkaroti /
tasyAbhito dve caturashre same sarvataH pAdonapuruShamAtre /
tAvakShNayA likhet /
shiShTaM pratyekamardhapaJNcamaM karoti /
ardhapaJNcamamardhapaJNcamaM ca nava /
navasu ShaTsu kShipteShu paJNcadasha /
tatpucchaM -- pucchaMsaMj~naM bhavati /
karaNAnyucyante //


sundararAjIyA vyAkhyA

athoktameva shyenacitaM prakArAntareNa vyAkhyAtuM brAhnaNaM punarupanyasyati------

shyena -- yate

puruShasya -- dyate

ShoDashyaH -- ShoDashAMshAH /
tAshcaturbhAgIyA iShTakAH viMshatyadhikaM shataM /
"shadantaviMshateshveti' DaH /
sAratniprAdeshaH saptavidhogniH puruShakShetrasya ShoDashIbhirviMshatyadhikaM shataM sampadyate //


tAsAM -- tmani

Atmani catvAriMshat ShoDashyo bhavanti //


tisraH --t tare

athAtmano vimAna Aha --

adhyardhAtmA

ShoDashInAM nirasnaprakAro 'pyayAna prati shroNyaMsAnityukto veditavyaH /

shira ttaraH

ShoDashabhAgor'dhAShTamA aN^gulayaH /
aratniprAdesharahitaprakR^itike tu pUrvavat pakShAyAmasya triMshadaN^gulahAnirdraShTavyA /
dvipuruShAyAme dvAtriMshat ShoDashyaH /
ShoDashabhAgena caikA /
evaM trayastriMshat /
tataH--

pakShA -- Shyanye

dakShiNeShAM dakShiNapUrvAShyardhAni nirasyet /
uttareShAmuttarapUrvANi /

pakShA namanaM pakShAN^gra triMshadaN^gulaM caturashrakR^itamutsR^ijya shirasi pakShasya sArdhasaptadashadvishatAN^gulasya madhye lekhAM kR^itvA pakShApyayasyAparAnte puruShamAtraM veNuM niyamya tasyAM lekhAyAM nipAtayet /
sA yatra nipatati lekhAyAM tatra nitodaM kuryAt /
shaN^kuM nihanyAt tatra puruShaM niyabhya tataH purastAtpuruShAnte nitodaM kR^itvA tadanuguNaM pUrvAparAvantAvAlikhet /
pUrvashyene dvipuruShAM rajjumityuktameva saMnamanamatra prakArAntareNoktamanusandhAtavyam //


ete -- khyAtaH

dvipu -- pucchaM aShTAdashAnAM ShoDashInAM karaNyo nava tilayukte saptaviMshatishatAN^gule pArshvayorakShNayArUpe bhavataH /
pucchAtmashirasAM ShoDashI saMkhyA bhUmau likhitvA draShTavyA //


kapardibhAShyam
