pAdeShTakAM tribhish caturthenaikaM caturthasavisheShArdhAbhyAM ceti  || ˘p¡us_19.4 ||

___________________________________________________________



___________________________________________________________


pakSheShTakAM caturbhir dvAbhyAM caturthAbhyAM dvisaptamAbhyAM ceti  || ˘p¡us_19.5 ||

___________________________________________________________



___________________________________________________________


pakShamadhyIyAM caturbhir dvAbhyAM caturthAbhyAM dvisaptamAbhyAM ceti  || ˘p¡us_19.6 ||

___________________________________________________________



___________________________________________________________


pakShAgrIyAM tribhish caturthenaikaM caturthasaptamAbhyAm ekaM caturthasavisheShasaptamAbhyAM ceti  || ˘p¡us_19.7 ||

___________________________________________________________



puruShasyAShTamena paJNcadashAN^gulena /
tribhiraShTamaiH -- tenaiva triguNitena paJNcacatvAriMshadaN^gulena /
caturthasavisheSheNa -- caturbhAgasavisheSheNa /
"pramANaM tR^itIyena vardhayet' ityAdinA vardhitena dvicatvAriMshadaN^gulena caturdashatilayuktena /
evametaishcaturbhiH kAritA ShoDashI /
ardheShTakAM tribhiH parigR^ihNIyAditi sarvatra sheShaH //


dvAbhyamiti -- triMshadaN^gulAbhyAM /
savisheSheNoktapramANena /
etaistribhiH kArayet /
pAdeti -- gatametat /
caturiti -- caturthenaikaM /
caturthasya savisheShaH

caturthasavisheShaH /
tasyArdhAbhyAm /
pakSheti pakShArthamiShTakA -- pakSheShTakA /
tAM caturbhiH parigR^ihNIyAt /
dvAbhyAM ceti -- dvAbhyAM caturthAbhyAM puruShasaptamAbhyAM /
asya namanamupariShTAdvakShyate /
pakShamadhya -- gataM caturthAbhyAM dvisaptamAbhyAM vakrabhUtAbhyAmityetaishcaturbhiH pakShamadhyIyAM karoti /
pakSheti -- gatam /
caturtheneti -- puruShacaturthenaikaM caturthasaptamAbhyAM vakrabhUtAbhyAmekaM caturthasavisheShasaptamAbhyAmeva //


karavindIyA vyAkhyA

ShoDa -- Neti

puruShasya ShoDashabhAge yA tiShThAti sA ShoDashI /
tAM caturbhiH catuShprakAraiH phalakaiHShoDashIM parigR^ihNIyAt -- sampAdayet /
aShTamena -- prakR^itatvAt purUShasya /
paJNcadashAN^guleneti yAvat /
tribhiraShTamaiH paJNcacatvAriMshadaN^gulaiH /
caturthena triMshadaN^gulena /
caturthasavisheSheNa dvicatvAriMshadaN^gulena sArdhacaturdashatilAdhikena akShNayAvasthitena /
itishabdashvArthe /
etenacaitena ceti -- aShTamI triraShTamyau pArshvamAnyau /
caturthatatsavisheShau tirya«bhAnyau /
caturthasyaiva saviseShaprAptayarthaM caturthashabdaH //
evametaishcaturbhi.H phalakaiH ShoDashIM kArayet //


ardhe -- ceti

parigR^ihNIyAditi sheShaH /
ardheShTakAM tribhiH phalakaiH parigR^ihNIyAt /
triMshadaN^gulAbhyAM dvicatvAriMshadaN^gulena sacaturdashatilena ca tribhiH phalakaiH //


pAde -- ceti

ekaviMshatyaN^gulAbhyAM sasaptatilAbhyAM triMshadaN^gulena caikena ceti tribhiH //


pakShA -- ti

triMshadaN^gulAbhyAM saptadashAN^gulAbhyAM paJNcatilAdhikAbhyAM ceti /
pakSheShTakAM dvAbhyAM caturthAbhyAM samAbhyAM ca kArayet /
asya ca namanamupariShTAdvakShyati //


pakSha -- ti

pakShamadhyamayogyA pakShamadhyIyA /
tAM triMshadaN^gulAbhyAM catu striMshadaN^gulabhyAM dvisaptadashAhgulAbhyAM dashatilAdhikAbhyAM ceti caturbhiH //


pakShA -- ti

pakShAgrayogyA pakShAgrIyA /
tAM triMshadaN^gulenaikaM paJNcatilAdhikasaptacatvAriMshadaN^gulenaikaM tathaikonaviMshatitilAdhikena ekonaShaShTayaN^gulenaikamiti tribhiH phalakaiH parigR^ihNIyAt /
evaM ShaT karaNAnyuktAni /
pakSheShTakAH pakShamadhyIyAH pakShAgrIyA iti trayANAM tatra tatropadhAne yogyatvAya kShetrasamatvAya

sundararAjIyA vyAkhyA

athakaraNAni--

ShoDashIM -- Neti

pUrvashyenacaturthyeShA /
etAM caturbhiH phalakaiH parigR^ihNIyAt /
tatrAShTamena tribhiraShTamairiti pArshvaphalake /
uttare tiryakphalake /
savisheShaM caturthaM caturthasya dvikaraNI caturdasha tilAH dvicatvAriMshadaN^gulAH /

ardhe Neti

pAde ceti

pUrvashyenanamanyeShA /

caturthe triMshadaN^gule pArshvaphalake /
saptame sapa§vratilasaptadashAN^gule tiryakphalake /

pakShamadhyI ceti

dve pakSheShTake /
samaste eShA /
pUvashyene dvitIyAvadrUpaM /

pakShA ceti

pakSheShTakA -- ardheShTakA /
samaste ekA /

kapardibhAShyam

___________________________________________________________


pakShakaraNyAHsaptamaM tirya«mAnI | puruShacaturthaM ca pArshvamAnI | tasyAkShNayA rajjvA karaNaM prajR^imbhayet  || ˘p¡us_19.8a ||

___________________________________________________________


dIrghIkuryAt /
anayeti karaNI /
pakShakaraNI -- pakShasya karaNI pakShakaraNI iShTakA /
tasyA uktaM karaNaM puruShasaptamaM tirya«bhAnI puruShacaturthI pArshvamAnIti /
pakSheShTakAM caturbhiriti /
tameva dIrghIbhUtaM karaNaM prajambhayet -- dIrghIkuryAt /
kathamekayA kShNayA rajjvAyatayA dIrghIkuryAtkaraNam?

___________________________________________________________


pakShanamanyAH saptamena phalakAni namayet  || ˘p¡us_19.8b ||

___________________________________________________________


pakShanamanIti nitodalekhAmUlayorantarAlam /
tatsaptadhA vibhajya ekena bhAgena /
kimuktaM bhavati? yAvatprajambhitena tasyAHsaptamI tiryagbhavati tAvatprajambhayoditi /
evaM yathA bhavati tathA phalakAni namayet /
nataM namanaM kuryAt /

pakShanamanI sA pakShAgrANAmapyevameva /
tatra shlokaH ----

tilaiHShoDashabhirnyUnaM tiryaksyAtShoDashAN^gulam /

tathA tathA caturbhyAM ca saptamAbhyAM ca nAmayet //


___________________________________________________________


upadhAne catasraH pAdeShTakAH purastAc chirasi | apareNa shiraso 'pyayaM paJNca | pUrveNa pakShApyayAv ekAdasha | apareNaikAdasha pUrveNa pucchApyayaM paJNcApareNa paJNca paJNcadasha pucchAgre  || ˘p¡us_19.9 ||

___________________________________________________________



upadadhyAditi sheShaH /
purastAcchirasi ghoNAkAre ekA /
tasyAH pashcAttisraH /
apareNeti -- karNAbharaNavat /
pAdeShTakA eva /
pUrveti -- Atmani pakShApyayayoH pUrastAdekAdasha apareNa pakShApyayAvekAdasha etA eva /
pUrveti -- pUcchasyApyayasya purastAt paJNca pashcAcca paJNca /
paJNcadasheti -- pucchAgre paJNcadasha /
tA evaitAH ShaTpaJNcAshatpAdeShTakAH //


ekonaviMshaH khaNDaH

--------

karavindIyA vyAkhyA

ca vakratA kAryetyAha ----

pakShaka -- yet

prathamyAt sAmarthyAcca pakSheShTakAkaraNIviShayamidam likhayA vibhaktasya pakShArdhasya karaNI pakShakaraNI /
sA sapAdAN^gulona dashashatAN^gulA /
tasyAHsaptamaM sAShTAdashatilA paJNcadashAN^gulA R^ijvavasthitA prajambyamAnasya karaNasya yathA tirya«nAnI bhavati tathA tatkaraNaM R^ijvakShNayA prajambhayet -- prakarSheNa namayet /
pArshvamAnI tu prajmbhyamAne 'pi karaNe puruShacaturthameva /
prajambhatiratrApi mAnArtha eva /
etaduktaM bhavati -- karaNasya ekasyAM koTyAM rajjuM prabadhya tAM koTimitArAM koTiM prati akShNayA balena karShayet /
yathA AkarShaNe kR^ite dvayoH koTyoH sannikarSheNa pArshvamAnyorantarAlamR^ijutvena pakShkaraNyAHsaptamaM bhavati na nyUtaM nApyadhikaM tathA prajambhayet /
tirya«nAnyorantarAlamR^ijvavasthitamapi puruShacaturthameva /
anena tirya«mAnyA hrAsaH kriyate vakratvAya kShetrasamatvAya ca /
athavA sAShTAdashatilaM paJNcadashAN^gulaM tirya«mAnIM kR^itvA triMshaDhaN^gulaM pArshvamAnIM ca kR^itvA tAbhyAM caturshraM vihR^itya tasyAkShNayArajjvA pakSheShTakAkaraNaM prajambhayet /
etaduktaM bhavati -- uktaprakArAkShNayArajjvadhikAM rajjuMmItvA tayA pakSheShTakAkaraNasyaikAM koTiM badhvA tAM koTiM anyA koTiM pratyakShNayA jambhayet -- manayet /
yathA tayoH koTayorantarAlaM etadakShNayArajjuHsambhavati tathA namayedityarthaH /
evaM kR^ite asya karaNasyaikAkShNayArajjuH sArdhaddvayaN^gulena drAghIyasI bhavati /
anyA tenaiva hasIyasI bhavati //


vyAkhyA dvitIyA yaiH kaishviduktA nAJNjasyabhAginI //


pakSheShTakAkaraNasya prajambhanena namanavidhimuktvA pakShamadhyIyApakShAgrIyAkaraNayornamanasid dhayarthaM tatphalakAnAM natirucyate -- pakShanamanI -- yayA mAtrayA pakSho namyate sA pakShanamanI /
sA ca pakShamadhyalekhAyAH prathamanitodAt pashcimamAtrA /
sA ca paJNcaviMshatitilAdhikapaJNcAshadaN^guletyuktA /
tasyAHsaptamaM sArdhAShTatilaM saptAN^gulaM /
tena phalakAni pakShamadhyIyApakShAgrIyAkaraNayordIrghAni yAni phalakAni tAni namayet -- vakIkuryAt /
ayamarthaH -- yathA madhye kR^itena namanena pakShmadhyIyAMbhAgadvayaM pakShakaraNyA saptamaM tirya«mAnI puruShacaturthaM ca pArshvamAnItyuktaprakAraM bhavati /
tathA dvisaptaphalakayormadhye saptamamAtre pakShanamanyAHsaptamena ekasmin phalake natimekasminnudaJNcaM kuryAt //


tatra shlokAH --

pakSheShTakAyAH karaNaM tathA rajjvA prajambhayet /

tasya tiryagyathA pakShakaraNyAHsaptamaM bhavet //


pakShamadhyIyAkaraNe drAghIyaH phalakadvaye /

namanIsaptamena syAnnatiHsaptamamAtrake //


pakShAgrIyAkaraNasyApyeShaiva namanakriyA /

saptameM'she natistasya bhAgone 'nyo bhavedR^ijuH //


sAShTAdashatilaM tiryagyathA paJNcadashAN^gulam /

bhAgAnAmiShTakAnAM ca tathA syAbhamanakriyA //


Adyashyene tvAdimasya karaNasya prajambhanam /
Sha

phalaM ShaShThaH pakShakaraNI ShaShThavyAso yathA bhavet //


dvitIyasya tR^itIyasya praShaShThAnAM nateH phalam /

vyAsasya pakShakaraNI ShaShThatA nAShTame natiH //


AdyashyenaviShayamidaM shlokadvayam //


pakSheShTakAH catasro 'tra ShaTca pAdeShTakA api /

coDAnAkasadAmardhajAnordashamakAritAH //


upa -- rasi

upadhAnakAle catasraH pAdeShTakAHshira (si) saH pUrvabhAge purastAdupadadhyAt /
tAsAM catasR^iNAmekA purastAt bAhyavisheShAt prAgagrA /
tataH pashcAttisraH /
tAsu madhyamA pratyagagrA //


apa -- paJNca

shiraso 'pyayasya parataH paJNca /
pratyagagre dve /
apucchAtpAdApyaye ityeva //


pUrve -- dasha

apareNa -- pakShApyayayoH purataH /
AtmanaikAdasha /
paJNca pratyagagrAH //


apasha -- sha

apareNa pashcimapakShApyayayoH pashcAdekAdasha /
ShTpratyagagrAH //


pUrve -- ca

pucchApyayasya purataH paJNca /
tAsu pratyagagrAH tisraH //


apa -- ca

pucchApyayasya purataH paJNca /
tAsu pratyagagre dve //


paJNca -- gre

pucchAgre paJNcadasha upadheyAH /
tAsu sapta pratyagagrAH /
tA etAHShaTpaJNcAshatpAdeShTakAH //


sundararAjIyA vyAkhyA

pakSha -- yet

pakShakaraNI -- pakShArdhasya tirya«mAnI pAdonanavashatAN^gulA /
ardhe tasya saptamaM paJNcadashAN^gulaM sAShTAdashAtilaM /
tasya karaNasya yathA tirya«nAnI bhavati pArshvamAnI triMshadaN^gulaiva tathAkShNayA rajjvA karaNaM prajambhayet -- namayet /
ekaH karNaH catvAriMshadaN^gulo dvAdashatilAnvitaH /
aparaH saptaviMshako viMshatitilayuktaH /
Aratni (prAdesha) rahite (Shve)(tve) ekaH karNaH sArdhatrayoviMshakaH /
anyaH paJNcatilonastricatvAriMshadaN^gulaH iShTakAvyAsash ca trayodashAN^gulastrayodashatilayuktaH /
atha pakShAgrIyApakShamadhyayornamanamAha --

pakSha yet

pakShanamanI -- puruShamAtrI /
tasyAH saptamena pakShAgrIyApakShamadhyayoH pakSheShTakAMshasya tiryakphalakAni namayet /
tasya sAShTAdashatilapaJNcadashAN^gulavyAsasya pakSheShTakAMshasya tiryakphalake yathA sapaJNcatile saptadashAN^gule bhavataH tathA phalakAni takShet /
dve pakSheShTake pArshvasaMhite pakShamadhyIyA ShaDashriH pakSheShTakAmuttarapUrvatIrghakarNAM bhUmau likhitvA tasyA dakShiNataH triMshadaN^gulaM samacaturashraM kR^itvA tasya dakShiNapUrvamardhaM a (pUrvama) kShNayAjahyAt /
sA pakShAgrIyA paJNcakoNA /
atrANUkAH paJNcadashabhAgIyAnAM sthAna iti vakShyamANatvAt aNUkasaMj~ne dve karaNe kArye /
triMshadaN^gule dve sa macaturashre dakShiNottare likhitvA dakShiNasya dakShiNapUrvamardhamakShNa yA nirasyet /
uttarasyottarAparaM /
etadekamaNUkaM /
trikoNaM dvitIyaM /
tasya ShaShTayaN^gulamekaM phalakaM /
anye caturthasavisheShe //


athopadhAnaM --

apa -- shirasi

agreNaikA /
tasyAH pashcAttisraH /

apa ---- paJNca

pAdeShTakAH /
udIcI rItiH /

pUrve -- ekAdasha

udIcyeva rItirAtmanyeva /

apa -- gre

etAH ShaTpaJNcAshadapyudagAyatAH //


ekonaviMshaH khaNDaH

--------

kapardibhAShyam


___________________________________________________________


catasrashcatasraH pakShAgrIyAH pakShAgrayoH pakShApyayayosh ca vishayAH  || ˘p¡us_20.1 ||

___________________________________________________________



___________________________________________________________


tA Atmani catasR^ibhish catasR^ibhiH ShoDashIbhir yathAyogaM paryupadadhyAt  || ˘p¡us_20.2 ||

___________________________________________________________



viparyasya kAritA uttare pakShe /
catasrashcatasro vishayAH /
pakShasandhyordakShiNapakShApyaye viparyasya kAritA uttare pakSheShTakA mAtram /
pakShayorAtmanyardheShTakAmAtraM /
tA iti vishayAH pratyavamR^ishyante /
Atmani catasR^ibhishcatasR^ibhiHShoDasIbhiH viparyasya kAritAH /
dakShiNapakShApyayasthA yathA tairetAbhishcatasR^ibhirupadadhyAt tathA catasR^ibhiruttarapakShApyayasthAH /
pratItyasminnarthe parishabdaH //


___________________________________________________________


catasrashcatasraH pakShamadhyIyAH pakShamadhyayoH  || ˘p¡us_20.3 ||

___________________________________________________________


___________________________________________________________


pakSheShTakAbhiH prAcIbhiH pakShau pracchAdayet  || ˘p¡us_20.4 ||

___________________________________________________________



pakShamadhye bhavA vakrabhUtAshcatasro dakShiNe pakShamadhye catasra evottarapakShamadhye /
pakSheShTakA uktalakShaNAH /
tAbhiH prAgA yatAbhiH pakShau prAcchAdayet /
pakShayorupadadhyAt /
viparyasya kAritAshvatvAriMshat //


___________________________________________________________


avashiShTaM ShoDashIbhiH prAcchAdayet  || ˘p¡us_20.5a ||

___________________________________________________________



shiShThamagnikShetraM ShoDashIbhiH upadadhyAt //


___________________________________________________________


antyA bAhyavisheShA anyatra shirasaH  || ˘p¡us_20.5b ||

___________________________________________________________


___________________________________________________________


aparasmin prastAre purastAc chirasi dve ShoDashyau bAhyavisheShe upadadhyAt  || ˘p¡us_20.6a ||

___________________________________________________________



ante bhavA antyAH -- agnayantasthAH /
tA bAhyavisheShAH bAhyataHsavisheShAH anyatra shirasaH -- shiro varjiyitvA /
Atmani madhye ShaT prAcyaH ShaT pratIcyaH /
Atmani rItidvayam /
avashiShTaM pucche ca /
tAsu yadi ShoDashIbirevopadhIyante saMkhyApUryate kiM tu bidyate /
catasR^iShvapi rItiShu bhedo varjanIyaH /
tasmAdardhAshvopadheyAH /
kathamanucyamAnA upadhIyante nocyamAnAH? uktA eva "yaccaturashraM trayashri vA sampadyetArdheShTakAbhiH pAdeShTakAbhirvA pracchAdayet' iti vadatA /
nanu yadyardhAshvopadhIyante atiricyate saMkhyA; naiSha doShaH; UnAdhikaprastAra ityuktaM pUrvasmin paTale /
pucche rItidvayam /
tisrastisror'dheShTakA upadhAya ShoDashyaH punashvottare pArshve ekaikor'dhaH /
evamAtmani dvayo rItyordakShiNatastisror'dheShTakAH /
tato dve ShoDashyau ekaikordhaH /
shirasi tiryagdve ShoDashyau /
evamaShTottaraM shatadvayaM /
aparasminniti -- pUrvabhAge dve ShoDashyau bAhyataHsavisheShe ghoNAkAre upadadhyAt /
viparyasya kAritA dakShiNataH //


___________________________________________________________


te 'pareNa dve vishaye abhyantaravisheShe  || ˘p¡us_20.6b ||

___________________________________________________________



___________________________________________________________


dvAbhyAm ardheShTakAbhyAM yathAyogaM paryupadadhyAt  || ˘p¡us_20.7a ||

___________________________________________________________



tAbhyAM pashcAdAtmani ardheShTakAmAtraM; sheShaM shirasi /

abhito yujyate yathA tathopadadhyAt /
catasra etA vishayAH //


karavindIyA vyAkhyA

cata -- yoH

pratyekaM catasraH //


pakShA -- yAH

cakAreNa pakShAgrIyA anukR^iShyante /
pakShApyayayoH catasrashcatasraH pakShAgrIyA vishayAH syuH /
tAH saptamena pakShayoH sherate /
avashiShTe caturthenAtmani //


tA A -- dhyAt

Atmani praviShTapakShAgrIyAparitashcatasR^ibhiH ShoDashIbhirH yathA yujyante tathopadadhyAt /
pakShAgrIyANAM ca yathA visheShAHsahitA bhaveyustathopadadhyAdityarthaH //


cata -- yoH

yathAyogamityeva /
gatam //


pakSha -- dayet

yathAyogamityeva /
catvAriMshatA catvAriMshatA pakSheShTakAbhiH prAgAyatAbhiH pakShau pracchAdayet //


ava -- yet

avashiShTaM anupahitamagnikShetraM pucchAvashiShTaM ShoDashIbhiH pracchAdayet /
pucchamadhye dve rItyau /
pUrvAshcaturiShTakAH /
pashcimAHShaDiShTakAH /
dve dve visheShasahite

syAtAM /
tA etA dasha Atmani /
Atmamadhye tisro rItayaH /
prAcyashcaturaShTakA Atmanyeva /
pashcAtpurastAccodIcyau dve rItyau caturiShTake /
tA viMshatiH /
shirasi dve ShoDashayau //


antyA -- rasaH



ante upadheyA antyAH /
pucche catasraH Atmani catasra /
bAhyavisheShAH -- bahirgatavisheShAH /
na cAtra saMkhyApUraNaM; saMkhyAH yAHsthAne dvishataviniyogAt /
tathAhi -- ShaTpaJNcAshat pAdeShTakAH -- aShTAvaShTau pakShAgrIyAsvatvAriMshaccatvAriMshatpakSheShTakAH /
aShTau /
pakShamadhyIyAshvatvAriMshat ShoDashyaH /
evaM dvishataH //


apa -- dhyAt



dvitIye prastAre shirasaH pUrvabhAge prAgagre bAhyavisheShe dve ShoDashyau //


te  -- She

tayoHShoDashyoH pashcAt prAgagre shirasyardhapAdeShTakAmAtre vishaye visheSheNAtmani /
evaM vishaye dve ShoDashyAvantarvisheShe //


dvAbhyAM -- dhyAt

te ityeva /
te vishaye iShTake dvAbhyAmardheShTakAbhyAM vishayAbhyAM yathAyogaM parigR^ihNIyAt /
ShoDashyorardheShTakayosh ca yathA visheShAHsaMhitA bhaveyuH tathopadadhyAdityarthaH //


sundararAjIyA vyAkhyA

cata -- grayoH

tAsAmardheShTakAmAtrANyAtmani /

tA dhyAt

dakShiNAgrAbhiH dakShiNApyayasthA udIcIritarAH //


catasra -- dhyIyAH

pakSha -- dayet

ashItyA prAgAyatAbhiH //


ava -- dayet

aNUkAH paJNcadashabhAgIyAnAM sthAna iti vakShyamANatvAt aNUkAbhiH saha pracchAdanabhedaparihArAya tatra pucchAtmashiraHsu pUrvanihitAbhiH pAdarItibhiHsaha ShoDasha rItayaH udIcyaH /
pucchAgre pAdarItiruktA /
dvitIyasyAM pArshvayoraNUke madhye catasraH ShoDashyaH /
evaM tR^itIyAShaShThItrayodashyo 'NUkAbhireva dviprakArAbhiH sandhyantarAle dvAdasha ShoDashyaH pragAyatAH shiraso 'parArdhe dve ShoDashyau dvishataH prastAraH //


antyA -- shirasaH

ca shabdo 'trAdhyAhartavyaH /
dvAbhyAM visheShAH /
anteShu yA upadheyAstA bAhyavisheShAH ShoDashyo bhaveyuH /
etaccAtmanyeva /
pakShayorashakyatvAt pucchabhedasambhavAcca /
tasmAdAtmanaH shroNyaMseShvaShTau ShoDashIrdakShi (NAgrA) NA udagagrAshcopadadhyAt /
ekaikatra dvedve /
asmin pakShe yaccaturashraM tryashri veti vakShyamANAbhiH pAdyAbhiH saMkhyApUraNaM /
tatra pucchApyayasya purastAddve ardhe shiraso 'pyayasya pashcAddve ardhe /
tAsAM madhye caturvishatiH pAdyAH /
pArshvayoH ShaT ShaT ShoDashyaH /
yadvA etAH pAdyAH ShoDashIshvaH ShaTtriMshatamuddhR^itya ShaTtriMshadar (dhyAr) dhA nidheyAH /
tatra dakShiNapArshvasthA prAguttaravisheShAH viparItA

uttarAH /
pucchamadhye ShaT ShoDashyaH prAgAyatAH /
tataH pA (tatprA) rshvayosvatasror'dheShTakAH /
sheShaM pUrvavadeva /
a(ta)tra Atmani prAcyaH paJNcarItyaH udIcyo vA aShTau //


apara -- dadhyAt

te pa -- sheShe

ete api prAgagre /

dvAbhyAM -- dadhyAt

tayoH ShoDashyormadhye shiraso 'pyaye dve ardheShTake ityarthaH /

kapardibhAShyam


___________________________________________________________


bAhyavisheShAbhyAM parigR^ihNIyAt  || ˘p¡us_20.7b ||

___________________________________________________________



ubhayatra tR^itIyApadashravaNAt vidhyantarametat na pUrvayorvisheShaNam /
cashabdo 'dhyAhartavyaH bAhyavisheShAbhyAM ceti /
bAhyavisheShAbhyAM cArdheShTakAbhyAM parigR^ihNIyAt /
shirasyanavakAshAdAtmanyeva /

___________________________________________________________


AtmanaH karaNInAM sandhiShu ShoDashyo bAhyavisheShA upadadhyAt  || ˘p¡us_20.8 ||

___________________________________________________________



AtmanaH karaNyaH, tAsAM sandhiShu shroNyaMseShu catasraH ShoDashyo bAhyavisheShAH pratyantavisheShAH //


___________________________________________________________


catasrash catasro 'rdheShTakAH pakShAgrayoH  || ˘p¡us_20.9a ||

___________________________________________________________



nakhAkAreShvardheShTakAshvopadheyAshcatasrashcatasraH //


___________________________________________________________


pakSheShTakAbhir udIcIbhiH pakShau pracchAdayet  || ˘p¡us_20.9b ||

___________________________________________________________


udagAyatAbhiH pakShayo rupadadhyAt /
ShaTpaJNcAshAdviparyasya kAritAH /

___________________________________________________________


tisrastisro 'rdheShTakAH pucchapArshvayoH  || ˘p¡us_20.10 ||

___________________________________________________________



tisrastisror'dheShTakAH pucchapArshvayorbAhyavisheShAH //


___________________________________________________________


avashiShTaM ShoDashIbhiH pracchAdayet  || ˘p¡us_20.11a ||

___________________________________________________________



avashiShTamagnikShetraM ShoDashIbhiH pracchAdayet //


___________________________________________________________


antyA bAhyavisheShA anyatra pucchAt  || ˘p¡us_20.11b ||

___________________________________________________________


gatametat /
pucchaM varjayitvA /

karavindIyA vyAkhyA

bAhya -- yAt

te ityeva /
te eva ShoDashyau bAhyavisheShAbhyAmanyAbhyAmardhAbhyAM parigR^ihNIyAt /
ete ardhe shirasyanavakAshAdAtmani bhavataH /
etaduktaM bhavati -- vishayaShoDashyoH purastAdvishayabhUte bahirvisheShe dve arve tathA'tmani vishayaShoDashyordakShiNata uttaratash ca vahirvisheShe anye ardhe iti //


Atma -- dhyAt

AtmanaH karaNya AtmakaraNyaH /
tAsAM sandhiShu shroNyaMseShu ShoDashyaH catasraH /
sarvatra chAndaso vibhaktivyatyayaH /
Atmani pakShApyayayoHsamIpeShu bAhyavisheShAshcatasraH ShoDashIrupadadhyAt /
antyA bAhyavisheShA iti vakShyamANe 'pi bAhyavisheShagrahaNaM saMkhyApUraNAya /
pAdAnAM cArdhAnAM ca upadhAnArthaM ShoDashInAmuddhvaraNe prasakte AsANuddharaNaM mA bhUdityevamartham //


cata -- yoH

pratipakShaM catasror'dheShTakAH bAhyavisheShA ityeva //


pakShe -- dayet

pakShayorudIcyaH pakSheShaTakAH sapta rItayaH //


tisrar -- shvayoH

bAhyavisheShA eva //


ava -- yet

avashiShTamAtmani trayastriMshat ShoDashIsthAnaM pucchadvAdashaShoDashIsthAnam //


antya -- cchAt

antyAHsarvA bAhyavisheShA bhaveyuH pucchAdanyatra /
pucche tvantyAHShoDashyo 'bhyantaravisheShA eva /

sundararAjIyA vyAkhyA

bAhya -- gR^ihNIyAt

te ShoDashyau bAhyavisheShAbhyAM dvAbhyAmardheShTakAbhyAM dakShiNata uttaratashvAtmani parigR^ihNIyAt //


Atma -- dadhyAt

aShTAshrerAtmano 'ShTau karaNyaH /
tatra dakShiNottarapArshvakaraNyoH shroNyaMsakaraNIbhiH saha catvAraH sandhayaH /
tatra shroNisandhyordve pratyagagre ShoDashyau /
aMsasandhyordve prAgagre /
evaM catasraH ShoDashyaH /
ye tu catvAraH pUrvApara (koTyoH) karaNyoHsandhayaH tatra pUrvayostAvadbAhyavisheShAbhyAM parigR^ihNIyAdityardheShTake ukte /
aparayorapi pUrvasAdR^ishyArthaM bhedaparihArArthaM cAdhyardhe evopadheye /

catasra -- yoH

pakShe -- dayet

ekaikaM ShaTpaJNcAshatA /

tisra -- yoH

bAhyavisheShAH /

kapardibhAShyam

___________________________________________________________


yac caturashraM tryashraM vA saMpadyetArdheShTakAbhiH pAdeShTakAbhir vA pracchAdayet  || ˘p¡us_20.12 ||

___________________________________________________________



sarvatra ShoDashya eva sherate /
yadi tathA kShipyeran bhidyeta sarvatra /
ato bhedaparihArAya yatne kriyamANe trikoNaM caturashraM vA prakAradvayaM sampadyate /
pUrvasmin prastAre catarashraM sampadyate trikoNaM ca /
iha trikoNameva /
tatra ardheShTakAbhiH pAdeShTakAbhirvA pracchAdayet upadadhyAt /
pucchApyaye catasraH ShoDashyo vishayAH /
prAcyau dve pratIcyau dve /
tAsAM pashcAt dasha ShoDashyaH /
tiryakpucche 'pi /
vishayAmAnabhito dvAvardhau dvAvAtmi /
tAsAM purastAccatasraH ShoDashyaH prAcyashcaturthyaH pratyarpitAH /
tAsAM purastAdviparyastAH ShaDuttare pArshve /
tAsAM purastAccatasror'dheShTakAH /
tAsAM purastAccatasraH ShoDashyaH pratIcyastAbhiH pratyarpitAH /
tAsAM purastAd dve ShoDashyau nAnAgre prAcyau /
tayormadhye dvAvardhau /
AtmanyardhapAdeShTakAmAtrI /
Atmani dvAvardhau vishayAvabhitaH /
ardhaShoDashyau sahitau /
evaM dvAdashonaM shatadvayam /
iha keciddIrghAyuShaHsUtrametadanAdR^itya svamanIShikayA karaNAntaramutpAdya saMkhyApUraNameva kurvanti /
kiM nAma teShAmashakyam? vayaM tu sUtrakAramatAnusAreNoktaM gR^ihNImaH /

karavindIyA vyAkhyA

evaM kShetrapUraNaM kR^itvA prakR^ititaH prAptaM saMkhyApUraNaM evaM kartavyamityAha----

yacca ---- dayet

evaM ShoDashIbhiH pracchAdyamAne saN^khyApUraNAya kAsuciduddhR^itAsu ca yat kShetraM caturashraM tryashri vA sambhavet tat kShetramardheShTakAbhiH pAdeShTakAbhirvA pracchAdayet -- tAbhiHsaMkhyAM pUrayedityarthaH nanu pracchAdayediti vacanena saN^khyApUraNaM katham? ucyate /
tattadagnau pracchAdanavidhyanantaraM saN^khyAM pUrayoditi vidhAnAt /
iha ca ShoDashIbhiH pracchAdite saN^khyAyA asamAptestatpUraNApekShayA dvitIyapracchAdanavacanaM saN^khyApUraNArthameveti gamyate /
kiJNca dvividhaH prAkR^ito 'gnaniH samacaturashramAtreShTakA asamacatu; rashramAtreShTakAsh ca /
prathame caturashrAgnau paJNcadashabhAgIyAbhirardheShTakA /
bhish ca saN^khyA pUritA /
dvitIye pAdeShTakANUkAShaDbAgIyAbhish ca pUritA /
tadihApe pAdA ardhA aNUkAsh ca vihi /
tAsAsanti /
tasmAt pAdeShTakAbhirardheShTakAbhish ca saN^khcA pUritAdvitIye ShoDashIbhish ca yathA yogaM saN^khyApUraNaM yuktamiti gamyate /
kiJNca saN^khyApUraNasya nyAyyatve sati atropadiShTeShTakAbhyo 'nyAbhiHsaN^khyApUraNasyAshakyatvAt pAdAbhirardhAbhish ca sukaratvAt tAbhireva saN^khyApUraNaM yuktataram /
ataH pracchAditAsu kAshciduddhR^itya pAdArdhaShoDashIbhairyathAyogaM yAvatsaN^khyamupadheyA iti //


sundararAjIyA vyAkhyA

ava dayet

yaccaturashraM trayashri veti pAdyArdhAbhiH saN^khyApUraNaM, tatrar(dhyAr) dhAbhiH pUraNapakShe Atmani prAcyaH ShaDrItayaH /
tatra dakShiNottarayormadhye ShaT ShaDar(dhyAr)dhAH /
dvitIyasyAM pashcAtpurastAcca dve ardhe ukte /
tayoH samIpe dve ShoDashyau prAgAyate /
tayormadhye 'ShTAvardheShTakAH /
evameva paJNcamI rItiH /
prAgAyatAbhiH dvAdashabhiH ShoDashIbhirmadhyarItI dve /
pucchApyaye dve ShoDashyau /
pratyagagrapucchaM paJNcadashAN^gulena pUrvAccatasraH ShoDashyaH udagAyatAH /
pucchAgre dakShiNator'dheShTakA pUrvamuktA /
tasyA udak ShoDashyudagagrA tasyA udagdve ardhe tato dve ShoDashyau tato dve ar(dhyer)dhe tataH ShoDashI /
tator(dhyAr)dhA pUrvamuktA /
evaM dvishataH prastAraH /
pAdyAbhiH pUraNapakShe Atmani dakShiNapArshve dvAdashArdhyA uddhR^itya vA aShTau catasraH ShoDashyo nidheyAH /
evamuttarapArshve 'pi /
asminnapi prastAre prakArAntaramAha ----

antya -- cchAt

atrApi vAshabdo 'dhyAhAryaH /
yathA pUrvasmin prastAre antyA bAhyavisheShA iti ShoDashyo vihitAH tathAtrApi shroNyaMseShu dve dve ShoDashyau prAgagre pratyagagre cetyaShTau nidheyAH /
etadapyashakyatvAtpakShayorna bhavati /
asmin pakShe shiro 'pyaye ardhenopadheye /
pucchApyaye 'pyardhe dve upadheye /
pArshvasthAshcatasro rItayordhe 'ShTakAbhiHpUraNIyAH /
madhyamarItyoH ShoDashaShoDashyaH pucchAgramadhye ShaT ShoDashyaH /
tataH pUrvasyAM madhye dve ShoDashyau /
sheSher'dhyAH /
tataH pUrvasyAM madhye dve prAcyau ShoDashyau /
sheShaM pUrvavadeva /
eSha dvishataH /
pAdyAbhiH pUraNapakShe 'pi pUrvavatsarvatrAvisheShAt pAdAyAbhiH sambhave 'pi viparItavisheShA upadheyAH /
kecittu antyA bAhyavisheShA iti pUrvamuktam /
tayoreva prastArayoH sheShamAhuH /
tadanupapannaM, antyAnAM ShoDashInAM aniyatavisheShANAmabhAvAt /
ubhayasmin prastAre prAhuH antyA iti na kevalaM ShoDashya eva gR^ihyante /
apitu yAH kAshvAntyA upadheyAH tAsh ca bAhyavisheShAH kAryA iti /
teShAM shirasi dve ShoDashyau bAhyavisheShe bAhyavisheShAbhyAM parigR^ihNIyAt /
AtmakaraNInAM sandhiShu ShoDashyo bAhyavisheShA iti bAhyavisheSha shabdakaM anarthakaM syAt /
anyatra shiraso 'nyatra pucchAditi ca virudhyete /
shirasi pAdyAnAM pucchapArshvayorardhyAr(dhA)nAM ca bAhyavisheShANAmeveShTatvAt //


yaccatu -- yet

prastAradvayasAdhAraNamidam /
ShoDashIbhiH pUrayitumashakyopi yAvaddvishatapUrti ardhAH pAdyA upadheyAH /
tatrArdhyArahitAbhiH pAdyAbhiH saN^khyAM pUrayitumashakyatvAt /
tasmAdardhyAbhiH saMmishrAbhirvA pAdyAbhiH pUraNam /
tatprakArash ca pUrvamekoktaH //


kapardibhAShyam

___________________________________________________________


aNUkAH paJNcadashabhAgIyAnAM sthAne  || ˘p¡us_20.13 ||

___________________________________________________________



___________________________________________________________


vyatyAsaM cinuyAd yAvataH prastArAMsh cikIrShet  || ˘p¡us_20.14 ||

___________________________________________________________



sthAnashabdaH prayogavAcI /
aNUkAshcaturbhAgIyAH saN^khyApUraNe coditAH paJNcadashabhAgIyAsh ca saN^ghayApUraNe coditA itI yAvat /
asmin prastAre saN^khyA na pUritA sUtrakAreNa /
tatra tAbhiHsaN^khyA pUrayitavyA yadi tAbhiH pUryate /
asminnagau tAvatA na shakyate aNUkAbhiHsaN^khyA pUraNam /
shakyate tu prakR^itau /
tasmAtprakR^ityarthau yogaH /
tatra shakyate dvitIye prastAre tAbhiH pUrayitum /
tatra dvishatapUraNamavashyaM kartavyam /
pratiprastAraM pUrayediti vacanAt /
iha tu sahasrasaMkhyaiva pUrayitavyA ityuktaM pUrvasmin paTale /
tasmAtprakR^ito yogaH /
tatra shlokAH ----

pakSheShTakAnAM karaNaM viparyasyArdhaviShyate /

pakShAgrIyAstathaivArdhaM viparyasyaiva kArayet //


viparyashcaiva kartavyAHShoDashyaH ShoDashIdvayam /

sAhasre 'tha dviShAhasre paJNcaShaShTiM vidurbudhAH //


upadhAne yathAsUtraM yathA vAtmani pakShayoH /

pucche shirasi shiShTe ca ShoDashInAM vidurbudhAH //


ShaTprAcyaH ShaTprIcyash ca Atmani dvAdasha kShipet /

shIrShNi dvayaM kShipettiryaguktA eva caturdasha //


shiShTaM rItidvayaM pucche tathA cAtmanyapi dvayam /

ShoDashArdheShTakAstAstu kShipecca triShu rItiShu //


ekaikamuttare pArshve tisrastisrastu dakShiNe /

shiShTe tiryagdashaiva syAdaShTottarashatadvayam //


pucchApyaye tu vishayAshcatasraHShoDashIH kShipet /

ShoDashyAvapyaye prAcyau te cAgre shirasi kShipet //


madhye tayosh ca dvAvardhau catasro vishayAH kShipet /

AtmanaHsheShe dvAvardhau ShoDashyau shirasi kShipet //


anyatsarMva yathAsUtraM dvAdashonaM shatadvayam /

Atmano dakShiNe pArshve catasro dakShiNAyatAH //


dvitIye cottare pArshve ShaD dve shroNyaMsayorapi /

shirasashvApyaye caikA shirasyapi ca dakShiNA //


etA nidheyAHShoDashyo viparyastAstare dvaye /

karanindIyA vyAkhyA

aNU -- ne



paribhASheyam /
paJNcadashabhAgIyAH prathamacaturashre uktAH /
tAsAM sthAne kAryasaMkhyApUraNe aNUkA bhaveyuH /
tasyAH paribhAShAyA atropadeshaH katham? ihopadiShTAH ShoDashyo 'pi kShetrasAmyAdaNUkAshabdena grAhyA bhaveyuH ityevamartham /
tena aNUkAbhishcaturashre 'gnau saMkhyApUraNam /
iha tu ShoDashIbhishvoti siddham /
kecidyaccaturashraM tryashri vA sampadyate ityetadapi paribhAShAmicchanti /
tena tatratatrAgnau tadapekShyA tAbhirapi saMkhyApUraNaM manyante /
atra punaH pracchAdayediti vacanaM pracchAdane 'pi caitA yathA bhaveyurityevamartham /
tena tatratatrAgnau sati sambhave satyAM cApekShAyAM tAbhiHsahaubhirapi pracchAdanaM syAt /

upadhAnakramaH dvitIyacityAM shirasi prA«bhukhe bAhyavisheShe dve ShoDashyau upadadhyAt /
tayoH pashcAt prA«bhukhe bAhyavisheShe vishaye dve ardhe /
tayoH pashcAttadvisheShashliShTavisheShe dve ShoDashyau vishaye Atmani /
tayordakShiNasyA dakShiNato bAhyavisheShamekamardham /
uttarasyA uttaratash ca bAhyavisheShamekamardham /
tayordakShiNata uttaratash ca bAhyavisheSheNaikaikamardham /
tataH pashcAdAtmani prAcyaHShaDrItayaH /
tatra dakShiNasyAM rItyAM purastAt bAhyavisheShA prAgagraikA ShoDshI /
pasvAcca bAhyavisheShA pratyagagraikA /
tayormadhye ShaDardheShTakAH /
tAsAM tisraH pratIcyastisra udIcyaH /
dvitIyasyAM rItyAM pashcAt bAhyavisheSheNa dakShiNAmukhe dve ardhe /
tatpurastAdardhavisheShayuktavisheShAt pratya«bhukhaikA ShoDashI /
tasyA /
purastAt ShaDardhAH /
tAsAM tisrastisraH prAcya pratIcyash ca /
tatpurastAtuttarato visheShA prAgagraikA ShoDashI /
tatpurastAttadvisheShashliShTavisheShamekamardham /
tatpurastAt pUrvopahitamardhamastyeveti dvAdasheShTakA eShA /
tR^itIyasyAM rItyAM shiro 'pyayaShoDashyAH pashcAdArabhya ApucchApyayamaShTau ShoDashya upadheyAH /
tAsAM catasraH prAcyashcatasraH pratIcyaH /
evamevottarAstisro rItayaH /
tatra tR^itIyAvaccaturthI /
dvitIyAvatpaJNcamI /
prathamAvat ShaShThI /
tatra tisR^iNAM dakShiNarItInAM dakShiNaM pArshvamuttararItInAmuttaraM pArshvam /
dakShiNAnAmuttarANaM ca dakShiNA pArshvarItidvayagatA /
atra pratIcyo mukulAtmakAH /
tatpratIpamukAH prAcyaH /
evaM shobhAM vitanvate /
pucche madhyamarItyantayorvishayaShoDasyordAkShiNata uttaratash ca dve ardhe bAhyavisheShe /
tataH pashcAnmadhye dve ShoDashyau /
te abhita(stitasra)stisro 'rdheShTakA ityaShTeShTakAH /
tataH pucchAgre ShaDbhiH ShoDashIbhirabhitor'dhAbhiraShTeShTakAH /
pakShAgrayoshcatasrashcatasror'dheShTakAH /
pakShadvaye pakSheShTakAHsapta rItayaH /
tA dvAdashashatamiShTakAH /
pAdeShTakAbhish ca pUraNapakShe etA eva rItayaH /
tatra visheShaH pucchagatopAntarItyAM bAhyAsvatasror'dheShTakA dvidhA kuryAt /
Atmani prathamadvitIyapaJNcamaShaShTheShu tanmadhyagatArdheShu pashcimato dve dve ardhe /
avashiShTAnyeShvardhasthAneShu ShoDashIyugmAnyupadadhyAt /
dvitIyApaJNcamyoshvArdhA dvidhA bhidyAt /
nanu bhedo varjanIya iti tatratatrAgnau yatnena parihR^itaH /
sa idAnIM pucche prAdurbubhUShati? naitatsAram /
niyatalokAnAmiShTakAnAmasaMbAdhena samuditAbhiriShTakAbiHsaN^khyAyAM pUritAyAM yadIShTakaikadeshe bheda upajAyate sa bhedo marShaNIya eva, avarjanIyatvAdekadeshabhedasya /
ata eva bhedavarjanaM svakaNThenoktamAcAryeNa dvishata eSha iti //


vyAtyAr -- Shet

gatam //


sundararAjIyA vyAkhyA



aNU ane

prakR^itau caturashrAgnau paJNcadashabhAgIyAnAM kAryaM bhedaparihAreNa saMkhyApUraNam /
iha tu tatkArye aNUkA upadheyAH /
tatra samacaturashrANAmaNUkAnAmupadhAne dvishataH kartuM na shakyate /
tasmAdaNUkakShetrANAM grahaNam /
tatrApi ShoDashyo na gR^ihyante /
avashiShTaM ShoDashIbhirityeva siddhatvAt bhedasambhavAcca /
tasmAda (nyA ) NUkakShetrAdi (dvi) prakArA iShTakAH kartavyAH /
darshite ca tAsAM karaNe (pUrvameva) /
AcAryeNa tu karaNe nopadiShTe /
antyA bAhyavisheShA ityasmin pakShe aNUkAnAmanupayogAt /
uktashvopadhAnaprakAraH /
aNUkAbhirvinaiva tasmin pakShe prathama eva prastAre aNUkAnAmupayogaH kartavyaH //


kapardibhAShyam

___________________________________________________________


kaN^kacid alajacid iti shyenacitA vyAkhyAtau  || ˘p¡us_21.1 ||

___________________________________________________________



kaN^kaH pakShivisheShaH alajash ca /
kaN^ka iva cetavyaH kaN^kacit /
alaja iva cetavyo 'lajacit /
tau shyenacitA vyAkhyAtau -- pUrveNaiva shyenena vyAkhyAtau /
mukhyatvAddvishataprastAratvAcca tasyaivAkR^itiH tAnyeva karaNAni sa evopadhAnamArgaH /
saN^kalpa eva bhedaH shyeno 'lajaH kaN^ka iti //


___________________________________________________________


evami va hi shyenasya varShIyAMsau pakShau pucchAd vakrau saMnataM pucchaM dIrgha AtmA maNDalaM shirash ca | tasmAc chrutisAmarthyAt  || ˘p¡us_21.2a ||

___________________________________________________________



hishabdaH prasiddhau /
shyeno 'pyevameva /
varShIyAMsau -- bR^ihantau /
pakShau /
kasmAt pucchAddIrghau? na kevalaM bR^ilantau kiM tu tau vakrau /
sannataM samya«nataM AtmasamIpe 'lpIyaH agre shyene pR^ithu ucyate tatsannatamiti /
dIrgha AtmA naM samacaturashraH na maNDalaH nApi dIrghacaturashraH /
amaNDalamivAdIrghacaturashrabhUtaM shiraH /
evamprakAro loke shyenaH /
evameva kaN^kAlajo loke /
tasmAttadAkArAveva kaN^kAlajau tenaiva vyAkhyAtau /
shrutisAmarthyAt /
sAmarthyamabhidhAnashaktiH /
etAvadeva shrutyAbhidhIyate /
ashakyatvAtsarvasAmyA (saMpA) pAdanasya /
na hyashaN^kanIyamarthaM vedo vidadhAti //


___________________________________________________________


ashirasko vAnAmnAnAt  || ˘p¡us_21.2b ||

___________________________________________________________



vAshabdaH pakShavyAvR^ittau /
ashiraska eva cetavyaH /
kuta ityAha -- AnAmnAnAt /
na hi shira AmnAyate /
tasya kathamanAmnAnamityatrAha ----


___________________________________________________________


j~nAyate ca | kaN^kacitaM shIrShaNvantaM cinvIta yaH kAmayeta sashIrSho 'muShmiMl loke saMbhaveyam iti vidyamAne kathaM brUyAt  || ˘p¡us_21.3 ||

___________________________________________________________



yadi shirasa AmnAnamasti shIrShaNvantaM cinvIteti kathaM brUyAdevetyarthaH /
yadi shirasa AmnAnaM nAsti tadA yujyata evaitadvisheShaNam /
itarathA visheShaNamanarthakameva syAt /
tasmAdashiraska eva cetavyaH /
cadyashiraskaH kimAkAraHsa ityAha--

___________________________________________________________


prAkR^itau vakrau pakShau saMnataM pucchaM vikArashravaNAt  || ˘p¡us_21.4a ||

___________________________________________________________



prakR^ityAM bhavau prAkR^itau /
tAveva pakShau vakrIkartavyau /
kutaH? vikArashravaNAt /
sannataM pucchaM -- pucchaM ca sannataM kartavyam /
vaktapakSho vyastapuccha iti vikAraHshrUyate /
pakShapucchAnAM ca vaktatA vyastatA ca prakR^itau nAsti /
tasmAdvikAratvaM pakShapucchAnAm //


___________________________________________________________


yathAprakR^ity AtmAvikArAt  || ˘p¡us_21.4b ||

___________________________________________________________


yathAprakR^ityAtmA /
kutaH? avikArAt /
nahi tatra vikAraHshrUyate /
tasmAtpraN^kR^itivadevAtmA catuHpuruShaHsamacaturashrash ca /
aratninAr'dhaprAdeshena vA pakShau vivadheyet /
dvipuruShAM rajjumityAdishyenavat /
nanu prakR^itAvaratninA vardhayedityuktam /
kimidamucyate aratninAr'dhaprAdeshena veti? aratninetyardhavikAratvapratipAdanaparaM, na pakShapucchAnAM tAvanmAtramAyAmamApAdayitum /
AtmanashcaturthaM caturbhAgIyAshvAShTau ityupadhAtavyamiti

shyenapratipAditaM na kartavyam /
yathAprakR^ityevAtmA kartavyaH /
kiM ca prAkR^itaM pucchamiti vacanAcca upadhAnavidhish ca na ghaTate /
shyena iva cetavya ityevaM kriyamANe prathamadvitIyAnAmeva vikAro netareShAm /
itarathA caturthAdayo 'pi vikR^itA bhaveyuH /
tathAbhUtAsh ca kartavyA bhaveyuH /
tasmAcca karaNAnupraveshena cetavya ityuktam /
shyenavadeva puccham /
karaNAnyucyante -- caturthaShaShThAbhyAM yathAyoganataM tatprathamam /
dve pUrvavatsaMhite dvitIyamityAdi /
athopadhAnavidhiH -- aShTAcatvAriMshatprathamA udIcIH pakShayoH /
shyenavatpuccham /
AtmanaHshroNyostisrastisraH paJNcamya udIcyaH /
tataHsaptasu rItiShu ShaTpaJNcAshaccaturthyaH dakShiNAyatA udagAyatAsh ca /
tAsAM purastAdaShTau paJNcamyaH udagAyatAH /
shroNyoshcatasraH paJNcamya akShNayA bhindyAt /
aShTau ShaShThayaHsampadyante /
eSha dvishataH prastAraH /
aparasmin prastAre catasrashcatasro dvitIyA nirNAmayorapyayayosh ca vishayAstR^itIyAH /
catasrashcatasraH pUrvavadaShTabhAgAvetAH /
pakSheShTakAbhiH pakShau pracchAdayet /
taddvAsaptatiH pucche shyenavat /
saptAShTamAbhiHshroNyaMseShu dve dve paJNcamyau prAcIH pratIcIsh ca /
prAcyaH sapta rItayaH /
caturmistR^itIyApaJNcamyo rItyormadhye triMshat ShaShThayaH ekA ca paJNcamI /
ekatra ShoDashAparatra caturdasha /
evaM dvishataH prastAraH /
athavA sa evAnupucchamardhapuruShavyAsaM saprAdeshaM puruShaM pratIcInamAyacchet /
tasya dakShiNato 'nyamityAdinA shyenavatpucchaM kuryAt /
pakShau prAkR^itau dvipuruShAyAmau /
karaNAni vakShyAmaH -- dvAdashAN^gulA yathA bhavati tatA tiryak caturthaShaShThAbhyAM namayet /
prathamaM te eva saMhite yathA tiShThataH tathA kArayet /
dvitIyaM tR^itIyamapi yat ShaDbhAgenAShTamabhAgena vA vardhayediti ta eva vA pucche caturthaM trayastriMshadaN^gulavistAraM paJNcacatvAriMshadaN^gulAyAmaM caturdashatilairUnaM savisheShaM paJNcamaM ardhasaptAN^gulavyAsaM ShaTpArshvaM ekonatriMshadAyAmaM tu ShaTtriMshadaN^gulaM caturdashatilaiHsaha pucchApyaye vishayayoH aShTAdashAN^gulaM pucche paJNcadashAN^kumeva /
AtmAni caturthAdayo vaikR^itAH /
pucche tu prAkR^itA eva /
AtmanyupadhAnavidhiHsa eva /
tatra shlokAH ----

arndha trayodashaM vyAsamashiraske havirbhuji /
tathA caturthaShaShThAbhyAM namayetprathamaM tu tat //


te dve tu saMhite prAcI dvitIyaM karaNaM bhavet /
tR^itIyamapi ShaDbhAgamaShTabhAgena vardhitam //


pakSheShTakAshcaturthAHsyuH pucchaM pucchavaducyate /
ShaTpaJNcAshaccaturthyaHsyustiryagdakShoda gAyatAH //


aShTau purastAttiryakca shroNyoH ShaTpaJNcamIH kShipet /
shroNyAshcatasraH paJNcamyo bhedavaddvishatastathA //


shyenavatpakShapuccheShu nidhAyAtmanyapi kShipet /
prAcyAM caiva pratIcyAM ca triMshadekA ca paJNcamI //


tAsAmevottare pArshve caturthyaH ShoDashadvayam /
prAcyashvaiva pratIcyash ca tathA ShoDasha dakShiNe //


prAcIshvaiva pratIcIsh ca shiShTe paJNcamIM kShipet /
karaNasya viparyAsaM caturthasyaiva neShyate //


saprAdeshe 'pi vA pucche vistAro dvAdashaM bhavet /
tathA caturthaShaShThAbhyAM namayetprathamaM tu tat //


te dve tu saMhite prAcI dvitIyaM karaNaM hi tat /
tR^itIyamapi ShaDbhAgamaShTabhAgena vardhitam //


dvAviMshatirdviguNitaM tilAnAM cApi viMshatiH /
savisheShashcaturthasya tiryaksatyadhikaM bhavet //


paJNcamaM prAkR^itaM vidyAt ShaShThasya vikR^itAstrayaH /
ShaShThasya pArshvaM tryadhikaM karNaH ShaTtriMshadaShTabhiH //


saptamAShTamayoH pArshvamUnatriMshamiheShyate /

AyAmashvApi ShaTtriMshaccaturdashatilaiHsaha //


caturthAdyAstu vikR^itAH pucche caivAtmani kShipet /

aShTAdashAN^gulaM pucche shayayoranyadAtmani //


karavindIyA vyAkhyA

kaN^ka -- tau

kaN^kAlajau pakShivisheShau /
kaN^kavaccIyate alajavaccIyat iti kaN^kacidalajacitau shyenacitA vyAkhyAtau /
tayorvimAneShTakAkaraNopadhAnAni shyenasyeva kAryANItyarthaH /
mukhyatvAt pUrvashyeneneti kecit /
AnantaryAddvitIyashyenenetyanye /
avisheShAdubhAbhyAmityapare /
uktaM shyenasvarUpamanubhAShate atraiva shiraso bhAvapratipAdanArtham //


eva r-- thyAt

evamivahIti gatam /
shyenasya varShIyAMsau dIrghatarau pucchAdvakrau pakShau sannataM pucchaM AtmasamIpe hrasIya agre vyastaM dIrgha AtmA na samacaturashraH amaNDalaH na maNDalAkAraH ---- IShanmaNDalaH /
na vA shirash ca vidyate /
taccApi na maNDalaM nApi samacaturashram /
evamiva shyeno loke dR^ishyate /
etAvadeva shyenasAdR^ishyamagneH /
kutaH? shrutisAmarthyAt -- sAmarthyamabhidhAnashaktiH /
etAvadeva shyenashrutyA vidhIyate /
yadetadvakrapakShatA vyastapucchatA dIrghAtmatAmaNDalatA sashiraskatA ca /
tasmAt kaN^kAlajAvapi tadAkArau cetavyAvityarthaH //


ashira -- nAt

ashirasko vA shyenaH anAmnAnAt /
nahi pakShapucchAtmagatavakratAdivacchirasa AmnAnamasti /
shyenavidhAnasAmarthyAcchiraso vidhAnamastIti gamyata iti kecit /
vayasAM vA eSha pratimayA cIyata iti prakR^itAvapi pakShAdivat shirovidhAnaM prasajyet /
naiSha doShaH /
tatra hi pakShapacchavidhAnaM parisaMkhyAnArtham /
tarhyatrApi taccodakAgatameveti tasmAt sashiraskaHshyenaH /
kiJNca vij~nAyate ca kaN^kacitaM shIrShaNvantaM cinvIteti /
yadi codakaprAptayA kaN^ke shiro vidyate tatkathaM brUyAt brAhyaNaM kaN^kacitaM shIrShaNvantaM cinvIteti? na brUyAdevetyarthaH /
tasmAdashiraskaH shyenaH /
kaN^ke shirovidhAnAt /
tathA te vayomAtrasAdR^ishye prakR^ite prApte shyenaprAptividhAnasAmarthyAdeva shyene shiro 'pyastIti gamyate /
"trivR^itte agne shiraH' ityAdinA shirasyupadhAnadarghanAcca /
atastayorvikalpa iti manvAnaH vAshabdaM brUte /
tatra kaN^kaHshyeno 'laja iti saN^kalapamAtrabhedaH nAkAre /
dAkShAyaNayaj~nAdivat ashiraskaHshyena ityucyate //


prAkR^i ---- rAt

prakR^itivadeva pakShau vakrau pucchAt sannataM vakrapakSho vyastapuccha iti vikArashravaNAt /
AtmA tu yathA prakR^ityA /
yadvA yathAprakR^itiravikR^itaH samacaturashraH catuShpuruSha ityarthaH /
avikArAt -- na hi vikAraH shrUyate /
pakShapuccheShu vikAragrahaNaM nAtmani /
tasmAt prAkR^ita evAtmA /
aratninArdhaprAdeshena ca ekaikaM pakShaM pravardhayet /
yadyapi prAkR^itau pakShAvityuktaM tathApi pucchasyAprAkR^itatvashraNAduktaprakArA puruShamAtratA gamyate /
tasmAtpucche prAdeshamupadhAya pakShayorvibhajediti kecinmanyante /
kecitpakShayoH prakR^ititvavidhAnAdAtmano 'vikAratvAcca pucchaM saprAdeshaM manyante /
ubhayasmin pakShe 'pyuktaprakAreNAbhyunneyA ityAcAryo manyate /
atra pucchasyAprakR^ititvapakShe prathamadvitIyakaraNAnAM vikAraH /
itarathA teShAmapi karaNAnyucyante /
caturthaShaShThAbhyAM prathamaM karaNaM yathArdhatrayodashavyAsaM bhavati tathA prajambhayet /
te dve prAcI saMhite /
tadditIyaM prathamasya ShaDbhAgamaN^gulaM tR^itIyam /
upadhAnamucyate ---- dakShiNe pakShe aShTAcatvAriMshatprathamA

udIcIstathottare dakShiNAH /
pucche 'shiraskapakShoktameva /
triMshadAtmani /
shroNyostisrAstisraH paJNcamya udagAyatAH dakShiNAyatAsh ca /
tAsAM purastAcatur(thAr)thInAmardheShTakAH sapta rItayaH /
tAH ShaTpaJNcAshat /
tAsAM purastAdaShTau paJNcamyaH /
shroNyaMseShu catasraH /
paJNcamIrakShNayAbhindyAt /
dvishata eSha prastAraH /
dvitIyaprastAre catasrashcatasro dvitIyAshcatasrashcatasra AtmAnamaShTabhAgAvetAH /
pakSheShTakAbhiH prAcIbhiH pakShau pracchAdayet /
ekaikasmin pakShe ShaTtriMshat /
pucche tu pUrvavaddvAdasha saptamyastrayodashAShTamyash ca /
shroNyaMseShu dve dve paJNcamyau prAcyau /
AtmasheShe caturthInA maShTeShTakAH prAcyaHsapta rItayaH /
tR^itIyapaJNcamarItyormadhye catasrashcaturthIruddhR^itya triMshataM ShaShTimekAM paJNcamImupadadhyAt /
tAsAmekatra ShoDasha ShaShTiriti /
tatra caturdasha ekatra paJNcamI /
eSha dvishataH prastAraH /
sapradeshapakShe pucche puruShavyAsaM prAdeshapuruShaM pratIcInamAyacchet /
tasya dakShiNato 'nyamuttaratashvetyAdinA pucchaM kuryAt /
pakShau prakR^itAveva /
karaNavisheSho yathA tiryagR^ijutvena dvAdashAN^gulaM bhavati tathA prathamaM karaNaM prajambhayet /
te dve prAjItyAdinA dvitIyam /
tR^itIyasyApi ShaDbAgamaShTabhAgena vardhitam /
caturthAdIni dvividhAni -- pucchacaturthe trayastriMshadahgulavistAraM /
tasya savisheShaH catushvatvAriMshadaN^gulayaH viMshati tilAdhikAH /
paJNcamamardhasaptadashaN^gulavyAsam /
ShaShThasya pArshvaM trayastriMshadaN^gulakam /
tAHShaTtriMshadaN^gulayaH /
sAShTamayoHsa eva vyAsaH /
pArshvamAnyAvakShNayAvasthite ekonatriMshadaN^gule /
AyAmaHShaTtriMshadaN^gulayaH caturdasha tilAsh ca /
pucchApyayavishayayoraShTAdashAN^gulam /
pucche paJNcadashAN^gulamAtmatilacaturthyAdayo vikR^itAH puccha upadheyAH /
prAkR^ita evAtmani upadhAnavidhiH /
sa eSha dvitIyashyenaH /
vikR^ite tatroktakaraNAnyevamunnIya kR^itvA cetavyam //


sundararAjIyA vyAkhyA

vyatyA -- cikIrShet

kaN^ka -- khyAtau

"kaN^kacitaM shIrShaNvantaM cinvIta yaH kAmayeta shIrShaNvAnamuShmin loke syAmiti' /
alajacitaM cinvIta catuHsItaM pratiShThAkAma' iti shrutAvagnI shyenacitA pUrveNottareNa vA vyAkhyAtau /
athoktasyaiva shyenacitaH prakArAntaraM vidhitsan uktau tAvatprakArau yuktatarAviti darshayitumAha --

evamiva ---- marthyAt

yathAsmAbhiruktaM evamiva hi patataH shyenasya pakShau pucchAdvarShIyAMsau vakrau ca madhyataH pucchaM ca sannatamapyayapradeshe AtmA ca AmaNDalaH IShanmaNDalarUpaH shirashvaivaM bhavati /
tasmAt---- tacchabdashruteH yacchabdAdhyAhAraH kAryaH /
yasmAdarthe vA hishabdaH /
yasmAdevaMrUpaH shyenasya pakShapucchAdiH pratyakSheNa dR^ishyate tatmAt shyenacitaM cinvIteti shrutisAmarthyAdevaMrUpapakShapucchAtmashiraskaH shyenacidityukta ityarthaH //


ashi ------ mnAmAt

ashirasko vA shyenacidbhavitumarhati /
anAmnAnAt; na(hi)ca shyenacitprakaraNe shira AmnAyate /
Atmano 'pyavikArasyaitadupalakShaNam /
ashiraska (tve) kalpe pramANAntaramastItyAha----

vij~nA -- brUyAt

yadi shyenAkR^itividhAnamAtreNaiva sashiraskatvaM bhavet /
tarhi kaN^kacito 'pi bhavedeva /
tathA ca tatra shIrShaNvantamiti visheSho na vaktavyaHsyAdityarthaH //


yadyashiraskastarhyasya kiM rUpamityAha ----

prAkR^itau -- shravaNAt

prAkR^itAveva pakShau pucchau ShaDaratniM paJNcAratniM vA /
tau dvipuruShAM rajjumubhayataHpAshAmityuktaprakAreNa vakrIkartavyau /
kecittu pUrvoktAyAma (bhAvAt) mArgAt ShaShTishatAN^gulayA rajjvA saMnamana (mapI)micchanti /
pucchaM ca prAkR^itameva sannataM ardhapuruShavyAsam /
puruShaM prAdeshAdhikaM pratIcInamAyacchet /
tasya dakShiNato 'nyamityAdi pUrvavat /
prAdeshapravR^iddhayabhAve pUrvavadeva /
vikArashravaNAditi ---- vakrapakSho vyastapuccho bhavatIti vacanAdityarthaH /

yathA kArAt

catuH puruShaH samacaturashra eva shyenacityAtmA vikArasyAshravaNAt

kapardibhAShyam

___________________________________________________________


yatho etac cheyanacitaM cinvIteti | yAvadAmnAnasArUpyaM tad vyAkhyAtam  || ˘p¡us_21.5 ||

___________________________________________________________



tatra yAvadAmnAnameva sArUpyaM grAhyam /
jAtivAcakAnAM shabdAnAM kimapi sAmAnyameva pravR^ittinimittaM dR^ishyate /
yathA gaurvAhIka iti /
evamatrApi yAvadAmnAnameva sArUpyaM gR^ihItvA shyenashabdo vartate /
tattu sArUyaM vyAkhyAtaM vakrapakSha ityAdinA //


___________________________________________________________


tristAvo 'gnir bhavatIty ashvamedhe vij~nAyate  || ˘p¡us_21.6 ||

___________________________________________________________



___________________________________________________________


tatra sarvAbyAso 'visheShAt  || ˘p¡us_21.7 ||

___________________________________________________________



tatra nAratniprAdeshasya saptavidhasyAbhyAsaH /
kutaH? avisheShAt; na hi kashvidvisheSho 'trAmnAyate /
tasmAtsarvasyAvR^ittiH /

___________________________________________________________


dIrghacaturashrANAM samAsena pakShapucchAnAM samAsa uktaH  || ˘p¡us_21.8 ||

___________________________________________________________


dIrghacaturashrANAM pakShapucchAnAM samAsavidhirUktaH /
"yadanyatsaptabhya' ityAdinA vidhAsaptamakaraNImityAdinA (ca) vA /
veNutrikaraNyA vA viharedityarthaH //


___________________________________________________________


ekaviMsho 'gnirbhavatIty ashvamedhe vij~nAyate  || ˘p¡us_21.9 ||

___________________________________________________________



gatametat /

___________________________________________________________


tatra puruShAbhyAso nAratniprAdeshAnAM saN^khyAsaMyogAt saN^khyAsaMyogAt  || ˘p¡us_21.10 ||

___________________________________________________________



samAptaH shulbaprashnaH



tatra puruShAbhyAsaH nAratniprAdeshAnAM /
kutaH? saMkhyAsaMyogAt -- ekaviMsha iti /
na saptavidha ityatrApi saMkhyA vidhIyate /
vAkyAntareNa tatra aratniprAdeshA nivishante /
na tatra saptasaMkhyAyAM nivishante /
tasmAtsaMkhyAsaMyogAt puruShAbhyAsa eva nAratniprAdeshAnAm /
tatra shloko bhavati ----

trividhena naraM proktaM tristAvati vibhAva (soH)sau /

eka (viMshe) vidhe tatau nyUnaM tilAnAM caiva sapta (bhiH)tiH //


dviruktirmaN^galArthA /

ityApastambasUtravivaraNe kapardisvAmibhAShye

shulbAkhyaprashne ShaShThaH paTalaH

------------

karavindIyA vyAkhyA

a(ya)tho -- khyAtam

shyenacitamiti vihitaM yatprakAraM yAvaccAsyAmnAnasArUpyaM mAnavihitaM shyenasArUpyaM tatsarvaM vyAkhyAtam /
tatra vakrapakShAdiguNairAmnAtena yacchayenasya sArUpyamuktaM; shyenAgagnerardhadashamA aratnaya ityAdinA cayanaprakAra uktaH, tena uktau kaN^kAlajau syAtAmityarthaH //


trisyA -- ShAt

AshvamedhikAgnestristAvavidhau sAratniprAdeshAbhyAsaH na puruShamAtrasya; visheShAbhAvAt /
avisheSheNa prAkR^itAgnij~natraiguNyavidhAnAdityarthaH //


dIrgha ---- ktaH

dIrghacaturashrANAM samAsa ityuktam /
evaM dve dIrghacaturashre samasyete; tannimitto nirhrAso vivR^iddhirveti /
yAvadicchan dIrghacaturashrANi samasyoditi /
tena tristAve 'gnau prathamaviharaNena samAsa uktaH //


eka -- gAt

ashvamedhe ekaviMshAgnishrutau puruShANAmevAbhyAsaH nAratniprAdeshAnAm /
"saptavidho vAva prAkR^ito 'gniriti' saptasaMkhyA pR^ithaksaMniveshanI /
samAnajAtIyeShu puruSheShveva saMyuktaH nAratnayAdiShu /
aratniprAdeshAstvaratninA dakShiNata iti vAkyena svarUpamAtreNa vihitA nArdhasaMkhyayA /
ataH prakR^itau puruShANAmeva saMkhyA saMyogAdashvamedhe 'pyekaviMshAgnau puruShANAmeva saMkhyAsaMyogo yukta iti aratniprAdeshAstvanabhyastA bhaveyuH /
puruShAbyAsAdanantaramaratninA dakShiNata iti kuryAdityarthaH /
etaduktaM bhavati -- tristAve ekaviMshaprastAradvayavidhestristAva ekaviMsha evAgniH brAhnaNadarshanAt /
dvAdasha dasha vA syAt /
dviruktiH prasnaparisamAptidyotanArthA //


iti shrIkaravindasvAmikR^itAyAM shulbapradIpikAyAM ShaShThaH paTalaH

----

sundararAjIyA vyAkhyA

nanu siraso 'bhAve shyenAkR^iterapUrvatvAt shyenacitaM cinvIteti vidhivAkyenaiva virodhaprasaN^gaH; tatrAha ------

a(ya)tho -- khyAtam

yadetacchayenacitaM cinvItoti; yattena yAvadAmAnAtam vakrapakSho vyastapucchaH iti vihitasArUpyamuktaM; anyathA pakShapucchavikAravidherAnarthakyaprasaN^gAditi bhAvaH /
asmin pakShe iShTakAnAM karaNAni dvipUruShayA rajjvA pakShasaMnamane puruShasya caturthAyAmaM paJNcamavyAsaM yathAyoganataM tat prathamaM; tasyakaisarNo 'ShTAdashAN^gulaH sapAdaikapaJNcadashAN^gulo 'nyaH /
dve dve pUrvavatsaMhite tat dvitIyam /
prathama paJNcame karaNe saMhite tR^itIyam; caturthapaJNcamaShaShThAni pUrvashyenacidvadeva /
pucche yAH ShaShThIcaturthyaH upadheyAstAsAmanye karaNe /
tatra caturthyAM pArshve pUrvavadeva ekA tirya«bAnI trayastriMshadaN^gulA anyA sArdhacatushvatvAriMshadaN^gulA ShaShThayAstu paJNcadashamekaM phalakaM /
trayastriMshadaN^gulaM dvitIyaM ShaTtriMshakaM sAShTatilaM tR^itIyam /
saptamasya tirya«bhAnyAvaratnimAtrau /
pArshvena (nava) viMshatyaN^gule /
karNashvaikaH /
(anyaH karNaH paJNcacatvAriMshadaN^gulaH ekAdashatilonaH /
aShTaprasya navaviMshake pArshve /
dvAdashikAShaTtriMshike tirashvayau shiraso 'bhAvAnnavamaM karaNaM na bhavati /
aratniprAdeshAbhAve puccheShTakAH pUrvashyenavadeva) /
pakShasthAnAJNca tadanuguNaM namanam /
upadhAne ca pakShayoH prathamA ashItirudIcyaH pucchaM pUrvashyenavadeva /
pucchApyayasthacaturthyoraShTAdashAN^gulam /
pucche pUrvashyenavadeva /
pucche paJNcadashAN^gulamAtmani /
AtmanyudIcyo nava rItayaH /
udIcIbhiriShTakAbhiH /
tAsAM madhyamAH sapta /
aShTAbhiH caturthIbhiH caturtharItyAM dakShiNarItau tataH ShaShTayashcatasraH dve caturthyau /
evameva ShaShThI rItiH /
shroNyaMseShu catasrashcatasraH ShaShThayaH /
sheShe ShaT paJNcamyaH /
eSha dvishataH prastAraH /
(tatrAshiraskasya shyenacitaH pakShayoH prathameShTakA udIcyo rItayaH /
triMshattriMshat /
pucche tu pUrvavat /
AtmanyudIcyo rItyo nava syuH /
tatrAdyarItigA AdyAsvatasraH ShaShThayR^iH syureva /
evamantyA piShTakAH /
dakShiNottarata ekaikA paJNcamIShTakA /
pucchApyayasthe tanmadhye ukte /
evaM dasheShTakAH antyA api rItaya evaM syuH /
paJNcamyaH madhyato 'dhike /
turayirItyAM caturthyau /
dve catasraH ShaShThikAH /
tatashcaturthyau pUrvavat ShaShThayaH /
catuthyau dve doShTakAH? evaM sheShamagniM caturthIbhiH pUrayet /
evaM navatirAtmasthAH prAstAre dvishateShTakAH) /
aparasmiMshcatasrashcatasraH nirnAmayordvitIyAH /
apyayayosh ca tR^itIyAH /
pakShayoH sheShe ShaTpaJNcAshat prathamAH prAcyaH pucche pUrvavat /
saptamyo 'ShTamyash ca Atmani nava rItyaH /
prAcyaH prAcIbhiriShTakAbhiH /
tatra pakShApyayasthAnAM pashcAtpurastAcca paJNcapaJNcamyaH ShaTca ShaShThayaH /
tA dakShiNottararItimadhye (saptarItyaH pUrvaprastAravat /
dvitIyaShaShThayo (dvitIyAShTamyo) rItyormadhye) ShoDashaShoDasha ShaShThayaH /
(tA dakShiNottare rItimadhye pUrvaprastAravat /
dvitIyAShTamyo rItyormadhyeShoDashaShoDasha ShaShThayaH /
evaM dvishataH prastAraH /
tatrAparasmin prastAre pakShe dvitIyAH /
pakShamadhyataH dvitIyAH /
apyaye sheShe prathamAH /
evamuttarapakShe prAcyaH /
imAH sarvA dvisaptatiH /
athAtmani prAcyo nava rItyasyuH /
AdyAyAM paJNcamIdvitIyam //

AdityapakShApyayagA dve ShaShThayau paJNcamI tathA /
paJNcamyekAntyarItyAto dve ShaShThayAvapyayaH puraH //

ShaShTayAvekA paJNcamI syAddvitIyasyAmathAvalau /
madhye ShoDasha ShaShThayaH syurevamaShTamarItigAH //


caturthaShaShTharItyau tu prathamottaravattathA /
AtmasheShaM caturthIbhiH ...... pucchagocarAH //


saptamyo dvAdashAShTamyastrayodasha ca pUrvavat /
evaM dvitIyaprastAro dvitIye 'ShTaka iShyate //)

kecitttu -- yathA prakR^ityeti vacanAdiShTakA api /
(Atmani prakR^itivadevetyAhuH /
tathA prathamakaraNasya pArshve catvAriMshadaN^gule /
aratnI eva (tirashvayau) tirya«bhAnyau (ekaH karNaH paJNcaviMshatikaHsaptadashatilaH /
anyastilatrayonaikaShaShThayaN^gulaH) /
dve sahite dvitIyaM (karaNyA aratni) prathamasyAratniprAdeshena yathAyoganatena vardhayet /
tR^itIyaM pucchAnnavamacaturthaShaShThasaptamAShTamAni pUrvavatprakR^itivadAtmana iShTakAH paJNcamabAgIyAH /
tatra prAdeshAH ShaDaN^gulavyAsAH kAryAH /
AtmAni dakShiNata uttarash ca dashA (dhyardhArH) dhyA udagAyatAH /
AtmasheShe paJNcamya udIcyo dasha rItayaH /
madhye dve uddhR^ityAShTAdashAN^gule pucchApyaye dve caturthyau AtmAnamaratninA veti dve abhitashcatasraH ShaDaN^gulavyAsAH /
pucchA pyayasthayoH pashcAtpaJNcArdhyAH prAcyaH /
puccha(visheShAH) sheShaM pUrvavat /
(pakShayostriMshattriMshat prathamA utIcyaH /
eSha dvishataH prastAraH /
aparasmiMstu tisrastisro nirNAmayoH /
dvitIyAH pakShasheShe dvicatvAriMshatprathamAH prAcyaH /
pucchapUrvavat) /
AtmanyudIcyo nava rItayaH /
tA A (tAsAmA) dyantAH (rItiH prAcIbhirardhyAbhiH /
antyAH paJNcamIbhiH madhyamarItInAM paJNcAnAmAdyAH anyAshvArdhyAH) shvatAH prAcyaH dvitIyasya AtyAmuddhR^itya tatrAShTau ShaDaN^gulavyAsAH upadadhyAt tatra pasvAtpurastAcca dve dve udagAyate /
madhye catasraH prAgAyatAH /
aShTamarItyA Adyante(ntye) dvitIyAmantyAM coddhR^itya navanavAShTAN^gulayaH dvishataH prastAraH /
yadA tu samacaturashrAbhirupadhIyante tadApyevameva pakShau /
pucchaM tu pUrvavadeva /
pakShApyaye dve aNUke AtmAnaM prAdeshena prApte 'bhito dve dve ShaDaN^gule etAH ShaDdashabhiH prAdeshaiH parigR^ihNIyAt /
AtmasheShe aratnayaH /
dvishataH prastAraH /
aparasmiMstu sandhyanatarAle paJNcacatvAriMshadaratnayaH /
shroNyaMseShu dvAdashadvAdasha (aNUkAHpAdAH) /
(pAdye) sheShe viMshatiraNUkAH /
Atma(madhya) gatamuddhR^itya navAShTAN^gulAH /
(dvishataH prastAraH) yadA tu ShaShThashatAN^gulayA rajjvA pakShayornamanaM tadA puruShasya paJNcamAyAmaM ShaShThavyAsamekaM vA prathamaM karaNam /
yathAyoganataM tatkarNastrayoviMshatyaN^gulaHsaikaviMshatitilaH /
anyaH saptatriMshaH saikAdashatilaH /
viMshatyaN^gulAyAmaM trayodashatilayuktaM caturdashAN^gulavyAsaM prAJNcaM caturashraM bhUmau likhitvA ShoDashAN^gulayA rajjvobhayataH pAshayA taM pakShavat saMnamayet /
taddva (ttR^itIyaM) devaprathamasya ShaDbAgamaShTabhAgena vardhayet /
yathAyoganatena ta (tatra)t tR^itIyaM /
anyAni pUrvavat /
upadhAne prathame prastAre nirnAmayoH ShaT ShaT dvitIyAH /
pakShasheShe prathamA dvAsaptatirudIcyaH /
pucchamAtmA ca pUrvavat /
shroNyaMseShu dve dve ShaShThayau /
dvishataH prastAraH /
apasmiMstu pakShayoH saptatiH prathamAH /
prAcyaH paJNcapaJNcApyayayoH /
tR^itIyAH pucchAtmanoH pUrvavat /
Atmani tu ShoDasha ShaShThIruddhR^ityAShTau paJNcamIH kShipet /
dvishataH prastAraH /
AtmanaH prakR^itivadiShTakA iti pakShe 'pi tadanuguNA iShTakA draShTavyA //


tri -- yate

"dvistAvAtristAvA vediH' ityatra liN^gasyAvivakShitatvAda gnesh ca vedesh ca vivakShi (vihi) tatvAtsamAsAntaH /
prAkR^itasyaivAgneH saptavidhasyaivAtra triguNatvam /
na tvanantara (guNasya) kR^itasyAbhyAsasya sarvAbhyAso visheSho 'taHsarvasya sAratniprAdeshasyaivAbhyAsaH; tristAvasya vidhau vidhAbhyAsavat puruShANAmiti visheShAshravaNAt /
evamardhatrayoviMshAH puruShA agnirbhavati /
puruShasya trikaraNo veNuHsapaJNcatilonAShTAdashatadvayAN^gulayaH puruShasthAnIyAH //


dIrghacatu -- uktaH

tulyayosh caturashrayor ity atraiva prakAra uktaH /
tirya«bhAnIpArshvamAnyosh ca trikaraNIpArshvamAnI ca //


ekaviM ---- yate

shAkhAntare "ekaviMshatiH puruShaH parimANa' ityekaviMshaH satomor'dhavidhaM paJNcAshadadhyardhAH ityatropadheyaH /
prAyikatvAdastome 'pi //


tatra asaMyogAt

saMkhyA hi tulyajAtIyasya saMkhyAntarasyaiva nivartikA; yathA vidhAbhyAseShviti bhAvaH /
asmin pakShe ardhadvAviMshAH puruShAstatra dve shate tisrashvAN^gulayaH ShaTtilAH puruShasthAnIyo veNuH /
tasya caturthapaJNcamaShaShThadashamA aNUkAratnyUrvasthiprAdeshA avagantavyAH /
aratniprAdeshAbhAve 'pi pakShadvaye 'pyekaviMshatireva puruShAH /
shrImadrAmAyaNe tvaShTAdashapuruShatvamasvamedhAgnerdR^ishyate ----

sa cityo rAjasiMhasya saJNcitaH kushalairdvijaiH /
gArUDo rukmapakSho vai triguNo 'ShTAdashAtmakaH //


iti /
sa tu shAkhAntare (Na) ShaDvidhasyApi kR^ititvadarshanAt /
tristAvo 'vagantavyaH /
uktaM hi ShaDvidhasyApi prakR^ititvaM bodhA yanena -- "ShaDvidhaM saptavidhaM dvAdashavidhaM vA yAvadvidhaM vA ceShyamANo bhavati' iti /
atra trayodashavidhAntAnagnIn citvAshvamedhamArabhate /
sa tataH paramagniM cinvAno dvAviMshatyAdividhameva cinvIta /
na tu pUrvavidham /
na jyAyAsaM citvA kanIyAsaM cinvIta' iti /
atha yo dvAviMshatividhAdUrdhvamapi vidhAmabhyasya tataH paramashvamedhamArabhate yathA triMshadvidhAnte; tasyApyashvamedhAgnistristAvaka ekaviMsho vA tasya prakArAntarAbhAvAt /
tataH paraM tu pUrvakR^itAdArabhyaikattriMshadvidhAdikam eva cinvIta /
pUrveShAM kR^itatvAt; vyaJNjitaM caitatsarvaM bodhAyanena -- "ashvamedhaH prAptashvedAharedata UrdhvAM vidhAmabyasyennetarAnAdriyeta /
atItaM cedAharedAhR^itya kR^itAnte prakR^ityAdadIta' iti //



iti shrI sundararAjIye shulbapradIpe ShaShThaH paTalaH


iti sundararAjIyaM saMpUrNaM samAptaH savyAkhya ApastambIyashulbaprashnaH
